caturdaśa daśa eva tu sahasrāṇi trigartānām narādhipa catvāri tu sahasrāṇi vāsudevasya ye anugāḥ dāryamāṇām camūm dṛṣṭvā bhagadattena māriṣa āhūyamānasya ca taiḥ abhavat hṛdayam dvidhā itas vā vinivarteyam gaccheyam vā yudhiṣṭhiram ekaḥ ratha sahasrāṇi nihantum vāsavī raṇe sa tu saṃvartayām āsa dvaidhībhāvena pāṇḍavaḥ rathena tu ratha agryāṇām akarot tām mṛṣā tadā tatas śata sahasrāṇi śarāṇām nata parvaṇām vyasṛjan arjune rājan saṃśaptaka mahā rathāḥ nā eva kuntī sutaḥ pārthaḥ nā eva kṛṣṇaḥ janārdanaḥ na hayāḥ na rathaḥ rājan dṛśyante sma śaraiḥ citāḥ yadā moham anuprāptaḥ sa svedaḥ ca janārdanaḥ tatas tān prāyaśas pārthaḥ vajra astreṇa nijaghnivān śataśas pāṇayaḥ chinnāḥ sa iṣu jyā tala kārmukāḥ ketavaḥ vājinaḥ sūtāḥ rathinaḥ ca apatan kṣitau druma acala agra ambudharaiḥ sama rūpāḥ su kalpitāḥ hata ārohāḥ kṣitau petuḥ dvipāḥ pārtha śara āhatāḥ vipraviddha kutha valgāḥ chinna bhāṇḍāḥ parāsavaḥ sa ārohāḥ turagāḥ petuḥ mathitāḥ pārtha mārgaṇaiḥ sa ṛṣṭi carma asi nakharāḥ sa mudgara paraśvadhāḥ saṃchinnāḥ bāhavaḥ petuḥ nṛṇām bhallaiḥ kirīṭinā bāla āditya ambuja indūnām tulya rūpāṇi māriṣa saṃchinnāni arjuna śaraiḥ śirāṃsi urvīm prapedire jajvāla alaṃkṛtaiḥ senā patribhiḥ prāṇabhojanaiḥ kṣobhayantam tadā senām dviradam nalinīm iva dhanaṃjayam bhūta gaṇāḥ sādhu sādhu iti apūjayan dṛṣṭvā tat karma pārthasya vāsavasya iva mādhavaḥ tatas saṃśaptakān hatvā bhūyiṣṭham ye vyavasthitāḥ bhagadattāya yāhi iti pārthaḥ kṛṣṇam acodayat saṃjayaḥ uvāca yiyāsataḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ pārthasya aśvān manojavān apraiṣīt hema saṃchannān droṇa anīkāya pāṇḍurān tam prayāntam kuru śreṣṭham svān trātum droṇa tāpitān suśarmā bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdham yuddha arthī pṛṣṭhatas anvayāt tatas śvetahayaḥ kṛṣṇam abravīt ajitam jayaḥ eṣa mām bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdham suśarmā āhvayate acyuta dvaidhībhūtam manaḥ me adya kṛtam saṃśaptakaiḥ idam kim nu saṃśaptakān hanmi svān rakṣāmi ahita arditān yena trigarta adhipatiḥ pāṇḍavam samupāhvayat tatas arjunaḥ suśarmāṇam viddhvā saptabhiḥ āśugaiḥ dhvajam dhanuḥ ca asya tathā kṣurābhyām samakṛntata trigarta adhipateḥ ca api bhrātaram ṣaḍbhiḥ āyasaiḥ sa aśvam sa sūtam tvaritaḥ pārthaḥ praiṣīt yama kṣayam tatas bhujaga saṃkāśām suśarmā śaktim āyasīm cikṣepa arjunam ādiśya vāsudevāya tomaram śaktim tribhiḥ śaraiḥ chittvā tomaram tribhiḥ arjunaḥ suśarmāṇam śara vrātaiḥ mohayitvā nyavartata tam vāsavam iva āyāntam bhūri varṣa śara oghiṇam rājan tāvaka sainyānām na ugram kaḥ cit avārayat na aśaknuvan te saṃsoḍhum sparśam agneḥ iva prajāḥ saṃveṣṭayan anīkāni śara varṣeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ suparṇa pāta vat rājan āyāt prāgjyotiṣam prati yat tadā anāmayat jiṣṇuḥ bharatānām apāyinām dhanuḥ kṣema karam saṃkhye dviṣatām aśru vardhanam kṛte kṣatra vināśāya dhanuḥ āyacchat arjunaḥ tathā vikṣobhyamāṇā sā pārthena tava vāhinī matim kṛtvā raṇe kruddhāḥ vīrāḥ jaya parājaye yathā naḍavanam kruddhaḥ prabhinnaḥ ṣaṣṭihāyanaḥ mṛdnīyāt tadvat āyastaḥ pārthaḥ amṛdnāt camūm tava tam rathena nara vyāghraḥ pratyagṛhṇāt abhīta vat kalpitābhyām yathāśāstram rathena ca gajena ca tatas jīmūta saṃkāśāt nāgāt indraḥ iva abhibhūḥ sa ca api śara varṣam tat śara varṣeṇa vāsaviḥ tatas prāgjyotiṣaḥ rājā śara varṣam nivārya tat śaraiḥ jaghne mahā bāhum pārtham kṛṣṇam ca bhārata codayām āsa tam nāgam vadhāya acyuta pārthayoḥ tam āpatantam dviradam dṛṣṭvā kruddham iva antakam saṃprāptam api nā iyeṣa parāvṛttam mahā dvipam sa āroham mṛtyusāt kartum smaran dharmam dhanaṃjayaḥ sa tu nāgaḥ dvipa rathān hayān ca ārujya māriṣa dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca prāgjyotiṣaḥ vā pārthasya tat me śaṃsa yathātatham saṃjayaḥ uvāca prāgjyotiṣeṇa saṃsaktau ubhau dāśārha pāṇḍavau mṛtyoḥ iva antikam prāptau sarva bhūtāni menire tathā hi śara varṣāṇi pātayati aniśam prabho atha kārṣṇāyasaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pūrṇa kārmuka niḥsṛtaiḥ avidhyat devakīputram hema puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ agni sparśa samāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ bhagadattena coditāḥ nirbhidya devakīputram kṣitim jagmuḥ śarāḥ tatas tasya pārthaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā śarāvāpam nihatya ca saḥ arka raśmi nibhān tīkṣṇān tomarān vai caturdaśa tatas prāgjyotiṣaḥ śaktim hema daṇḍām ayasmayīm tatas chatram dhvajam ca eva chittvā rājñaḥ arjunaḥ śaraiḥ bhagadattaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ vyasṛjat tomarān mūrdhni śvetāśvasya unnanāda ca parivṛttam kirīṭam tam yamayan eva phalgunaḥ su dṛṣṭaḥ kriyatām loke iti rājānam abravīt evam uktaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ śara varṣeṇa pāṇḍavam tasya pārthaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā tūṇīrān saṃnikṛtya ca abhimantrya aṅkuśam kruddhaḥ vyasṛjat pāṇḍava urasi urasā pratijagrāha pārtham saṃchādya keśavaḥ tatas arjunaḥ klānta manāḥ keśavam pratyabhāṣata iti uktvā puṇḍarīkākṣa pratijñām svām na rakṣasi yadi aham vyasanī vā syām aśaktaḥ vā nivāraṇe sa bāṇaḥ sa dhanuḥ ca aham sa sura asura mānavān śaktaḥ lokān imān jetum tat ca api viditam tava śṛṇu guhyam idam pārtha yathā vṛttam purā anagha caturmūrtiḥ aham śaśvat loka trāṇa artham udyataḥ ātmānam pravibhajya iha lokānām hitam ādadhe ekā mūrtiḥ tapaḥ caryām kurute me bhuvi sthitā aparā paśyati jagat kurvāṇam sādhu asādhunī aparā kurute karma mānuṣam lokam āśritā śete caturthī tu aparā nidrām varṣa sahasrikām yā asau varṣa sahasra ante mūrtiḥ uttiṣṭhate mama vara arhebhyaḥ varān śreṣṭhān tasmin kāle dadāti sā tam tu kālam anuprāptam viditvā pṛthivī tadā prāyācata varam yam mām naraka arthāya tam śṛṇu devānām asurāṇām ca avadhyaḥ tanayaḥ astu me upetaḥ vaiṣṇava astreṇa tat me tvam dātum arhasi evam varam aham śrutvā jagatyāḥ tanaye tadā amogham astram adadam vaiṣṇavam tat aham purā narakasya abhirakṣā artham na enam kaḥ cit vadhiṣyati anena astreṇa te guptaḥ sutaḥ para bala ardanaḥ bhaviṣyati durādharṣaḥ sarva lokeṣu sarvadā tathā iti uktvā gatā devī kṛta kāmā manasvinī sa ca api āsīt durādharṣaḥ narakaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ tasmāt prāgjyotiṣam prāptam tat astram pārtha māmakam na asya avadhyaḥ asti lokeṣu sa indra rudreṣu māriṣa yathā aham jaghnivān pūrvam hita artham narakam tathā evam uktaḥ tatas pārthaḥ keśavena mahātmanā bhagadattam śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sahasā samavākirat tatas pārthaḥ mahā bāhuḥ asaṃbhrāntaḥ mahā manāḥ samāsādya tu tam nāgam bāṇaḥ vajraḥ iva acalam sa tu viṣṭabhya gātrāṇi dantābhyām avanim yayau nadan ārta svaram prāṇān utsasarja mahā dvipaḥ tatas candra ardha bimbena śareṇa nata parvaṇā bibheda hṛdayam rājñaḥ bhagadattasya pāṇḍavaḥ sa bhinna hṛdayaḥ rājā bhagadattaḥ kirīṭinā śarāsanam śarān ca eva gatāsuḥ pramumoca ha śirasaḥ tasya vibhraṣṭaḥ papāta ca vara aṅkuśaḥ nāla tāḍana vibhraṣṭam palāśam nalināt iva sa hema mālī tapanīya bhāṇḍāt papāta nāgāt giri saṃnikāśāt su puṣpitaḥ māruta vega rugṇaḥ mahīdhara agrāt iva karṇikāraḥ tatas aparān tava jaya kāṅkṣiṇaḥ narān babhañja vāyuḥ balavān drumān iva saṃjayaḥ uvāca hatvā prāgjyotiṣam pārthaḥ pradakṣiṇam avartata ārchetām arjunam saṃkhye bhrātarau vṛṣaka acalau avidhyetām mahā vegaiḥ niśitaiḥ āśugaiḥ bhṛśam vṛṣakasya hayān sūtam dhanuḥ chatram ratham dhvajam tilaśas vyadhamat pārthaḥ saubalasya śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas arjunaḥ śara vrātaiḥ nānā praharaṇaiḥ api gāndhārān vyākulān cakre saubala pramukhān punar tatas pañcaśatān vīrān gāndhārān udyata āyudhān prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya kruddhaḥ bāṇaiḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avatīrya mahā bhujaḥ tau eka ratham ārūḍhau bhrātarau vṛṣaka acalau śara varṣeṇa bībhatsum avidhyetām punar punar syālau tava mahātmānau rājānau vṛṣaka acalau bhṛśam nijaghnatuḥ pārtham indram vṛtra balau iva labdha lakṣyau tu gāndhārau ahatām pāṇḍavam punar nidāgha vārṣikau māsau lokam gharmāmbubhiḥ yathā saṃśliṣṭa aṅgau sthitau rājan jaghāna eka iṣuṇā arjunaḥ tau rathāt siṃha saṃkāśau lohita akṣau mahā bhujau gatāsū petatuḥ vīrau sodaryau eka lakṣaṇau yaśaḥ daśa diśaḥ puṇyam gamayitvā vyavasthitau dṛṣṭvā vinihatau saṃkhye mātulau apalāyinau bhṛśam mumucuḥ aśrūṇi putrāḥ tava viśām pate nihatau bhrātarau dṛṣṭvā māyā śata viśāradaḥ kṛṣṇau saṃmohayan māyām vidadhe śakuniḥ tatas laguḍa ayaḥ guḍa aśmānaḥ śataghnyaḥ ca sa śaktayaḥ gadā parigha nistriṃśa śūla mudgara paṭṭiśāḥ sa kampana ṛṣṭi nakharāḥ musalāni paraśvadhāḥ kṣurāḥ kṣurapra nālīkāḥ vatsadantāḥ trisaṃdhinaḥ cakrāṇi viśikhāḥ prāsāḥ vividhāni āyudhāni ca khara uṣṭra mahiṣāḥ siṃhāḥ vyāghrāḥ sṛmara cillikāḥ ṛkṣāḥ sālāvṛkāḥ gṛdhrāḥ kapayaḥ atha sarīsṛpāḥ vividhāni ca rakṣāṃsi kṣudhitāni arjunam prati visṛjan iṣu jālāni sahasā tāni atāḍayat te hanyamānāḥ śūreṇa pravaraiḥ sāyakaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ viruvantaḥ mahā rāvān vineśuḥ sarvatas hatāḥ tasmāt ca tamasaḥ vācaḥ krūrāḥ pārtham abhartsayan tat tamaḥ astreṇa mahatā jyotiṣeṇa arjunaḥ avadhīt hate tasmin jala oghāḥ tu prādurāsan bhayānakāḥ ambhasaḥ tasya nāśa artham āditya astram atha arjunaḥ prāyuṅkta ambhaḥ tatas tena prāyaśas astreṇa śoṣitam evam bahuvidhāḥ māyāḥ saubalasya kṛtāḥ kṛtāḥ tathā hatāsu māyāsu trastaḥ arjuna śara āhataḥ apāyāt javanaiḥ aśvaiḥ śakuniḥ prākṛtaḥ yathā abhyavarṣat śara ogheṇa kauravāṇām anīkinīm sā hanyamānā pārthena putrasya tava vāhinī dvaidhībhūtā mahā rāja gaṅgā iva āsādya parvatam ke cit duryodhanam rājan ardyamānāḥ kirīṭinā gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣaḥ śrutaḥ dakṣiṇatas mayā śaṅkha dundubhi nirghoṣam vāditrāṇām ca nisvanam gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣaḥ vyatikramya aspṛśat divam tatas punar dakṣiṇatas saṃgrāmaḥ citra yodhinām nānāvidhāni anīkāni putrāṇām tava bhārata arjunaḥ vyadhamat kāle divi iva abhrāṇi mārutaḥ tam vāsavam iva āyāntam bhūri varṣa śara oghiṇam mahā iṣvāsam nara vyāghram na ugram kaḥ cit avārayat te hanyamānāḥ pārthena tvadīyāḥ vyathitāḥ bhṛśam te arjunena śarāḥ muktāḥ kaṅka patrāḥ tanu chidaḥ śalabhāḥ iva saṃpetuḥ saṃvṛṇvānāḥ diśaḥ daśa turagam rathinam nāgam padātim api māriṣa na ca dvitīyam vyasṛjat kuñjara aśva nareṣu saḥ pṛthak eka śara ārugṇāḥ nipetuḥ te gatāsavaḥ hataiḥ manuṣyaiḥ turagaiḥ ca sarvatas śara abhivṛṣṭaiḥ dviradaiḥ ca pātitaiḥ tadā śva gomāyu baḍa abhināditam vicitram āyodha śiraḥ babhūva ha pitā sutam tyajati suhṛd varam suhṛd tathā eva putraḥ pitaram śara āturaḥ sva rakṣaṇe kṛta matayaḥ tadā janāḥ tyajanti vāhān api pārtha pīḍitāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca teṣu anīkeṣu bhagneṣu pāṇḍu putreṇa saṃjaya calitānām drutānām ca katham āsīt manaḥ hi vaḥ anīkānām prabhagnānām vyavasthānam a paśyatām duṣkaram pratisaṃdhānam tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca tathā api tava putrasya priya kāmāḥ viśām pate yaśaḥ pravīrāḥ lokeṣu rakṣantaḥ droṇam anvayuḥ samudyateṣu śastreṣu saṃprāpte ca yudhiṣṭhire sātyakeḥ ca eva śūrasya dhṛṣṭadyumnasya ca abhibho droṇam droṇam iti krūrāḥ pāñcālāḥ samacodayan droṇam droṇam iti hi eke mā droṇam iti ca apare kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca droṇa dyūtam avartata yam yam sma bhajate droṇaḥ pāñcālānām ratha vrajam tatra tatra sma pāñcālyaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ atha dhīyate vīrāḥ samāsadan vīrān agacchan bhīravaḥ parān akampanīyāḥ śatrūṇām babhūvuḥ tatra pāṇḍavāḥ akampayan tu anīkāni smarantaḥ kleśam ātmanaḥ te tu amarṣa vaśam prāptāḥ hrīmantaḥ sattva coditāḥ tyaktvā prāṇān nyavartanta ghnantaḥ droṇam mahā āhave ayasām iva saṃpātaḥ śilānām iva ca abhavat dīvyatām tumule yuddhe prāṇaiḥ amita tejasām dṛṣṭa pūrvam mahā rāja śruta pūrvam atha api vā prākampata iva pṛthivī tasmin vīra avasādane pravartatā bala oghena mahatā bhāra pīḍitā samāsādya tu pāṇḍūnām anīkāni sahasraśas droṇena caratā saṃkhye prabhagnāni śitaiḥ śaraiḥ teṣu pramathyamāneṣu droṇena adbhuta karmaṇā paryavārayat āsādya droṇam senāpatiḥ svayam tat adbhutam abhūt yuddham droṇa pāñcālyayoḥ tadā śara sphuliṅgaḥ cāpa arciḥ dahan kakṣam iva analaḥ tam dahantam anīkāni droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān pūrva abhibhāṣī su ślakṣṇam smayamānaḥ abhyabhāṣata nīla kim bahubhiḥ dagdhaiḥ tava yodhaiḥ śara arciṣā tam padma nikara ākāram padma patra nibha īkṣaṇam vyākośa padma ābha mukham nīlaḥ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ droṇāyaneḥ śiraḥ kāyāt dhartum aicchat patatri vat tasya udyata aseḥ su nasam śiraḥ kāyāt sa kuṇḍalam bhallena apāharat drauṇiḥ smayamānaḥ iva anagha saṃpūrṇa candra ābha mukhaḥ padma patra nibha īkṣaṇaḥ tatas pravivyathe senā pāṇḍavī bhṛśam ākulā acintayan ca te sarve pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ katham naḥ vāsaviḥ trāyāt śatrubhyaḥ iti māriṣa dakṣiṇena tu senāyāḥ kurute kadanam balī saṃśaptaka avaśeṣasya nārāyaṇa balasya ca saṃjayaḥ uvāca pratighātam tu sainyasya na amṛṣyata vṛkodaraḥ saḥ abhinat bāhlikam ṣaṣṭyā karṇam ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ tasya droṇaḥ śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ tīkṣṇa dhāraiḥ ayasmayaiḥ jīvita antam abhiprepsuḥ marmaṇi āśu jaghāna ha karṇaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ aśvatthāmā ca saptabhiḥ droṇam pañcāśatā iṣūṇām karṇam ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ duryodhanam dvādaśabhiḥ drauṇim ca aṣṭābhiḥ āśugaiḥ ārāvam tumulam kurvan abhyavartata tān raṇe tasmin saṃtyajati prāṇān mṛtyu sādhāraṇīkṛte ajātaśatruḥ tān yodhān bhīmam trāta iti acodayat yuyudhāna prabhṛtayaḥ mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau te sametya su saṃrabdhāḥ sahitāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ mahā iṣvāsa varaiḥ guptam droṇa anīkam bibhitsavaḥ samāpetuḥ mahā vīryāḥ bhīma prabhṛtayaḥ rathāḥ tān pratyagṛhṇāt avyagraḥ droṇaḥ api rathinām varaḥ mahā balān atirathān vīrān samara śobhinaḥ bāhyam mṛtyu bhayam kṛtvā tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavān yayuḥ āsīt śakti asi saṃpātaḥ yuddham āsīt paraśvadhaiḥ nikṛṣṭam asi yuddham ca babhūva kaṭuka udayam kuñjarāṇām ca saṃghātaiḥ yuddham āsīt su dāruṇam apatat kuñjarāt anyaḥ hayāt anyaḥ tu avākśirāḥ naraḥ bāṇena nirbhinnaḥ rathāt anyaḥ ca māriṣa śiraḥ pradhvaṃsayām āsa vakṣasi ākramya kuñjaraḥ apare api aparān jaghnuḥ vāraṇāḥ patitān narān viṣāṇaiḥ ca avanim gatvā vyabhindan rathinaḥ bahūn nara antraiḥ ke cid apare viṣāṇa ālagna saṃsravaiḥ babhramuḥ śataśas nāgāḥ mṛdnantaḥ śataśas narān kāṃsya āyasa tanutrāṇān nara aśva ratha kuñjarān patitān pothayām cakruḥ dvipāḥ sthūla naḍān iva gṛdhra patra adhivāsāṃsi śayanāni narādhipāḥ hrīmantaḥ kāla saṃpakvāḥ su duḥkhāni adhiśerate yuga ardham chinnam ādāya pradudrāva tathā hayaḥ sa asiḥ bāhuḥ nipatitaḥ śiraḥ chinnam sa kuṇḍalam gajena ākṣipya balinā rathaḥ saṃcūrṇitaḥ kṣitau rathinā tāḍitaḥ nāgaḥ nārācena apatat vyasuḥ sa ārohaḥ ca apatat vājī gajena ātāḍitaḥ bhṛśam hā tāta hā putra sakhe kva asi tiṣṭha kva dhāvasi upāśāmyat rajaḥ bhaumam bhīrūn kaśmalam āviśat āsīt keśa parāmarśaḥ muṣṭi yuddham ca dāruṇam nakhaiḥ dantaiḥ ca śūrāṇam a dvīpe dvīpam icchatām sa dhanuḥ ca aparasya api sa śaraḥ sa aṅkuśaḥ tathā anyaḥ prāptasya ca anyasya śiraḥ kāyāt apāharat śabdam abhyadravat ca anyaḥ śabdāt anyaḥ adravat bhṛśam svān anyaḥ atha parān anyaḥ jaghāna niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ giri śṛṅga upamaḥ ca atra nārācena nipātitaḥ mātaṅgaḥ nyapatat bhūmau nadī rodhe iva uṣṇage adhyatiṣṭhat padā bhūmau saha aśvam saha sārathim śūrān praharataḥ dṛṣṭvā kṛtāstrān rudhira ukṣitān bahūn api āviśan mohaḥ bhīrūn hṛdaya durbalān tatas senāpatiḥ śīghram ayam kālaḥ iti bruvan nitya abhitvaritān eva tvarayām āsa pāṇḍavān kurvantaḥ śāsanam tasya pāṇḍaveyāḥ yaśasvinaḥ gṛhṇīta ādravata anyonyam vibhītāḥ vinikṛntata tatas droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ drauṇiḥ rājā jayadrathaḥ te tu ārya dharma saṃrabdhāḥ durnivāryāḥ durāsadāḥ śara ārtāḥ na juhuḥ droṇam pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha tatas droṇaḥ abhisaṃkruddhaḥ visṛjan śataśas śarān cedi pāñcāla pāṇḍūnām akarot kadanam mahat tasya jyā tala nirghoṣaḥ śuśruve dikṣu māriṣa vajra saṃghāta saṃkāśaḥ trāsayan pāṇḍavān bahūn etasmin antare jiṣṇuḥ hatvā saṃśaptakān balī abyayāt tatra yatra sma droṇaḥ pāṇḍūn pramardati tam śara ogha mahā vartam śoṇita udam mahā hradam tīrṇaḥ saṃśaptakān hatvā pratyadṛśyata phalgunaḥ dīpyamānam apaśyāma tejasā vānaradhvajam sa pāṇḍava yuga anta arkaḥ kurūn api abhyatītapat pradadāha kurūn sarvān arjunaḥ śastra tejasā tāḍyamānāḥ kṣitim jagmuḥ mukta śastrāḥ śara arditāḥ pārtha bāṇa hatāḥ ke cit nipetuḥ vigata asavaḥ teṣām utpatatām kān cit patitān ca parāṅmukhān te viśīrṇa ratha aśva ibhāḥ prāyaśas ca parāṅmukhāḥ kuravaḥ karṇa karṇa iti hā hā iti ca vicukruśuḥ tam ādhirathiḥ ākrandam vijñāya śaraṇa eṣiṇām sa bhārata ratha śreṣṭhaḥ sarva bhārata harṣaṇaḥ śara oghān śara jālena vidudhāva dhanaṃjayaḥ astram astreṇa saṃvārya prāṇadat visṛjan śarān dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca bhīmaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ arjuna astram tu rādheyaḥ saṃvārya śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ teṣām trayāṇām cāpāni ciccheda viśikhaiḥ tribhiḥ te nikṛtta āyudhāḥ śūrāḥ nirviṣāḥ bhujagāḥ iva ratha śaktīḥ samutkṣipya bhṛśam siṃhāḥ iva anadan tāḥ bhuja agraiḥ mahā vegāḥ visṛṣṭāḥ bhujaga upamāḥ dīpyamānāḥ mahā śaktyaḥ jagmuḥ ādhirathim prati nanāda balavān karṇaḥ pārthāya visṛjan śarān arjunaḥ ca api rādheyam viddhvā saptabhiḥ āśugaiḥ karṇāt avarajam bāṇaiḥ jaghāna niśitaiḥ tribhiḥ tatas śatruṃjayam hatvā pārthaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ajihmagaiḥ paśyatām dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām ekena eva kirīṭinā vara asinā karṇa pakṣān jaghāna daśa pañca ca punar sva ratham āsthāya dhanuḥ ādāya ca aparam vivyādha daśabhiḥ karṇam sūtam aśvān ca pañcabhiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api asi varam carma ca ādāya bhāsvaram jaghāna candravarmāṇam bṛhatkṣatram ca pauravam tatas sva ratham āsthāya pāñcālyaḥ anyat ca kārmukam ādāya karṇam vivyādha trisaptatyā nadan raṇe sūtaputram catuḥṣaṣṭyā viddhvā siṃhaḥ iva anadat bhallabhyām sādhu muktābhyām chittvā karṇasya kārmukam punar karṇam tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ bāhvoḥ urasi ca arpayat nimajjamānam rādheyam ujjahruḥ sātyaka arṇavāt nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca sātyakim jugupuḥ raṇe evam eṣa mahā raudraḥ kṣaya artham sarva dhanvinām tāvakānām pareṣām ca tyaktvā prāṇān abhūt raṇaḥ padāti ratha nāga aśvaiḥ gaja aśva ratha pattayaḥ aśvaiḥ aśvāḥ gajaiḥ nāgāḥ rathinaḥ rathibhiḥ saha saṃsaktāḥ samadṛśyanta pattayaḥ ca api pattibhiḥ evam su kalilam yuddham āsīt kravyāda harṣaṇam mahadbhiḥ taiḥ abhītānām yama rāṣṭra vivardhanam nirasta jihvā daśana īkṣaṇāḥ kṣitau kṣayam gatāḥ pramathita varma bhūṣaṇāḥ vipothitāḥ haya gaja pāda tāḍitāḥ bhṛśa ākulāḥ ratha khura nemibhiḥ hatāḥ pramodane śvāpada pakṣi rakṣasām jana kṣaye vartati tatra dāruṇe mahā balāḥ te kupitāḥ parasparam niṣūdayantaḥ praviceruḥ ojasā saṃjayaḥ uvāca rajasvalā bhṛśa udvignā vīkṣamāṇā diśaḥ daśa avahāram tatas kṛtvā bhāradvājasya saṃmate labdha lakṣyaiḥ paraiḥ dīnāḥ bhṛśa avahasitāḥ raṇe ślāghamāneṣu bhūteṣu phalgunasya amitān guṇān abhiśastāḥ iva abhūvan dhyāna mūka tvam āsthitāḥ praṇayāt abhimānāt ca dviṣat vṛddhyā ca durmanāḥ śṛṇvatām sarva bhūtānām saṃrabdhaḥ vākya kovidaḥ tathā hi nā agrahīḥ prāptam samīpe adya yudhiṣṭhiram jighṛkṣataḥ rakṣyamāṇaḥ sa amaraiḥ api pāṇḍavaiḥ varam dattvā mama prītaḥ paścāt vikṛtavān asi āśā bhaṅgam na kurvanti bhaktasya āryāḥ katham cana na arhase mā anyathā jñātum ghaṭamānam tava priye sa sura asura gandharvāḥ sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ na alam lokāḥ raṇe jetum pālyamānam kirīṭinā viśvasṛj yatra govindaḥ pṛtanāriḥ adya eṣām pravaram vīram pātayiṣye mahā ratham na hi ajñātam asādhyam vā tasya saṃkhye asti kim cana droṇena vyāhṛte tu evam saṃśaptaka gaṇāḥ punar āhvayan arjunam saṃkhye dakṣiṇām abhitas diśam tatra arjunasya atha paraiḥ sārdham samabhavat raṇaḥ tādṛśaḥ yādṛśaḥ nā anyaḥ śrutaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ api vā kva cit sa kṛtvā duṣkaram karma hatvā vīrān sahasraśas ṣaṭsu vīreṣu saṃsaktaḥ dauḥśāsani vaśam gataḥ vayam parama saṃhṛṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ śoka karśitāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca raṇe vinihatam śrutvā bhṛśam me dīryate manaḥ dāruṇaḥ kṣatra dharmaḥ ayam vihitaḥ dharma kartṛbhiḥ yatra rājya īpsavaḥ śūrāḥ bāle śastram apātayan bibhitsatā ratha anīkam saubhadreṇa amita ojasā vikrīḍitam yathā saṃkhye tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca tat te kārtsnyena vakṣyāmi śṛṇu rājan samāhitaḥ vikrīḍitam kumāreṇa yathā anīkam bibhitsatā dāva agni abhiparītānām bhūri gulma tṛṇa drume vanaukasām iva araṇye tvadīyānām abhūt bhayam saṃjayaḥ uvāca samare ati ugra karmāṇaḥ karmabhiḥ vyañjita śramāḥ sa kṛṣṇāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pañca devaiḥ api durāsadāḥ sattva karma anvayaiḥ buddhyā prakṛtyā yaśasā śriyā na eva bhūtaḥ na bhavitā kṛṣṇa tulya guṇaḥ pumān satya dharma paraḥ dātā vipra pūjā ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ sadā eva tridivam prāptaḥ rājā kila yudhiṣṭhiraḥ yuga ante ca antakaḥ rājan jāmadagnyaḥ ca vīryavān raṇa sthaḥ bhīmasenaḥ ca kathyante sadṛśāḥ trayaḥ pratijñā karma dakṣasya raṇe gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ upamām na adhigacchāmi pārthasya sadṛśīm kṣitau nakule aprātirūpyam ca śauryam ca niyatāni ṣaḍ śruta gāmbhīrya mādhurya sattva vīrya parākramaiḥ sadṛśaḥ devayoḥ vīraḥ sahadevaḥ kila aśvinoḥ ye ca kṛṣṇe guṇāḥ sphītāḥ pāṇḍaveṣu ca ye guṇāḥ abhimanyau kila ekasthāḥ dṛśyante guṇa saṃcayāḥ karmabhiḥ bhīmasenasya sadṛśaḥ bhīma karmaṇaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca saṃjayaḥ uvāca cakravyūhaḥ mahā rājaḥ ācāryeṇa abhikalpitaḥ tatra śakra upamāḥ sarve rājānaḥ viniveśitāḥ saṃghātaḥ rāja putrāṇām sarveṣām abhavat tadā kṛta abhisamayāḥ sarve suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ rakta ambara dharāḥ sarve sarve rakta vibhūṣaṇāḥ teṣām daśa sahasrāṇi babhūvuḥ dṛḍha dhanvinām karṇa duḥśāsana kṛpaiḥ vṛtaḥ rājā mahā rathaiḥ devarāja upamaḥ śrīmān śveta chatra abhisaṃvṛtaḥ sindhurājaḥ tathā atiṣṭhat śrīmān meruḥ iva acalaḥ sindhurājasya pārśva sthāḥ aśvatthāma purogamāḥ sutāḥ tava mahā rāja triṃśat tridaśa saṃnibhāḥ gāndhāra rājaḥ kitavaḥ śalyaḥ bhūriśravāḥ tathā pārśvatas sindhurājasya vyarājanta mahā rathāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tat anīkam anādhṛṣyam bhāradvājena rakṣitam sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ ārjuniḥ kṣatradharmā ca bṛhatkṣatraḥ ca vīryavān cedipaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca mādrī putrau ghaṭotkacaḥ yudhāmanyuḥ ca vikrāntaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca aparājitaḥ uttamaujāḥ ca durdharṣaḥ virāṭaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ draupadeyāḥ ca saṃrabdhāḥ śaiśupāliḥ ca vīryavān kekayāḥ ca mahā vīryāḥ sṛñjayāḥ ca sahasraśas ete ca anye ca sa gaṇāḥ kṛtāstrāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ samavetān tu tān sarvān bhāradvājaḥ api vīryavān asaṃbhrāntaḥ śara ogheṇa mahatā samavārayat droṇam te na abhyavartanta velām iva jalāśayāḥ pīḍyamānāḥ śaraiḥ rājan droṇa cāpa viniḥsṛtaiḥ na śekuḥ pramukhe sthātum bhāradvājasya pāṇḍavāḥ yat enam na abhyavartanta pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ saha tam āyāntam abhikruddham droṇam dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bahudhā cintayām āsa droṇasya prativāraṇam aśakyam tu tam anyena droṇam matvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ aviṣahyam gurum bhāram saubhadre samavāsṛjat tvam vā arjunaḥ vā kṛṣṇaḥ vā bhindyāt pradyumnaḥ eva vā abhimanyo varam tāta yācatām dātum arhasi pitṝṇām mātulānām ca sainyānām ca eva sarvaśas kṣipram astram samādāya droṇa anīkam viśātaya pitṝṇām jayam ākāṅkṣan avagāhe bhinadmi ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca bhindhi anīkam yudhā śreṣṭha dvāram saṃjanayasva naḥ vayam tvā anugamiṣyāmaḥ yena tvam tāta yāsyasi dhanaṃjaya samam yuddhe tvām vayam tāta saṃyuge praṇidhāya anuyāsyāmaḥ rakṣantaḥ sarvatomukhāḥ bhīmaḥ uvāca aham tvā anugamiṣyāmi dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ atha sātyakiḥ pāñcālāḥ kekayāḥ matsyāḥ tathā sarve prabhadrakāḥ sakṛt bhinnam tvayā vyūham tatra tatra punar punar vayam pradhvaṃsayiṣyāmaḥ nighnamānāḥ varān varān aham etat pravekṣyāmi droṇa anīkam durāsadam tat karma adya kariṣyāmi hitam yat vaṃśayoḥ dvayoḥ śiśunā ekena saṃgrāme kālyamānāni saṃghaśas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca evam te bhāṣamāṇasya balam saubhadra vardhatām rakṣitam puruṣa vyāghraiḥ mahā iṣvāsaiḥ prahāribhiḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca sumitra aśvān raṇe kṣipram droṇa anīkāya codaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca acodayata yantāram droṇa anīkāya bhārata tena saṃcodyamānaḥ tu yāhi yāhi iti sārathiḥ atibhāraḥ ayam āyuṣman āhitaḥ tvayi pāṇḍavaiḥ ācāryaḥ hi kṛtī droṇaḥ parama astre kṛta śramaḥ sārathe kaḥ nu ayam droṇaḥ samagram kṣatram eva vā airāvata gatam śakram saha amara gaṇaiḥ aham na mama etat dviṣat sainyam kalām arhati ṣoḍaśīm api viśvajitam viṣṇum mātulam prāpya sūtaja pitaram ca arjunam saṃkhye na bhīḥ mām upayāsyati tatas abhimanyuḥ tām vācam kadarthīkṛtya sāratheḥ yāhi iti eva abravīt enam droṇa anīkāya māciram tatas saṃcodayām āsa hayān asya tri hāyanān na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ sūtaḥ hema bhāṇḍa paricchadān te preṣitāḥ sumitreṇa droṇa anīkāya vājinaḥ droṇam abhyadravan rājan mahā vega parākramāḥ tam udīkṣya tathā āyāntam sarve droṇa purogamāḥ abhyavartanta kauravyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca tam anvayuḥ yuyutsayā droṇa mukhān mahā rathān samāsadat siṃha śiśuḥ yathā gajān te viṃśati pade yattāḥ saṃprahāram pracakrire āsīt gāṅgaḥ iva āvartaḥ muhūrtam udadheḥ iva śūrāṇām yudhyamānānām nighnatām itaretaram saṃgrāmaḥ tumulaḥ rājan prāvartata su dāruṇaḥ droṇasya miṣataḥ vyūham bhittvā prāviśat ārjuniḥ tam praviṣṭam parān ghnantam śatru madhye mahā balam nānā vāditra ninadaiḥ kṣveḍita utkruṣṭa garjitaiḥ huṃkāraiḥ siṃhanādaiḥ ca tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti nisvanaiḥ ghoraiḥ halahalā śabdaiḥ mā gāḥ tiṣṭha ehi mām iti bṛṃhitaiḥ śiñjitaiḥ hāsaiḥ khura nemi svanaiḥ api teṣām āpatatām vīraḥ pūrvam śīghram atho dṛḍham te hanyamānāḥ ca tathā nānā liṅgaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas teṣām śarīraiḥ ca śarīra avayavaiḥ ca saḥ saṃtastāra kṣitim kṣipram kuśaiḥ vedim iva adhvare baddha godhā aṅguli trāṇān sa śarāvara kārmukān sa asi carma aṅkuśa abhīśūn sa tomara paraśvadhān sa guḍa ayomukha prāsān sa ṛṣṭi tomara paṭṭiśān sa bhinḍipāla parighān sa śakti vara kampanān sa pratoda mahā śaṅkhān sa kuntān sa kaca grahān sa mudgara kṣepaṇīyān sa pāśa parigha upalān sa keyūra aṅgadān bāhūn hṛdya gandha anulepanān saṃciccheda ārjuniḥ vṛttān tvadīyānām sahasraśas taiḥ sphuradbhiḥ mahā rāja śuśubhe lohita ukṣitaiḥ pañca āsyaiḥ pannagaiḥ chinnaiḥ garuḍena iva māriṣa su nāsā ānana keśāntaiḥ avraṇaiḥ cāru kuṇḍalaiḥ saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭha puṭaiḥ krodhāt kṣaradbhiḥ śoṇitam bahu cāru sraj mukuṭa uṣṇīṣaiḥ maṇi ratna virājitaiḥ vināla nalina ākāraiḥ divākara śaśi prabhaiḥ dviṣat śirobhiḥ pṛthivīm avatastāra phālguṇiḥ vīṣā mukhān vitriveṇūn vyasta daṇḍaka bandhurān vijaṅgha kūbara akṣān ca vinemīn anarān api praśātita upakaraṇān hata yodhān sahasraśas śaraiḥ viśakalīkurvan dikṣu sarvāsu adṛśyata tūṇān varmāṇi atha u kakṣyāḥ graiveyān atha kambalān ghaṇṭāḥ śuṇḍān viṣāṇa agrān kṣura pālān padānugān śaraiḥ niśita dhārā agraiḥ śātravāṇām aśātayat vanāyu jān pārvatīyān kāmboja āraṭṭa bāhlikān sthira vāladhi karṇa akṣān javanān sādhu vāhinaḥ su ārūḍhān śikṣitaiḥ yodhaiḥ śakti ṛṣṭi prāsa yodhibhiḥ vidhvasta cāmara kuthān viprakīrṇa prakīrṇakān nirasta jihvā nayanān niṣkīrṇa antra yakṛt ghanān hata ārohān bhinna bhāṇḍān kravyāda gaṇa modanān nikṛtta varma kavacān śakṛt mūtra asṛj āplutān nipātayan aśva varān tāvakān saḥ abhyarocata ekaḥ viṣṇuḥ iva acintyaḥ kṛtvā prāk karma duṣkaram vyahanat sa padāti oghān tvadīyān eva bhārata evam ekena tām senām saubhadreṇa śitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhṛśam viprahatām dṛṣṭvā skandena iva āsurīm camūm tvadīyāḥ tava putrāḥ ca vīkṣamāṇāḥ diśaḥ daśa saṃśuṣka āsyāḥ calat netrāḥ prasvinnāḥ loma harṣaṇāḥ palāyana kṛta utsāhāḥ nirutsāhāḥ dviṣat jaye hatān putrān tathā pitṝn suhṛd saṃbandhi bāndhavān saṃjayaḥ uvāca tām prabhagnām camūm dṛṣṭvā saubhadreṇa amita ojasā tatas rājānam āvṛttam saubhadram prati saṃyuge dṛṣṭvā droṇaḥ abravīt yodhān paryāpnuta narādhipam purā abhimanyuḥ lakṣyam naḥ paśyatām hanti vīryavān tam ādravata mā bhaiṣṭa kṣipram rakṣata kauravam tatas kṛtajñāḥ balinaḥ suhṛdaḥ jita kāśinaḥ trāsyamānāḥ bhayāt vīram parivavruḥ tava ātmajam droṇaḥ drauṇiḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ kṛtavarmā ca saubalaḥ bṛhadbalaḥ madra rājaḥ bhūriḥ bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ pauravaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ ca visṛjantaḥ śitān śarān saubhadram śara varṣeṇa mahatā samavākiran āsyāt grāsam iva ākṣiptam mamṛṣe nā arjuna ātmajaḥ tān śara ogheṇa mahatā sa aśva sūtān mahā rathān tasya nādam tatas śrutvā siṃhasya iva āmiṣa eṣiṇaḥ na amṛṣyanta su saṃrabdhāḥ punar droṇa mukhāḥ rathāḥ te enam koṣṭhakīkṛtya ratha vaṃśena māriṣa vyasṛjan iṣu jālāni nānā liṅgāni saṃghaśas tatas te kopitāḥ tena śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ śūrāṇām yudhyamānānām nighnatām itaretaram abhimanyoḥ pareṣām ca na āsīt kaḥ cit parāṅmukhaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ tribhiḥ droṇaḥ tu saptadaśabhiḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ viviṃśatiḥ tu viṃśatyā kṛtavarmā ca saptabhiḥ bṛhadbalaḥ tathā aṣṭābhiḥ aśvatthāmā ca saptabhiḥ bhūriśravāḥ tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ madra īśaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ āśugaiḥ dvābhyām śarābhyām śakuniḥ tribhiḥ duryodhanaḥ nṛpaḥ nṛtyan iva mahā rāja cāpa hastaḥ pratāpavān dāntaiḥ aśmaka dāyādam tvaramāṇaḥ abhyahārayat vivyādha ca enam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tasya abhimanyuḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ sūtam hayān dhvajam bāhū dhanuḥ śiraḥ ca urvyām smayamānaḥ abhyapātayat saṃcacāla balam sarvam palāyana parāyaṇam tatas karṇaḥ kṛpaḥ droṇaḥ drauṇiḥ gāndhāra rāj śalaḥ śalyaḥ bhūriśravāḥ krāthaḥ somadattaḥ viviṃśatiḥ vṛṣasenaḥ suṣeṇaḥ ca kuṇḍabhedī pratardanaḥ śaram ādatta karṇāya para kāya avabhedanam tasya bhittvā tanutrāṇam deham nirbhidya ca āśugaḥ prāviśat dharaṇīm rājan valmīkam iva pannagaḥ saṃcacāla raṇe karṇaḥ kṣiti kampe yathā acalaḥ athā anyaiḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ suṣeṇam dīrgha locanam kuṇḍabhedim ca saṃkruddhaḥ tribhiḥ trīn avadhīt balī karṇaḥ tam pañcaviṃśatyā nārācānām samarpayat aśvatthāmā ca viṃśatyā kṛtavarmā ca saptabhiḥ sa śara ardita sarva aṅgaḥ kruddhaḥ śakrātmaja ātmajaḥ vicaran dṛśyate sainye pāśa hastaḥ iva antakaḥ śalyam ca bāṇa varṣeṇa samīpa stham avākirat udakrośat mahā bāhuḥ tava sainyāni bhīṣayan tam hi viddham tathā dṛṣṭvā saubhadreṇa yaśasvinā saṃprādravat camūḥ sarvā bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ prekṣantaḥ tam mahā bāhum rukma puṅkhaiḥ samāvṛtam tvadīyāḥ ca palāyante mṛgāḥ siṃha arditāḥ iva sa tu raṇa yaśasā abhipūjyamānaḥ pitṛ sura cāraṇa siddha yakṣa saṃghaiḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca tathā pramathamānam tam mahā iṣvāsam ajihmagaiḥ ārjunim māmakāḥ sarve ke tu enam samavākiran saṃjayaḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan kumārasya raṇe vikrīḍitam mahat bibhitsataḥ ratha anīkam bhāradvājena rakṣitam madra īśam sāditam dṛṣṭvā saubhādreṇa āśugaiḥ raṇe śalyāt avarajaḥ kruddhaḥ kiran bāṇān samabhyayāt sa viddhvā daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ sa aśva yantāram ārjunim udakrośat mahā śabdam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tasya ārjuniḥ śiraḥ grīvam pāṇi pādam dhanuḥ hayān chatram dhvajam niyantāram triveṇum śamī upaskaram cakre yuga īṣām tūṇīrān anukarṣam ca sāyakaiḥ patākām cakragoptārau sarva upakaraṇāni ca vyadhamat lāghavāt tat ca dadṛśe na asya kaḥ cana sa papāta kṣitau kṣīṇaḥ praviddha ābharaṇa ambaraḥ anugāḥ ca asya vitrastāḥ prādravan sarvatodiśam ārjuneḥ karma tat dṛṣṭvā praṇeduḥ ca samantataḥ nādena sarva bhūtāni sādhu sādhu iti bhārata śalya bhrātari atha ārugṇe bahuśas tasya sainikāḥ kula adhivāsa nāmāni śrāvayantaḥ arjuna ātmajam rathaiḥ aśvaiḥ gajaiḥ ca anye pādātaiḥ ca bala utkaṭāḥ huṃkāraiḥ kṣveḍita utkruṣṭaiḥ siṃhanādaiḥ sa garjitaiḥ tān tathā bruvataḥ dṛṣṭvā saubhadraḥ prahasan iva yaḥ yaḥ sma prāharat pūrvam tam tam vivyādha patribhiḥ saṃdarśayiṣyan astrāṇi citrāṇi ca laghūni ca ārjuniḥ samare śūraḥ mṛdu pūrvam ayudhyata vāsudevāt upāttam yat yat astram ca dhanaṃjayāt adarśayata tat kārṣṇiḥ kṛṣṇābhyām aviśeṣayan dūram asyan gurum bhāram sādhayan ca punar punar saṃdadhat visṛjan ca iṣūn nirviśeṣam adṛśyata cāpa maṇḍalam eva asya visphurat dikṣu adṛśyata jyā śabdaḥ śuśruve tasya tala śabdaḥ ca dāruṇaḥ hrīmān amarṣī saubhadraḥ māna kṛt priya darśanaḥ saṃmimānayiṣuḥ vīrān iṣvāsān ca api ayudhyata mṛduḥ bhūtvā mahā rāja dāruṇaḥ samapadyata varṣa abhyatītaḥ bhagavān śaradi iva divākaraḥ śarān vicitrān mahataḥ rukma puṅkhān śilā śitān kṣurapraiḥ vatsadantaiḥ ca vipāṭhaiḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ avākirat ratha anīkam bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca dvaidhībhavati me cittam hriyā tuṣṭyā ca saṃjaya vistareṇa eva me śaṃsa sarvam gāvalgaṇe punar vikrīḍitam kumārasya skandasya iva asuraiḥ saha saṃjayaḥ uvāca ekasya ca bahūnām ca yathā āsīt tumulaḥ raṇaḥ abhimanyuḥ kṛta utsāhaḥ kṛta utsāhān ariṃdamān droṇam karṇam kṛpam śalyam drauṇim bhojam bṛhadbalam nānā nṛpān nṛpa sutān sainyāni vividhāni ca alāta cakra vat sarvān caran bāṇaiḥ samabhyayāt tat dṛṣṭvā caritam tasya saubhadrasya amita ojasaḥ athā bravīt mahā prājñaḥ bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān harṣeṇa utphulla nayanaḥ kṛpam ābhāṣya sa tvaram ghaṭṭayan iva marmāṇi tava putrasya māriṣa abhimanyum raṇe dṛṣṭvā tadā raṇa viśāradam eṣa gacchati saubhadraḥ pārthānām agratas yuvā nandayan suhṛdaḥ sarvān rājānam ca yudhiṣṭhiram nakulam sahadevam ca bhīmasenam ca pāṇḍavam bandhūn saṃbandhinaḥ ca anyān madhyasthān suhṛdaḥ tathā droṇasya prīti saṃyuktam śrutvā vākyam tava ātmajaḥ ārjunim prati saṃkruddhaḥ droṇam dṛṣṭvā smayan iva duḥsāsanam madra rājam tān tān ca anyān mahā rathān sarva mūrdhāvasiktānām ācāryaḥ brahma vittamaḥ arjunasya sutam tu eṣa śiṣya tvāt abhirakṣati putrāḥ śiṣyāḥ ca dayitāḥ tat apatyam ca dharmiṇām saṃrakṣyamāṇaḥ droṇena manyate vīryam ātmanaḥ ātma saṃbhāvitaḥ mūḍhaḥ tam pramathnīta māciram evam uktāḥ tu te rājñā sātvatīputram abhyayus saṃrabdhāḥ tam jighāṃsantaḥ bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ abravīt kuru śārdūlaḥ duryodhanam idam vacaḥ aham enam haniṣyāmi mahā rāja bravīmi te miṣatām pāṇḍu putrāṇām pāñcālānām ca paśyatām utkruśya ca abravīt vākyam kuru rājam idam punar śrutvā kṛṣṇau mayā grastam saubhadram atimāninau gamiṣyataḥ preta lokam jīva lokāt na saṃśayaḥ tau ca śrutvā mṛtau vyaktam pāṇḍoḥ kṣetra udbhavāḥ sutāḥ eka ahnā sa suhṛd vargāḥ klaibyāt dhāsyanti jīvitam śivena dhyāhi mā rājan eṣa hanmi ripum tava abhimanyuḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ ṣaḍviṃśatyā samarpayat duḥśāsanaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ prabhinnaḥ iva kuñjaraḥ tau maṇḍalāni citrāṇi rathābhyām savya dakṣiṇam caramāṇau ayudhyetām ratha śikṣā viśāradau atha paṇava mṛdaṅga dundubhīnām kṛkara mahānaka bheri jharjharāṇām saṃjayaḥ uvāca abhimanyuḥ smayan dhīmān duḥśāsanam atha abravīt diṣṭyā paśyāmi saṃgrāme māninam śatrum āgatam niṣṭhuram tyakta dharmāṇam ākrośana parāyaṇam yat sabhāyām tvayā rājñaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śṛṇvataḥ kopitaḥ paruṣaiḥ vākyaiḥ dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ lobhasya jñāna nāśasya drohasya atyāhitasya ca pitṝṇām mama rājyasya haraṇasya ugra dhanvinām śāsitā asmi adya te bāṇaiḥ sarva sainyasya paśyataḥ amarṣitāyāḥ kṛṣṇāyāḥ kāṅkṣitasya ca me pituḥ evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ bāṇam duḥśāsana antakam duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja kaśmalam ca āviśat mahat sārathiḥ tvaramāṇaḥ tu duḥśāsanam acetasam raṇa madhyāt apovāha saubhadra śara pīḍitam pāṇḍavāḥ draupadeyāḥ ca virāṭaḥ ca samīkṣya tam pāñcālāḥ kekayāḥ ca eva siṃhanādam atha anadan vāditrāṇi ca sarvāṇi nānā liṅgāni sarvaśas prāvādayanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ pāṇḍūnām tatra sainikāḥ paśyantaḥ smayamānāḥ ca saubhadrasya viceṣṭitam atyanta vairiṇam dṛptam dṛṣṭvā śatrum parājitam dharma māruta śakrāṇām āśvinoḥ pratimāḥ tathā dhārayantaḥ dhvaja agreṣu draupadeyāḥ mahā rathāḥ sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍinau kekayāḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca matsya pāñcāla sṛṃjayāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca mudā yuktāḥ yudhiṣṭhira purogamāḥ abhyavartanta sahitāḥ droṇa anīkam bibhitsavaḥ jayam ākāṅkṣamāṇānām śūrāṇām anivartinām paśya duḥśāsanam vīram abhimanyu vaśam gatam pratapantam iva ādityam nighnantam śātravān raṇe saubhadram udyatāḥ trātum abhidhāvanti pāṇḍavāḥ tatas karṇaḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ abhimanyum durāsadam tasya ca anucarān tīkṣṇaiḥ vivyādha parama iṣubhiḥ avajñā pūrvakam vīraḥ saubhadrasya raṇa ajire tam tadā nā aśakat kaḥ cit droṇāt vārayitum raṇe ārujantam ratha śreṣṭhān vajrahastam iva asurān saubhadram śataśas avidhyat uttama astrāṇi darśayan saḥ astraiḥ astra vidām śreṣṭhaḥ rāma śiṣyaḥ pratāpavān sa tathā pīḍyamānaḥ tu rādheyena astra vṛṣṭibhiḥ samare amara saṃkāśaḥ saubhadraḥ na vyaṣīdata tatas śilā śitaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bhallaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ chittvā dhanūṃṣi śūrāṇām ārjuniḥ karṇam ārdayat sa dhvajam kārmukam ca asya chittvā bhūmau nyapātayat tatas kṛcchra gatam karṇam dṛṣṭvā karṇāt anantaraḥ saubhadram abhyayāt tūrṇam dṛḍham udyamya kārmukam tatas uccukruśuḥ pārthāḥ teṣām ca anucarāḥ janāḥ vāditrāṇi ca saṃjaghnuḥ saubhadram ca api tuṣṭuvuḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca saḥ abhigarjan dhanuṣpāṇiḥ jyām vikarṣan punar punar tayoḥ mahātmanoḥ tūrṇam ratha antaram avāpatat pitṛpaitāmaham karma kurvāṇam atimānuṣam dṛṣṭvā arditam śaraiḥ kārṣṇim tvadīyāḥ hṛṣitāḥ abhavan śiraḥ pracyāvayām āsa sa rathāt prāpatat bhuvi karṇikāram iva uddhūtam vātena mathitam nagāt bhrātaram nihatam dṛṣṭvā rājan karṇaḥ vyathām yayau vimukhīkṛtya karṇam tu saubhadraḥ kaṅka patribhiḥ anyān api mahā iṣvāsān tūrṇam eva abhidudruve jhaṣaḥ kruddhaḥ iva abhindat abhimanyuḥ mahā yaśāḥ śalabhaiḥ iva ca ākāśe dhārābhiḥ iva ca āvṛte abhimanyoḥ śaraiḥ rājan na prājñāyata kim cana tāvakānām tu yodhānām vadhyatām niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ saubhadraḥ tu tatas śaṅkham pradhmāpya puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ śīghram abhyapatat senām bhāratīm bharata ṛṣabha sa kakṣe agniḥ iva utsṛṣṭaḥ nirdahan tarasā ripūn ratha nāga aśva manujān ardayan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sa praviśya akarot bhūmim kabandha gaṇa saṃkulām svān eva abhimukhān ghnantaḥ prādravan jīvita arthinaḥ te ghorāḥ raudra karmāṇaḥ vipāṭhāḥ pṛthavaḥ śitāḥ nighnantaḥ ratha nāga aśvān jagmuḥ āśu vasuṃdharām sa āyudhāḥ sa aṅguli trāṇāḥ sa khaḍgāḥ sa aṅgadāḥ raṇe dṛśyante bāhavaḥ chinnāḥ hema ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ śarāḥ cāpāni khaḍgāḥ ca śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi ca sa kuṇḍalāni sragvīṇi bhūmau āsan sahasraśas apaskaraiḥ adhiṣṭhānaiḥ īṣā daṇḍaka bandhuraiḥ śakti cāpa āyudhaiḥ ca api patitaiḥ ca mahā dhvajaiḥ nihataiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ aśvaiḥ vāraṇaiḥ ca viśām pate agamya kalpā pṛthivī kṣaṇena āsīt su dāruṇā vadhyatām rāja putrāṇām krandatām itaretaram prādurāsīt mahā śabdaḥ bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhanaḥ sa śabdaḥ bharata śreṣṭha diśaḥ sarvāḥ vyanādayat vyacarat sa diśaḥ sarvāḥ pradiśaḥ ca āhitān rujan tam tadā na anupaśyāma sainyena rajasā āvṛtam ādadānam gaja aśvānām nṛṇām ca āyūṃṣi bhārata kṣaṇena bhūyas apaśyāma sūryam madhyaṃdine yathā abhimanyum mahā rāja pratapantam dviṣat gaṇān sa vāsava samaḥ saṃkhye vāsavasya ātmaja ātmajaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca yuddheṣu kuśalam vīram kula putram tanutyajam gāhamānam anīkāni sat aśvaiḥ tam tri hāyanaiḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīmasenaḥ śikhaṇḍī sātyakiḥ yamau dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ virāṭaḥ ca drupadaḥ ca sa kekayaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca saṃrabdhaḥ matsyāḥ ca anvapatan raṇe abhyadravan parīpsantaḥ vyūḍha anīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ tān dṛṣṭvā dravataḥ śūrān tvadīyāḥ vimukhāḥ abhavan jāmātā tava tejasvī viṣṭambhayiṣuḥ ādravat vārdhakṣatriḥ upāsedhat pravaṇāt iva kuñjarān dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca yat ekaḥ pāṇḍavān kruddhān putra gṛddhīn avārayat tat asya brūhi me vīryam karma ca agryam mahātmanaḥ kim dattam hutam iṣṭam vā su taptam atha vā tapaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca mānāt sa taptavān rājā vara arthī su mahat tapaḥ indriyāṇi indriya arthebhyaḥ priyebhyaḥ saṃnivartya saḥ kṣudh pipāsā ātapa sahaḥ kṛśaḥ dhamanisaṃtataḥ varam vṛṇīṣva prītaḥ asmi jayadratha kim icchasi uvāca praṇataḥ rudram prāñjaliḥ niyata ātmavān pāṇḍaveyān aham saṃkhye bhīma vīrya parākramān dhārayiṣyasi saṃgrāme caturaḥ pāṇḍu nandanān ekaḥ saṃdhārayām āsa pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm tasya jyā tala ghoṣeṇa kṣatriyān bhayam āviśat dṛṣṭvā tu kṣatriyāḥ bhāram saindhave sarvam arpitam saṃjayaḥ uvāca śṛṇu tat sarvam ākhyāsye yathā pāṇḍūn ayodhayat tam ūhuḥ sāratheḥ vaśyāḥ saindhavāḥ sādhu vāhinaḥ vikurvāṇāḥ bṛhantaḥ aśvāḥ śvasana upama raṃhasaḥ tasya abhyaśobhayat ketuḥ vārāhaḥ rājataḥ mahān sa visphārya mahat cāpam kiran iṣu gaṇān bahūn tat khaṇḍam pūrayām āsa yat vyadārayat ārjuniḥ sa sātyakim tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ ca vṛkodaram dhṛṣṭadyumnam tathā ṣaṣṭyā virāṭam daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ drupadam pañcabhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ daśabhiḥ ca śikhaṇḍinam kekayān pañcaviṃśatyā draupadeyān tribhiḥ tribhiḥ yudhiṣṭhiram ca saptatyā tatas śeṣān apānudat atha asya śita pītena bhallena ādiśya kārmukam akṣṇoḥ nimeṣa mātreṇa saḥ anyat ādāya kārmukam vivyādha daśabhiḥ pārtha tān ca eva anyān tribhiḥ tribhiḥ tasya tat lāghavam jñātvā bhīmaḥ bhallaiḥ tribhiḥ punar saḥ anyat ādāya balavān sajyam kṛtvā ca kārmukam bhīmasya apothayat ketum dhanuḥ aśvān ca māriṣa tatas tvadīyāḥ saṃhṛṣṭāḥ sādhu sādhu iti cukruśuḥ saṃkruddhān pāṇḍavān ekaḥ yat dadhāra astra tejasā pāṇḍūnām darśitaḥ panthāḥ saindhavena nivāritaḥ yatamānāḥ tu te vīrāḥ matsya pāñcāla kekayāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca anvapadyanta pratyaikaśyena saindhavam yaḥ yaḥ hi yatate bhettum droṇa anīkam tava ahitaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca saindhavena niruddheṣu jaya gṛddhiṣu pāṇḍuṣu praviśya tu ārjuniḥ senām satya saṃdhaḥ durāsadām vyakṣobhayata tejasvī makaraḥ sāgaram yathā tam tathā śara varṣeṇa kṣobhayantam ariṃdamam yathā pradhānāḥ saubhadram abhyayus kuru sattamāḥ teṣām tasya ca saṃmardaḥ dāruṇaḥ samapadyata sṛjatām śara varṣāṇi prasaktam amita ojasām vṛṣasenasya yantāram hatvā ciccheda kārmukam tasya vivyādha balavān śaraiḥ aśvān ajihmagaiḥ vātāyamānaiḥ atha taiḥ aśvaiḥ apahṛtaḥ raṇāt tena antareṇa abhimanyoḥ yantā apāsārayat ratham ratha vrajāḥ tatas hṛṣṭāḥ sādhu sādhu iti cukruśuḥ tam siṃham iva saṃkruddham pramathnantam śaraiḥ arīn ārāt āyāntam abhyetya vasātīyaḥ abhyayāt drutam saḥ abhimanyum śaraiḥ ṣaṣṭyā rukma puṅkhaiḥ avākirat tam ayasmaya varmāṇam iṣuṇā āśu pātinā vasātyam nihatam dṛṣṭvā kruddhāḥ kṣatriya puṃgavāḥ parivavruḥ tadā rājan tava pautram jighāṃsavaḥ visphārayantaḥ cāpāni nānā rūpāṇi anekaśas teṣām śarān sa iṣvasanān śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi ca sa kuṇḍalāni sragvīṇi kruddhaḥ ciccheda phālguniḥ sa khaḍgāḥ sa aṅguli trāṇāḥ sa paṭṭiśa paraśvadhāḥ adṛśyanta bhujāḥ chinnāḥ hema ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ apaskaraiḥ adhiṣṭhānaiḥ īṣā daṇḍaka bandhuraiḥ anukarṣaiḥ patākābhiḥ tathā sārathi vājibhiḥ rathaiḥ ca bhagnaiḥ nāgaiḥ ca hataiḥ kīrṇā abhavat mahī nihataiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ śūraiḥ nānā janapada īśvaraiḥ jaya gṛddhaiḥ vṛtā bhūmiḥ dāruṇā samapadyata kāñcanam yat yat asya āsīt varma ca ābharaṇāni ca dhanuṣaḥ ca śarāṇām ca tat apaśyāma kevalam tam tadā na aśakat kaḥ cit cakṣurbhyām abhivīkṣitum saṃjayaḥ uvāca ādadānaḥ tu śūrāṇām āyūṃṣi abhavat ārjuniḥ antakaḥ sarva bhūtānām prāṇān kāle iva āgate sa śakraḥ iva vikrāntaḥ śakra sūnoḥ sutaḥ balī satyaśravasi ca ākṣipte tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ aham pūrvam aham pūrvam iti kṣatriya puṃgavāḥ spardhamānāḥ samājagmuḥ jighāṃsantaḥ arjuna ātmajam kṣatriyāṇām anīkāni pradrutāni abhidhāvatām jagrāsa timiḥ āsādya kṣudra matsyān iva arṇave mahā grāha gṛhītā iva vāta vega bhaya arditā samakampata sā senā vibhraṣṭā nauḥ iva arṇave trastām āśvāsayan senām atrastaḥ vākyam abravīt alam trāsena vaḥ śūrāḥ na eṣa kaḥ cit mayi sthite aham enam grahīṣyāmi jīva grāham na saṃśayaḥ sa tasya iṣvasanam chittvā phālguṇiḥ savya dakṣiṇau dṛṣṭvā rukmaratham rugṇam putram śalyasya māninam jīva grāham jighṛkṣantam saubhadreṇa yaśasvinā saṃgrāma durmadāḥ rājan rāja putrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ vayasyāḥ śalya putrasya suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ tāla mātrāṇi cāpāni vikarṣantaḥ mahā rathāḥ ārjunim śara varṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayan śūraiḥ śikṣā bala upetaiḥ taruṇaiḥ ati amarṣaṇaiḥ dṛṣṭvā ekam samare śūram saubhadram aparājitam chādyamānam śara vrātaiḥ hṛṣṭaḥ duryodhanaḥ abhavat adṛśyam ārjunim cakruḥ nimeṣāt te nṛpa ātmajāḥ sa sūta aśva dhvajam tasya syandanam tam ca māriṣa ācitam samapaśyāma śvāvidham śalalaiḥ iva ekaḥ sa śatadhā rājan dṛśyate sma sahasradhā bibheda śatadhā rājan śarīrāṇi mahīkṣitām prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtām saṃkhye preṣitāḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ rājan prāpuḥ amum lokam śarīrāṇi avanim yayuḥ dhanūṃṣi aśvān niyantṝn ca dhvajān bāhūn ca sa aṅgadān śirāṃsi ca śitaiḥ bhallaiḥ teṣām ciccheda phālguniḥ cūta ārāmaḥ yathā bhagnaḥ pañca varṣa phala upagaḥ kruddha āśīviṣa saṃkāśān su kumārān sukha ucitān ekena nihatān dṛṣṭvā bhītaḥ duryodhanaḥ abhavat rathinaḥ kuñjarān aśvān padātīn ca avamarditān dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaḥ kṣipram upāyāt tam amarṣitaḥ tayoḥ kṣaṇam iva āpūrṇaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata atha abhavat te vimukhaḥ putraḥ śara śata arditaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca saṃgrāmam tumulam ghoram jayam ca eva mahātmanaḥ kim tu na ati adbhutam teṣām yeṣām dharmaḥ vyapāśrayaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca saṃśuṣka āsyāḥ calat netrāḥ prasvinnāḥ loma harṣiṇaḥ palāyana kṛta utsāhāḥ nirutsāhāḥ dviṣat jaye hatān bhrātṝn pitṝn putrān suhṛd saṃbandhi bāndhavān tān prabhagnān tathā dṛṣṭvā droṇaḥ drauṇiḥ bṛhadbalaḥ kṛpaḥ duryodhanaḥ karṇaḥ kṛtavarmā atha saubalaḥ te api pautreṇa te rājan prāyaśas vimukhīkṛtāḥ tam te abhiṣiṣicuḥ bāṇaiḥ meghāḥ girim iva ambubhiḥ pautram tu tava durdharṣam lakṣmaṇam priya darśanam pituḥ samīpe tiṣṭhantam śūram udyata kārmukam āsasāda raṇe kārṣṇiḥ mattaḥ mattam iva dvipam lakṣmaṇena tu saṃgamya saubhadraḥ para vīra hā śaraiḥ su niśitaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bāhvoḥ urasi ca arpitaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ vai mahā bāhuḥ daṇḍa āhataḥ iva uragaḥ su dṛṣṭaḥ kriyatām lokaḥ amum lokam gamiṣyasi paśyatām bāndhavānām tvām nayāmi yama sādanam su nasam subhru keśāntam śiraḥ ahārṣīt sa kuṇḍalam lakṣmaṇam nihatam dṛṣṭvā hā hā iti uccukruśuḥ janāḥ tatas droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ droṇa putraḥ bṛhadbalaḥ kṛtavarmā ca hārdikyaḥ ṣaṭ rathāḥ paryavārayan sa tān viddhvā śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ vimukhīkṛtya ca ārjuniḥ āvavruḥ tasya panthānam gaja anīkena daṃśitāḥ kaliṅgāḥ ca niṣādāḥ ca krātha putraḥ ca vīryavān tat prasaktam iva atyartham yuddham āsīt viśām pate tatas tat kuñjara anīkam vyadhamat dhṛṣṭam ārjuniḥ yathā vivāt nityagatiḥ jaladān śataśas ambare tatas krāthaḥ śara vrātaiḥ ārjunim samavākirat atha itare saṃnivṛttāḥ punar droṇa mukhāḥ rathāḥ parama astrāṇi dhunvānāḥ saubhadram abhidudruvuḥ tān nivārya ārjuniḥ bāṇaiḥ krāthaputram atha ardayat śara ogheṇa aprameyeṇa tvaramāṇaḥ jighāṃsayā sa dhanuḥ bāṇa keyūrau bāhū sa mukuṭam śiraḥ chatram dhvajam niyantāram aśvān ca asya nyapātayat kula śīla śruta balaiḥ kīrtyā ca astra balena ca yukte tasmin hate vīrāḥ prāyaśas vimukhāḥ abhavan dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca tathā praviṣṭam taruṇam saubhadram aparājitam kula anurūpam kurvāṇam saṃgrāmeṣu apalāyinam plavamānam iva ākāśe ke śūrāḥ samavārayan saṃjayaḥ uvāca abhimanyuḥ praviśya eva tāvakān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ akarot vimukhān sarvān pārthivān pāṇḍu nandanaḥ tam tu droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ drauṇiḥ ca sa bṛhadbalaḥ kṛtavarmā ca hārdikyaḥ ṣaṭ rathāḥ paryavārayan dṛṣṭvā tu saindhave bhāram atimātram samāhitam sainyam tava mahā rāja yudhiṣṭhiram upādravat tāla mātrāṇi cāpāni vikarṣantaḥ mahā rathāḥ tān tu sarvān mahā iṣvāsān sarva vidyāsu niṣṭhitān vyaṣṭambhayat raṇe bāṇaiḥ saubhadraḥ para vīra hā droṇam pañcāśatā viddhvā viṃśatyā ca bṛhadbalam aśītyā kṛtavarmāṇam kṛpam ṣaṣṭyā śilīmukhaiḥ avidhyat daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ aśvatthāmānam ārjuniḥ sa karṇam karṇinā karṇe pītena niśitena ca phālguniḥ dviṣatām madhye vivyādha parama iṣuṇā pātayitvā kṛpasya aśvān tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī tatas vṛndārakam vīram kurūṇām kīrti vardhanam putrāṇām tava vīrāṇām paśyatām avadhīt balī tam drauṇiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām samarpayat varam varam amitrāṇām ārujantam abhīta vat sa tu bāṇaiḥ śitaiḥ tūrṇam pratyavidhyata māriṣa paśyatām dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām aśvatthāmānam ārjuniḥ ṣaṣṭyā śarāṇām tam drauṇiḥ tigma dhāraiḥ su tejanaiḥ tasmin droṇaḥ bāṇa śatam putra gṛddhī nyapātayat aśvatthāmā tathā aṣṭau ca parīpsan pitaram raṇe karṇaḥ dvāviṃśatim bhallān kṛtavarmā caturdaśa bṛhadbalaḥ tu pañcāśat kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ daśa tān tu pratyavadhīt sarvān daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ taiḥ ardyamānaḥ saubhadraḥ sarvatas niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tam kosalānām adhipaḥ karṇinā atāḍayat hṛdi sa tasya aśvān dhvajam cāpam sūtam ca apātayat kṣitau iyeṣa phālguneḥ kāyāt śiraḥ hartum sa kuṇḍalam sa kosalānām bhartāram rāja putram bṛhadbalam babhañja ca sahasrāṇi daśa rājan mahātmanām sṛjatām aśivāḥ vācaḥ khaḍga kārmuka dhāriṇām viṣṭambhayan mahā iṣvāsān yodhān tava śara ambubhiḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca sa karṇam karṇinā karṇe punar vivyādha phālguniḥ śaraiḥ pañcāśatā ca enam avidhyat kopayan bhṛśam karṇaḥ api vibabhau śūraḥ śaraiḥ citraḥ asṛj āplutaḥ tau ubhau śara citra aṅgau rudhireṇa samukṣitau babhūvatuḥ mahātmānau puṣpitau iva kiṃśukau atha karṇasya sacivān ṣaṭ śūrān citra yodhinaḥ atha itarān mahā iṣvāsān daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ māgadhasya punar putram hatvā ṣaḍbhiḥ ajihmagaiḥ sa aśvam sa sūtam taruṇam aśva ketum apātayat mārtikāvatakam bhojam tatas kuñjara ketanam kṣurapreṇa samunmathya nanāda visṛjan śarān sūtam ekena vivyādha daśabhiḥ ca arjuna ātmajam tatas dauḥśāsanim kārṣṇiḥ viddhvā saptabhiḥ āśugaiḥ pitā tava āhavam tyaktvā gataḥ kāpuruṣaḥ yathā diṣṭyā tvam api jānīṣe yoddhum na tu adya mokṣyase nārācam visasarja asmai tam drauṇiḥ tribhiḥ ācchinat tasya ārjuniḥ dhvajam chittvā śalyam tribhiḥ atāḍayat tam śalyaḥ navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ gārdhra patraiḥ atāḍayat tasya ārjuniḥ dhvajam chittvā ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī tam vivyādha āyasaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ saḥ apakrāmat ratha antaram sūryabhāsam ca pañca etān hatvā vivyādha saubalam atha abravīt tadā droṇam karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ vṛṣā purā sarvān pramathnāti brūhi asya vadham āśu naḥ tatas droṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ sarvān tān pratyabhāṣata śīghra tām nara siṃhasya pāṇḍaveyasya paśyata dhanuḥ maṇḍalam eva asya ratha mārgeṣu dṛśyate saṃdadhānasya viśikhān śīghram ca eva vimuñcataḥ ārujan iva me prāṇān mohayan api sāyakaiḥ praharṣayati mā bhūyas saubhadraḥ para vīra hā antaram yasya saṃrabdhāḥ na paśyanti mahā rathāḥ na viśeṣam prapaśyāmi raṇe gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ atha karṇaḥ punar droṇam āha ārjuni śara arditaḥ sthātavyam iti tiṣṭhāmi pīḍyamānaḥ abhimanyunā tejasvinaḥ kumārasya śarāḥ parama dāruṇāḥ kṣiṇvanti hṛdayam me adya ghorāḥ pāvaka tejasaḥ tam ācāryaḥ abravīt karṇam śanakais prahasan iva abhedyam asya kavacam yuvā ca āśu parākramaḥ upadiṣṭā mayā asya pituḥ kavaca dhāraṇā tām eṣa nikhilām vetti dhruvam parapuraṃjayaḥ śakyam tu asya dhanuḥ chettum jyām ca bāṇaiḥ samāhitaiḥ abhīśavaḥ hayāḥ ca eva tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī atha enam vimukhīkṛtya paścāt praharaṇam kuru aśvān asya avadhīt bhojaḥ gautamaḥ pārṣṇisārathī śeṣāḥ tu chinna dhanvānam śara varṣaiḥ avākiran tvaramāṇāḥ tvarā kāle viratham ṣaṭ mahā rathāḥ śara varṣaiḥ akaruṇāḥ bālam ekam avākiran khaḍga carma dharaḥ śrīmān utpapāta vihāyasam mārgaiḥ sa kaiśika ādyaiḥ ca lāghavena balena ca ārjuniḥ vyacarat vyomni bhṛśam vai pakṣirāj iva mayi eva nipatati eṣa sa asiḥ iti ūrdhva dṛṣṭayaḥ vivyadhuḥ tam mahā iṣvāsāḥ samare chidra darśinaḥ vyasi carmā iṣu pūrṇa aṅgaḥ saḥ antarikṣāt punar kṣitim sa cakra reṇu ujjvala śobhita aṅgaḥ babhau atīva unnata cakra pāṇiḥ raṇe abhimanyuḥ kṣaṇadā subhadraḥ sa vāsubhadra anukṛtim prakurvan sruta rudhira kṛta eka rāga vaktraḥ bhrukuṭi puṭa akuṭilaḥ ati siṃhanādaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca viṣṇoḥ svasā ānandi karaḥ sa viṣṇu āyudha bhūṣitaḥ rarāja atirathaḥ saṃkhye janārdanaḥ iva aparaḥ māruta uddhūta keśāntam udyata ari vara āyudham vapuḥ samīkṣya pṛthvīśāḥ duḥsamīkṣyam suraiḥ api tat cakram bhṛśam udvignāḥ saṃcicchiduḥ anekadhā mahā rathaḥ tatas kārṣṇiḥ saṃjagrāha mahā gadām vidhanuḥ syandana asiḥ taiḥ vicakraḥ ca aribhiḥ kṛtaḥ abhimanyuḥ gadā pāṇiḥ aśvatthāmānam ādravat sa gadām udyatām dṛṣṭvā jvalantīm aśanīm iva apākrāmat rathopasthāt vikramān trīn nara ṛṣabhaḥ tasya aśvān gadayā hatvā tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī śara ācita aṅgaḥ saubhadraḥ śvāvidh vat pratyadṛśyata jaghāna ca asya anucarān gāndhārān saptasaptatim punar brahma vasātīyān jaghāna rathinaḥ daśa kekayānām rathān sapta hatvā ca daśa kuñjarān dauḥśāsani ratham sa aśvam gadayā samapothayat tatas dauḥśāsaniḥ kruddhaḥ gadām udyamya māriṣa abhidudrāva saubhadram tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tau udyata gadau vīrau anyonya vadha kāṅkṣiṇau tau anyonyam gadā agrābhyām saṃhatya patitau kṣitau dauḥśāsaniḥ atha utthāya kurūṇām kīrti vardhanaḥ prottiṣṭhamānam saubhadram gadayā mūrdhni atāḍayat kṣobhayitvā camūm sarvām nalinīm iva kuñjaraḥ tam tathā patitam śūram tāvakāḥ paryavārayan dāvam dagdhvā yathā śāntam pāvakam śiśirātyaye vimṛdya taru śṛṅgāṇi saṃnivṛttam iva anilam astam gatam iva ādityam taptvā bhārata vāhinīm upaplutam yathā somam saṃśuṣkam iva sāgaram tam bhūmau patitam dṛṣṭvā tāvakāḥ te mahā rathāḥ mudā paramayā yuktāḥ cukruśuḥ siṃha vat muhur āsīt paramakaḥ harṣaḥ tāvakānām viśām pate itareṣām tu vīrāṇām netrebhyaḥ prāpatat jalam abhikrośanti bhūtāni antarikṣe viśām pate dṛṣṭvā nipatitam vīram cyutam candram iva ambarāt droṇa karṇa mukhaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ mahā rathaiḥ dyauḥ yathā pūrṇa candreṇa nakṣatra gaṇa mālinī rukma puṅkhaiḥ ca saṃpūrṇā rudhira ogha pariplutā uttamāṅgaiḥ ca vīrāṇām bhrājamānaiḥ sa kuṇḍalaiḥ vicitraiḥ ca paristomaiḥ patākābhiḥ ca saṃvṛtā cāmaraiḥ ca kuthābhiḥ ca praviddhaiḥ ca ambara uttamaiḥ ratha aśva nara nāgānām alaṃkāraiḥ ca su prabhaiḥ cāpaiḥ ca viśikhaiḥ chinnaiḥ śakti ṛṣṭi prāsa kampanaiḥ vividhaiḥ āyudhaiḥ ca anyaiḥ saṃvṛtā bhūḥ aśobhata vājibhiḥ ca api nirjīvaiḥ svapadbhiḥ śoṇita ukṣitaiḥ sa ārohaiḥ viṣamā bhūmiḥ saubhadreṇa nipātitaiḥ sa aṅkuśaiḥ sa mahāmātraiḥ sa varma āyudha ketubhiḥ pṛthivyām anukīrṇaiḥ ca vyaśva sārathi yodhibhiḥ padāti saṃghaiḥ ca hataiḥ vividha āyudha bhūṣaṇaiḥ bhīrūṇām trāsa jananī ghora rūpā abhavat mahī tam dṛṣṭvā patitam bhūmau candra arka sadṛśa dyutim tāvakānām parā prītiḥ pāṇḍūnām ca abhavat vyathā saṃprādravat camūḥ sarvā dharmarājasya paśyataḥ dīryamāṇam balam dṛṣṭvā saubhadre vinipātite ajātaśatruḥ svān vīrān idam vacanam abravīt svargam eṣa gataḥ śūraḥ yaḥ hataḥ na parāṅmukhaḥ saṃstambhayata mā bhaiṣṭa vijeṣyāmaḥ raṇe ripūn iti evam sa mahā tejāḥ duḥkhitebhyaḥ mahā dyutiḥ dharmarājaḥ yudhām śreṣṭhaḥ bruvan duḥkham apānudat yuddhe hi āśīviṣa ākārān rāja putrān raṇe bahūn pūrvam nihatya saṃgrāme paścāt ārjuniḥ anvagāt hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi kausalyam ca mahā ratham kṛṣṇa arjuna samaḥ kārṣṇiḥ śakra sadma gataḥ dhruvam ratha aśva nara mātaṅgān vinihatya sahasraśas a vitṛptaḥ sa saṃgrāmāt a śocyaḥ puṇya karma kṛt vayam tu pravaram hatvā teṣām taiḥ śara pīḍitāḥ niveśāya abhyupāyāma sāyāhne rudhira ukṣitāḥ nirīkṣamāṇāḥ tu vayam pare ca āyodhanam śanais apayātāḥ mahā rāja glānim prāptāḥ vicetasaḥ tatas niśāyāḥ divasasya ca aśivaḥ śivā rutaḥ saṃdhiḥ avartata adbhutaḥ vara asi śakti ṛṣṭi varūtha carmaṇām vibhūṣaṇānām ca samākṣipan prabhām divam ca bhūmim ca samānayan iva priyām tanum bhānuḥ upaiti pāvakam mahā abhra kūṭa acala śṛṅga saṃnibhaiḥ gajaiḥ anekaiḥ iva vajra pātitaiḥ mahā rathaiḥ bhūḥ śuśubhe vicūrṇitaiḥ puraiḥ iva amitra hataiḥ narādhipa ratha aśva vṛndaiḥ saha sādibhiḥ hataiḥ praviddha bhāṇḍa ābharaṇaiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ praviddha varma ābharaṇāḥ vara āyudhāḥ vipanna hasti aśva ratha anugāḥ narāḥ mahārha śayyā āstaraṇa ucitāḥ sadā kṣitau anāthāḥ iva śerate hatāḥ atīva hṛṣṭāḥ śva sṛgāla vāyasāḥ baḍāḥ suparṇāḥ ca vṛkāḥ tarakṣavaḥ vayāṃsi asṛkpāni atha rakṣasām gaṇāḥ piśāca saṃghāḥ ca su dāruṇāḥ raṇe vapām vilumpanti hasanti gānti ca prakarṣamāṇāḥ kuṇapāni anekaśas śarīra saṃghāṭa vahā asṛj jalā ratha uḍupā kuñjara śaila saṃkaṭā manuṣya śīrṣa upala māṃsa kardamā uvāha madhyena raṇa ajiram bhṛśam bhaya āvahā jīva mṛta pravāhinī pibanti ca aśnanti ca yatra durdṛśāḥ piśāca saṃghāḥ vividhāḥ su bhairavāḥ su nanditāḥ prāṇabhṛtām bhayaṃkarāḥ samāna bhakṣāḥ śva sṛgāla pakṣiṇaḥ tathā tat āyodhanam ugra darśanam niśā mukhe pitṛpati rāṣṭra saṃnibham nirīkṣamāṇāḥ śanakais jahuḥ narāḥ samutthita aruṇḍa kula upasaṃkulam apeta vidhvasta mahārha bhūṣaṇam nipātitam śakra samam mahā ratham raṇe abhimanyum dadṛśuḥ tadā janāḥ vyapoḍha havyam sadasi iva pāvakam saṃjayaḥ uvāca vimukta ratha saṃnāhāḥ sarve nikṣipta kārmukāḥ upopaviṣṭāḥ rājānam parivārya yudhiṣṭhiram tat eva duḥkham dhyāyantaḥ saubhadra gata mānasāḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā vilalāpa su duḥkhitaḥ droṇa anīkam asaṃbādham mama priya cikīrṣayā yasya śūrāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ pratyanīka gatāḥ raṇe atyanta śatruḥ asmākam yena duḥśāsanaḥ śaraiḥ kṣipram hi abhimukhaḥ saṃkye visaṃjñaḥ vimukhīkṛtaḥ sa tīrtvā dustaram vīraḥ droṇa anīka mahā arṇavam prāpya dauḥśāsanim kārṣṇiḥ yātaḥ vaivasvata kṣayam subhadrām vā mahābhāgām priyam putram a paśyatīm tau ubhau prativakṣyāmaḥ hṛṣīkeśa dhanaṃjayau priya kāmaḥ jaya ākāṅkṣī kṛtavān idam apriyam madhu lipsuḥ hi na apaśyam prapātam idam īdṛśam bhūṣaṇeṣu ca saḥ asmābhiḥ bālaḥ yudhi puraskṛtaḥ katham hi bālaḥ taruṇaḥ yuddhānām a viśāradaḥ bībhatsoḥ kopa dīptasya dagdhāḥ kṛpaṇa cakṣuṣā alubdhaḥ matimān hrīmān kṣamāvān rūpavān balī vapuṣmān māna kṛt vīraḥ priyaḥ satya parāyaṇaḥ yasya ślāghanti vibudhāḥ karmāṇi ūrjita karmaṇaḥ nivāta kavacān jaghne kālakeyān ca vīryavān akṣṇoḥ nimeṣa mātreṇa paulomāḥ sa gaṇāḥ hatāḥ bhayam tu su mahat prāptam dhārtarāṣṭram mahat balam pārthaḥ putra vadhāt kruddhaḥ kauravān śoṣayiṣyati kṣudraḥ kṣudra sahāyaḥ ca sva pakṣa kṣayam āturaḥ vyaktam duryodhanaḥ dṛṣṭvā śocan hāsyati jīvitam imam samīkṣya aprativīrya pauruṣam nipātitam deva vara ātmaja ātmajam saṃjayaḥ uvāca tasmin ahani nirvṛtte ghore prāṇabhṛtām kṣaye āditye astaṃgate śrīmān saṃdhyā kāle upasthite vyapayāteṣu sainyeṣu vāsāya bharata ṛṣabha hatvā saṃśaptaka vrātān divyaiḥ astraiḥ kapidhvajaḥ prāyāt sva śibiram jiṣṇuḥ jaitram āsthāya tam ratham kim nu me hṛdayam trastam vākyam sajjati keśava spandanti ca api aniṣṭāni gātram sīdati ca acyuta aniṣṭam ca eva me śliṣṭam hṛdayāt na apasarpati bhuvi yat dikṣu ca api ugrāḥ utpātāḥ trāsayanti mām bahu prakārāḥ dṛśyante sarve eva agha śaṃsinaḥ vāsudevaḥ uvāca vyaktam śivam tava bhrātuḥ sa amātyasya bhaviṣyati mā śucaḥ kim cit eva anyat tatra aniṣṭam bhaviṣyati saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas saṃdhyām upāsya eva vīrau vīra avasādane tatas sva śibiram prāptau hata ānandam hata tviṣam dhvasta ākāram samālakṣya śibiram para vīra hā bībhatsuḥ abravīt kṛṣṇam asvastha hṛdayaḥ tatas na adya nandanti tūryāṇi maṅgalyāni janārdana miśrāḥ dundubhi nirghoṣaiḥ śaṅkhāḥ ca āḍambaraiḥ saha vīṇāḥ vā na adya vādyante śamyātāla svanaiḥ saha maṅgalyāni ca gītāni na gāyanti paṭhanti ca stuti yuktāni ramyāṇi mama anīkeṣu bandinaḥ yodhāḥ ca api hi mām dṛṣṭvā nivartante hi adhomukhāḥ karmāṇi ca yathāpūrvam kṛtvā na abhivadanti mām na hi śudhyati me bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭvā sva janam ākulam api pāñcāla rājasya virāṭasya ca mānada sarveṣām ca eva yodhānām sāmagryam syāt mama acyuta na ca mām adya saubhadraḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha raṇāt āyāntam ucitam pratyudyāti hasan iva dadṛśāte bhṛśa asvasthān pāṇḍavān naṣṭa cetasaḥ dṛṣṭvā bhrātṝn ca putrān ca vimanāḥ vānaradhvajaḥ na ca abhimanyum paśyāmi na ca mām pratinandatha mayā śrutaḥ ca droṇena cakra vyūhaḥ vinirmitaḥ na ca upadiṣṭaḥ tasya āsīt mayā anīka vinirgamaḥ kaccit na bālaḥ yuṣmābhiḥ para anīkam praveśitaḥ bhittvā anīkam mahā iṣvāsaḥ pareṣām bahuśas yudhi lohita akṣam mahā bāhum jātam siṃham iva adriṣu upendra sadṛśam brūta katham āyodhane hataḥ sukumāram mahā iṣvāsam vāsavasya ātmaja ātmajam vārṣṇeyī dayitam śūram mayā satata lālitam ambāyāḥ ca priyam nityam kaḥ avadhīt kāla coditaḥ sadṛśaḥ vṛṣṇi siṃhasya keśavasya mahātmanaḥ subhadrāyāḥ priyam nityam draupadyāḥ keśavasya ca yadi putram na paśyāmi yāsyāmi yama sādanam mṛdu kuñcita keśāntam bālam bāla mṛga īkṣaṇam smita abhibhāṣiṇam dāntam guru vākya karam sadā bālye api a bāla karmāṇam priya vākyam amatsaram mahā utsāham mahā bāhum dīrgha rājīva locanam bhakta anukampinam dāntam na ca nīca anusāriṇam kṛtajñam jñāna saṃpannam kṛtāstram anivartinam sveṣām priya hite yuktam pitṝṇām jaya gṛddhinam na ca pūrva prahartāram saṃgrāme naṣṭa saṃbhramam yadi putram na paśyāmi yāsyāmi yama sādanam su lalāṭam su keśāntam su bhrū akṣi daśanacchadam a paśyataḥ tat vadanam kā śāntiḥ hṛdayasya me a śṛṇvataḥ svanam tasya kā śāntiḥ hṛdayasya me rūpam ca apratirūpam tat tridaśeṣu api durlabham a paśyataḥ adya vīrasya kā śāntiḥ hṛdayasya me abhivādana dakṣam tam pitṝṇām vacane ratam na adya aham yadi paśyāmi kā śāntiḥ hṛdayasya me sukumāraḥ sadā vīraḥ mahārha śayana ucitaḥ bhūmau anātha vat śete nūnam nāthavatām varaḥ śayānam samupāsanti yam purā parama striyaḥ tam adya vipraviddha aṅgam upāsanti aśivāḥ śivāḥ bodhayanti adya tam nūnam śvāpadāḥ vikṛtaiḥ svaraiḥ nūnam adya rajaḥ dhvastam raṇe reṇuḥ kariṣyati bhāgya hīnasya kālena yathā me nīyase balāt sā adya saṃyamanī nūnam sadā su kṛtinām gatiḥ sva bhābhiḥ bhāsitā ramyā tvayā atyartham virājate nūnam vaivasvataḥ ca tvā varuṇaḥ ca priya atithiḥ duḥkhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ yudhiṣṭhiram apṛcchata kaccit sa kadanam kṛtvā pareṣām pāṇḍu nandana asahāyaḥ sahāya arthī mām anudhyātavān dhruvam pīḍyamānaḥ śaraiḥ bālaḥ tāta sādhu abhidhāva mām subhadrāyām ca saṃbhūtaḥ na evam vaktum iha arhati vajra sāra mayam nūnam hṛdayam su dṛḍham mama a paśyataḥ dīrgha bāhum rakta akṣam yat na dīryate katham bāle mahā iṣvāse nṛśaṃsāḥ marma bhedinaḥ svasrīye vāsudevasya mama putre akṣipan śarān upayāntam ripūn hatvā saḥ adya mām kim na paśyati nūnam sa patitaḥ śete dharaṇyām rudhira ukṣitaḥ śobhayan medinīm gātraiḥ ādityaḥ iva pātitaḥ raṇe vinihatam śrutvā śoka ārtā vai vinaṃkṣyati subhadrā vakṣyate kim mām abhimanyum apaśyatī vajra sāra mayam nūnam hṛdayam yat na yāsyati sahasradhā vadhūm dṛṣṭvā rudatīm śoka karśitām hṛṣṭānām dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām siṃhanādaḥ mayā śrutaḥ yuyutsuḥ ca api kṛṣṇena śrutaḥ vīrān upālabhan a śaknuvantaḥ bībhatsum bālam hatvā mahā rathāḥ kim nadadhvam adharma jñāḥ pārthe vai dṛśyatām balam kim tayoḥ vipriyam kṛtvā keśava arjunayoḥ mṛdhe siṃha vat nadata prītāḥ śoka kāle upasthite āgamiṣyati vaḥ kṣipram phalam pāpasya karmaṇaḥ iti tān prati bhāṣan vai vaiśyāputraḥ mahāmatiḥ kimartham etat ākhyātam tvayā kṛṣṇa raṇe mama adhakṣyam tān aham sarvān tadā krūrān mahā rathān sarveṣām eṣa vai panthāḥ śūrāṇām anivartinām kṣatriyāṇām viśeṣeṇa yeṣām yuddhena jīvikā eṣā vai yudhyamānānām śūrāṇām anivartinām dhruvam yuddhe hi maraṇam śūrāṇām anivartinām gataḥ puṇya kṛtām lokān abhimanyuḥ na saṃśayaḥ etat ca sarva vīrāṇām kāṅkṣitam bharata ṛṣabha saṃgrāme abhimukhāḥ mṛtyum prapnuyāma iti mānada sa ca vīrān raṇe hatvā rāja putrān mahā balān vīraiḥ ākāṅkṣitam mṛtyum saṃprāptaḥ abhimukhaḥ raṇe mā śucaḥ puruṣa vyāghra pūrvaiḥ eṣa sanātanaḥ dharma kṛdbhiḥ kṛtaḥ dharmaḥ kṣatriyāṇām raṇe kṣayaḥ tvayi śoka samāviṣṭe nṛpāḥ ca suhṛdaḥ tava etān tvam vacasā sāmnā samāśvāsaya mānada evam āśvāsitaḥ pārthaḥ kṛṣṇena adbhuta karmaṇā tatas abravīt tadā bhrātṝn sarvān pārthaḥ sa gadgadān sa dīrgha bāhuḥ pṛthu aṃsaḥ dīrgha rājīva locanaḥ abhimanyuḥ yathā vṛttaḥ śrotum icchāmi aham tathā saṃgrāme sa anubandhān tān mama putrasya vairiṇaḥ katham ca vaḥ kṛtāstrāṇām sarveṣām śastra pāṇinām yadi evam aham ajñāsyam aśaktān rakṣaṇe mama putrasya pāṇḍu pāñcālān mayā guptaḥ bhavet tatas katham ca vaḥ ratha sthānām śara varṣāṇi muñcatām aho vaḥ pauruṣam nā asti na ca vaḥ asti parākramaḥ yatra abhimanyuḥ samare paśyatām vaḥ nipātitaḥ ātmānam eva garheyam yat aham vaḥ su durbalān yuṣmān ājñāya niryātaḥ bhīrūn a kṛta niśramān āho svid bhūṣaṇa arthāya varma śastra āyudhāni vaḥ vācaḥ ca vaktum saṃsatsu mama putram arakṣatām evam uktvā tatas vākyam tiṣṭhan ca apavara asimān putra śoka abhisaṃtaptam aśru pūrṇa mukham tadā na abhibhāṣṭum śaknuvanti draṣṭum vā suhṛdaḥ arjunam anyatra vāsudevāt vā jyeṣṭāt vā pāṇḍu nandanāt bahu mānāt priya tvāt ca tau enam vaktum arhataḥ tatas tam putra śokena bhṛśam pīḍita mānasam rājīva locanam kruddham rājā vacanam abravīt yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca tvayi yāte mahā bāho saṃśaptaka balam prati vayam droṇam varayāmaḥ sma sarvaśas prativyūhya ratha anīkam yatamānam tathā raṇe sa vāryamāṇaḥ rathibhiḥ rakṣitena mayā tathā asmān api jaghāna āśu pīḍayan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ te pīḍyamānāḥ droṇena droṇa anīkam na śaknumaḥ sa tathā coditaḥ asmābhiḥ sadaśvaḥ iva vīryavān prāviśat tat balam bālaḥ suparṇaḥ iva sāgaram te anuyātāḥ vayam vīram sātvatī putram āhave praveṣṭu kāmāḥ tena eva yena sa prāviśat camūm tatas droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ drauṇiḥ ca sa bṛhadbalaḥ kṛtavarmā ca saubhadram ṣaṭ rathāḥ paryavārayan yatamānaḥ param śaktyā bahubhiḥ virathīkṛtaḥ tatas dauḥśāsaniḥ kṣipram tathā taiḥ virathīkṛtam saṃśayam paramam prāpya diṣṭāntena abhyayojayat sa tu hatvā sahasrāṇi dvipa aśva ratha sādinām rāja putra śatam ca agryam vīrān ca alakṣitān bahūn bṛhadbalam ca rājānam svargeṇa ājau prayojya ha tatas parama dharma ātmā diṣṭāntam upajagmivān saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas arjunaḥ vacaḥ śrutvā dharmarājena bhāṣitam viṣaṇṇa vadanāḥ sarve parigṛhya dhanaṃjayam pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām vāsaviḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ kampamānaḥ jvareṇa iva niḥśvasan ca muhur muhur pāṇim pāṇau viniṣpiṣya śvasamānaḥ aśru netravān na ced vadha bhayāt bhītaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān prahāsyati na ca asmān śaraṇam gacchet kṛṣṇam vā puruṣottamam dhārtarāṣṭra priya karam mayi vismṛta sauhṛdam rakṣamāṇāḥ ca tam saṃkhye ye mām yotsyanti ke cana api droṇa kṛpau vīrau chādayiṣyāmi tān śaraiḥ yadi etat evam saṃgrāme na kuryām puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ mā sma puṇya kṛtām lokān prāpnuyām śūra saṃmatān ye lokāḥ mātṛ hantṝṇām ye ca api pitṛ ghātinām guru dāra gāminām ye ca piśunānām ca ye tathā sādhūn asūyatām ye ca ye ca api parivādinām ye ca nikṣepa hartṝṇām ye ca viśvāsa ghātinām bhukta pūrvām striyam ye ca nindatām agha śaṃsinām brahma ghnānām ca ye lokāḥ ye ca go ghātinām api pāyasam vā yava annam vā śākam kṛsaram eva vā saṃyāva apūpa māṃsāni ye ca lokāḥ vṛthā aśnatām veda adhyāyinam atyartham saṃśitam vā dvijottamam avamanyamānaḥ yān yāti vṛddhān sādhūn tathā gurūn spṛśatām brāhmaṇam gām ca pādena agnim ca yām labhet yā apsu śleṣma purīṣam vā mūtram vā muñcatām gatiḥ tām gaccheyam gatim ghorām na ced dhanyām jayadratham utkocinām mṛṣā uktīnām vañcakānām ca yā gatiḥ ātma apahāriṇām yā ca yā ca mithyā abhiśaṃsinām bhṛtyaiḥ saṃdṛśyamānānām putra dāra āśritaiḥ tathā a saṃvibhajya kṣudrāṇām yā gatiḥ mṛṣṭam aśnatām tām gaccheyam gatim ghorām na ced dhanyām jayadratham saṃśritam vā api yaḥ tyaktvā sādhum tad vacane ratam na bibharti nṛśaṃsa ātmā nindate ca upakāriṇam arhate prātiveśyāya śrāddham yaḥ na dadāti ca teṣām gatim iyām kṣipram na ced dhanyām jayadratham dharmāt apetāḥ ye ca anye mayā na atra anukīrtitāḥ ye ca anukīrtitāḥ kṣipram teṣām gatim avāpnuyām yadi vyuṣṭām imām rātrim śvas na hanyām jayadratham imām ca api aparām bhūyas pratijñām me nibodhata iha eva saṃpraveṣṭā aham jvalitam jātavedasam asura sura manuṣyāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ vā uragāḥ vā pitṛ rajanicarāḥ vā brahma deva ṛṣayaḥ vā caram acaram api idam yat param ca api tasmāt tat api mama ripum tam rakṣitum nā eva śaktāḥ tat api śara śataiḥ aham prabhāte bhṛśam abhipatya ripoḥ śiraḥ abhihartā evam uktvā vicikṣepa gāṇḍīvam savya dakṣiṇam arjunena pratijñāte pāñcajanyam janārdanaḥ sa pāñcajanyaḥ acyuta vaktra vāyunā bhṛśam su pūrṇa udara niḥsṛta dhvaniḥ jagat sa pātāla viyat diś īśvaram prakampayām āsa yuga atyaye yathā tatas vāditra ghoṣāḥ ca prādurāsan samantataḥ siṃhanādāḥ ca pāṇḍūnām pratijñāte mahātmanā saṃjayaḥ uvāca śrutvā tu tam mahā śabdam pāṇḍūnām putra gṛddhinām śoka saṃmūḍha hṛdayaḥ duḥkhena abhihataḥ bhṛśam majjamānaḥ iva agādhe vipule śoka sāgare jagāma samitim rājñām saindhavaḥ vimṛśan bahu sa teṣām naradevānām sakāśe paridevayan abhimanyoḥ pituḥ bhītaḥ sa vrīḍaḥ vākyam abravīt yaḥ asau pāṇḍoḥ kila kṣetre jātaḥ śakreṇa kāminā tat svasti vaḥ astu yāsyāmi sva gṛham jīvita īpsayā atha vā stha pratibalāḥ trātum mām kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ droṇa duryodhana kṛpāḥ karṇa madra īśa bāhlikāḥ duḥśāsana ādayaḥ śaktāḥ trātum api na trāyeyuḥ bhavantaḥ mām samastāḥ patayaḥ kṣiteḥ praharṣam pāṇḍaveyānām śrutvā mama mahat bhayam sīdanti iva ca me aṅgāni mumūrṣoḥ iva pārthivāḥ vadhaḥ nūnam pratijñātaḥ mama gāṇḍīvadhanvanā tathā hi hṛṣṭāḥ krośanti śoka kāle api pāṇḍavāḥ na devāḥ na ca gandharvāḥ na asura uraga rākṣasāḥ tasmāt mām anujānīta bhadram vaḥ astu nara ṛṣabhāḥ adarśanam gamiṣyāmi na mām drakṣyanti pāṇḍavāḥ evam vilapamānam tam bhayāt vyākula cetasam ātma kārya garīyaḥ tvāt rājā duryodhanaḥ abravīt madhye kṣatriya vīrāṇām tiṣṭhantam prārthayet yudhi aham vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ citrasenaḥ viviṃśatiḥ bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ śalyaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ durāsadaḥ purumitraḥ jayaḥ bhojaḥ kāmbojaḥ ca sudakṣiṇaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ subāhuḥ ca kaliṅgaḥ ca api udāyudhaḥ vinda anuvindau āvantyau droṇaḥ drauṇiḥ sa saubalaḥ tvam ca api rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ svayam śūraḥ amita dyutiḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ daśa ekā ca madīyāḥ tava rakṣaṇe evam āśvāsitaḥ rājan putreṇa tava saindhavaḥ upasaṃgrahaṇam kṛtvā droṇāya sa viśām pate upopaviśya praṇataḥ paryapṛcchat idam tadā vidyā viśeṣam icchāmi jñātum ācārya tattvataḥ droṇaḥ uvāca na tu te yudhi saṃtrāsaḥ kāryaḥ pārthāt katham cana aham hi rakṣitā tāta bhayāt tvām na atra saṃśayaḥ vyūhiṣyāmi ca tam vyūham yam pārthaḥ na tariṣyati pitṛpaitāmaham mārgam anuyāhi narādhipa bhuja vīrya arjitān lokān divyān prāpsyasi anuttamān kuravaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca eva vṛṣṇayaḥ anye ca mānavāḥ paryāyeṇa vayam sarve kālena balinā hatāḥ para lokam gamiṣyāmaḥ svaiḥ svaiḥ karmabhiḥ anvitāḥ kṣatra dharma āśritāḥ śūrāḥ kṣatriyāḥ prāpnuvanti tān saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam āśvāsitaḥ rājan bhāradvājena saindhavaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca vāsudevaḥ mahā bāhuḥ dhanaṃjayam abhāṣata bhrātṝṇām matam ājñāya tvayā vācā pratiśrutam dhārtarāṣṭrasya śibire mayā praṇihitāḥ carāḥ te ime śīghram āgamya pravṛttim vedayanti naḥ tvayā vai saṃpratijñāte sindhurāja vadhe tadā siṃhanādaḥ sa vāditraḥ su mahān iha taiḥ śrutaḥ tena śabdena vitrastāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sa saindhavāḥ na akasmāt siṃhanādaḥ ayam iti matvā vyavasthitāḥ su mahān śabda saṃpātaḥ kauravāṇām mahā bhuja āsīt nāga aśva pattīnām ratha ghoṣaḥ ca bhairavaḥ tatas vimanasaḥ sarve trastāḥ kṣudra mṛgāḥ iva āsan suyodhana amātyāḥ sa ca rājā jayadrathaḥ athā utthāya saha amātyaiḥ dīnaḥ śibiram ātmanaḥ āyāt sauvīra sindhūnām īśvaraḥ bhṛśa duḥkhitaḥ sa mantra kāle saṃmantrya sarvāḥ naiḥśreyasīḥ kriyāḥ mām asau putra hantā iti śvas abhiyātā dhanaṃjayaḥ tām na devāḥ na gandharvāḥ na asura uraga rākṣasāḥ utsahante anyathā kartum pratijñām savyasācinaḥ te mām rakṣata saṃgrāme mā vaḥ mūrdhni dhanaṃjayaḥ padam kṛtvā āpnuyāt lakṣyam tasmāt atra vidhīyatām anujānīhi mām rājan gamiṣyāmi gṛhān prati evam uktaḥ tu avāk śīrṣaḥ vimanāḥ sa suyodhanaḥ śrutvā abhiśaptavantam tvām dhyānam eva anvapadyata mṛdu ca ātma hitam ca eva sa apekṣam idam uktavān na aham paśyāmi bhavatām tathāvīryam dhanurdharam vāsudeva sahāyasya gāṇḍīvam dhunvataḥ dhanuḥ kaḥ arjunasya agratas tiṣṭhet sākṣāt api śatakratuḥ maheśvaraḥ api pārthena śrūyate yodhitaḥ purā dānavānām sahasrāṇi hiraṇyapura vāsinām sa amarān api lokān trīn nihanyāt iti me matiḥ saḥ aham icchāmi anujñātum rakṣitum vā mahātmanā sa rājñā svayam ācāryaḥ bhṛśam ākranditaḥ arjuna saṃvidhānam ca vihitam rathāḥ ca kila sajjitāḥ karṇaḥ bhūriśravāḥ drauṇiḥ vṛṣasenaḥ ca durjayaḥ kṛpaḥ ca madra rājaḥ ca ṣaṭ ete asya purogamāḥ śakaṭaḥ padmapaḥ ca ardhaḥ vyūhaḥ droṇena kalpitaḥ padma karṇika madhya sthaḥ sūcī pāśe jayadrathaḥ sthāsyate rakṣitaḥ vīraiḥ sindhurāj yuddha durmadaiḥ aviṣahyatamāḥ hi ete niścitāḥ pārtha ṣaṭ rathāḥ etān a jitvā sa gaṇān na eva prāpyaḥ jayadrathaḥ teṣām ekaikaśas vīryam ṣaṇṇām tvam anucintaya sahitāḥ hi nara vyāghrāḥ na śakyāḥ jetum añjasā bhūyas ca cintayiṣyāmi nītim ātma hitāya vai mantrajñaiḥ sacivaiḥ sārdham suhṛdbhiḥ kārya siddhaye ṣaṭ rathān dhārtarāṣṭrasya manyase yān bala adhikān teṣām vīryam mama ardhena na tulyam iti lakṣaye astram astreṇa sarveṣām eteṣām madhusūdana droṇasya miṣataḥ saḥ aham sa gaṇasya vilapyataḥ mūrdhānam sindhurājasya pātayiṣyāmi bhū tale yadi sādhyāḥ ca rudrāḥ ca vasavaḥ ca saha aśvinaḥ marutaḥ ca saha indreṇa viśvedevāḥ tathā asurāḥ pitaraḥ saha gandharvāḥ suparṇāḥ sāgara adrayaḥ dyauḥ viyat pṛthivī ca iyam diśaḥ ca sa digīśvarāḥ grāmya āraṇyāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca tathā api bāṇaiḥ nihatam śvas draṣṭāsi raṇe mayā satyena te śape kṛṣṇa tathā eva āyudham ālabhe yaḥ ca goptā mahā iṣvāsaḥ tasya pāpasya durmateḥ draṣṭāsi śvas mahā iṣvāsān nārācaiḥ tigma tejanaiḥ śṛṅgāṇi iva gireḥ vajraiḥ dāryamāṇān mayā yudhi nara nāga aśva dehebhyaḥ visraviṣyati śoṇitam gāṇḍīva preṣitāḥ bāṇāḥ manaḥ nila samāḥ jave nṛ nāga aśvān videha asūn kartāraḥ ca sahasraśas yamāt kuberāt varuṇāt rudrāt indrāt ca yat mayā upāttam astram ghoram vai tat draṣṭāraḥ narāḥ yudhi brāhmeṇa astreṇa ca astrāṇi hanyamānāni saṃyuge mayā draṣṭāsi sarveṣām saindhavasya abhirakṣiṇām śara vega samutkṛttaiḥ rājñām keśava mūrdhabhiḥ āstīryamāṇām pṛthivīm draṣṭāsi śvas mayā yudhi kravyādān tarpayiṣyāmi drāvayiṣyāmi śātravān suhṛdaḥ nandayiṣyāmi pātayiṣyāmi saindhavam bahu āgaskṛt kusaṃbandhī pāpa deśa samudbhavaḥ mayā saindhavakaḥ rājā hataḥ svān śocayiṣyati sarva kṣīra anna bhoktāraḥ pāpa ācārāḥ raṇa ajire mayā sa rājakāḥ bāṇaiḥ nunnāḥ naṃkṣyanti saindhavāḥ tathā prabhāte kartāsmi yathā kṛṣṇa suyodhanaḥ gāṇḍīvam ca dhanuḥ divyam yoddhā ca aham nara ṛṣabha tvam ca yantā hṛṣīkeśa kim nu syāt ajitam mayā evam etām pratijñām me satyām viddhi janārdana mā avamaṃsthāḥ mama astrāṇi mā avamaṃsthāḥ dhanuḥ dṛḍham mā avamaṃsthāḥ balam bāhvoḥ mā avamaṃsthāḥ dhanaṃjayam yathā hi yātvā saṃgrāme na jīye vijayāmi ca dhruvam vai brāhmaṇe satyam dhruvā sādhuṣu saṃnatiḥ śrīḥ dhruvā ca api dakṣeṣu dhruvaḥ nārāyaṇe jayaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam uktvā hṛṣīkeśam svayam ātmānam ātmanā saṃdideśa arjunaḥ nardan vāsaviḥ keśavam prabhum yathā prabhātām rajanīm kalpitaḥ syāt rathaḥ mama tathā kāryam tvayā kṛṣṇa kāryam hi mahat udyatam saṃjayaḥ uvāca tām niśām duḥkha śoka ārtau śvasantau iva ca uragau nara nārāyaṇau kruddhau jñātvā devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ vyathitāḥ cintayām āsuḥ kim svid etat bhaviṣyati vavuḥ ca dāruṇāḥ vātāḥ rūkṣāḥ gora abhiśaṃsinaḥ śuṣka aśanyaḥ ca niṣpetuḥ sa nirghātāḥ sa vidyutaḥ cacāla ca api pṛthivī sa śaila vana kānanā cukṣubhuḥ ca mahā rāja sāgarāḥ makara ālayāḥ pratisrotas pravṛttāḥ ca tathā gantum samudragāḥ ratha aśva nara nāgānām pravṛttam adharottaram kravyādānām pramoda artham yama rāṣṭra vivṛddhaye vāhanāni śakṛt mūtre mumucuḥ ruruduḥ ca ha tān dṛṣṭvā dāruṇān sarvān utpātān loma harṣaṇān śrutvā mahā balasya ugrām pratijñām savyasācinaḥ atha kṛṣṇam mahā bāhuḥ abravīt pākaśāsaniḥ āśvāsaya subhadrām tvam bhaginīm snuṣayā saha snuṣā viśoke kuru mādhava tatas arjuna gṛham gatvā vāsudevaḥ su durmanāḥ bhaginīm putra śoka ārtām āśvāsayata duḥkhitām mā śokam kuru vārṣṇeyi kumāram prati sa snuṣā sarveṣām prāṇinām bhīru niṣṭhā eṣā kāla nirmitā sadṛśam maraṇam hi etat tava putrasya mā śucaḥ diṣṭyā mahā rathaḥ vīraḥ pituḥ tulya parākramaḥ kṣātreṇa vidhinā prāptaḥ vīra abhilaṣitām gatim jitvā su bahuśas śatrūn preṣayitvā ca mṛtyave gataḥ puṇya kṛtām lokān sarva kāmaduhaḥ akṣayān vīra sūḥ vīra patnī tvam vīra śvaśura bāndhavā mā śucaḥ tanayam bhadre gataḥ sa paramām gatim prāpsyate ca api asau kṣudraḥ saindhavaḥ bāla ghātakaḥ asya avalepasya phalam sa suhṛd gaṇa bāndhavaḥ vyuṣṭāyām tu varārohe rajanyām pāpa karma kṛt na hi mokṣyati pārthāt sa praviṣṭaḥ api amarāvatīm śvas śiraḥ śroṣyase tasya saindhavasya raṇe hṛtam samantapañcakāt bāhyam viśokā bhava mā rudaḥ kṣatra dharmam puraskṛtya gataḥ śūraḥ satām gatim yām vayam prāpnuyāma iha ye ca anye śastra jīvinaḥ vyūḍha uraskaḥ mahā bāhuḥ anivartī vara praṇud anu jātaḥ ca pitaram mātṛ pakṣam ca vīryavān sahasraśas ripūn hatvā hataḥ śūraḥ mahā rathaḥ āśvāsaya snuṣām rājñi mā śucaḥ kṣatriye bhṛṣam yadi ca manuja pannagāḥ piśācāḥ rajanicarāḥ patagāḥ sura asurāḥ ca saṃjayaḥ uvāca subhadrā putra śoka ārtā vilalāpa su duḥkhitā hā putra mama mandāyāḥ katham saṃyugam etya ha nidhanam prāptavān tāta pitṛ tulya parākramaḥ katham indīvara śyāmam su daṃṣṭram cāru locanam mukham te dṛśyate vatsa guṇṭhitam raṇa reṇunā nūnam śūram nipatitam tvām paśyanti anivartinam su śiraḥ grīva bāhu aṃsam vyūḍha uraskam nirudaram cāru upacita sarva aṅgam svakṣam śastra kṣata ācitam bhūtāni tvā nirīkṣante nūnam candram iva uditam śayanīyam purā yasya spardhya āstaraṇa saṃvṛtam bhūmau adya katham śeṣe vipraviddhaḥ sukha ucitaḥ yaḥ anvāsyata purā vīraḥ vara strībhiḥ mahā bhujaḥ yaḥ astūyata purā hṛṣṭaiḥ sūta māgadha bandibhiḥ pāṇḍaveṣu ca nātheṣu vṛṣṇi vīreṣu ca abhibho pāñcāleṣu ca vīreṣu hataḥ kena asi anātha vat viśāla akṣam su keśāntam cāru vākyam sugandhi ca dhik vīryam vṛṣṇi vīrāṇām pāñcālānām ca dhik balam dhik kekayān tathā cedīn matsyān ca eva atha sṛñjayān ye tvā raṇe gatam vīram na jānanti nipātitam adya paśyāmi pṛthivīm śūnyām iva hata tviṣam svasrīyam vāsudevasya putram gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ katham tvā viratham vīram drakṣyāmi anyaiḥ nipātitam hā vīra dṛṣṭaḥ naṣṭaḥ ca dhanam svapnaḥ iva asi me imām te taruṇīm bhāryām tvad ādhibhiḥ abhiplutām katham saṃdhārayiṣyāmi vivatsām iva dhenukām vihāya phala kāle mām su gṛddhām tava darśane nūnam gatiḥ kṛtāntasya prājñaiḥ api su durvidā yatra tvam keśave nāthe saṃgrāme anātha vat hataḥ yajvanām dāna śīlānām brāhmaṇānām kṛtātmanām carita brahmacaryāṇām puṇya tīrtha avagāhinām kṛtajñānām vadānyānām guru śuśrūṣiṇām api sahasra dakṣiṇānām ca yā gatiḥ tām avāpnuhi yā gatiḥ yudhyamānānām śūrāṇām anivartinām hatvā arīn nihatānām ca saṃgrāme tām gatim vraja go sahasra pradātṝṇām kratu dānām ca yā gatiḥ naiveśikam ca abhimatam dadatām yā gatiḥ śubhā brahmacaryeṇa yām yānti munayaḥ saṃśita vratā ekapatnyaḥ ca yām yānti tām gatim vraja putraka rājñām su caritaiḥ yā ca gatiḥ bhavati śāśvatī catur āśramiṇām puṇyaiḥ pāvitānām su rakṣitaiḥ dīna anukampinām yā ca satatam saṃvibhāginām paiśunyāt ca nivṛttānām tām gatim vraja putraka vratinām dharma śīlānām guru śuśrūṣiṇām api amogha atithinām yā ca tām gatim vraja putraka ṛtu kāle svakām patnīm gacchatām yā manasvinām na ca anya dāra sevīnām tām gatim vraja putraka sāmnā ye sarva bhūtāni gacchanti gata matsarāḥ nāruṃtudānām kṣamiṇām yā gatiḥ tām avāpnuhi madhu māṃsa nivṛttānām madāt dambhāt tathā anṛtāt para upatāpa tyaktānām tām gatim vraja putraka hrīmantaḥ sarva śāstra jñāḥ jñāna tṛptāḥ jita indriyāḥ yām gatim sādhavaḥ yānti tām gatim vraja putraka evam vilapatīm dīnām subhadrām śoka karśitām abhyapadyata pāñcālī vairāṭī sahitā tadā tāḥ prakāmam ruditvā ca vilapya ca su duḥkhitāḥ sa upacāraḥ tu kṛṣṇaḥ tām duḥkhitām bhṛśa duḥkhitaḥ siktvā ambhasā samāśvāsya tat tat uktvā hitam vacaḥ visaṃjña kalpām rudatīm apaviddhām pravepatīm bhaginīm puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ idam vacanam abravīt subhadre mā śucaḥ putram pāñcāli āśvāsaya uttarām gataḥ abhimanyuḥ prathitām gatim kṣatriya puṃgavaḥ kuryāma tat vayam karma kriyāsuḥ suhṛdaḥ ca naḥ kṛtavān yādṛś adyā ekaḥ tava putraḥ mahā rathaḥ evam āśvāsya bhaginīm draupadīm api ca uttarām pārthasya eva mahā bāhuḥ pārśvam āgāt ariṃdamaḥ tatas abhyanujñāya nṛpān kṛṣṇaḥ bandhūn viveśa antaḥpuram rājan te anye jagmuḥ yathālayam saṃjayaḥ uvāca spṛṣṭvā ambhaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ sthaṇḍile śubha lakṣaṇe saṃtastāra śubhām śayyām darbhaiḥ vaiḍūrya saṃnibhaiḥ alaṃcakāra tām śayyām parivārya āyudha uttamaiḥ tatas spṛṣṭa udakam pārtham vinītāḥ paricārakāḥ naityakam cakruḥ naiśam traiyambakam balim tatas prīta manāḥ pārthaḥ gandhaiḥ mālyaiḥ ca mādhavam alaṃkṛtya upahāram tam naiśam asmai nyavedayat supyatām pārtha bhadram te kalyāṇāya vrajāmi aham sthāpayitvā tatas dvāḥsthān goptṝn ca ātta āyudhān narān dāruka anugataḥ śrīmān viveśa śibiram svakam śiśye ca śayane śubhre bahu kṛtyam vicintayan na pāṇḍavānām śibire kaḥ cit suṣvāpa tām niśām prajāgaraḥ sarva janam āviveśa viśām pate putra śoka abhibhūtena pratijñātaḥ mahātmanā sahasā sindhurājasya vadhaḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā tat katham nu mahā bāhuḥ vāsaviḥ para vīra hā pratijñām saphalām kuryāt iti te samacintayan kaṣṭam hi idam vyavasitam pāṇḍavena mahātmanā putra śoka abhitaptena pratijñā mahatī kṛtā bhrātaraḥ ca api vikrāntāḥ bahulāni balāni ca jitvā ripu gaṇān ca eva pārayatu arjunaḥ vratam a hatvā sindhurājam hi dhūmaketum pravekṣyati tasmin hi vijayaḥ kṛtsnaḥ pāṇḍavena samāhitaḥ yadi naḥ su kṛtam kim cit yadi dattam hutam yadi evam kathayatām teṣām jayam āśaṃsatām prabho smṛtvā pratijñām pārthasya dārukam pratyabhāṣata jayadratham haniṣyāmi śvobhūte iti dāruka akṣauhiṇyaḥ hi tāḥ sarvāḥ rakṣiṣyanti jayadratham droṇaḥ ca saha putreṇa sarva astra vidhi pāragaḥ ekaḥ vīraḥ sahasrākṣaḥ daitya dānava marditā saḥ aham śvas tat kariṣyāmi yathā kuntī sutaḥ arjunaḥ na hi dārāḥ na mitrāṇi jñātayaḥ na ca bāndhavāḥ kaḥ cit na anyaḥ priyataraḥ kuntī putrāt mama arjunāt udīkṣitum na śaktaḥ aham bhavitā na ca tat tathā aham dhvajinyaḥ śatrūṇām sa hayāḥ sa ratha dvipāḥ arjuna arthe haniṣyāmi sa karṇāḥ sa suyodhanāḥ śvas nirīkṣantu me vīryam trayaḥ lokāḥ mahā āhave dhanaṃjaya artham samare parākrāntasya dāruka śvas narendra sahasrāṇi rāja putra śatāni ca sa aśva dvipa rathāni ājau vidraviṣyanti dāruka śvas tām cakra pramathitām drakṣyase nṛpa vāhinīm mayā kruddhena samare pāṇḍava arthe nipātitām śvas sa devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ piśāca uraga rākṣasāḥ jñāsyanti lokāḥ sarve mām suhṛdam savyasācinaḥ yaḥ tam dveṣṭi sa mām dveṣṭi yaḥ tam anu sa mām anu iti saṃkalpyatām buddhyā śarīra ardham mama arjunaḥ yathā tvam aprabhātāyām asyām niśi ratha uttamam kalpayitvā yathāśāstram ādāya vrata saṃyataḥ gadām kaumodakīm divyām śaktim cakram dhanuḥ śarān viśvakarma kṛtaiḥ divyaiḥ aśvān api ca bhūṣitān balāhakam meghapuṣpam sainyam sugrīvam eva ca yuktvā vāji varān yattaḥ kavacī tiṣṭha dāruka pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣam ārṣabheṇa eva pūritam śrutvā tu bhairavam nādam upayāyāḥ javena mām eka ahnā aham amarṣam ca sarva duḥkhāni ca eva ha bhrātuḥ pitṛṣvaseyasya vyapaneṣyāmi dāruka sarva upāyaiḥ yatiṣyāmi yathā bībhatsuḥ āhave paśyatām dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām haniṣyati jayadratham āśaṃse sārathe tatra bhavitā asya dhruvaḥ jayaḥ dārukaḥ uvāca evam ca etat kariṣyāmi yathā mām anuśāsasi su prabhātām imām rātrim jayāya vijayasya hi saṃjayaḥ uvāca āsasāda mahā tejāḥ dhyāyantam garuḍadhvajaḥ pratyutthānam tu kṛṣṇasya sarva avastham dhanaṃjayaḥ nā alopayata dharma ātmā bhaktyā premṇā ca sarvadā tatas kṛṣṇaḥ mahā tejāḥ jānan pārthasya niścayam kuntī putram idam vākyam āsīnaḥ sthitam abravīt mā viṣāde manaḥ pārtha kṛthāḥ kālaḥ hi durjayaḥ kālaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni niyacchati pare vidhau kimartham ca viṣādaḥ te tat brūhi vadatām vara na śocitavyam viduṣā śokaḥ kārya vināśanaḥ ābabhāṣe tadā vidvān idam vacanam arthavat mayā pratijñā mahatī jayadratha vadhe kṛtā śvas asmi hantā durātmānam putra ghnam iti keśava mad pratijñā vighāta artham dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ kila acyuta pṛṣṭhatas saindhavaḥ kāryaḥ sarvaiḥ guptaḥ mahā rathaiḥ daśa ca ekā ca tāḥ kṛṣṇa akṣauhiṇyaḥ su durjayāḥ pratijñāyām ca hīnāyām katham jīveta madvidhaḥ duḥkha upāyasya me vīra vikāṅkṣā parivartate saṃspṛśya ambhaḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ prāc mukhaḥ samavasthitaḥ idam vākyam mahā tejāḥ babhāṣe puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ hita artham pāṇḍu putrasya saindhavasya vadhe vṛtaḥ pārtha pāśupatam nāma parama astram sanātanam tam devam manasā dhyāyan joṣam āssva dhanaṃjaya tatas kṛṣṇa vacaḥ śrutvā saṃspṛśya ambhaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ bhūmau āsīnaḥ ekāgraḥ jagāma manasā bhavam tatas praṇihite brāhme muhūrte śubha lakṣaṇe jyotirbhiḥ ca samākīrṇam siddha cāraṇa sevitam vāyu vega gatiḥ pārthaḥ kham bheje saha keśavaḥ keśavena gṛhītaḥ sa dakṣiṇe vibhunā bhuje prekṣamāṇaḥ bahūn bhāvān jagāma adbhuta darśanān udīcyām diśi dharma ātmā saḥ apaśyat śvetaparvatam kuberasya vihāre ca nalinīm padma bhūṣitām sarit śreṣṭhām ca tām gaṅgām vīkṣamāṇaḥ bahu udakām sadā puṣpa phalaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ upetām sphaṭika upalām siṃha vyāghra samākīrṇām nānā mṛga gaṇa ākulām puṇya āśramavatīm ramyām manojña aṇḍaja sevitām
