mandarasya pradeśān ca kiṃnara udgīta nāditān hema rūpya mayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ nānā oṣadhi vidīpitān tathā mandāra vṛkṣaiḥ ca puṣpitaiḥ upaśobhitān snigdha añjana caya ākāram saṃprāptaḥ kālaparvatam puṇyam himavataḥ pādam maṇimantam ca parvatam brahmatuṅgam nadīḥ ca anyāḥ tathā janapadān api su śṛṅgam śata śṛṅgam ca śaryāti vanam eva ca puṇyam aśvaśiraḥ sthānam sthānam ātharvaṇasya ca vṛṣadaṃśam ca śaila indram mahā mandaram eva ca apsarobhiḥ samākīrṇam kiṃnaraiḥ ca upaśobhitam tān ca śailān vrajan pārthaḥ prekṣate saha keśavaḥ śubhaiḥ prasravaṇaiḥ juṣṭān hema dhātu vibhūṣitān candra raśmi prakāśa aṅgīm pṛthivīm pura mālinīm samudrān ca adbhuta ākārān apaśyat bahula ākarān viyat dyām pṛthivīm ca eva paśyan viṣṇu pade vrajan vismitaḥ saha kṛṣṇena kṣiptaḥ bāṇaḥ iva atyagāt graha nakṣatra somānām sūrya agnyoḥ ca sama tviṣam samāsādya tu tam śailam śaila agre samavasthitam sahasram iva sūryāṇām dīpyamānam sva tejasā śūlinam jaṭilam gauram valkala ajina vāsasam nayanānām sahasraiḥ ca vicitra aṅgam mahā ojasam pārvatyā sahitam devam bhūta saṃghaiḥ ca bhāsvaraiḥ gīta vāditra saṃhrādaiḥ tāla lāsya samanvitam valgita āsphoṭita utkruṣṭaiḥ puṇya gandhaiḥ ca sevitam goptāram sarva bhūtānām iṣvāsa dharam acyutam vāsudevaḥ tu tam dṛṣṭvā jagāma śirasā kṣitim lokādim viśvakarmāṇam ajam īśānam avyayam manasaḥ paramām yonim kham vāyum jyotiṣām nidhim sraṣṭāram vāridhārāṇām bhuvaḥ ca prakṛtim parām deva dānava yakṣāṇām mānavānām ca sādhanam carācarasya sraṣṭāram pratihartāram eva ca kāla kopam mahātmānam śakra sūrya guṇa udayam avandata tadā kṛṣṇaḥ vāc manaḥ buddhi karmabhiḥ yam prapaśyanti vidvāṃsaḥ sūkṣma adhyātma pada eṣiṇaḥ tam ajam kāraṇa ātmānam jagmatuḥ śaraṇam bhavam arjunaḥ ca api tam devam bhūyas bhūyas abhyavandata jñātvā ekam bhūta bhavya ādim sarva bhūta bhava udbhavam svāgatam vām nara śreṣṭhau uttiṣṭhetām gata klamau kim ca vām īpsitam vīrau manasaḥ kṣipram ucyatām yena kāryeṇa saṃprāptau yuvām tat sādhayāmi vām vriyatām ātmanaḥ śreyaḥ tat sarvam pradadāni vām tatas tat vacanam śrutvā pratyutthāya kṛtāñjalī vāsudeva arjunau śarvam tuṣṭuvāte mahā matī mahādevāya bhīmāya tryambakāya ca śambhave īśānāya bhagaghnāya namaḥ astu andhakaghātine vilohitāya dhūmrāya vyādhāya anaparājite nityam nīlaśikhaṇḍāya śūline divyacakṣuṣe vṛṣadhvajāya piṅgāya jaṭine brahmacāriṇe tapyamānāya salile brahmaṇyāya ajitāya ca viśvātmane viśvasṛje viśvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhate namaḥ namaḥ te sevyāya bhūtānām prabhave sadā brahma vaktrāya śarvāya śaṃkarāya śivāya ca evam stutvā mahādevam vāsudevaḥ saha arjunaḥ tam ca upahāram sva kṛtam naiśam naityakam ātmanaḥ tatas abhipūjya manasā śarvam kṛṣṇam ca pāṇḍavaḥ tatas pārthasya vijñāya vara arthe vacanam prabhuḥ vāsudeva arjunau devaḥ smayamānaḥ abhyabhāṣata saraḥ amṛta mayam divyam abhyāśe śatru sūdanau yena deva arayaḥ sarve mayā yudhi nipātitāḥ tatas ānīyatām kṛṣṇau sa śaram dhanuḥ uttamam tathā iti uktvā tu tau vīrau tam śarvam pārṣadaiḥ saha nirdiṣṭam yat vṛṣāṅkena puṇyam sarva artha sādhakam tat jagmatuḥ asaṃbhrāntau nara nārāyaṇau ṛṣī nāgam antar jale ghoram dadṛśāte arjuna acyutau dvitīyam ca aparam nāgam sahasra śirasam varam vamantam vipulām jvālām dadṛśāte agni varcasam tatas kṛṣṇaḥ ca pārthaḥ ca saṃspṛśya apaḥ kṛtāñjalī dhanuḥ bāṇaḥ ca śatru ghnam tat dvaṃdvam samapadyata tatas pārśvāt vṛṣāṅkasya brahmacārī nyavartata piṅga akṣaḥ tapasaḥ kṣetram balavān nīla lohitaḥ sa tat gṛhya dhanuḥ śreṣṭham tasthau sthānam samāhitaḥ tasya maurvīm ca muṣṭim ca sthānam ca ālakṣya pāṇḍavaḥ śrutvā mantram bhava proktam jagrāha acintya vikramaḥ sarasi eva ca tam bāṇam mumoca atibalaḥ prabhuḥ tatas prītam bhavam jñātvā smṛtimān arjunaḥ tadā varam āraṇyakam dattam darśanam śaṃkarasya ca tasya tat matam ājñāya prītaḥ prādāt varam bhavaḥ tat ca pāśupatam ghoram pratijñāyāḥ ca pāraṇam saṃhṛṣṭa romā durdharṣaḥ kṛtam kāryam amanyata vavandatuḥ ca saṃhṛṣṭau śirobhyām tau maheśvaram anujñātau kṣaṇe tasmin bhavena arjuna keśavau prāptau sva śibiram vīrau mudā paramayā yutau indrāviṣṇū yathā prītau jambhasya vadha kāṅkṣiṇau saṃjayaḥ uvāca tayoḥ saṃvadatoḥ eva kṛṣṇa dārukayoḥ tadā sā atyagāt rajanī rājan atha rājā anvabudhyata paṭhanti pāṇisvanikāḥ māgadhāḥ madhuparkikāḥ vaitālikāḥ ca sūtāḥ ca tuṣṭuvuḥ puruṣa ṛṣabham nartakāḥ ca api anṛtyanta jaguḥ gītāni gāyakāḥ kuru vaṃśa stava arthāni madhuram raktakaṇṭhinaḥ mṛdaṅgāḥ jharjharāḥ bheryaḥ paṇava ānaka gomukhāḥ āḍambarāḥ ca śaṅkhāḥ ca dundubhyaḥ ca mahā svanāḥ evam etāni sarvāṇi tathā anyāni api bhārata vādayanti sma saṃhṛṣṭāḥ kuśalāḥ sādhu śikṣitāḥ sa megha sama nirghoṣaḥ mahān śabdaḥ aspṛśat divam utthāya avaśya kārya artham yayau snānagṛham tatas tatas śukla ambarāḥ snātāḥ taruṇa aṣṭa uttaram śatam snāpakāḥ kāñcanaiḥ kumbhaiḥ pūrṇaiḥ samupatasthire bhadrāsane su upaviṣṭaḥ paridhāya ambaram laghu utsāditaḥ kaṣāyeṇa balavadbhiḥ su śikṣitaiḥ hariṇā candanena aṅgam anulipya mahā bhujaḥ sragvī ca akliṣṭa vasanaḥ prāc mukhaḥ prāñjaliḥ sthitaḥ jajāpa japyam kaunteyaḥ satām mārgam anuṣṭhitaḥ tatas agni śaraṇam dīptam praviveśa vinīta vat mantra pūtābhiḥ arcitvā niścakrāma gṛhāt tatas dvitīyām puruṣa vyāghraḥ kakṣyām niṣkramya pārthivaḥ dāntān veda vrata snātān snātān avabhṛtheṣu ca sahasra anucarān saurān aṣṭau daśa śatāni ca akṣataiḥ sumanobhiḥ ca vācayitvā mahā bhujaḥ tān dvijān madhu sarpirbhyām phalaiḥ śreṣṭhaiḥ su maṅgalaiḥ prādāt kāñcanam ekaikam niṣkam viprāya pāṇḍavaḥ alaṃkṛtam ca aśva śatam vāsāṃsi iṣṭāḥ ca dakṣiṇāḥ tathā gāḥ kapilāḥ dogdhrīḥ sa ṛṣabhāḥ pāṇḍu nandanaḥ hema śṛṅgī rūpya khurāḥ dattvā cakre pradakṣiṇam svastikān vardhamānān ca nandyāvartān ca kāñcanān mālyam ca jala kumbhān ca jvalitam ca hutāśanam pūrṇāni akṣata pātrāṇi rucakān rocanān tathā su alaṃkṛtāḥ śubhāḥ kanyāḥ dadhi sarpiḥ madhu udakam maṅgalyān pakṣiṇaḥ ca eva yat ca anyat api pūjitam dṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭvā ca kaunteyaḥ bāhyām kakṣyām agāt tatas tatas tasya mahā bāhoḥ tiṣṭhataḥ paricārakāḥ sauvarṇam sarvatobhadram muktā vaiḍūrya maṇḍitam parārdhya āstaraṇa āstīrṇam sa uttaracchadam ṛddhimat tatra tasya upaviṣṭasya bhūṣaṇāni mahātmanaḥ upajahruḥ mahārhāṇi preṣyāḥ śubhrāṇi sarvaśas rūpam āsīt mahā rāja dviṣatām śoka vardhanam pāṇḍaraiḥ candra raśmi ābhaiḥ hema daṇḍaiḥ ca cāmaraiḥ dodhūyamānaḥ śuśubhe vidyudbhiḥ iva toyadaḥ saṃstūyamānaḥ sūtaiḥ ca vandyamānaḥ ca bandibhiḥ tatas muhūrtāt āsīt tu bandinām nisvanaḥ mahān nemi ghoṣaḥ ca rathinām khura ghoṣaḥ ca vājinām hrādena gaja ghaṇṭānām śaṅkhānām ninadena ca narāṇām pada śabdaiḥ ca kampati iva sma medinī tatas śuddhāntam āsādya jānubhyām bhū tale sthitaḥ kuṇḍalī baddha nistriṃśaḥ saṃnaddha kavacaḥ yuvā abhipraṇamya śirasā dvāḥsthaḥ dharmātmajāya vai nyavedayat dhṛṣīkeśam upayātam mahātmane arghyam ca eva āsanam ca asmai dīyatām parama arcitam tatas praveśya vārṣṇeyam upaveśya varāsane yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca kaccit jñānāni sarvāṇi prasannāni tava acyuta saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas kṣattā prakṛtayaḥ nyavedayat upasthitāḥ anujñātaḥ ca rājñā sa prāveśayata tam janam virāṭam bhīmasenam ca dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca sātyakim śikhaṇḍinam yamau ca eva cekitānam ca kekayān ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriya ṛṣabham upatasthuḥ mahātmānam viviśuḥ ca āsaneṣu te ekasmin āsane vīrau upaviṣṭau mahā balau kṛṣṇaḥ ca yuyudhānaḥ ca mahātmānau mahā dyutī tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ teṣām śṛṇvatām madhusūdanam abravīt puṇḍarīkākṣam ābhāṣya madhuram vacaḥ ekam tvām vayam āśritya sahasrākṣam iva amarāḥ prārthayāmaḥ jayam yuddhe śāśvatāni sukhāni ca tvam hi rājya vināśam ca dviṣadbhiḥ ca nirākriyām kleśān ca vividhān kṛṣṇa sarvān tān api vettha naḥ arjunasya yathā satyā pratijñā syāt cikīrṣitā sa bhavān tārayatu asmāt duḥkha amarṣa mahā arṇavāt pāram titīrṣatām adya plavaḥ naḥ bhava mādhava rathī yat kurute kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ yatnam āsthitaḥ vāsudevaḥ uvāca sa amareṣu api lokeṣu sarveṣu na tathāvidhaḥ śarāsana dharaḥ kaḥ cit yathā pārthaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ vīryavān astra saṃpannaḥ parākrāntaḥ mahā balaḥ yuddha śauṇḍaḥ sadā amarṣī tejasā paramaḥ nṛṇām sa yuvā vṛṣabha skandhaḥ dīrgha bāhuḥ mahā balaḥ siṃha ṛṣabha gatiḥ śrīmān dviṣataḥ te haniṣyati aham ca tat kariṣyāmi yathā kuntī sutaḥ arjunaḥ adya tam pāpa karmāṇam kṣudram saubhadra ghātinam apunar darśanam mārgam iṣubhiḥ kṣepsyate arjunaḥ tasya adya gṛdhrāḥ śyenāḥ ca vaḍa gomāyavaḥ tathā bhakṣayiṣyanti māṃsāni ye ca anye puruṣādakāḥ rājadhānīm yamasya adya hataḥ prāpsyati saṃkule saṃjayaḥ uvāca tathā saṃbhāṣatām teṣām prādurāsīt dhanaṃjayaḥ didṛkṣuḥ bharata śreṣṭham rājānam sa suhṛd gaṇam tam praviṣṭam śubhām kakṣyām abhivādya agratas sthitam samutthāya arjunam premṇā sasvaje pāṇḍava ṛṣabhaḥ mūrdhni ca enam upāghrāya pariṣvajya ca bāhunā āśiṣaḥ paramāḥ procya smayamānaḥ abhyabhāṣata yādṛś rūpā hi te chāyā prasannaḥ ca janārdanaḥ dṛṣṭavān asmi bhadram te keśavasya prasāda jam tatas tat kathayām āsa yathādṛṣṭam dhanaṃjayaḥ āśvāsana artham suhṛdām tryambakena samāgamam tatas śirobhiḥ avanim spṛṣṭvā sarve ca vismitāḥ namaskṛtya vṛṣāṅkāya sādhu sādhu iti atha abruvan anujñātāḥ tatas sarve suhṛdaḥ dharmasūnunā tvaramāṇāḥ su saṃnaddhāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ yuddhāya niryayuḥ abhivādya tu rājānam yuyudhāna acyuta arjunāḥ hṛṣṭāḥ viniryayuḥ te vai yudhiṣṭhira niveśanāt tatra gatvā hṛṣīkeśaḥ kalpayām āsa sūta vat babhau ratha varaḥ kḷptaḥ śiśuḥ divasakṛt yathā tatas puruṣa śārdūlaḥ sajjaḥ sajjam puraḥsaraḥ kṛta āhnikāya pārthāya nyavedayata tam ratham tam tu loke varaḥ puṃsām kirīṭī hema varma bhṛt bāṇa bāṇāsanī vā aham pradakṣiṇam avartata stūyamānaḥ jaya āśībhiḥ āruroha mahā ratham sa rathe rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ kāñcane kāñcana āvṛtaḥ anvārurohatuḥ pārtham yuyudhāna janārdanau śaryāteḥ yajñam āyāntam yathā indram devam aśvinau atha jagrāha govindaḥ raśmīn raśmivatām varaḥ mātaliḥ vāsavasya iva vṛtram hantum prayāsyataḥ sa tābhyām sahitaḥ pārthaḥ ratha pravaram āsthitaḥ sahitaḥ budha śukrābhyām tamaḥ nighnan yathā śaśī prayāntam arjunam sūtāḥ māgadhāḥ ca eva tuṣṭuvuḥ sa jaya āśīḥ sa puṇya ahaḥ sūta māgadha nisvanaḥ yuktaḥ vāditra ghoṣeṇa teṣām rati karaḥ abhavat tam anuprayataḥ vāyuḥ puṇya gandha vahaḥ śuciḥ vavau saṃharṣayan pārtham dviṣataḥ ca api śoṣayan pāṇḍavānām tvadīyānām viparītāni māriṣa dṛṣṭvā arjunaḥ nimittāni vijayāya pradakṣiṇam yuyudhānam mahā iṣvāsam idam vacanam abravīt yathā hi imāni liṅgāni dṛśyante śini puṃgava yiyāsuḥ yama lokāya mama vīryam pratīkṣate sa tvam adya mahā bāho rājānam paripālaya tvayi ca aham parāśvasya pradyumne vā mahā rathe rājani eva parā guptiḥ kāryā sarva ātmanā tvayā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca śvobhūte kim akārṣuḥ te duḥkha śoka samanvitāḥ jānantaḥ tasya karmāṇi kuravaḥ savyasācinaḥ katham tat kilbiṣam kṛtvā nirbhayāḥ brūhi māmakāḥ putra śoka abhisaṃtaptam kruddham mṛtyum iva antakam āyāntam puruṣa vyāghram katham dadṛśuḥ āhave dṛṣṭvā putra paridyūnam kim akurvanta māmakāḥ kim nu saṃjaya saṃgrāme vṛttam duryodhanam prati babhūvuḥ ye manaḥ grāhyāḥ śabdāḥ śruti sukha āvahāḥ stuvatām na adya śrūyante putrāṇām śibire mama sūta māgadha saṃghānām nartakānām ca sarvaśas śabdena nāditā abhīkṣṇam abhavat yatra me śrutiḥ dīnānām adya tam śabdam na śṛṇomi samīritam āsīnaḥ aham purā tāta śabdam aśrauṣam uttamam niveśanam hata utsāham putrāṇām mama lakṣaye anyeṣām ca sutānām me na tathā śrūyate dhvaniḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ yam śiṣyāḥ paryupāsate droṇaputram mahā iṣvāsam putrāṇām me parāyaṇam vitaṇḍā ālāpa saṃlāpaiḥ huta yācita vanditaiḥ gītaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ iṣṭaiḥ ramate yaḥ divāniśam upāsyamānaḥ bahubhiḥ kuru pāṇḍava sātvataiḥ sūta tasya gṛhe śabdhaḥ na adya drauṇeḥ yathā purā droṇaputram mahā iṣvāsam gāyanāḥ nartakāḥ ca ye atyartham upatiṣṭhanti teṣām na śrūyate dhvaniḥ vinda anuvindayoḥ sāyam śibire yaḥ mahā dhvaniḥ śrūyate saḥ adya na tathā kekayānām ca veśmasu nitya pramuditānām ca tāla gīta svanaḥ mahān nṛtyatām śrūyate tāta gaṇānām saḥ adya na dhvaniḥ sapta tantūn vitanvānāḥ yam upāsanti yājakāḥ saumadattim śruta nidhim teṣām na śrūyate dhvaniḥ droṇasya āsīt a virataḥ gṛhe tat na śṛṇomi aham nānā deśa samutthānām gītānām yaḥ abhavat svanaḥ vāditra nāditānām ca saḥ adya na śrūyate mahān yadā prabhṛti upaplavyāt śāntim icchan janārdanaḥ āgataḥ sarva bhūtānām anukampā artham acyutaḥ vāsudevena tīrthena putra saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ kāla prāptam aham manye mā tvam duryodhana atigāḥ śame ced yācamānam tvam pratyākhyāsyasi keśavam pratyācaṣṭa sa dāśārham ṛṣabham sarva dhanvinām tatas duḥśāsanasya eva karṇasya ca matam dvayoḥ anvavartata hitvā mām kṛṣṭaḥ kālena durmatiḥ śalyaḥ bhūriśravāḥ ca eva purumitraḥ jayaḥ tathā aśvatthāmā kṛpaḥ droṇaḥ dyūtam na icchanti saṃjaya eteṣām matam ājñāya yadi varteta putrakaḥ sa jñāti mitraḥ sa suhṛd ciram jīvet anāmayaḥ ślakṣṇāḥ madhura saṃbhāṣāḥ jñāti madhye priyaṃvadāḥ kulīnāḥ saṃmatāḥ prājñāḥ sukham prāpsyanti pāṇḍavāḥ arhanti ardham pṛthivyāḥ te bhoktum sāmarthya sādhanāḥ teṣām api samudra antā pitṛpaitāmahī mahī niyujyamānāḥ sthāsyanti pāṇḍavāḥ dharma vartmani santi naḥ jñātayaḥ tāta yeṣām śroṣyanti pāṇḍavāḥ anyeṣām ca eva vṛddhānām bharatānām mahātmanām kam vā tvam manyase teṣām yaḥ tvā brūyāt atas anyathā kṛṣṇaḥ na dharmam saṃjahyāt sarve te ca tvad anvayāḥ mayā api ca uktāḥ te vīrāḥ vacanam dharma saṃhitam na anyathā prakariṣyanti dharma ātmānaḥ hi pāṇḍavāḥ vṛkodara arjunau yatra vṛṣṇi vīraḥ ca sātyakiḥ uttama ojāḥ ca pāñcālyaḥ yudhāmanyuḥ ca durjayaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca durdharṣaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca aparājitaḥ aśmakāḥ kekayāḥ ca eva kṣatradharmā ca saumakiḥ caidyaḥ ca cekitānaḥ ca putraḥ kāśyasya ca abhibhuḥ draupadeyāḥ virāṭaḥ ca drupadaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ kaḥ etān jātu yudhyeta loke asmin vai jijīviṣuḥ divyam astram vikurvāṇān saṃhareyuḥ ariṃdamāḥ duḥśāsana caturthānām nā anyam paśyāmi pañcamam yeṣām abhīśu hastaḥ syāt viṣvaksenaḥ rathe sthitaḥ saṃnaddhaḥ ca arjunaḥ yoddhā teṣām na asti parājayaḥ teṣām mama vilāpānām na hi duryodhanaḥ smaret teṣām vidura vākyānām uktānām dīrghadarśinām dṛṣṭvā imām phala nirvṛttim manye śocanti putrakāḥ hima atyaye yathā kakṣam śuṣkam vāta īritaḥ mahān agniḥ dahet tathā senām māmikām sa dhanaṃjayaḥ ācakṣva tat hi naḥ sarvam kuśalaḥ hi asi saṃjaya yat upāyāt tu sāyāhne kṛtvā pārthasya kilbiṣam na jātu tasya karmāṇi yudhi gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ apakṛtvā mahat tāta soḍhum śakṣyanti māmakāḥ kim nu duryodhanaḥ kṛtyam karṇaḥ kṛtyam kim abravīt duḥśāsanaḥ saubalaḥ ca teṣām evam gate api sarveṣām samavetānām putrāṇām mama saṃjaya yat vṛttam tāta saṃgrāme mandasya apanayaiḥ bhṛśam rājya kāmasya mūḍhasya rāga upahata cetasaḥ durnītam vā su nītam vā tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca hanta te saṃpravakṣyāmi sarvam pratyakṣa darśivān śuśrūṣasva sthiraḥ bhūtvā tava hi apanayaḥ mahān vilāpaḥ niṣphalaḥ rājan mā śucaḥ bharata ṛṣabha an atikramaṇīyaḥ ayam kṛtāntasya adbhutaḥ vidhiḥ mā śucaḥ bharata śreṣṭha diṣṭam etat purātanam yadi hi tvam purā dyūtāt kuntī putram yudhiṣṭhiram nivartayethāḥ putrān ca na tvām vyasanam āvrajet nivartitāḥ syuḥ saṃrabdhāḥ na tvām vyasanam āvrajet tat te buddhi vyabhīcāram upalapsyanti pāṇḍavāḥ pāñcālāḥ vṛṣṇayaḥ sarve ye ca anye api mahājanāḥ sa kṛtvā pitṛ karma tvam putram saṃsthāpya sat pathe tat te vilapitam sarvam mayā rājan niśāmitam arthe niviśamānasya viṣa miśram yathā madhu na tathā manyate kṛṣṇaḥ rājānam pāṇḍavam purā na bhīṣmam nā eva ca droṇam yathā tvām manyate nṛpa vyajānata yadā tu tvām rāja dharmāt adhas cyutam tadā prabhṛti kṛṣṇaḥ tvām na tathā bahu manyate paruṣāṇi ucyamānān ca yathā pārthān upekṣase tasya anubandhaḥ prāptaḥ tvām putrāṇām rājya kāmukam pitṛpaitāmaham rājyam apavṛttam tadā anagha atha pārthaiḥ jitām kṛtsnām pṛthivīm pratyapadyathāḥ pāṇḍunā āvarjitam rājyam kauravāṇām yaśaḥ tathā tatas ca abhyadhikam bhūyas pāṇḍavaiḥ dharma cāribhiḥ teṣām tat tādṛśam karma tvām āsādya su niṣphalam yat pitryāt bhraṃśitāḥ rājyāt tvayā iha āmiṣa gṛddhinā na hi rakṣanti rājānaḥ yudhyantaḥ jīvitam raṇe camūm vigāhya pārthānām yudhyante kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ yām tu kṛṣṇa arjunau senām yām sātyaki vṛkodarau yeṣām yoddhā guḍākeśaḥ yeṣām mantrī janārdanaḥ yeṣām ca sātyakiḥ goptā yeṣām goptā vṛkodaraḥ anyatra kauraveyebhyaḥ ye vā teṣām padānugāḥ kṣatra dharma rataiḥ śūraiḥ tāvat kurvanti kauravāḥ kurūṇām pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham tat sarvam śṛṇu tattvataḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tasyām niśāyām vyuṣṭāyām droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ svāni anīkāni sarvāṇi prākrāmat vyūhitum tatas śūrāṇām garjatām rājan saṃkruddhānām amarṣiṇām śrūyante sma giraḥ citrāḥ paraspara vadha eṣiṇām visphārya ca dhanūṃṣi ājau jyāḥ karaiḥ parimṛjya ca viniḥśvasantaḥ prākrośan kva idānīm sa dhanaṃjayaḥ vikośān su tsarūn anye kṛtadhārān samāhitān pītān ākāśa saṃkāśān asīn ke cit ca cikṣipuḥ carantaḥ tu asi mārgān ca dhanuḥ mārgān ca śikṣayā saṃgrāma manasaḥ śūrāḥ dṛśyante sma sahasraśas sa ghaṇṭāḥ candana ādigdhāḥ svarṇa vajra vibhūṣitāḥ samutkṣipya gadāḥ ca anye paryapṛcchanta pāṇḍavam anye bala mada unmattāḥ parighaiḥ bāhu śālinaḥ cakruḥ saṃbādham ākāśam ucchrita indra dhvaja upamaiḥ nānā praharaṇaiḥ ca anye vicitra sraj alaṃkṛtāḥ saṃgrāma manasaḥ śūrāḥ tatra tatra vyavasthitāḥ kva arjunaḥ kva ca govindaḥ kva ca mānī vṛkodaraḥ kva ca te suhṛdaḥ teṣām āhvayantaḥ raṇe tadā tatas śaṅkham upādhmāya tvarayan vājinaḥ svayam teṣu anīkeṣu sarveṣu sthiteṣu āhava nandiṣu bhāradvājaḥ mahā rāja jayadratham atha abravīt aśvatthāmā ca śalyaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ kṛpaḥ tathā śatam ca aśva sahasrāṇām rathānām ayutāni ṣaḍ dviradānām prabhinnānām sahasrāṇi caturdaśa padātīnām sahasrāṇi daṃśitāni ekaviṃśatiḥ gavyūtiṣu tri mātreṣu mām an āsādya tiṣṭhata tatrastham tvām na saṃsoḍhum śaktāḥ devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ kim punar pāṇḍavāḥ sarve samāśvasihi saindhava saṃprāyāt saha gāndhāraiḥ vṛtaḥ taiḥ ca mahā rathaiḥ varmibhiḥ sādibhiḥ yattaiḥ prāsa pāṇibhiḥ āsthitaiḥ cāmara āpīḍinaḥ sarve jāmbūnada vibhūṣitāḥ te ca eva sapta sāhasrāḥ dvi sāhasrāḥ ca saindhavāḥ mattānām adhirūḍhānām hasti ārohaiḥ viśāradaiḥ nāgānām bhīma rūpāṇām varmiṇām raudra karmiṇām tatas duḥśāsanaḥ ca eva vikarṇaḥ ca tava ātmajau dīrghaḥ dvādaśa gavyūtiḥ paśca ardhe pañca vistṛtaḥ vyūhaḥ sa cakra śakaṭaḥ bhāradvājena nirmitaḥ sūcī padmasya madhya sthaḥ gūḍhaḥ vyūhaḥ punar kṛtaḥ evam etam mahā vyūham vyūhya droṇaḥ vyavasthitaḥ sūcī mukhe mahā iṣvāsaḥ kṛtavarmā vyavasthitaḥ anantaram ca kāmbojaḥ jalasaṃdhaḥ ca māriṣa tatas śata sahasrāṇi yodhānām anivartinām vyavasthitāni sarvāṇi śakaṭe sūci rakṣiṇaḥ teṣām ca pṛṣṭhatas rāja balena mahatā vṛtaḥ śveta varma ambara uṣṇīṣaḥ vyūḍha uraskaḥ mahā bhujaḥ patākinam śoṇa hayam vedī kṛṣṇa ajina dhvajam droṇasya ratham ālokya prahṛṣṭāḥ kuravaḥ abhavan siddha cāraṇa saṃghānām vismayaḥ su mahān abhūt droṇena vihitam dṛṣṭvā vyūham kṣubdha arṇava upamam sa śaila sāgara vanām nānā janapada ākulām graset vyūhaḥ kṣitim sarvām iti bhūtāni menire ahita hṛdaya bhedanam mahat vai śakaṭam avekṣya kṛtam nananda rājā saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas vyūḍheṣu anīkeṣu samutkruṣṭeṣu māriṣa tāḍyamānāsu bherīṣu mṛdaṅgeṣu nadatsu ca anīkānām ca saṃhrāde vāditrāṇām ca nisvane pradhmāpiteṣu śaṅkheṣu saṃnāde loma harṣaṇe raudre muhūrte saṃprāpte savyasācī vyadṛśyata vaḍānām vāyasānām ca purastāt savyasācinaḥ bahulāni sahasrāṇi prākrīḍan tatra bhārata mṛgāḥ ca ghora saṃnādāḥ śivāḥ ca aśiva darśanāḥ dakṣiṇena prayātānām asmākam prāṇadan tathā viṣvak vātāḥ sa nirghātāḥ rūkṣāḥ śarkara varṣiṇaḥ nākuliḥ tu śatānīkaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkāni prājñau tau vyūhatuḥ tadā tribhiḥ aśva sahasraiḥ ca padātīnām śataiḥ śataiḥ agratas sarva sainyānām sthitvā durmarṣaṇaḥ abravīt adya gāṇḍīvadhanvānam tapantam yuddha durmadam aham āvārayiṣyāmi velā iva makara ālayam adya paśyantu saṃgrāme dhanaṃjayam amarṣaṇam viṣaktam mayi durdharṣam aśma kūṭam iva aśmani evam bruvan mahā rāja mahātmā sa mahāmatiḥ mahā iṣvāsaiḥ vṛtaḥ rājan mahā iṣvāsaḥ vyavasthitaḥ daṇḍapāṇiḥ iva asahyaḥ mṛtyuḥ kālena coditaḥ śūla pāṇiḥ iva akṣobhyaḥ varuṇaḥ pāśavān iva yuga anta agniḥ iva arciṣmān pradhakṣyan vai punar prajāḥ śubhra varma ambara dharaḥ su aṅgadī cāru kuṇḍalī ratha pravaram āsthāya naraḥ nārāyaṇa anugaḥ vidhunvan gāṇḍivam saṃkhye babhau sūryaḥ iva uditaḥ saḥ agra anīkasya mahataḥ iṣu pāte dhanaṃjayaḥ vyavasthāpya ratham sajjam śaṅkham dadhmau pratāpavān atha kṛṣṇaḥ api asaṃbhrāntaḥ pārthena saha māriṣa prādhmāpayat pāñcajanyam śaṅkha pravaram ojasā tayoḥ śaṅkha praṇādena tava sainye viśām pate āsan saṃhṛṣṭa romāṇaḥ kampitāḥ gata cetasaḥ yathā trasanti bhūtāni sarvāṇi aśani nisvanāt tathā śaṅkha praṇādena vitresuḥ tava sainikāḥ prasusruvuḥ śakṛt mūtram vāhanāni ca sarvaśas vyaṣīdanta narāḥ rājan śaṅkha śabdena māriṣa visaṃjñāḥ ca abhavan ke cit ke cit rājan vitatrasuḥ tatas kapiḥ mahā nādam saha bhūtaiḥ dhvaja ālayaiḥ akarot vyādita āsyaḥ ca bhīṣayan tava sainikān tatas śaṅkhāḥ ca bheryaḥ ca mṛdaṅgāḥ ca ānakaiḥ saha nānā vāditra saṃhrādaiḥ kṣveḍita āsphoṭita ākulaiḥ siṃhanādaiḥ sa vāditraiḥ samāhūtaiḥ mahā rathaiḥ tasmin su tumule śabde bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhane atīva hṛṣṭaḥ dāśārham abravīt pākaśāsaniḥ codaya aśvān hṛṣīkeśa yatra durmarṣaṇaḥ sthitaḥ etat bhittvā gaja anīkam pravekṣyāmi ari vāhinīm evam uktaḥ mahā bāhuḥ keśavaḥ savyasācinā sa saṃprahāraḥ tumulaḥ saṃpravṛttaḥ su dāruṇaḥ ekasya ca bahūnām ca ratha nāga nara kṣayaḥ tatas sāyaka varṣeṇa parjanyaḥ iva vṛṣṭimān parān avākirat pārthaḥ parvatān iva nīradaḥ avākiran bāṇa jālaiḥ tatas kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau tatas kruddhaḥ mahā bāhuḥ vāryamāṇaḥ paraiḥ yudhi śirāṃsi rathinām pārthaḥ kāyebhyaḥ apāharat śaraiḥ udbhrānta nayanaiḥ vaktraiḥ saṃdaṣṭa uṣṭha puṭaiḥ śubhaiḥ sa kuṇḍala śirastrāṇaiḥ vasudhā samakīryata puṇḍarīka vanāni iva vidhvastāni samantataḥ vinikīrṇāni yodhānām vadanāni cakāśire adṛśyanta yathā rājan megha saṃghāḥ sa vidyutaḥ śirasām patatām rājan śabdaḥ abhūt pṛthivī tale kālena paripakvānām tālānām patatām iva kaḥ cit khaḍgam viniṣkṛṣya bhujena udyamya tiṣṭhati na ajānanta śirāṃsi urvyām patitāni nara ṛṣabhāḥ a mṛṣyamāṇāḥ kaunteyam saṃgrāme jaya gṛddhinaḥ hayānām uttamāṅgaiḥ ca hasti hastaiḥ ca medinī bāhubhiḥ ca śirobhiḥ ca vīrāṇām samakīryata ayam pārthaḥ kutas pārthaḥ eṣa pārthaḥ iti prabho tava sainyeṣu yodhānām pārtha bhūtam iva abhavat niṣṭanantaḥ sa rudhirāḥ visaṃjñāḥ gāḍha vedanāḥ śayānāḥ bahavaḥ vīrāḥ kīrtayantaḥ suhṛd janam sa bhinḍipālāḥ sa prāsāḥ sa śakti ṛṣṭi paraśvadhāḥ sa niryūhāḥ sa nistriṃśāḥ sa śarāsana tomarāḥ sa bāṇa varma ābharaṇāḥ sa gadāḥ sa aṅgadāḥ raṇe mahā bhujaga saṃkāśāḥ bāhavaḥ parigha upamāḥ udveṣṭanti viceṣṭanti saṃveṣṭanti ca sarvaśas vegam kurvanti saṃrabdhāḥ nikṛttāḥ parama iṣubhiḥ tasya tasya antakaḥ bāṇaḥ śarīram upasarpati yat tasya ghaṭamānasya kṣipram vikṣipataḥ śarān lāghavāt pāṇḍu putrasya vyasmayanta pare janāḥ āvartamānam āvṛttam yudhyamānam ca pāṇḍavaḥ tathā arjunaḥ gaja anīkam avadhīt kaṅka patribhiḥ antakāle yathā bhūmiḥ vinikīrṇaiḥ mahīdharaiḥ yathā madhyaṃdine sūryaḥ duṣprekṣyaḥ prāṇibhiḥ sadā prabhagnam drutam āvignam atīva śara pīḍitam mārutena iva mahatā megha anīkam vidhūyatā prakālyamānam tat sainyam nā aśakat prativīkṣitum pratodaiḥ cāpa koṭībhiḥ huṃkāraiḥ sādhu vāhitaiḥ kaśā pārṣṇi abhighātaiḥ ca vāgbhiḥ ugrābhiḥ eva ca codayantaḥ hayān tūrṇam palāyante sma tāvakāḥ sādinaḥ rathinaḥ ca eva pattayaḥ ca arjuna arditāḥ pārṣṇi aṅguṣṭha aṅkuśaiḥ nāgān codayantaḥ tathā apare śaraiḥ saṃmohitāḥ ca anye tam eva abhimukhāḥ yayau dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca ke nu tatra raṇe vīrāḥ pratyudīyuḥ dhanaṃjayam āho svid śakaṭa vyūham praviṣṭāḥ mogha niścayāḥ droṇam āśritya tiṣṭhantaḥ prākāram akutobhayāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca hata vīre hata utsāhe palāyana kṛtakṣaṇe pākaśāsaninā abhīkṣṇam vadhyamāne śara uttamaiḥ na tatra kaḥ cit saṃgrāme śaśāka arjunam īkṣitum tatas tava sutaḥ rājan dṛṣṭvā sainyam tathāgatam duḥśāsanaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ yuddhāya arjunam abhyayāt sa kāñcana vicitreṇa kavacena samāvṛtaḥ jāmbūnada śirastrāṇaḥ śūraḥ tīvra parākramaḥ nāga anīkena mahatā grasan iva mahīm imām duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja savyasācinam āvṛṇot hrādena gaja ghaṇṭānām śaṅkhānām ninadena ca jyā kṣepa ninadaiḥ ca eva virāveṇa ca dantinām bhūḥ diśaḥ ca antarikṣam ca śabdena āsīt samāvṛtam tān dṛṣṭvā patataḥ tūrṇam aṅkuśaiḥ abhicoditān vyālamba hastān saṃrabdhān sa pakṣān iva parvatān siṃhanādena mahatā nara siṃhaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ gaja anīkam amitrāṇām abhitas vyadhamat śaraiḥ mahā ūrmiṇam iva uddhūtam śvasanena mahā arṇavam kirīṭī tat gaja anīkam prāviśat makaraḥ yathā kāṣṭhā atītaḥ iva ādityaḥ pratapan yuga saṃkṣaye dadṛśe dikṣu sarvāsu pārthaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ khura śabdena ca aśvānām nemi ghoṣeṇa tena ca devadattasya ghoṣeṇa gāṇḍīva ninadena ca śaraiḥ āśīviṣa sparśaiḥ nirbhinnāḥ savyasācinā te gajāḥ viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ yudhi gāṇḍīva coditaiḥ aneka śata sāhasraiḥ sarva aṅgeṣu samarpitāḥ ārāvam paramam kṛtvā vadhyamānāḥ kirīṭinā nipetuḥ aniśam bhūmau chinna pakṣāḥ iva adrayaḥ apare dantaveṣṭeṣu kumbheṣu ca kaṭeṣu ca śaraiḥ samarpitāḥ nāgāḥ krauñca vat vyanadan muhur gaja skandha gatānām ca puruṣāṇām kirīṭinā ācchidyanta uttamāṅgāni bhallaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ sa kuṇḍalānām patatām śirasām dharaṇī tale padmānām iva saṃghātaiḥ pārthaḥ cakre nivedanam yantra baddhāḥ vikavacāḥ vraṇa ārtāḥ rudhira ukṣitāḥ maurvīm dhanuḥ dhvajam ca eva yugān īṣāḥ tathā eva ca rathinām kuṭṭayām āsa bhallaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ maṇḍalena eva dhanuṣā nṛtyan pārthaḥ sma dṛśyate muhūrtāt nipatanti anye vāraṇāḥ vasudhā tale sa cāpāḥ sa aṅguli trāṇāḥ sa khaḍgāḥ sa aṅgadāḥ raṇe adṛśyanta bhujāḥ chinnāḥ hema ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ su upaskaraiḥ adhiṣṭhānaiḥ īṣā daṇḍaka bandhuraiḥ nihataiḥ vāraṇaiḥ aśvaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ ca nipātitaiḥ adṛśyata mahī tatra dāruṇa pratidarśanā evam duḥśāsana balam vadhyamānam kirīṭinā tatas duḥśāsanaḥ trastaḥ saha anīkaḥ śara arditaḥ droṇam trātāram ākāṅkṣan śakaṭa vyūham abhyagāt saṃjayaḥ uvāca duḥśāsana balam hatvā savyasācī dhanaṃjayaḥ sindhurājam parīpsan vai droṇa anīkam upādravat kṛtāñjaliḥ idam vākyam kṛṣṇasya anumate abravīt bhavat prasādāt icchāmi praveṣṭum durbhidām camūm tathā kṛṣṇa samaḥ ca eva satyam etat bravīmi te aśvatthāmā yathā tāta rakṣaṇīyaḥ tava anagha tava prasādāt icchāmi sindhu rājānam āhave nihantum dvipadām śreṣṭha pratijñām rakṣa me vibho mām a jitvā na bībhatso śakyaḥ jetum jayadrathaḥ etāvat uktvā tam droṇaḥ śara vrātaiḥ avākirat sa ratha aśva dhvajam tīkṣṇaiḥ prahasan vai sa sārathim tatas arjunaḥ śara vrātān droṇasya āvārya sāyakaiḥ vivyādha ca raṇe droṇam anumānya viśām pate kṣatra dharmam samāsthāya navabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ punar tasya iṣūn iṣubhiḥ chittvā droṇaḥ vivyādha tau ubhau viṣa agni jvalana prakhyaiḥ iṣubhiḥ kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau iyeṣa pāṇḍavaḥ tasya bāṇaiḥ chettum śarāsanam droṇaḥ śaraiḥ asaṃbhrāntaḥ jyām ciccheda āśu vīryavān arjunam ca śaraiḥ vīram smayamānaḥ abhyavākirat viśeṣayiṣyan ācāryam sarva astra viduṣām varam mumoca ṣaṣ śatān bāṇān gṛhītvā ekam iva drutam punar sapta śatān anyān sahasram ca anivartinām cikṣepa ayutaśas ca anyān te aghnan droṇasya tām camūm manuṣya vāji mātaṅgāḥ viddhāḥ petuḥ gatāsavaḥ vidrutāḥ ca raṇe petuḥ saṃchinna āyudha jīvitāḥ rathinaḥ ratha mukhyebhyaḥ sa hayāḥ śara pīḍitāḥ cūrṇita ākṣipta dagdhānām vajra anila hutāśanaiḥ tulya rūpāḥ gajāḥ petuḥ giri agra ambuda veśmanām petuḥ aśva sahasrāṇi prahatāni arjuna iṣubhiḥ haṃsāḥ himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe vāri viprahatāḥ iva ratha aśva dvipa patti oghāḥ salila oghāḥ iva adbhutāḥ yuga anta āditya raśmi ābhaiḥ hatāḥ tam pāṇḍava āditya śara aṃśu jālam kuru pravīrān yudhi niṣṭapantam sa droṇa meghaḥ śara varṣa vegaiḥ prācchādayat meghaḥ iva arka raśmīn atha atyartha visṛṣṭena dviṣatām asu bhojinā ājaghne vakṣasi droṇaḥ nārācena dhanaṃjayam sa vihvalita sarva aṅgaḥ kṣiti kampe yathā acalaḥ droṇaḥ tu pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ vāsudevam atāḍayat arjunam ca trisaptatyā dhvajam ca asya tribhiḥ śaraiḥ viśeṣayiṣyan śiṣyam ca droṇaḥ rājan parākramī adṛśyam arjunam cakre nimeṣāt śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ prasaktān patataḥ adrākṣma bhāradvājasya sāyakān maṇḍalīkṛtam eva asya dhanuḥ ca adṛśyata adbhutam droṇa sṛṣṭāḥ su bahavaḥ kaṅka patra paricchadāḥ tat dṛṣṭvā tādṛśam yuddham droṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ tadā pārtha pārtha mahā bāho na naḥ kāla atyayaḥ bhavet pārthaḥ ca api abravīt kṛṣṇam yatheṣṭam iti keśava tatas pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā droṇam prāyāt mahā bhujaḥ parivṛttaḥ ca bībhatsuḥ agacchat visṛjan śarān tatas abravīt smayan droṇaḥ kva idam pāṇḍava gamyate na ca asti sa pumān loke yaḥ tvām yudhi parājayet saṃjayaḥ uvāca tam cakrarakṣau pāñcālyau yudhāmanyu uttamaujasau anvayātām mahātmānau viśantam tāvakam balam tatas jayaḥ mahā rāja kṛtavarmā ca sāttvataḥ kāmbojaḥ ca śrutāyuḥ ca dhanaṃjayam avārayan teṣām daśa sahasrāṇi rathānām anuyāyinām abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayaḥ atha vasātayaḥ mācellakāḥ lalitthāḥ ca kekayāḥ madrakāḥ tathā nārāyaṇāḥ ca gopālāḥ kāmbojānām ca ye gaṇāḥ karṇena vijitāḥ pūrvam saṃgrāme śūra saṃmatāḥ bhāradvājam puraskṛtya tyaktātmānaḥ arjunam prati putra śoka abhisaṃtaptam kruddham mṛtyum iva antakam gāhamānam anīkāni mātaṅgam iva yūthapam mahā iṣvāsam parākrāntam nara vyāghram avārayan tatas pravavṛte yuddham tumulam loma harṣaṇam saṃjayaḥ uvāca drutam samanuyātaḥ ca droṇena rathinām varaḥ kiran iṣu gaṇān tikṣṇān sva raśmīn iva bhāskaraḥ tāpayām āsa tat sainyam deham vyādhi gaṇaḥ yathā chatrāṇi ca apaviddhāni rathāḥ cakraiḥ vinā kṛtāḥ vidrutāni ca sainyāni śara ārtāni samantataḥ iti āsīt tumulam yuddham na prājñāyata kim cana teṣām āyacchatām saṃkhye parasparam ajihmagaiḥ arjunaḥ dhvajinīm rājan abhīkṣṇam samakampayat satyām cikīrṣamāṇaḥ tu pratijñām satya saṃgaraḥ abhyadravat ratha śreṣṭham śoṇāśvam śvetavāhanaḥ tam droṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā marma bhidbhiḥ ajihmagaiḥ antevāsinam ācāryaḥ mahā iṣvāsam samardayat tam tūrṇam iva bībhatsuḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ abhyadhāvat iṣūn asyan iṣu vega vighātakān tasya āśu kṣipataḥ bhallān bhallaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tat adbhutam apaśyāma droṇasya ācāryakam yudhi kṣaran iva mahā meghaḥ vāri dhārāḥ sahasraśas droṇa meghaḥ pārtha śailam vavarṣa śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ arjunaḥ śara varṣam tat brahmāstreṇa eva māriṣa pratijagrāha tejasvī bāṇaiḥ bāṇān viśātayan droṇaḥ tu pañcaviṃśatyā śvetavāhanam ārdayat vāsudevam ca saptatyā bāhvoḥ urasi ca āśugaiḥ pārthaḥ tu prahasan dhīmān ācāryam sa śara oghiṇam visṛjantam śitān bāṇān avārayata tam yudhi āvarjayetām durdharṣam yugānta agnim iva utthitam varjayan niśitān bāṇān droṇa cāpa viniḥsṛtān kirīṭamālī kaunteyaḥ bhoja anīkam nyapātayat saḥ antarā kṛtavarmāṇam kāmbojam ca sudakṣiṇam tam arjunaḥ śitena ājau rājan vivyādha patriṇā ekaikam pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānām samārpayat śaraiḥ agni śikhā ākāraiḥ kruddha āśīviṣa saṃnibhaiḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya kṛtavarmā mahā rathaḥ pañcabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ tūrṇam vivyādha urasi bhārata punar ca niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pārtham vivyādha pañcabhiḥ tam pārthaḥ navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare viṣaktam dṛśya kaunteyam kṛtavarma ratham prati cintayām āsa vārṣṇeyaḥ na naḥ kāla atyayaḥ bhavet tatas kṛṣṇaḥ abravīt pārtham kṛtavarmaṇi mā dayām kuru sāṃbandhikam kṛtvā pramathya enam viśātaya tatas sa kṛtavarmāṇam mohayitvā arjunaḥ śaraiḥ abhyagāt javanaiḥ aśvaiḥ kāmbojānām anīkinīm amarṣitaḥ tu hārdikhyaḥ praviṣṭe śvetavāhane vidhunvan sa śaram cāpam pāñcālyābhyām samāgataḥ cakrarakṣau tu pāñcālyau arjunasya padānugau paryavārayat āyāntau kṛtavarmā ratheṣubhiḥ tau avidhyat tatas bhojaḥ sarva pāraśavaiḥ śaraiḥ tau api enam vivyadhatuḥ daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ athā anyat dhanuḥ ādāya hārdikyaḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ kṛtvā vidhanuṣau vīrau śara varṣaiḥ avākirat tau anye dhanuṣī sajye kṛtvā bhojam vijaghnatuḥ tena antareṇa bībhatsuḥ viveśa amitra vāhinīm na lebhāte tu tau dvāram vāritau kṛtavarmaṇā dhārtarāṣṭreṣu anīkeṣu yatamānau nara ṛṣabhau anīkāni ardayan yuddhe tvaritaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ na avadhīt kṛtavarmāṇam prāptam api ari sūdanaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā tu tathā āyāntam śūraḥ rājā śrutāyudhaḥ kṣurapreṇa su tīkṣṇena pārtha ketum atāḍayat tam arjunaḥ navatyā tu śarāṇām nata parvaṇām sa tat na mamṛṣe rājan pāṇḍaveyasya vikramam atha enam saptasaptatyā nārācānām samārpayat tasya arjunaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā śarāvāpam nikṛtya ca athā anyat dhanuḥ ādāya sa rājā krodha mūrchitaḥ vāsavim navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ bāhvoḥ urasi ca arpayat śaraiḥ aneka sāhasraiḥ pīḍayām āsa bhārata aśvān ca asya avadhīt tūrṇam sārathim ca mahā rathaḥ vivyādha ca enam saptatyā nārācānām mahā balaḥ hata aśvam ratham utsṛjya sa tu rājā śrutāyudhaḥ varuṇasya ātmajaḥ vīraḥ sa tu rājā śrutāyudhaḥ parṇāśā jananī yasya śīta toyā mahā nadī tasya mātā abravīt vākyam varuṇam putra kāraṇāt avadhyaḥ ayam bhavet loke śatrūṇām tanayaḥ mama sarveṇa avaśya martavyam jātena saritām vare durdharṣaḥ tu eṣa śatrūṇām raṇeṣu bhavitā sadā iti uktvā varuṇaḥ prādāt gadām mantra puraskṛtām yām āsādya durādharṣaḥ sarva loke śrutāyudhaḥ sa tayā vīra ghātinyā janārdanam atāḍayat pratijagrāha tām kṛṣṇaḥ pīnena aṃsena vīryavān na akampayata śaurim sā vindhyam girim iva anilaḥ pratyabhyayāt tam vipra ūḍhā kṛtyā iva duradhiṣṭhitā jaghāna ca āsthitam vīram śrutāyudham amarṣaṇam hatvā śrutāyudham vīram jagatīm anvapadyata hāhākāraḥ mahān tatra sainyānām samajāyata svena astreṇa hatam dṛṣṭvā śrutāyudham ariṃdamam ayudhyamānāya hi sā keśavāya narādhipa kṣiptā śrutāyudhena atha tasmāt tam avadhīt gadā yathā uktam varuṇena ājau tathā sa nidhanam gataḥ vyasuḥ ca api apatat bhūmau prekṣatām sarva dhanvinām patamānaḥ tu sa babhau parṇāśāyāḥ priyaḥ sutaḥ tatas sarvāṇi sainyāni senā mukhyāḥ ca sarvaśas prādravanta hatam dṛṣṭvā śrutāyudham ariṃdamam kāmboja rājasya putraḥ śūraḥ sudakṣiṇaḥ tasya pārthaḥ śarān sapta preṣayām āsa bhārata te tam śūram vinirbhidya prāviśan dharaṇī talam saḥ atividdhaḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ gāṇḍīva preṣitaiḥ mṛdhe vāsudevam tribhiḥ viddhvā punar pārtham ca pañcabhiḥ bhallābhyām bhṛśa tīkṣṇābhyām tam ca vivyādha pāṇḍavaḥ sarva pāraśavīm ca eva śaktim śūraḥ sudakṣiṇaḥ sa ghaṇṭām prāhiṇot ghorām kruddhaḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvane tam caturdaśabhiḥ pārthaḥ nārācaiḥ kaṅka patribhiḥ sa aśva dhvaja dhanuḥ sūtam vivyādha acintya vikramaḥ ratham ca anyaiḥ su bahubhiḥ cakre viśakalam śaraiḥ bibheda hṛdi bāṇena pṛthu dhāreṇa pāṇḍavaḥ sa bhinna marmā srasta aṅgaḥ prabhraṣṭa mukuṭa aṅgadaḥ papāta abhimukhaḥ śūraḥ yantra muktaḥ iva dhvajaḥ gireḥ śikhara jaḥ śrīmān su śākhaḥ su pratiṣṭhitaḥ śete sma nihataḥ bhūmau kāmboja āstaraṇa ucitaḥ su darśanīyaḥ tāmra akṣaḥ karṇinā sa sudakṣiṇaḥ putraḥ kāmboja rājasya pārthena vinipātitaḥ hatam śrutāyudham dṛṣṭvā kāmbojam ca sudakṣiṇam saṃjayaḥ uvāca hate sudakṣiṇe rājan vīre ca eva śrutāyudhe abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayaḥ atha vasātayaḥ abhyavarṣan tatas rājan śara varṣaiḥ dhanaṃjayam teṣām ṣaṣṭi śatān āryān prāmathnāt pāṇḍavaḥ śaraiḥ te sma bhītāḥ palāyanta vyāghrāt kṣudra mṛgāḥ iva teṣām āpatatām tūrṇam gāṇḍīva preṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ śirāṃsi pātayām āsa bāhūn ca eva dhanaṃjayaḥ śirobhiḥ patitaiḥ tatra bhūmiḥ āsīt nirantarā abhra chāyā iva ca eva āsīt dhvāṅkṣa gṛdhra vaḍaiḥ yudhi teṣu tu utsādyamāneṣu krodha amarṣa samanvitau śrutāyuḥ ca acyutāyuḥ ca dhanaṃjayam ayudhyatām tau enam śara varṣāṇi savya dakṣiṇam asyatām tvarā yuktau mahā rāja prārthayānau mahat yaśaḥ tau arjunam sahasreṇa patriṇām nata parvaṇām pūrayām āsatuḥ kruddhau taḍāgam jaladau yathā ājaghāna ratha śreṣṭhaḥ pītena niśitena ca saḥ atividdhaḥ balavatā śatruṇā śatru karśanaḥ ājagāma param moham mohayan keśavam raṇe śūlena bhṛśa tīkṣṇena tāḍayām āsa pāṇḍavam kṣate kṣāram sa hi dadau pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ pārthaḥ api bhṛśa saṃviddhaḥ dhvaja yaṣṭim samāśritaḥ siṃhanādaḥ mahān āsīt hatam matvā dhanaṃjayam kṛṣṇaḥ ca bhṛśa saṃtaptaḥ dṛṣṭvā pārtham vicetasam āśvāsayat suhṛdyābhiḥ vāgbhiḥ tatra dhanaṃjayam vāsudevam ca vārṣṇeyam śara varṣaiḥ samantataḥ pretarāja puram prāpya punar pratyāgataḥ yathā saṃchannam śara jālena ratham dṛṣṭvā sa keśavam śatrū ca abhimukhau dṛṣṭvā dīpyamānau iva analau prāduścakre tatas pārthaḥ śākram astram mahā rathaḥ tasmāt āsan sahasrāṇi śarāṇām nata parvaṇām te jaghnuḥ tau mahā iṣvāsau tābhyām sṛṣṭān ca sāyakān viceruḥ ākāśa gatāḥ pārtha bāṇa vidāritāḥ pratihatya śarān tūrṇam śara vegena pāṇḍavaḥ śrutāyuṣaḥ ca nidhanam vadhaḥ ca eva acyutāyuṣaḥ tayoḥ padānugān hatvā punar pañcaśatān rathān abhyagāt bhāratīm senām nighnan pārthaḥ varān varān śrutāyuṣam ca nihatam prekṣya ca eva acyutāyuṣam ayutāyuḥ ca saṃkruddhaḥ dīrghāyuḥ ca eva bhārata kirantau vividhān bāṇān pitṛ vyasana karśitau tau arjunaḥ muhūrtena śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ na aśaknuvan vārayitum pārtham kṣatriya puṃgavāḥ aṅgāḥ tu gaja vāreṇa pāṇḍavam paryavārayan kruddhāḥ sahasraśas rājan śikhitāḥ hasti sādinaḥ duryodhana samādiṣṭāḥ kuñjaraiḥ parvata upamaiḥ prācyāḥ ca dākṣiṇātyāḥ ca kaliṅga pramukhāḥ nṛpāḥ teṣām āpatatām śīghram gāṇḍīva preṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ nicakarta śirāṃsi ugrau bāhūn api subhūṣaṇān taiḥ śirobhiḥ mahī kīrṇā bāhubhiḥ ca saha aṅgadaiḥ babhau kanaka pāṣāṇā bhujagaiḥ iva saṃvṛtā bāhavaḥ viśikhaiḥ chinnāḥ śirāṃsi unmathitāni ca cyavamānāni adṛśyanta drumebhyaḥ iva pakṣiṇaḥ śaraiḥ sahasraśas viddhāḥ dvipāḥ prasruta śoṇitāḥ vyadṛśyanta adrayaḥ kāle gairika ambu sravāḥ iva nihatāḥ śerate sma anye bībhatsoḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ gaja pṛṣṭha gatāḥ mlecchāḥ nānā vikṛta darśanāḥ nānā veṣa dharāḥ rājan nānā śastra ogha saṃvṛtāḥ rudhireṇa anulipta aṅgāḥ bhānti citraiḥ śaraiḥ hatāḥ śoṇitam nirvamanti sma dvipāḥ pārtha śara āhatāḥ sahasraśas chinna gātrāḥ sa ārohāḥ sa padānugāḥ cukruśuḥ ca nipetuḥ ca babhramuḥ ca apare diśaḥ bhṛśam trastāḥ ca bahudhā svānena mamṛduḥ gajāḥ sa antara āyudhikāḥ mattāḥ dvipāḥ tīkṣṇa viṣa upamāḥ vidanti asura māyām ye su ghorāḥ ghora cakṣuṣaḥ yavanāḥ pāradāḥ ca eva śakāḥ ca sunikaiḥ saha go yoni prabhavāḥ mlecchāḥ kāla kalpāḥ prahāriṇaḥ dārva abhisārāḥ daradāḥ puṇḍrāḥ ca saha bāhlikaiḥ na te sma śakyāḥ saṃkhyātum vrātāḥ śata sahasraśas vṛṣṭiḥ tathāvidhā hi āsīt śalabhānām iva āyatiḥ abhra chāyām iva śaraiḥ sainye kṛtvā dhanaṃjayaḥ muṇḍa ardha muṇḍa jaṭilān aśucīn jaṭila ānanān mlecchān aśātayat sarvān sametān astra māyayā śaraiḥ ca śataśas viddhāḥ te saṃghāḥ saṃgha cāriṇaḥ prādravanta raṇe bhītāḥ giri gahvara vāsinaḥ gaja aśva sādi mlecchānām patitānām śataiḥ śaraiḥ vaḍāḥ kaṅkāḥ vṛkāḥ bhūmau apiban rudhiram mudā śara varṣa plavām ghorām keśa śaivala śāḍvalām prāvartayat nadīm ugrām śoṇita ogha taraṅgiṇīm śirastrāṇa kṣudra matsyām yuga ante kāla saṃbhṛtām akarot gaja saṃbādhām nadīm uttara śoṇitām dehebhyaḥ rāja putrāṇām nāga aśva ratha sādinām tathā āsīt pṛthivī sarvā śoṇitena pariplutā ṣaṣ sahasrān varān vīrān punar daśa śatān varān prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya kṣatriyān kṣatriya ṛṣabhaḥ śaraiḥ sahasraśas viddhāḥ vidhivat kalpitāḥ dvipāḥ śerate bhūmim āsādya śailāḥ vajra hatāḥ iva prabhinnaḥ iva mātaṅgaḥ mṛdnan naḍa vanam yathā bhūri druma latā gulmam śuṣka indhana tṛṇa ulapam nirdahet analaḥ araṇyam yathā vāyu samīritaḥ sainya araṇyam tava tathā kṛṣṇa anila samīritaḥ śara arciḥ adahat kruddhaḥ pāṇḍava agniḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ śūnyān kurvan rathopasthān mānavaiḥ saṃstaran mahīm prānṛtyat iva saṃbādhe cāpa hastaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ vajra kalpaiḥ śaraiḥ bhūmim kurvan uttara śoṇitām prāviśat bhāratīm senām saṃkruddhaḥ vai dhanaṃjayaḥ tam śrutāyuḥ tathā ambaṣṭhaḥ vrajamānam nyavārayat tasya arjunaḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅka patra paricchadaiḥ nyapātayat dhayān śīghram yatamānasya māriṣa dhanuḥ ca asya aparaiḥ chittvā śaraiḥ pārthaḥ vicakrame ambaṣṭhaḥ tu gadām gṛhya krodha paryākula īkṣaṇaḥ āsasāda raṇe pārtham keśavam ca mahā ratham ratham āvārya gadayā keśavam samatāḍayat gadayā tāḍitam dṛṣṭvā keśavam para vīra hā arjunaḥ bhṛśa saṃkruddhaḥ saḥ ambaṣṭham prati bhārata tatas śaraiḥ hema puṅkhaiḥ sa gadam rathinām varam tatas aparaiḥ śaraiḥ ca api gadām tasya mahātmanaḥ atha tām patitām dṛṣṭvā gṛhya anyām mahatīm gadām arjunam vāsudevam ca punar punar atāḍayat tasya arjunaḥ kṣuraprābhyām sa gadau udyatau bhujau ciccheda indra dhvaja ākārau śiraḥ ca anyena patriṇā ratha anīka avagāḍhaḥ ca vāraṇa aśva śataiḥ vṛtaḥ saḥ adṛśyata tadā pārthaḥ ghanaiḥ sūryaḥ iva āvṛtaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas praviṣṭe kaunteye sindhurāja jighāṃsayā droṇa anīkam vinirbhidya bhoja anīkam ca dustaram kāmbojasya ca dāyāde hate rājan sudakṣiṇe prabhagnam sva balam dṛṣṭvā putraḥ te droṇam abhyayāt gataḥ sa puruṣa vyāghraḥ pramathya imām mahā camūm arjunasya vighātāya dāruṇe asmin jana kṣaye senā kakṣam dahati me vahniḥ kakṣam iva utthitaḥ jayadrathasya goptāraḥ saṃśayam paramam gatāḥ sthirā buddhiḥ narendrāṇām āsīt brahma vidām vara na atikramiṣyati droṇam jātu jīvan dhanaṃjayaḥ jānāmi tvām mahābhāga pāṇḍavānām hite ratam prīṇāmi ca yathāśakti tat ca tvam na avabudhyase pāṇḍavān satatam prīṇāsi asmākam vipriye ratān asmān eva upajīvan tvam asmākam vipriye rataḥ na adāsyat ced varam mahyam bhavān pāṇḍava nigrahe na avārayiṣyam gacchantam aham sindhupatim gṛhān mayā tu āśaṃsamānena tvattaḥ trāṇam abuddhinā āśvāsitaḥ sindhupatiḥ mohāt dattaḥ ca mṛtyave yama daṃṣṭra antaram prāptaḥ mucyeta api hi mānavaḥ sa tathā kuru śoṇāśva yathā rakṣyeta saindhavaḥ mama ca ārta pralāpānām mā krudhaḥ pāhi saindhavam droṇaḥ uvāca na abhyasūyāmi te vācam aśvatthāmnā asi me samaḥ satyam tu te pravakṣyāmi tat juṣasva viśām pate sārathiḥ pravaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śīghrāḥ ca asya haya uttamāḥ alpam ca vivaram kṛtvā tūrṇam yāti dhanaṃjayaḥ kim nu paśyasi bāṇa oghān krośa mātre kirīṭinaḥ paścāt rathasya patitān kṣiptān śīghram hi gacchataḥ na ca aham śīghra yāne adya samarthaḥ vayasā anvitaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ca me grāhyaḥ miṣatām sarva dhanvinām evam mayā pratijñātam kṣatra madhye mahā bhuja tasmāt vyūha mukham hitvā na aham yāsyāmi phalgunam tulya abhijana karmāṇam śatrum ekam sahāyavān rājā śūraḥ kṛtī dakṣaḥ vairam utpādya pāṇḍavaiḥ vīra svayam prayāhi āśu yatra yātaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ katham tvām api atikrāntaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ mayā śakyaḥ ācārya pratibādhitum api śakyaḥ raṇe jetum vajra hastaḥ puraṃdaraḥ na arjunaḥ samare śakyaḥ jetum parapuraṃjayaḥ yena bhojaḥ ca hārdikyaḥ bhavān ca tridaśa upamaḥ sudakṣiṇaḥ ca nihataḥ sa ca rājā śrutāyudhaḥ śrutāyuḥ ca acyutāyuḥ ca mlecchāḥ ca śataśas hatāḥ tam katham pāṇḍavam yuddhe dahantam ahitān bahūn kṣamam ced manyase yuddham mama tena adya śādhi mām paravān asmi bhavati preṣya kṛt rakṣa me yaśaḥ droṇaḥ uvāca eṣa te kavacam rājan tathā badhnāmi kāñcanam yathā na bāṇāḥ na astrāṇi viṣahiṣyanti te raṇe yadi tvām sa asura surāḥ sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ na kṛṣṇaḥ na ca kaunteyaḥ na ca anyaḥ śastrabhṛt raṇe śarān arpayitum kaḥ cit kavace tava śakṣyati tvaramāṇaḥ svayam yāhi na ca asau tvām sahiṣyate saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam uktvā tvaran droṇaḥ spṛṣṭvā ambhaḥ varma bhāsvaram droṇaḥ uvāca sarīsṛpāḥ ca ye śreṣṭhāḥ tebhyaḥ te svasti bhārata svāhā svadhā śacī ca eva svasti kurvantu te sadā asitaḥ devalaḥ ca eva viśvāmitraḥ tathā aṅgirāḥ dhātā vidhātā loka īśaḥ diśaḥ ca sa digīśvarāḥ diggajāḥ ca eva catvāraḥ kṣitiḥ kham gaganam grahāḥ adhastāt dharaṇīm yaḥ asau sadā dhārayate nṛpa sa śeṣaḥ pannaga śreṣṭhaḥ svasti tubhyam prayacchatu purā vṛtreṇa daityena bhinna dehāḥ sahasraśas hṛta tejaḥ balāḥ sarve tadā sa indrāḥ divaukasaḥ brahmāṇam śaraṇam jagmuḥ vṛtrāt bhītāḥ mahā asurāt devāḥ ūcuḥ pramarditānām vṛtreṇa devānām deva sattama droṇaḥ uvāca atha pārśve sthitam viṣṇum śakra ādīn ca sura uttamān prāha tathyam idam vākyam viṣaṇṇān sura sattamān rakṣyāḥ me satatam devāḥ saha indrāḥ sa dvijātayaḥ tvaṣṭrā purā tapaḥ taptvā varṣa ayuta śatam tadā vṛtraḥ vinirmitaḥ devāḥ prāpya anujñām maheśvarāt na a gatvā śaṃkara sthānam bhagavān dṛśyate haraḥ dṛṣṭvā haniṣyatha ripum kṣipram gacchata mandaram yatra āste tapasām yoniḥ dakṣa yajña vināśanaḥ pinākī sarva bhūta īśaḥ bhaga netra nipātanaḥ apaśyan tejasām rāśim sūrya koṭi sama prabham saḥ abravīt svāgatam devāḥ brūta kim karavāṇi aham amogham darśanam mahyam kāma prāptiḥ atas astu vaḥ mūrtīḥ īkṣaṣva naḥ deva prahāraiḥ jarjarīkṛtāḥ śaraṇam tvām prapannāḥ sma gatiḥ bhava maheśvara viditam me yathā devāḥ kṛtyā iyam su mahā balā tvaṣṭuḥ tejaḥ bhavā ghorā durnivāryā akṛtātmabhiḥ avaśyam tu mayā kāryam sāhyam sarva divaukasām mama idam gātra jam śakra kavacam gṛhya bhāsvaram droṇaḥ uvāca sa tena varmaṇā guptaḥ prāyāt vṛtra camūm prati nānāvidhaiḥ ca śastra oghaiḥ pātyamānaiḥ mahā raṇe aṅgirāḥ prāha putrasya mantra jñasya bṛhaspateḥ tava adya deha rakṣā artham mantreṇa nṛpa sattama saṃjayaḥ uvāca punar eva vacaḥ prāha śanais ācārya puṃgavaḥ hiraṇyagarbheṇa yathā baddham viṣṇoḥ purā raṇe yathā ca brahmaṇā baddham saṃgrāme tārakā maye preṣayām āsa rājānam yuddhāya mahate dvijaḥ sa saṃnaddhaḥ mahā bāhuḥ ācāryeṇa mahātmanā rathānām ca sahasreṇa trigartānām prahāriṇām tathā danti sahasreṇa mattānām vīrya śālinām aśvānām ayutena eva tathā anyaiḥ ca mahā rathaiḥ vṛtaḥ prāyāt mahā bāhuḥ arjunasya ratham prati nānā vāditra ghoṣeṇa yathā vairocaniḥ tathā tatas śabdaḥ mahān āsīt sainyānām tava bhārata agādham prasthitam dṛṣṭvā samudram iva kauravam saṃjayaḥ uvāca praviṣṭayoḥ mahā rāja pārtha vārṣṇeyayoḥ tadā duryodhane prayāte ca pṛṣṭhatas puruṣa ṛṣabhe pāṇḍavāḥ somakaiḥ sārdham tatas yuddham avartata pāñcālānām kurūṇām ca vyūhasya puratas adbhutam rājan kadā cit nā asmābhiḥ dṛṣṭam tādṛś na ca śrutam yādṛś madhya gate sūrye yuddham āsīt viśām pate dhṛṣṭadyumna mukhāḥ pārthāḥ vyūḍha anīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ vayam droṇam puraskṛtya sarva śastrabhṛtām varam pārṣata pramukhān pārthān abhyavarṣāma sāyakaiḥ mahā meghau iva udīrṇau miśra vātau hima atyaye jāhnavī yamune nadyau prāvṛṣi iva ulbaṇa udake nānā śastra purovātaḥ dvipa aśva ratha saṃvṛtaḥ gadā vidyut mahā raudraḥ saṃgrāma jaladaḥ mahān bhāradvāja anila uddhūtaḥ śara dhārā sahasravān abhyavarṣat mahā raudraḥ pāṇḍu senā agnim uddhatam vyakṣobhayat anīkāni pāṇḍavānām dvijottamaḥ bibhitsantaḥ mahā setum vāri oghāḥ prabalāḥ iva vārayām āsa tān droṇaḥ jala oghān acalaḥ yathā pāṇḍavān samare kruddhān pāñcālān ca sa kekayān atha apare api rājānaḥ parāvṛtya samantataḥ mahā balāḥ raṇe śūrāḥ pāñcālān anvavārayan tatas raṇe nara vyāghraḥ pārṣataḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha saṃjaghāna asakṛt droṇam bibhitsuḥ ari vāhinīm yathā eva śara varṣāṇi droṇaḥ varṣati pārṣate tathā eva śara varṣāṇi dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ abhyavarṣata sa nistriṃśa purovātaḥ śakti prāsa ṛṣṭi saṃvṛtaḥ jyā vidyut ca apasaṃhrādaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna balāhakaḥ śara dhārā aśma varṣāṇi vyasṛjat sarvatodiśam nighnan ratha vara aśva oghān chādayām āsa vāhinīm yam yam ārchat śaraiḥ droṇaḥ pāṇḍavānām ratha vrajam tatas tatas śaraiḥ droṇam apākarṣata pārṣataḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam samāsādya tridhā sainyam abhidyata pāṇḍavaiḥ hanyamānāḥ ca droṇam eva apare avrajan sainyāni aghaṭayat yāni droṇaḥ tu rathinām varaḥ vyadhamat ca api tāni asya dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ tridhā bhūtāḥ vadhyante pāṇḍu sṛñjayaiḥ agopāḥ paśavaḥ araṇye bahubhiḥ śvāpadaiḥ iva kālaḥ saṃgrasate yodhān dhṛṣṭadyumnena mohitān ku nṛpasya yathā rāṣṭram durbhikṣa vyādhi taskaraiḥ drāvyate tadvat āpannā pāṇḍavaiḥ tava vāhinī cakṣūṃṣi pratihanyante sainyena rajasā tathā tridhā bhūteṣu sainyeṣu vadhyamāneṣu pāṇḍavaiḥ amarṣitaḥ tatas droṇaḥ pāñcālān vyadhamat śaraiḥ mṛdnataḥ tāni anīkāni nighnataḥ ca api sāyakaiḥ babhūva rūpam droṇasya kālāgneḥ iva dīpyataḥ ratham nāgam hayam ca api ca viśām pate ekaikena iṣuṇā saṃkhye nirbibheda mahā rathaḥ pāṇḍavānām tu sainyeṣu na asti kaḥ cit sa bhārata dadhāra yaḥ raṇe bāṇān droṇa cāpa cyutān śitān tathā eva pārṣatena api kālyamānam balam tava abhavat sarvatas dīptam śuṣkam vanam iva agninā vadhyamāneṣu sainyeṣu droṇa pārṣata sāyakaiḥ tyaktvā prāṇān param śaktyā prāyudhyanta sma sainikāḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca yudhyatām bharata ṛṣabha na āsīt kaḥ cit mahā rāja yaḥ atyākṣīt saṃyugam bhayāt viviṃśatiḥ citrasenaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ vinda anuvindau āvantyau kṣemadhūrtiḥ ca vīryavān trayāṇām tava putrāṇām trayaḥ eva anuyāyinaḥ bāhlīka rājaḥ tejasvī kula putraḥ mahā rathaḥ śaibyaḥ govāsanaḥ rājā yodhaiḥ daśa śata avaraiḥ putram parākrāntam avārayat madrāṇām īśvaraḥ śalyaḥ rājā rājānam āvṛṇot duḥśāsanaḥ tu avasthāpya svam anīkam amarṣaṇaḥ svakena aham anīkena saṃnaddha kavaca āvṛtaḥ catur śataiḥ mahā iṣvāsaiḥ cekitānam avārayam śakuniḥ tu saha anīkaḥ mādrī putram avārayat gāndhārakaiḥ sapta śataiḥ cāpa śakti śara asibhiḥ vinda anuvindau āvantyau virāṭam matsyam ārchatām prāṇān tyaktvā mahā iṣvāsau mitra arthe abhyudyatau yudhi śikhaṇḍinam yājñasenim rundhānam aparājitam bāhlikaḥ pratisaṃyattaḥ parākrāntam avārayat dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca pāñcālyam krūraiḥ sārdham prabhadrakaiḥ ghaṭotkacam tathā śūram rākṣasam krūra yodhinam alāyudhaḥ adravat tūrṇam kruddham āyāntam āhave saindhavaḥ pṛṣṭhatas tu āsīt sarva sainyasya bhārata rakṣitaḥ parama iṣvāsaiḥ kṛpa prabhṛtibhiḥ rathaiḥ drauṇiḥ dakṣiṇatas rājan sūtaputraḥ ca vāmatas pṛṣṭhagopāḥ tu tasya āsan saumadatti purogamāḥ kṛpaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ ca śalaḥ śalyaḥ ca durjayaḥ nītimantaḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ sarve yuddha viśāradāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca rājan saṃgrāmam āścaryam śṛṇu kīrtayataḥ mama kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca yathā yuddham avartata ayodhayan raṇe pārthāḥ droṇa anīkam bibhitsavaḥ rakṣamāṇāḥ svakam vyūham droṇasya api ca sainikāḥ vinda anuvindau āvantyau virāṭam daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ virāṭaḥ ca mahā rāja tau ubhau samare sthitau parākrāntau parākramya yodhayām āsa sa anugau teṣām yuddham samabhavat dāruṇam śoṇita udakam siṃhasya dvipa mukhyābhyām prabhinnābhyām yathā vane vāhlīkam rabhasam yuddhe yājñaseniḥ mahā balaḥ vāhlīkaḥ yājñasenim tu hema puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ bhīrūṇām trāsa jananam śūrāṇām harṣa vardhanam tābhyām tatra śaraiḥ muktaiḥ antarikṣam diśaḥ tathā abhavat saṃvṛtam sarvam na prājñāyata kim cana vāhlīka rājaḥ saṃrabdhaḥ draupadeyān mahā rathān manaḥ pañca indriyāṇi iva śuśubhe yodhayan raṇe ayodhayan te ca bhṛśam tam śara oghaiḥ samantataḥ indriya arthāḥ yathā deham śaśvat dehabhṛtām vara vārṣṇeyam sātyakim yuddhe putraḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tava īṣat mūrchām jagāma āśu sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ samāśvastaḥ tu vārṣṇeyaḥ tava putram mahā ratham vivyādha daśabhiḥ tūrṇam sāyakaiḥ kaṅka patribhiḥ tau anyonyam dṛḍham viddhau anyonya śara vikṣatau rejatuḥ samare rājan puṣpitau iva kiṃśukau aśobhata param lakṣmyā puṣpa āḍhyaḥ iva kiṃśukaḥ anadat bhairavam nādam vāhinyāḥ pramukhe tava dadṛśuḥ sarva bhūtāni śakra jambhau yathā purā śakunim rabhasam yuddhe kṛta vairam ca bhārata mādrī putrau ca saṃrabdhau śaraiḥ ardayatām mṛdhe tad mūlaḥ sa mahā rāja prāvartata jana kṣayaḥ uddhukṣitaḥ ca putreṇa tava krodha hutāśanaḥ yaḥ imām pṛthivīm rājan dagdhum sarvām samudyataḥ śakuniḥ pāṇḍu putrābhyām kṛtaḥ sa vimukhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃprāyāt javanaiḥ aśvaiḥ droṇa anīkāya saubalaḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ tathā śūram rākṣasam tam alāyudham yādṛśam hi purā vṛttam rāma rāvaṇayoḥ mṛdhe tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā madra rājānam āhave viddhvā pañcāśatā bāṇaiḥ punar vivyādha saptabhiḥ yathā pūrvam mahat yuddham śambara amararājayoḥ viviṃśatiḥ citrasenaḥ vikarṇaḥ ca tava ātmajaḥ ayodhayan bhīmasenam mahatyā senayā vṛtāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tathā tasmin pravṛtte tu saṃgrāme loma harṣaṇe kauraveyān tridhā bhūtān pāṇḍavāḥ samupādravan jalasaṃdham mahā bāhuḥ bhīmasenaḥ nyavārayat yudhiṣṭhiraḥ saha anīkaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam āhave kirantam śara varṣāṇi rocamānaḥ iva aṃśumān dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rāja droṇam abhyadravat raṇe kurūṇām somakānām ca saṃkruddhānām parasparam saṃkṣaye tu tathā bhūte vartamāne mahā bhaye dvaṃdvībhūteṣu sainyeṣu yudhyamāneṣu abhīta vat droṇaḥ pāñcāla putreṇa balī balavatā saha puṇḍarīka vanāni iva vidhvastāni samantataḥ cakrāte droṇa pāñcālyau nṛṇām śīrṣāṇi anekaśas vinikīrṇāni vīrāṇām anīkeṣu samantataḥ vastra ābharaṇa śastrāṇi dhvaja varma āyudhāni ca tapanīya vicitra aṅgāḥ saṃsiktāḥ rudhireṇa ca saṃsaktāḥ iva dṛśyante megha saṃghāḥ sa vidyutaḥ kuñjara aśva narān saṃkhye pātayantaḥ patatribhiḥ tāla mātrāṇi cāpāni vikarṣantaḥ mahā rathāḥ asi carmāṇi cāpāni śirāṃsi kavacāni ca viprakīryanta śūrāṇām saṃprahāre mahātmanām gṛdhrāḥ kaṅkāḥ vaḍāḥ śyenāḥ vāyasāḥ jambukāḥ tathā bahavaḥ piśitāśāḥ ca tatra adṛśyanta māriṣa bhakṣayantaḥ sma māṃsāni pibantaḥ ca api śoṇitam vilumpantaḥ sma keśān ca majjāḥ ca bahudhā nṛpa ākarṣantaḥ śarīrāṇi śarīra avayavān tathā nara aśva gaja saṃghānām śirāṃsi ca tatas tatas kṛtāstrāḥ raṇa dīkṣābhiḥ dīkṣitāḥ śara dhāriṇaḥ raṇe jayam prārthayantaḥ bhṛśam yuyudhire tadā asi mārgān bahuvidhān viceruḥ tāvakāḥ raṇe ṛṣṭibhiḥ śaktibhiḥ prāsaiḥ śūla tomara paṭṭiśaiḥ gadābhiḥ parighaiḥ ca anye vyāyudhāḥ ca bhujaiḥ api rathinaḥ rathibhiḥ sārdham aśva ārohāḥ ca sādibhiḥ mātaṅgāḥ vara mātaṅgaiḥ padātāḥ ca padātibhiḥ kṣībāḥ iva anye ca unmattāḥ raṅgeṣu iva ca cāraṇāḥ vartamāne tathā yuddhe nirmaryāde viśām pate dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ hayān aśvaiḥ droṇasya vyatyamiśrayat te hayā sādhu aśobhanta vimiśrāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ pārāvata savarṇāḥ ca rakta śoṇāḥ ca saṃyuge hayāḥ śuśubhire rājan meghāḥ iva sa vidyutaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca saṃprekṣya droṇam abhyāśam āgatam cikīrṣuḥ duṣkaram karma pārṣataḥ para vīra hā īṣayā samatikramya droṇasya ratham āviśat jaghāna ardheṣu ca aśvānām tat sainyāni abhyapūjayan khaḍgena carataḥ tasya śoṇa aśvān adhitiṣṭhataḥ yathā śyenasya patanam vaneṣu āmiṣa gṛddhinaḥ tathā evā āsīt abhīsāraḥ tasya droṇam jighāṃsataḥ tatas śara śatena asya śata candram samākṣipat droṇaḥ drupada putrasya khaḍgam ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ hayān ca eva catuḥṣaṣṭyā śarāṇām jaghnivān balī dhvajam chatram ca bhallābhyām tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī athā asmai tvaritaḥ bāṇam aparam jīvita antakam ākarṇapūrṇam cikṣepa vajram vajradharaḥ yathā tam caturdaśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ bāṇam ciccheda sātyakiḥ siṃhena iva mṛgam grastam nara siṃhena māriṣa droṇena mocayām āsa pāñcālyam śini puṃgavaḥ sātyakim prekṣya goptāram pāñcālyasya mahā āhave śarāṇām tvaritaḥ droṇaḥ ṣaḍviṃśatyā samarpayat tatas droṇam śineḥ pautraḥ grasantam iva sṛñjayān pratyavidhyat śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ ṣaḍviṃśatyā stanāntare tatas sarve rathāḥ tūrṇam pāñcālāḥ jaya gṛddhinaḥ sātvata abhisṛte droṇe dhṛṣṭadyumnam amocayan dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca bāṇe tasmin nikṛtte tu dhṛṣṭadyumne ca mokṣite tena vṛṣṇi pravīreṇa yuyudhānena saṃjaya amarṣitaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca saṃpradrutaḥ krodha viṣaḥ vyādita āsya śarāsanaḥ tīkṣṇa dhārā iṣu daśanaḥ śita nārāca daṃṣṭravān saṃrambha amarṣa tāmra akṣaḥ mahā ahiḥ iva niḥśvasan nara vīra pramuditaiḥ śoṇaiḥ aśvaiḥ mahā javaiḥ rukma puṅkhān śarān asyan yuyudhānam upādravat śara pāta mahā varṣam ratha ghoṣa balāhakam kārmuka ākarṣa vikṣiptam nārāca bahu vidyutam dṛṣṭvā eva abhipatantam tam śūraḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ uvāca sūtam śaineyaḥ prahasan yuddha durmadaḥ etam vai brāhmaṇam krūram sva karmaṇi anavasthitam āśrayam dhārtarāṣṭrasya rājñaḥ duḥkha bhaya āvaham śīghram prajavitaiḥ aśvaiḥ pratyudyāhi prahṛṣṭa vat ācāryam rāja putrāṇām satatam śūra māninam tatas rajata saṃkāśāḥ mādhavasya haya uttamāḥ droṇasya abhimukhāḥ śīghram agacchan vāta raṃhasaḥ iṣu jāla āvṛtam ghoram andhakāram anantaram anādhṛṣyam iva anyeṣām śūrāṇām abhavat tadā tatas śīghra astra viduṣoḥ droṇa sātvatayoḥ tadā na antaram śara vṛṣṭīnām dṛśyate nara siṃhayoḥ iṣūṇām saṃnipātena śabdaḥ dhārā abhighāta jaḥ śuśruve śakra muktānām aśanīnām iva svanaḥ nārācaiḥ atividdhānām śarāṇām rūpam ābabhau āśīviṣa vidaṣṭānām sarpāṇām iva bhārata tayoḥ jyā tala nirghoṣaḥ vyaśrūyata su dāruṇaḥ ajasram śaila śṛṅgāṇām vajreṇa āhanyatām iva ubhayoḥ tau rathau rājan te ca aśvāḥ tau ca sārathī rukma puṅkhaiḥ śaraiḥ channāḥ citra rūpāḥ babhuḥ tadā nirmalānām a jihmānām nārācānām viśām pate nirmukta āśīviṣa ābhānām saṃpātaḥ abhūt su dāruṇaḥ sravadbhiḥ śoṇitam gātraiḥ prasrutau iva vāraṇau anyonyam abhividhyetām jīvitānta karaiḥ śaraiḥ garjita utkruṣṭa saṃnādāḥ śaṅkha dundubhi nisvanāḥ upāramat mahā rāja vyājahāra na kaḥ cana tūṣṇīṃbhūtāni anīkāni yodhāḥ yuddhāt upāraman dadṛśe dvairatham tābhyām jāta kautūhalaḥ janaḥ rathinaḥ hasti yantāraḥ haya ārohāḥ padātayaḥ hasti anīkāni atiṣṭhanta tathā anīkāni vājinām muktā vidruma citraiḥ ca maṇi kāñcana bhūṣitaiḥ dhvajaiḥ ābharaṇaiḥ citraiḥ kavacaiḥ ca hiraṇmayaiḥ vaijayantī patākābhiḥ paristoma aṅga kambalaiḥ vimalaiḥ niśitaiḥ śastraiḥ hayānām ca prakīrṇakaiḥ jātarūpa mayībhiḥ ca rājatībhiḥ ca mūrdhasu gajānām kumbha mālābhiḥ dantaveṣṭaiḥ ca bhārata sa balākāḥ sa khadyotāḥ sa airāvata śatahradāḥ adṛśyanta uṣṇa paryāye meghānām iva vāgurāḥ apaśyan asmadīyāḥ ca te ca yaudhiṣṭhirāḥ sthitāḥ vimāna agra gatāḥ devāḥ brahma śakra purogamāḥ siddha cāraṇa saṃghāḥ ca vidyādhara mahā uragāḥ gata pratyāgata ākṣepaiḥ citraiḥ śastra vighātibhiḥ anyonyam samavidhyetām śaraiḥ tau droṇa sātyakī tatas droṇasya dāśārhaḥ śarān ciccheda saṃyuge patribhiḥ su dṛḍhaiḥ āśu dhanuḥ ca eva mahā dyute nimeṣa antara mātreṇa bhāradvājaḥ aparam dhanuḥ sajyam cakāra tat ca āśu ciccheda asya sa sātyakiḥ sajyam sajyam punar ca asya ciccheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas asya saṃyuge droṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā karma atimānuṣam bhīṣme ca puruṣa vyāghre yat idam sātvatām vare tam ca asya manasā droṇaḥ pūjayām āsa vikramam tutoṣa astra vidām śreṣṭhaḥ tathā devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ na tām ālakṣayām āsuḥ laghu tām śīghrakāriṇaḥ devāḥ ca yuyudhānasya gandharvāḥ ca viśām pate astraiḥ astra vidām śreṣṭhaḥ yodhayām āsa bhārata tasya astrāṇi astra māyābhiḥ pratihanya sa sātyakiḥ tasya ati mānuṣam karma dṛṣṭvā anyaiḥ asamam raṇe yuktam yogena yoga jñāḥ tāvakāḥ samapūjayan astram divyam mahā iṣvāsaḥ vāruṇam samudairayat hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt dṛṣṭvā divya astra dhāriṇau na viceruḥ tad ākāśe bhūtāni ākāśa gāni api astre te vāruṇa āgneye tābhyām bāṇa samāhite tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna mukhaiḥ sārdham virāṭaḥ ca sa kekayaḥ matsyāḥ śālveya senāḥ ca droṇam ājagmuḥ añjasā duḥśāsanam puraskṛtya rāja putrāḥ sahasraśas tatas yuddham abhūt rājan tava teṣām ca dhanvinām rajasā saṃvṛte loke śara jāla samāvṛte saṃjayaḥ uvāca rajasā kīryamāṇāḥ ca mandībhūtāḥ ca sainikāḥ tiṣṭhatām yudhyamānānām punar āvartatām api bhajyatām jayatām ca eva jagāma tat ahar śanais tathā teṣu viṣakteṣu sainyeṣu jaya gṛddhiṣu ratha mārga pramāṇam tu kaunteyaḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ yatra yatra rathaḥ yāti pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ ratha śikṣām tu dāśārhaḥ darśayām āsa vīryavān uttama adhama madhyāni maṇḍalāni vidarśayan te tu nāma aṅkitāḥ pītāḥ kāla jvalana saṃnibhāḥ snāyu naddhāḥ su parvāṇaḥ pṛthavaḥ dīrgha gāminaḥ vaiṇava ayasmaya śarāḥ su āyatāḥ vividha ānanāḥ rudhiram patagaiḥ sārdham prāṇinām papuḥ āhave ratha sthitaḥ krośa mātre yān asyati arjunaḥ śarān tārkṣya māruta raṃhobhiḥ vājibhiḥ sādhu vāhibhiḥ tathā agacchat dhṛṣīkeśaḥ kṛtsnam vismāpayan jagat yathā yayau arjunasya manaḥ bhiprāya śīghra gaḥ praviśya tu raṇe rājan keśavaḥ para vīra hā senā madhye hayān tūrṇam codayām āsa bhārata kṛcchreṇa ratham ūhuḥ tam kṣudh pipāsā śrama anvitāḥ kṣatāḥ ca bahubhiḥ śastraiḥ yuddha śauṇḍaiḥ anekaśas maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi viceruḥ te muhur muhur hatānām vāji nāgānām rathānām ca naraiḥ saha upariṣṭāt atikrāntāḥ śaila ābhānām sahasraśas saha senau samārchetām pāṇḍavam klānta vāhanam tau arjunam catuḥṣaṣṭyā saptatyā ca janārdanam śarāṇām ca śatena aśvān avidhyetām mudā anvitau ācchādayetām saṃrabdhau siṃhanādam ca nedatuḥ tayoḥ tu dhanuṣī citre bhallābhyām śvetavāhanaḥ athā anye dhanuṣī rājan pragṛhya samare tadā pāṇḍavam bhṛśa saṃkruddhau ardayām āsatuḥ śaraiḥ tayoḥ tu bhṛśa saṃkruddhaḥ śarābhyām pāṇḍu nandanaḥ ciccheda dhanuṣī tūrṇam bhūyas eva dhanaṃjayaḥ tathā anyaiḥ viśikhaiḥ tūrṇam hema puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ jaghāna aśvān sa padātān tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī jyeṣṭhasya ca śiraḥ kāyāt kṣurapreṇa nyakṛntata sa papāta hataḥ pṛthvyām vāta rugṇaḥ iva drumaḥ vindam tu nihatam dṛṣṭvā anuvindaḥ pratāpavān hata aśvam ratham utsṛjya gadām gṛhya mahā balaḥ gadayā gadinām śreṣṭhaḥ nṛtyan iva mahā rathaḥ tasya arjunaḥ śaraiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ grīvām pādau bhujau śiraḥ tatas tau nihatau dṛṣṭvā tayoḥ rājan padānugāḥ abhyadravanta saṃkruddhāḥ kirantaḥ śataśas śarān tān arjunaḥ śaraiḥ tūrṇam nihatya bharata ṛṣabha tayoḥ senām atikramya kṛcchrāt niryāt dhanaṃjayaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā kuravaḥ trastāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ ca abhavan punar abhyavarṣan tadā pārtham samantāt bharata ṛṣabha śrāntam ca enam samālakṣya jñātvā dūre ca saindhavam tān tu dṛṣṭvā su saṃrabdhān utsmayan puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ śanakais iva dāśārham arjunaḥ vākyam abravīt śara arditāḥ ca glānāḥ ca hayāḥ dūre ca saindhavaḥ kim iha anantaram kāryam jyāyiṣṭham tava rocate brūhi kṛṣṇa yathātattvam tvam hi prājñatamaḥ sadā bhavat netrāḥ raṇe śatrūn vijeṣyanti iha pāṇḍavāḥ aham āvārayiṣyāmi sarva sainyāni keśava saṃjayaḥ uvāca gāṇḍīvam dhanuḥ ādāya tasthau giriḥ iva acalaḥ tam abhyadhāvan krośantaḥ kṣatriyāḥ jaya kāṅkṣiṇaḥ idam chidram iti jñātvā dharaṇī stham dhanaṃjayam vikarṣantaḥ ca cāpāni visṛjantaḥ ca sāyakān chādayantaḥ śaraiḥ pārtham meghāḥ iva divākaram ratha siṃham ratha udārāḥ siṃham mattāḥ iva dvipāḥ astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya dviṣatām sarvatas vibhuḥ iṣubhiḥ bahubhiḥ tūrṇam sarvān eva samāvṛṇot tatra antarikṣe bāṇānām pragāḍhānām viśām pate saṃgharṣeṇa mahā arciṣmān pāvakaḥ samajāyata tatra tatra mahā iṣvāsaiḥ śvasadbhiḥ śoṇita ukṣitaiḥ saṃrabdhaiḥ ca aribhiḥ vīraiḥ prārthayadbhiḥ jayam mṛdhe śara ūrmiṇam dhvaja āvartam nāga nakram duratyayam uṣṇīṣa kamaṭha channam patākā phena mālinam ratha sāgaram akṣobhyam mātaṅga aṅga śilā citam velā bhūtaḥ tadā pārthaḥ patribhiḥ samavārayat asaṃbhrāntaḥ mahā bāhuḥ arjunam vākyam abravīt udapānam iha aśvānām na alam asti raṇe arjuna abhihatya arjunaḥ cakre vāji pānam saraḥ śubham śara vaṃśam śara sthūṇam śara ācchādanam adbhutam śara veśma akarot pārthaḥ tvaṣṭā iva adbhuta karma kṛt śara veśmani pārthena kṛte tasmin mahā raṇe saṃjayaḥ uvāca vāsudevaḥ rathāt tūrṇam avatīrya mahā dyutiḥ mocayām āsa turagān vitunnān kaṅka patribhiḥ a dṛṣṭa pūrvam tat dṛṣṭvā siṃhanādaḥ mahān abhūt siddha cāraṇa saṃghānām sainikānām ca sarvaśas padātinam tu kaunteyam yudhyamānam nara ṛṣabhāḥ na asaṃbhramat tadā pārthaḥ tat asya puruṣān ati vyasṛjanta śara oghān te pāṇḍavam prati pārthivāḥ na ca avyathata dharma ātmā vāsaviḥ para vīra hā sa tāni śara jālāni gadāḥ prāsān ca vīryavān āgatān agrasat pārthaḥ saritaḥ sāgaraḥ yathā sarveṣām pārthiva indrāṇām agrasat tān śara uttamān apūjayan mahā rāja kauravāḥ parama adbhutam yat aśvān pārtha govindau mocayām āsatuḥ raṇe athā utsmayan hṛṣīkeśaḥ strī madhye iva bhārata upāvartayat avyagraḥ tān aśvān puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ miṣatām sarva sainyānām tvadīyānām viśām pate teṣām śramam ca glānim ca vepathum vamathum vraṇān sarvam vyapānudat kṛṣṇaḥ kuśalaḥ hi aśva karmaṇi śalyān uddhṛtya pāṇibhyām parimṛjya ca tān hayān upāvṛtya yathānyāyam pāyayām āsa vāri saḥ sa tān labdha udakān snātān jagdha annān vigata klamān yojayām āsa saṃhṛṣṭaḥ punar eva ratha uttame sa tam ratha varam śauriḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ samāsthāya mahā tejāḥ sa arjunaḥ prayayau drutam dṛṣṭvā kuru bala śreṣṭhāḥ punar vimanasaḥ abhavan viniḥśvasantaḥ te rājan bhagna daṃṣṭrāḥ iva uragāḥ dhik aho dhik gataḥ pārthaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ca iti abruvan pṛthak krośatām yatamānānām asaṃsaktau paraṃtapau darśayitvā ātmanaḥ vīryam prayātau sarva rājasu tau prayātau punar dṛṣṭvā tadā anye sainikāḥ bruvan tvaradhvam kuravaḥ sarve vadhe kṛṣṇa kirīṭinoḥ ratham yuktvā hi dāśārhaḥ miṣatām sarva dhanvinām jayadrathāya yāti eṣa kadarthīkṛtya naḥ raṇe tatra ke cit mithas rājan samabhāṣanta bhūmipāḥ a dṛṣṭa pūrvam saṃgrāme tat dṛṣṭvā mahat adbhutam sarva sainyāni rājā ca dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ atyayam gataḥ duryodhana aparādhena kṣatram kṛtsnā ca medinī tat karotu vṛthā dṛṣṭiḥ dhārtarāṣṭraḥ an upāya vid tatas śīghrataram prāyāt pāṇḍavaḥ saindhavam prati nivartamāne tigmāṃśau hṛṣṭaiḥ pīta udakaiḥ hayaiḥ tam prayāntam mahā bāhum sarva śastrabhṛtām varam na aśaknuvan vārayitum yodhāḥ kruddham iva antakam vidrāvya tu tatas sainyam pāṇḍavaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ yathā mṛga gaṇān siṃhaḥ saindhava arthe vyaloḍayat gāhamānaḥ tu anīkāni tūrṇam aśvān acodayat balāka varṇān dāśārhaḥ pāñcajanyam vyanādayat kaunteyena agratas sṛṣṭāḥ nyapatan pṛṣṭhatas śarāḥ tūrṇāt tūrṇataram hi aśvāḥ te avahan vāta raṃhasaḥ vāta uddhūta patākā antam ratham jalada nisvanam ghoram kapi dhvajam dṛṣṭvā viṣaṇṇāḥ rathinaḥ abhavan divākare atha rajasā sarvatas saṃvṛte bhṛśam śara ārtāḥ ca raṇe yodhāḥ na kṛṣṇau śekuḥ īkṣitum apanīyatsu śalyeṣu dhiṣṭhitam puruṣa ṛṣabham saṃjayaḥ uvāca sraṃsantaḥ iva majjānaḥ tāvakānām bhayāt nṛpa tau dṛṣṭvā samatikrāntau vāsudeva dhanaṃjayau sthirībūtāḥ mahātmānaḥ pratyagacchan dhanaṃjayam ye gatāḥ pāṇḍavam yuddhe krodha amarṣa samanvitāḥ tau atītya ratha anīkam vimuktau puruṣa ṛṣabhau dadṛśāte yathā rāhoḥ āsyāt muktau prabhākarau tathā kṛṣṇau adṛśyetām senā jālam vidārya tat vimuktau śastra saṃbādhāt droṇa anīkāt su durbhidāt adṛśyetām mahātmānau kāla sūryau iva uditau adṛśyetām mahātmānau śatru saṃbādha kāriṇau vyakṣobhayetām senām tau samudram makarau iva tāvakāḥ tava putrāḥ ca droṇa anīka sthayoḥ tayoḥ tau tu dṛṣṭvā vyatikrāntau droṇa anīkam mahā dyutī na aśaśaṃsuḥ mahā rāja sindhurājasya jīvitam āśā balavatī rājan putrāṇām abhavat tava droṇa hārdikyayoḥ kṛṣṇau na mokṣyete iti prabho tām āśām viphalām kṛtvā nistīrṇau tau paraṃtapau droṇa anīkam mahā rāja bhoja anīkam ca dustaram atha dṛṣṭvā vyatikrāntau jvalitau iva pāvakau nirāśāḥ sindhurājasya jīvitam na āśaśaṃsire jayadratha vadhe vācaḥ tāḥ tāḥ kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau asau madhye kṛtaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ mahā rathaiḥ tathā api enam haniṣyāvaḥ iti kṛṣṇau abhāṣatām iti kṛṣṇau mahā bāhū mithas kathayatām tadā pītvā vāri samāśvastau tathā eva āstām ariṃdamau vyāghra siṃha gaja ākīrṇān atikramya iva parvatān adṛśyetām mahā bāhū yathā mṛtyu jarā atigau droṇāt āśīviṣa ākārāt jvalitāt iva pāvakāt tau muktau sāgara prakhyāt droṇa anīkāt ariṃdamau adṛśyetām mudā yuktau samuttīrya arṇavam yathā rocamānau adṛśyetām indra agnyoḥ sadṛśau raṇe udbhinna rudhirau kṛṣṇau bhāradvājasya sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ citau vyarocetām karṇikāraiḥ iva acalau droṇa grāha hradāt muktau śakti āśīviṣa saṃkaṭāt ayaḥ śara ugra makarāt kṣatriya pravara ambhasaḥ jyā ghoṣa tala nirhrādāt gadā nistriṃśa vidyutaḥ bāhubhyām iva saṃtīrṇau sindhu ṣaṣṭhāḥ samudragāḥ tapānte saritaḥ pūrṇāḥ mahā grāha samākulāḥ iti kṛṣṇau mahā iṣvāsau yaśasā loka viśrutau rurum nipāne lipsantau vyāghra vat tau atiṣṭhatām lohita akṣau mahā bāhū saṃyattau kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau sindhurājam abhiprekṣya hṛṣṭau vyanadatām muhur tayoḥ āsīt pratibhrājaḥ sūrya pāvakayoḥ iva harṣaḥ eva tayoḥ āsīt droṇa anīka pramuktayoḥ samīpe saindhavam dṛṣṭvā śyenayoḥ āmiṣam yathā sahasā petatuḥ kruddhau kṣipram śyenau iva āmiṣe tau tu dṛṣṭvā vyatikrāntau hṛṣīkeśa dhanaṃjayau sindhurājasya rakṣā artham parākrāntaḥ sutaḥ tava kṛṣṇa pārthau mahā iṣvāsau vyatikramya atha te sutaḥ agratas puṇḍarīkākṣam pratīyāya narādhipa tatas sarveṣu sainyeṣu vāditrāṇi prahṛṣṭa vat siṃhanāda ravāḥ ca āsan śaṅkha dundubhi miśritāḥ dṛṣṭvā duryodhanam tatra kṛṣṇayoḥ pramukhe sthitam ye ca te sindhurājasya goptāraḥ pāvaka upamāḥ te prahṛṣyanta samare dṛṣṭvā putram tava abhibho dṛṣṭvā duryodhanam kṛṣṇaḥ tu atikrāntam saha anugam abravīt arjunam rājan prāpta kālam idam vacaḥ vāsudevaḥ uvāca āpad gatam imam manye na asti asya sadṛśaḥ rathaḥ dūra pātī mahā iṣvāsaḥ kṛtāstraḥ yuddha durmadaḥ dṛḍha astraḥ citra yodhī ca dhārtarāṣṭraḥ mahā balaḥ kṛtī ca satatam pārtha nityam dveṣṭi ca pāṇḍavān atra vaḥ dyūtam āyātam vijayāya itarāya vā eṣa mūlam anarthānām pāṇḍavānām mahā rathaḥ saḥ ayam prāptaḥ tava ākṣepam paśya sāphalyam ātmanaḥ katham hi rājā rājya arthī tvayā gaccheta saṃyugam diṣṭyā tu idānīm saṃprāptaḥ eṣa te bāṇa gocaram sa yathā jīvitam jahyāt tathā kuru dhanaṃjaya aiśvarya mada saṃmūḍhaḥ nā eṣa duḥkham upeyivān na ca te saṃyuge vīryam jānāti puruṣa ṛṣabha tvām hi lokāḥ trayaḥ pārtha sa sura asura mānuṣāḥ jahi enam vai mahā bāho yathā vṛtram puraṃdaraḥ nikṛtyā dharmarājam ca dyūte vañcitavān ayam bahūni su nṛśaṃsāni kṛtāni etena mānada yuṣmāsu pāpa matinā apāpeṣu eva nityadā tam anāryam sadā kṣudram puruṣam kāma cāriṇam āryām yuddhe matim kṛtvā jahi pārtha a vicārayan nikṛtyā rājya haraṇam vana vāsam ca pāṇḍava parikleśam ca kṛṣṇāyāḥ hṛdi kṛtvā parākrama diṣṭyā eṣa tava bāṇānām gocare parivartate pratighātāya kāryasya diṣṭyā ca yatate agratas diṣṭyā jānāti saṃgrāme yoddhavyam hi tvayā saha diṣṭyā ca sa phalāḥ pārtha sarve kāmāḥ hi kāmitāḥ tasmāt jahi raṇe pārtha dhārtarāṣṭram kula adhamam vairasya asyāḥ tu avabhṛthaḥ mūlam chindhi durātmanām saṃjayaḥ uvāca tam tathā iti abravīt pārthaḥ kṛtya rūpam idam mama yena etat dīrgha kālam naḥ bhuktam rājyam akaṇṭakam api tasyāḥ anarhāyāḥ parikleśasya mādhava kṛṣṇāyāḥ śaknuyām gantum padam keśa pradharṣaṇe iti evam vādinau hṛṣṭau kṛṣṇau śvetān haya uttamān preṣayām āsatuḥ saṃkhye prepsantau tam narādhipam yat arjuna hṛṣīkeśau pratyudyātaḥ a vicārayan mahān nādaḥ hi abhūt tatra dṛṣṭvā rājānam āhave abhyavaikṣanta rājānaḥ bhīma rūpāḥ samantataḥ dṛṣṭvā tu pārtham saṃrabdham vāsudevam ca māriṣa tatas prahṛṣṭaḥ dāśārhaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ ca dhanaṃjayaḥ vyākrośetām mahā nādam dadhmatuḥ ca ambuja uttamau tau hṛṣṭa rūpau saṃprekṣya kauraveyāḥ ca sarvaśas tathā tu dṛṣṭvā yodhāḥ te prahṛṣṭau kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau hataḥ rājā hataḥ rājā iti ūcuḥ evam bhaya arditāḥ vyetu vaḥ bhīḥ aham kṛṣṇau preṣayiṣyāmi mṛtyave iti uktvā sainikān sarvān jaya apekṣī narādhipaḥ pārtham ābhāṣya saṃrambhāt idam vacanam abravīt pārtha yat śikṣitam te astram divyam mānuṣam eva ca tat darśaya mayi kṣipram yadi jātaḥ asi pāṇḍunā asmat parokṣam karmāṇi pravadanti kṛtāni te svāmi satkāra yuktāni yāni tāni iha darśaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam uktvā arjunam rājā tribhiḥ marma atigaiḥ śaraiḥ tam caturdaśabhiḥ pārthaḥ citra puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ prāhiṇot niśitān bāṇān te ca abhraśyanta varmaṇaḥ aṣṭāviṃśat tu tān bāṇān astān viprekṣya niṣphalān abravīt para vīra ghnaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ arjunam idam vacaḥ adṛṣṭa pūrvam paśyāmi śilānām iva sarpaṇam tvayā saṃpreṣitāḥ pārtha na artham kurvanti patriṇaḥ kaccit gāṇḍīvataḥ prāṇāḥ tathā eva bharata ṛṣabha muṣṭiḥ ca te yathāpūrvam bhujayoḥ ca balam tava na ced vidheḥ ayam kālaḥ prāptaḥ syāt adya paścimaḥ tava ca eva asya śatroḥ ca tat mama ācakṣva pṛcchataḥ vismayaḥ me mahān pārtha tava dṛṣṭvā śarān imān vajra aśani samāḥ ghorāḥ para kāya avabhedinaḥ śarāḥ kurvanti te na artham pārtha kā adya viḍambanā droṇena eṣā matiḥ kṛṣṇa dhārtarāṣṭre niveśitā jānan tvam api vai kṛṣṇa mām vimohayase katham eṣa duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇa droṇena vihitām imām tiṣṭhati abhīta vat saṃkhye bibhrat kavaca dhāraṇām strī vat eṣa bibharti etām yuktām kavaca dhāraṇām paśya bāhvoḥ ca me vīryam dhanuṣaḥ ca janārdana saṃjayaḥ uvāca vikṛṣyamāṇān tena evam dhanuḥ madhya gatān śarān tān asya astreṇa ciccheda drauṇiḥ sarva astra ghātinā tān nikṛttān iṣūn dṛṣṭvā dūratas brahma vādinā nyavedayat keśavāya vismitaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ na etat astram mayā śakyam dvis prayoktum janārdana avidhyata raṇe rājan śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ bhūyas evā abhyavarṣat ca samare kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau śara varṣeṇa mahatā tatas ahṛṣyanta tāvakāḥ cakruḥ vāditra ninadān siṃhanāda ravān tathā tatas kruddhaḥ raṇe pārthaḥ parisaṃlihan na apaśyata tatas asya aṅgam yat na syāt varma rakṣitam hayān cakāra nirdehān ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī dhanuḥ asya ācchinat citram hasta āvāpam ca vīryavān ratham ca śakalīkartum savyasācī pracakrame duryodhanam ca bāṇābhyām tīkṣṇābhyām virathīkṛtam tam kṛcchrām āpadam prāptam dṛṣṭvā parama dhanvinaḥ samāpetuḥ parīpsantaḥ dhanaṃjaya śara arditam astra varṣeṇa mahatā jana oghaiḥ ca api saṃvṛtau tatra vyaṅgīkṛtāḥ petuḥ śataśas atha ratha dvipāḥ te hatāḥ hanyamānāḥ ca nyagṛhṇan tam ratha uttamam tatas arjunam vṛṣṇi vīraḥ tvaritaḥ vākyam abravīt tatas visphārya balavat gāṇḍīvam jaghnivān ripūn mahatā śara varṣeṇa tala śabdena ca arjunaḥ pāñcajanyam ca balavat dadhmau tāreṇa keśavaḥ niḥsattvāḥ ca sa sattvāḥ ca kṣitau petuḥ tadā janāḥ jayadrathasya goptāraḥ tatas kṣubdhāḥ saha anugāḥ te dṛṣṭvā sahasā pārtham goptāraḥ saindhavasya tu bāṇa śabda ravān ca ugrān vimiśrān śaṅkha nisvanaiḥ prāduścakruḥ mahātmānaḥ siṃhanāda ravān api tam śrutvā ninadam ghoram tāvakānām samutthitam tena śabdena mahatā pūritā iyam vasuṃdharā sa śailā sa arṇava dvīpā sa pātālā viśām pate sa śabdaḥ bharata śreṣṭha vyāpya sarvāḥ diśaḥ daśa tāvakāḥ rathinaḥ tatra dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau saṃrambham paramam prāptāḥ tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ atha kṛṣṇau mahābhāgau tāvakāḥ dṛśya daṃśitau saṃjayaḥ uvāca tāvakāḥ tu samīkṣya eva vṛṣṇi andhaka kuru uttamau dīpayantaḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ jvaladbhiḥ iva pāvakaiḥ rukma pṛṣṭhaiḥ ca duṣprekṣyaiḥ kārmukaiḥ pṛthivīpate bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ karṇaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ jayadrathaḥ kṛpaḥ ca madra rājaḥ ca drauṇiḥ ca rathinām varaḥ te pibantaḥ iva ākāśam aśvaiḥ aṣṭau mahā rathāḥ te daṃśitāḥ su saṃrabdhāḥ rathaiḥ megha ogha nisvanaiḥ samāvṛṇvan diśaḥ sarvāḥ pārtham ca viśikhaiḥ śitaiḥ kaulūtakāḥ hayāḥ citrāḥ vahantaḥ tān mahā rathān vyaśobhanta tadā śīghrāḥ dīpayantaḥ diśaḥ daśa ājāneyaiḥ mahā vegaiḥ nānā deśa samutthitaiḥ kuru yodha varāḥ rājan tava putram parīpsavaḥ dhanaṃjaya ratham śīghram sarvatas samupādravan te pragṛhya mahā śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ puruṣa sattamāḥ pūrayantaḥ divam rājan pṛthivīm ca sa sāgarām devadattam ca kaunteyaḥ pāñcajanyam ca keśavaḥ pṛthivīm ca antarikṣam ca diśaḥ ca eva samāvṛṇot sarva śabdān atikramya pūrayām āsa rodasī tasmin tathā vartamāne dāruṇe nāda saṃkule bhīrūṇām trāsa janane śūrāṇām harṣa vardhane pravāditāsu bherīṣu jharjhareṣu ānakeṣu ca mṛdaṅgeṣu ca rāja indra vādyamāneṣu anekaśas mahā ratha samākhyātāḥ duryodhana hita eṣiṇaḥ amṛṣyamāṇāḥ tam śabdam kruddhāḥ parama dhanvinaḥ nānādeśyāḥ mahīpālāḥ sva sainya parirakṣiṇaḥ amarṣitāḥ mahā śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ vīrāḥ mahā rathāḥ tat prayuktam iva ākāśam śūraiḥ śaṅkha nināditam sa śabdaḥ su mahān rājan diśaḥ sarvāḥ vyanādayat trāsayām āsa tat sainyam yugānte iva saṃbhṛtaḥ tatas duryodhanaḥ aṣṭau ca rājānaḥ te mahā rathāḥ jayadrathasya rakṣā artham pāṇḍavam paryavārayan tam arjunaḥ pṛṣatkānām śataiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ atāḍayat karṇam dvādaśabhiḥ viddhvā vṛṣasenam tribhiḥ tathā śalyasya sa śaram cāpam muṣṭau ciccheda vīryavān gṛhītvā dhanuḥ anyat tu śalyaḥ vivyādha pāṇḍavam bhūriśravāḥ tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ hema puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ karṇaḥ dvātriṃśatā ca eva vṛṣasenaḥ ca pañcabhiḥ jayadrathaḥ trisaptatyā kṛpaḥ ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas śarāṇām ṣaṣṭyā tu drauṇiḥ pārtham avākirat vāsudevam ca saptatyā punar pārtham ca pañcabhiḥ prahasan tu nara vyāghraḥ śveta aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ karṇam dvādaśabhiḥ viddhvā vṛṣasenam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ śalyasya samare cāpam muṣṭideśe nyakṛntata saumadattim tribhiḥ viddhvā śalyam ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ śitaiḥ agni śikhā ākāraiḥ drauṇim vivyādha ca aṣṭabhiḥ gautamam pañcaviṃśatyā śaindhavam ca śatena ha punar drauṇim ca saptatyā śarāṇām saḥ abhyatāḍayat bhūriśravāḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ pratodam cicchide hareḥ arjunam ca trisaptatyā bāṇānām ājaghāna ha tatas śara śataiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ tān arīn śvetavāhanaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca dhvajān bahuvidha ākārān bhrājamānān ati śriyā pārthānām māmakānām ca tān mama ācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca dhvajān bahuvidha ākārān śṛṇu teṣām mahātmanām teṣām tu ratha muhyānām ratheṣu vividhāḥ dhvajāḥ pratyadṛśyanta rāja indra jvalitāḥ iva pāvakāḥ kāñcanāḥ kāñcana āpīḍāḥ kāñcana sraj alaṃkṛtāḥ kāñcanāni iva śṛṅgāṇi kāñcanasya mahā gireḥ te dhvajāḥ saṃvṛtāḥ teṣām patākābhiḥ samantataḥ nānā varṇa virāgābhiḥ vibabhuḥ sarvatas vṛtāḥ patākāḥ ca tatas tāḥ tu śvasanena samīritāḥ nṛtyamānāḥ vyadṛśyanta raṅga madhye vilāsikāḥ indrāyudha savarṇa ābhāḥ patākāḥ bharata ṛṣabha dodhūyamānāḥ rathinām śobhayanti mahā rathān siṃha lāṅgūlam ugra āsyam dhajam vānara lakṣaṇam sa vānara varaḥ rājan patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ trāsayām āsa tat sainyam dhvajaḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ tathā eva siṃha lāṅgūlam droṇaputrasya bhārata nandanam kaurava indrāṇām drauṇeḥ lakṣaṇam ucchritam āhave kham mahā rāja dadṛśe pūrayan iva patākī kāñcana sragvī dhvajaḥ karṇasya saṃyuge ācāryasya ca pāṇḍūnām brāhmaṇasya yaśasvinaḥ go vṛṣaḥ gautamasya āsīt kṛpasya su pariṣkṛtaḥ sa tena bhrājate rājan go vṛṣeṇa mahā rathaḥ mayūraḥ vṛṣasenasya kāñcanaḥ maṇi ratnavān vyāhariṣyan iva atiṣṭhat senā agram api śobhayan yathā skandasya rāja indra mayūreṇa virājatā sauvarṇīm pratipaśyāma sītām apratimām śubhām sā sītā bhrājate tasya ratham āsthāya māriṣa sarva bīja virūḍhā iva yathā sītā śriyā vṛtā dhvaja agre alohita arka ābhaḥ hema jāla pariṣkṛtaḥ yathā devāsure yuddhe purā pūṣā sma śobhate saumadatteḥ punar yūpaḥ yajña śīlasya dhīmataḥ dhvajaḥ sūryaḥ iva ābhāti somaḥ ca atra pradṛśyate sa yūpaḥ kāñcanaḥ rājan saumadatteḥ virājate rājasūye makha śreṣṭhe yathā yūpaḥ samucchritaḥ ketuḥ kāñcana citra aṅgaiḥ mayūraiḥ upaśobhitaḥ sa ketuḥ śobhayām āsa sainyam te bharata ṛṣabha yathā śvetaḥ mahā nāgaḥ devarāja camūm tathā nāgaḥ maṇi mayaḥ rājñaḥ dhvajaḥ kanaka saṃvṛtaḥ kiṅkiṇī śata saṃhrādaḥ bhrājan citre ratha uttame vyabhrājata bhṛśam rājan putraḥ tava viśām pate dhvajena mahatā saṃkhye kurūṇām ṛṣabhaḥ tadā vyadīpayan te pṛtanām yuga anta āditya saṃnibhāḥ tatas citrāṇi śubhrāṇi su mahānti mahā rathāḥ kārmukāṇi ādaduḥ tūrṇam arjuna arthe paraṃtapāḥ tathā eva dhanuḥ āyacchat pārthaḥ śatru vināśanaḥ gāṇḍīvam divya karmā tat rājan durmantrite tava tava aparādhāt hi narāḥ nihatāḥ bahudhā yudhi nānā digbhyaḥ samāhūtāḥ sa hayāḥ sa ratha dvipāḥ teṣām āsīt vyatikṣepaḥ garjatām itaretaram duryodhana mukhānām ca pāṇḍūnām ṛṣabhasya ca tatra adbhutam param cakre kaunteyaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ aśobhata mahā bāhuḥ gāṇḍīvam vikṣipan dhanuḥ jigīṣuḥ tān nara vyāghrān jighāṃsuḥ ca jayadratham tatra arjunaḥ mahā rāja śaraiḥ muktaiḥ sahasraśas adṛśyān akarot yodhān tāvakān śatru tāpanaḥ tatas te api nara vyāghrāḥ pārtham sarve mahā rathāḥ adṛśyam samare cakruḥ sāyaka oghaiḥ samantataḥ saṃvṛte nara siṃhaiḥ taiḥ kurūṇām ṛṣabhe arjune dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca arjune saindhavam prāpte bhāradvājena saṃvṛtāḥ pāñcālāḥ kurubhiḥ sārdham kim akurvata saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca aparāhṇe mahā rāja saṃgrāme loma harṣaṇe pāñcālānām kurūṇām ca droṇe dyūtam avartata pāñcālāḥ hi jighāṃsantaḥ droṇam saṃhṛṣṭa cetasaḥ abhyavarṣanta garjantaḥ śara varṣāṇi māriṣa tatas su tumulaḥ teṣām saṃgrāmaḥ avartata adbhutaḥ pāñcālānām kurūṇām ca ghoraḥ devāsura upamaḥ sarve droṇa ratham prāpya pāñcālāḥ paṇḍavaiḥ saha tam abhyagāt bṛhatkṣatraḥ kekayānām mahā rathaḥ pravapan niśitān bāṇān mahā indra aśani saṃnibhān tam tu pratyudiyāt śīghram kṣemadhūrtiḥ mahā yaśāḥ vimuñcan niśitān bāṇān śataśas atha sahasraśas dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca cedīnām ṛṣabhaḥ ati bala uditaḥ tam āpatantam sahasā vyādita āsyam iva antakam vīradhanvā mahā iṣvāsaḥ tvaramāṇaḥ samabhyayāt yudhiṣṭhiram mahā rāja jigīṣum samavasthitam saha anīkam tatas droṇaḥ nyavārayata vīryavān nakulam kuśalam yuddhe parākrāntam parākramī sahadevam tathā āyāntam durmukhaḥ śatru karśanaḥ śaraiḥ aneka sāhasraiḥ samavākirat āśugaiḥ śaraiḥ su niśitaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ kampayan vai muhur muhur draupadeyān nara vyāghrān muñcataḥ sāyaka uttamān saṃrabdhān rathinām śreṣṭhān saumadattiḥ avārayat bhīmasenam tathā kruddham bhīma rūpaḥ bhayānakam pratyavārayat āyāntam ārṣyaśṛṅgiḥ mahā rathaḥ yādṛś eva purā vṛttam rāma rāvaṇayoḥ nṛpa tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ droṇam navatyā nata parvaṇām tam droṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā nijaghāna stanāntare roṣitaḥ bharata śreṣṭha kaunteyena yaśasvinā bhūyas eva tu viṃśatyā sāyakānām samācinot sa aśva sūta dhvajam droṇaḥ paśyatām sarva dhanvinām tān śarān droṇa muktān tu śara varṣeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ avārayata dharma ātmā darśayan pāṇi lāghavam athā enam chinna dhanvānam tvaramāṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ śaraiḥ aneka sāhasraiḥ purayām āsa sarvatas adṛśyam dṛśya rājānam bhāradvājasya sāyakaiḥ hṛtaḥ rājā iti rāja indra brāhmaṇena yaśasvinā sa kṛcchram paramam prāptaḥ dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tyaktvā tat kārmukam chinnam bhāradvājena saṃyuge tatas tān sāyakān sarvān droṇa muktān sahasraśas chittvā ca tān śarān rājā krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ śaktim jagrāha samare girīṇām api dāraṇīm svarṇa daṇḍām mahā ghorām aṣṭa ghaṇṭām bhaya āvahām samutkṣipya ca tām hṛṣṭaḥ nanāda balavat balī śaktim samudyatām dṛṣṭvā dharmarājena saṃyuge prajvālayantī gaganam diśaḥ ca vidiśaḥ tathā droṇa antikam anuprāptā dīpta āsyā pannagī yathā tām āpatantīm sahasā prekṣya droṇaḥ viśām pate tat astram bhasmasāt kṛtvā tām śaktim ghora darśanām jagāma syandanam tūrṇam pāṇḍavasya yaśasvinaḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā droṇa astram tat samudyatam aśāmayat mahā prājñaḥ brahmāstreṇa eva bhārata kṣurapreṇa ca tīkṣṇena ciccheda asya mahat dhanuḥ tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam droṇaḥ kṣatriya mardanaḥ gadām cikṣepa sahasā dharmaputrāya māriṣa tām āpatantīm sahasā gadām dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ gadām evā agrahīt kruddhaḥ cikṣepa ca paraṃtapaḥ saṃgharṣāt pāvakam muktvā sameyātām mahī tale tatas droṇaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ dharmarājasya māriṣa caturbhiḥ niśitaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ hayān jaghne śara uttamaiḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya yudhiṣṭhiraḥ viratham tam samālokya vyāyudham ca viśeṣataḥ muñcan iṣu gaṇān tīkṣṇān laghu hastaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ abhidudrāva rājānam siṃhaḥ mṛgam iva ulbaṇaḥ hā hā iti sahasā śabdaḥ pāṇḍūnām samajāyata hṛtaḥ rājā hṛtaḥ rājā bhāradvājena māriṣa iti āsīt su mahān śabdaḥ pāṇḍu sainyasya sarvatas apāyāt javanaiḥ aśvaiḥ kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca bṛhatkṣatram atha āyāntam kekayam dṛḍha vikramam kṣemadhūrtiḥ mahā rāja vivyādha urasi mārgaṇaiḥ bṛhatkṣatraḥ tu tam rājā navatyā nata parvaṇām athā enam chinna dhanvānam śareṇa nata parvaṇā vivyādha hṛdaye tūrṇam pravaram sarva dhanvinām vyaśva sūta dhvajam cakre kṣemadhūrtim mahā ratham jahāra nṛpateḥ kāyāt śiraḥ jvalita kuṇḍalam sa kirīṭam mahīm prāpya babhau jyotiḥ iva ambarāt tam nihatya raṇe hṛṣṭaḥ bṛhatkṣatraḥ mahā rathaḥ sahasā abhyapatat sainyam tāvakam pārtha kāraṇāt dhṛṣṭaketum atha āyāntam droṇa hetoḥ parākramī vīradhanvā mahā iṣvāsaḥ vārayām āsa bhārata mahā vane tīvra madau vāraṇau iva yūthapau giri gahvaram āsādya śārdūlau iva roṣitau yuyudhāte mahā vīryau paraspara jighāṃsayā tat yuddham āsīt tumulam prekṣaṇīyam viśām pate siddha cāraṇa saṃghānām vismaya adbhuta darśanam vīradhanvā tatas kruddhaḥ dhṛṣṭaketoḥ śarāsanam śaktim jagrāha vipulām rukma daṇḍām ayasmayīm tām tu śaktim mahā vīryām dorbhyām āyamya bhārata sa tayā vīra ghātinyā śaktyā tu abhihataḥ bhṛśam nirbhinna hṛdayaḥ tūrṇam nipapāta rathāt mahīm tasmin vinihate śūre trigartānām mahā rathe sahadeve tatas ṣaṣṭim sāyakān durmukhaḥ akṣipat nanāda ca mahā nādam tarjayan pāṇḍavam raṇe bhrātā bhrātaram āyāntam vivyādha prahasan iva tam raṇe
