rabhasam dṛṣṭvā saha devam mahā balam durmukhaḥ navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ tāḍayām āsa bhārata jaghāna caturaḥ vāhān caturbhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ hata aśvam tu ratham tyaktvā durmukhaḥ vimanāḥ tadā yathā dāśarathiḥ rāmaḥ kharam hatvā mahā balam hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt trigartānām janeśvara rāja putram hatam dṛṣṭvā niramitram mahā balam sātyakim vyāghradattaḥ tu śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ cakre adṛśyam sa aśva sūtam sa dhvajam pṛtanā antare tān nivārya śarān śūraḥ śaineyaḥ kṛtahasta vat sa aśva sūta dhvajam bāṇaiḥ vyāghradattam apātayat māgadhāḥ sarvatas yattāḥ yuyudhānam upādravan visṛjantaḥ śarān ca eva tomarān ca sahasraśas bhindipālān tathā prāsān mudgarān musalān api ayodhayan raṇe śūrāḥ sātvatam yuddha durmadam māgadhān dravataḥ dṛṣṭvā hata śeṣān samantataḥ nāśayitvā raṇe sainyam tvadīyam mādhava uttamaḥ vidhunvānaḥ dhanuḥ śreṣṭham vyabhrājata mahā yaśāḥ bhajyamānam balam rājan sātvatena mahātmanā na abhyavartata yuddhāya trāsitam dīrgha bāhunā tatas droṇaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ sahasā udvṛtya cakṣuṣī sātyakim satya karmāṇam svayam eva abhidudruve saṃjayaḥ uvāca draupadeyān mahā iṣvāsān saumadattiḥ mahā yaśāḥ te pīḍitāḥ bhṛśam tena raudreṇa sahasā vibho pramūḍhāḥ nā eva vividuḥ mṛdhe kṛtyam sma kim cana nākuliḥ tu śatānīkaḥ saumadattim nara ṛṣabham dvābhyām viddhvā anadat dhṛṣṭaḥ śarābhyām śatru tāpanaḥ sa tān prati mahā rāja cikṣipe pañca sāyakān ekaikam hṛdi ca ājaghne ekaikena mahā yaśāḥ tatas te bhrātaraḥ pañca śaraiḥ viddhāḥ mahātmanā parivārya rathaiḥ vīram vivyadhuḥ sāyakaiḥ bhṛśam ārjuniḥ tu hayān tasya caturbhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ nanāda balavat nādam vivyādha ca śitaiḥ śaraiḥ yaudhiṣṭhiraḥ dhvajam tasya chittvā bhūmau apātayat nākuliḥ ca aśva yantāram rathanīḍāt apāharat sāhadeviḥ tu tam jñātvā bhrātṛbhiḥ vimukhīkṛtam kṣurapreṇa śiraḥ rājan nicakarta mahā manāḥ bhrājayantam raṇa uddeśam bāla sūrya sama prabham saumadatteḥ śiraḥ dṛṣṭvā nipatat tat mahātmanaḥ yodhayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ lakṣmaṇam rāvaṇiḥ yathā saṃprayuddhau raṇe dṛṣṭvā tau ubhau nara rākṣasau vismayaḥ sarva bhūtānām praharṣaḥ ca abhavat tadā ārṣyaśṛṅgim tatas bhīmaḥ navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tat rakṣaḥ samare viddham kṛtvā nādam bhaya āvaham sa bhīmam pañcabhiḥ viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ bhīma anugān jaghāna āśu rathān triṃśat ariṃdamaḥ punar catuḥśatān hatvā bhīmam vivyādha patriṇā saḥ atividdhaḥ tadā bhīmaḥ rākṣasena mahā balaḥ pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām mārutiḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ vikṛṣya kārmukam ghoram bhāra sādhanam uttamam alambusam śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ ardayām āsa sarvatas sa viddhaḥ bahubhiḥ bāṇaiḥ nīlāñjana caya upamaḥ śuśubhe sarvatas rājan pradīptaḥ iva kiṃśukaḥ sa vadhyamānaḥ samare bhīma cāpa cyutaiḥ śaraiḥ smaran bhrātṛ vadham ca eva pāṇḍavena mahātmanā ghoram rūpam atho kṛtvā bhīmasenam abhāṣata tiṣṭha idānīm raṇe pārtha paśya me adya parākramam parokṣam mama tat vṛttam yat bhrātā me hataḥ tvayā mahātā śara varṣeṇa bhṛśam tam samavākirat bhīmaḥ tu samare rājan adṛśye rākṣase tadā ākāśam pūrayām āsa śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ sa vadhyamānaḥ bhīmena nimeṣāt ratham āsthitaḥ jagāma dharaṇīm kṣudraḥ kham ca eva sahasā agamat uccāvacāni rūpāṇi cakāra su bahūni ca uccāvacāḥ tathā vācaḥ vyājahāra samantataḥ tena pāṇḍava sainyānām mṛditāḥ yudhi vāraṇāḥ hayāḥ ca bahavaḥ rājan pattayaḥ ca tathā punar śoṇita udām ratha āvartām hasti grāha samākulām chatra haṃsām kardaminīm bāhu pannaga saṃkulām nadīm pravartayām āsa rakṣaḥ gaṇa samākulām vahantīm bahudhā rājan cedi pāñcāla sṛñjayān pāṇḍavāḥ bhṛśa saṃvignāḥ prāpaśyan tad sya vikramam tāvakānām tu sainyānām praharṣaḥ samajāyata vāditra ninadaḥ ca ugraḥ su mahān loma harṣaṇaḥ tam śrutvā ninadam ghoram tava sainyasya pāṇḍavaḥ na amṛṣyata yathā nāgaḥ tala śabdam samīritam tatas krodha abhitāmra akṣaḥ nirdahan iva pāvakaḥ saṃdadhe tvāṣṭram astram sa svayam tvaṣṭā iva māriṣa tatas śara sahasrāṇi prādurāsan samantataḥ rākṣasasya mahā māyām hatvā rākṣasam ārdayat sa vadhyamānaḥ bahudhā bhīmasenena rākṣasaḥ saṃtyajya saṃyuge bhīmam droṇa anīkam upādravat anādayan siṃhanādaiḥ pāṇḍavāḥ sarvatodiśam apūjayat mārutim ca saṃhṛṣṭāḥ te mahā balam prahrādam samare jitvā yathā śakram marut gaṇāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca haiḍimbaḥ prayayau tūrṇam vivyādha ca śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tayoḥ pratibhayam yuddham āsīt rākṣasa siṃhayoḥ kurvatoḥ vividhāḥ māyāḥ śakra śambarayoḥ iva alambusaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ ghaṭotkacam atāḍayat ghaṭotkacaḥ tu viṃśatyā nārācānām stanāntare viddhvā viddhvā anadat dhṛṣṭaḥ pūrayan kham samantataḥ tathā tau bhṛśa saṃkruddhau rākṣasa indrau mahā balau nirviśeṣam ayudhyetām māyābhiḥ itaretaram māyā yuddhe su kuśalau māyā yuddham ayudhyatām yām yām ghaṭotkacaḥ yuddhe māyām darśayate nṛpa tām tām alambusaḥ rājan māyayā eva nijaghnivān tam tathā yudhyamānam tu māyā yuddha viśāradam alambusam rākṣasa indram dṛṣṭvā akrudhyanta pāṇḍavāḥ te enam bhṛśa saṃkruddhāḥ sarvatas pravarāḥ rathaiḥ te enam koṣṭhakīkṛtya ratha vaṃśena māriṣa sa teṣām astra vegam tam pratihatya astra māyayā mārutim pañcaviṃśatyā bhaimasenim ca pañcabhiḥ nakulam ca trisaptatyā drupadeyān ca māriṣa pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ viddhvā ghoram nādam nanāda ha tam bhīmasenaḥ navabhiḥ sahadevaḥ ca pañcabhiḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śatena eva rākṣasam pratyavidhyata nakulaḥ ca catuḥṣaṣṭyā draupadeyāḥ tribhiḥ tribhiḥ haiḍimbaḥ rākṣasam viddhvā yuddhe pañcāśatā śaraiḥ prativivyādha tān sarvān pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ tam kruddham rākṣasam yuddhe pratikruddhaḥ tu rākṣasaḥ haiḍimbaḥ bharata śreṣṭha śaraiḥ vivyādha saptabhiḥ vyasṛjat sāyakān tūrṇam svarṇa puṅkhān śilā śitān te śarāḥ nata parvāṇaḥ viviśuḥ rākṣasam tadā ruṣitāḥ pannagāḥ yadvat girim ugrāḥ mahā balāḥ tatas te pāṇḍavāḥ rājan samantāt niśitān śarān preṣayām āsuḥ udvignāḥ haiḍimbaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ sa vadhyamānaḥ samare pāṇḍavaiḥ jita kāśibhiḥ dagdha adri kūṭa śṛṅga ābham bhinnāñjana caya upamam niṣpipeṣa kṣitau kṣipram pūrṇa kumbham iva aśmani sa visphuṭita sarva aṅgaḥ cūrṇita asthi vibhūṣaṇaḥ ghaṭotkacena vīreṇa hataḥ sāla kaṭaṅkaṭaḥ tatas sumanasaḥ pārthāḥ hate tasmin niśācare cukruśuḥ siṃhanādān ca vāsāṃsi ādudhuvuḥ ca ha tāvakāḥ ca hatam dṛṣṭvā rākṣasa indram mahā balam alambusam bhīma rūpam viśīrṇam iva parvatam janāḥ ca tat dadṛśire rakṣaḥ kautūhala anvitāḥ yadṛcchayā nipatitam bhūmau aṅgārakam yathā sa pūjyamānaḥ pitṛbhiḥ sa bāndhavaiḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ karmaṇi duṣkare kṛte tatas ninādaḥ su mahān samutthitaḥ sa śaṅkha nānāvidha bāṇa ghoṣavān dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca saṃjaya ācakṣva tattvena param kautūhalam hi me saṃjayaḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan mahā prājña saṃgrāmam loma harṣaṇam droṇasya pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham yuyudhāna purogamaiḥ vadhyamānam balam dṛṣṭvā yuyudhānena māriṣa tam āpatantam sahasā bhāradvājam mahā ratham sātyakiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām samārpayat droṇaḥ api yudhi vikrāntaḥ yuyudhānam samāhitaḥ avidhyat pañcabhiḥ tūrṇam hema puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ te varma bhittvā su dṛḍham dviṣat piśita bhojanāḥ abhyaguḥ dharaṇīm rājan śvasantaḥ iva pannagāḥ droṇam pañcāśatā avidhyat nārācaiḥ agni saṃnibhaiḥ tatas kruddhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ bhūyas eva mahā balaḥ sātvatam pīḍayām āsa śatena nata parvaṇā sa vadhyamānaḥ samare bhāradvājena sātyakiḥ na abhyapadyata kartavyam kim cit eva viśām pate viṣaṇṇa vadanaḥ ca api yuyudhānaḥ abhavat nṛpa bhāradvājam raṇe dṛṣṭvā visṛjantam śitān śarān tam tu saṃprekṣya te putrāḥ sainikāḥ ca viśām pate prahṛṣṭa manasaḥ bhūtvā siṃha vat vyanadan muhur tam śrutvā ninadam ghoram pīḍyamānam ca mādhavam eṣa vṛṣṇi varaḥ vīraḥ sātyakiḥ satya karma kṛt grasyate yudhi vīreṇa bhānumān iva rāhuṇā dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca pāñcālyam idam āha janādhipa abhidrava drutam droṇam kim nu tiṣṭhasi pārṣata krīḍate sūtra baddhena pakṣiṇā bālakaḥ yathā pṛṣṭhatas anugamiṣyāmi tvām aham saha sainikaḥ sātyakim mokṣayasva adya yama daṃṣṭra antaram gatam evam uktvā tatas rājā sarva sainyena pāṇḍavaḥ abhyadravat raṇe droṇam yuyudhānasya kāraṇāt tatra ārāvaḥ mahān āsīt droṇam ekam yuyutsatām pāṇḍavānām ca bhadram te sṛñjayānām ca sarvaśas abhyavarṣan śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅka barhiṇa vājitaiḥ ātitheya gṛham prāpya nṛpate atithayaḥ yathā bhāradvājam ca te sarve na śekuḥ prativīkṣitum tān tu sarvān mahā iṣvāsān droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ vadhyamānāḥ raṇe rājan pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayāḥ tathā trātāram na adhyagacchanta paṅka magnāḥ iva dvipāḥ droṇasya ca vyadṛśyanta visarpantaḥ mahā śarāḥ tasmin droṇena nihatāḥ pāñcālāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ mahā ratha samākhyātāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃmatāḥ pāṇḍūnām sarva sainyeṣu pāñcālānām tathā eva ca droṇam sma dadṛśuḥ śūram vinighnantam varān varān kekayānām śatam hatvā vidrāvya ca samantataḥ droṇaḥ tasthau mahā rāja vyādita āsyaḥ iva antakaḥ pāñcālān sṛñjayān matsyān kekayān pāṇḍavān api droṇaḥ ajayat mahā bāhuḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas teṣām samabhavat śabdaḥ vadhyatām droṇa sāyakaiḥ vanaukasām iva araṇye dahyatām dhūmaketunā tatra devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ pitaraḥ ca bruvan nṛpa ete dravanti pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca sa sainikāḥ tam tathā samare droṇam nighnantam somakān raṇe aśṛṇot sahasā pārthaḥ pāñcajanyasya nisvanam pūritaḥ vāsudevena śaṅkha rāj svanate bhṛśam yudhyamāneṣu vīreṣu saindhavasya abhirakṣiṣu gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣe vipranaṣṭe samantataḥ kaśmala abhihataḥ rājā cintayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ na nūnam svasti pārthasya yathā nadati śaṅkha rāj kauravāḥ ca yathā hṛṣṭāḥ vinadanti muhur muhur evam saṃcintayitvā tu vyākulena antarātmanā ajātaśatruḥ kaunteyaḥ sātvatam pratyabhāṣata bāṣpa gadgadayā vācā muhyamānaḥ muhur muhur kṛtyasya anantara apekṣī śaineyam śini puṃgavam yaḥ sa dharmaḥ purā dṛṣṭaḥ sadbhiḥ śaineya śāśvataḥ sāṃparāye suhṛd kṛtye tasya kālaḥ ayam āgataḥ tvattaḥ suhṛttamam kam cit na abhijānāmi sātyake yathā ca keśavaḥ nityam pāṇḍavānām parāyaṇam tathā tvam api vārṣṇeya kṛṣṇa tulya parākramaḥ saḥ aham bhāram samādhāsye tvayi tam voḍhum arhasi tvam hi satya vrataḥ śūraḥ mitrāṇām abhayaṃkaraḥ pṛthivīm vā dvijātibhyaḥ yaḥ dadyāt samam eva tat śrutāḥ ca bahavaḥ asmābhiḥ rājānaḥ ye divam gatāḥ dattvā imām pṛthivīm kṛtsnām brāhmaṇebhyaḥ yathāvidhi evam tvām api dharma ātman prayāce aham kṛtāñjaliḥ pṛthivī dāna tulyam syāt adhikam vā phalam vibho ekaḥ eva sadā kṛṣṇaḥ mitrāṇām abhayaṃkaraḥ raṇe saṃtyajati prāṇān dvitīyaḥ tvam ca sātyake śūraḥ eva sahāyaḥ syāt na itaraḥ prākṛtaḥ janaḥ īdṛśe tu parāmarde vartamānasya mādhava ślāghan eva hi karmāṇi śataśas tava pāṇḍavaḥ mahā balaḥ mahā vīryaḥ sa mahātmā mahā rathaḥ śiṣyaḥ mama sakhā ca eva priyaḥ asya aham priyaḥ ca me rāmaḥ vā api aniruddhaḥ vā pradyumnaḥ vā mahā rathaḥ gadaḥ vā sāraṇaḥ vā api sāmbaḥ vā saha vṛṣṇibhiḥ sahāya artham mahā rāja saṃgrāma uttama mūrdhani sāhāyye viniyokṣyāmi nā asti me anyaḥ hi tad samaḥ parokṣam tvad guṇān tathyān kathayan ārya saṃsadi yat ca api tīrthāni caran agaccham dvārakām prati tatra aham api te bhaktim arjunam prati dṛṣṭavān pūrvam eva tu yātāḥ te kauravāṇām mahā rathāḥ bhīmasenaḥ vayam ca eva saṃyattāḥ saha sainikāḥ droṇam āvārayiṣyāmaḥ yadi tvām prati yāsyati paśya śaineya sainyāni dravamāṇāni saṃyuge mahāntam ca raṇe śabdam dīryamāṇām ca bhāratīm dhārtarāṣṭra balam tāta vikṣiptam savyasācinā atyanta apacitaiḥ śūraiḥ phalgunaḥ para vīra hā paśya etat dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām anīkam su durāsadam śṛṇu dundubhi nirghoṣam śaṅkha śabdān ca puṣkalān siṃhanāda ravān ca eva ratha nemi svanān tathā nāgānām śṛṇu śabdam ca pattīnām ca sahasraśas sādinām dravatām ca eva śṛṇu kampayatām mahīm purastāt saindhava anīkam droṇa anīkasya pṛṣṭhatas tasmin ca nihate yuddhe katham jīveta mādṛśaḥ śyāmaḥ yuvā guḍākeśaḥ darśanīyaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ laghu astraḥ citra yodhī ca praviṣṭaḥ tāta bhāratīm tat na jānāmi vārṣṇeya yadi jīvati vā na vā kurūṇām ca api tat sainyam sāgara pratimam mahat ekaḥ eva ca bībhatsuḥ praviṣṭaḥ tāta bhāratīm aviṣahyām mahā bāhuḥ suraiḥ api mahā mṛdhe pratyakṣam te mahā bāho yathā asau carati dvijaḥ yugapad ca sametānām kāryāṇām tvam vicakṣaṇaḥ na aham śocāmi dāśārham goptāram jagataḥ prabhum sa hi śaktaḥ raṇe tāta trīn lokān api saṃgatān prajahyāt samare prāṇān tasmāt vindāmi kaśmalam tasya tvam padavīm gaccha gaccheyuḥ tvādṛśāḥ yathā tādṛśasya īdṛśe kāle mādṛśena abhicoditaḥ raṇe vṛṣṇi pravīrāṇām dvau eva atirathau smṛtau pradyumnaḥ ca mahā bāhuḥ tvam ca sātvata viśrutaḥ astre nārāyaṇa samaḥ saṃkarṣaṇa samaḥ bale vīra tāyām nara vyāghra dhanaṃjaya samaḥ hi asi tat tvām yat abhivakṣyāmi tat kuruṣva mahā bala na anyathā tām mahā bāho saṃprakartum iha arhasi parityajya priyān prāṇān raṇe vicara vīra vat na hi śaineya dāśārhāḥ raṇe rakṣanti jīvitam bhīrūṇām asatām mārgaḥ nā eṣa dāśārha sevitaḥ tava arjunaḥ guruḥ tāta dharma ātmā śini puṃgava vāsudevaḥ guruḥ ca api tava pārthasya dhīmataḥ praviśa etat balam tāta dhārtarāṣṭrasya durmateḥ praviśya ca yathānyāyam saṃgamya ca mahā rathaiḥ yathārham ātmanaḥ karma raṇe sātvata darśaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca prīti yuktam ca hṛdyam ca madhura akṣaram eva ca kāla yuktam ca citram ca svatayā ca abhibhāṣitam dharmarājasya tat vākyam niśamya śini puṃgavaḥ sātyakiḥ bharata śreṣṭha pratyuvāca yudhiṣṭhiram evaṃvidhe tathā kāle madṛśam prekṣya saṃmatam na me dhanaṃjayasya arthe prāṇāḥ rakṣyāḥ katham cana kuśalī aham kuśalinam samāsādya dhanaṃjayam avaśyam tu mayā sarvam vijñāpyaḥ tvam narādhipa dṛḍham tu abhiparītaḥ aham arjunena punar punar āryām yuddhe matim kṛtvā yāvat dhanmi jayadratham tvayi vā aham mahā bāho pradyumne vā mahā rathe jānīṣe hi raṇe droṇam rabhasam śreṣṭha saṃmatam pratijñā ca api te nityam śrutā droṇasya mādhava śaktaḥ ca api raṇe droṇaḥ nigṛhītum yudhiṣṭhiram dharmarājam yathā droṇaḥ nigṛhṇīyāt raṇe balāt nigṛhīte nara śreṣṭhe bhāradvājena mādhava evam gate nara śreṣṭha pāṇḍave satya vādini yadi droṇaḥ raṇe kruddhaḥ nigṛhṇīyāt yudhiṣṭhiram jaya artham ca yaśaḥ artham ca rakṣa rājānam āhave sa bhavān mayi nikṣepaḥ nikṣiptaḥ savyasācinā bhāradvājāt bhayam nityam paśyamānena te prabho tasya api ca mahā bāho nityam paśyati saṃyuge na anyam hi pratiyoddhāram raukmiṇeyāt ṛte prabho mām vā api manyate yuddhe bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥ saḥ aham saṃbhāvanām ca etām ācārya vacanam ca tat pṛṣṭhatas nā utsahe kartum tvām vā tyaktum mahīpate ācāryaḥ laghu hasta tvāt abhedya kavaca āvṛtaḥ upalabhya raṇe krīḍet yathā śakuninā śiśuḥ yadi kārṣṇiḥ dhanuṣpāṇiḥ iha syāt makara dhvajaḥ tasmai tvām visṛjeyam vai sa tvām rakṣet yathā arjunaḥ yaḥ pratīyāt raṇe droṇam yāvat gacchāmi pāṇḍavam udīcyāḥ dākṣiṇātyāḥ ca ye ca anye api mahā rathāḥ ye ca karṇa mukhāḥ rājan ratha udārāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ete arjunasya kruddhasya kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm udyuktā pṛthivī sarvā sa sura asura mānuṣā sa rākṣasa gaṇā rājan sa kiṃnara mahā uragā jaṅgamāḥ sthāvaraiḥ sārdham na alam pārthasya saṃyuge evam jñātvā mahā rāja vyetu te bhīḥ dhanaṃjaye yatra vīrau mahā iṣvāsau kṛṣṇau satya parākramau daivam kṛtāstra tām yogam amarṣam api ca āhave kṛtajña tām dayām ca eva bhrātuḥ tvam anucintaya droṇe citra astra tām saṃkhye rājan tvam anucintaya ācāryaḥ hi bhṛśam rājan nigrahe tava gṛdhyati pratijñām ātmanaḥ rakṣan satyām kartum ca bhārata na hi aham tvā mahā rāja a nikṣipya mahā āhave dṛṣṭvā śreyaḥ param buddhyā tatas rājan praśādhi mām yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca na tu me śudhyate bhāvaḥ śvetāśvam prati māriṣa kariṣye paramam yatnam ātmanaḥ rakṣaṇam prati ātma saṃrakṣaṇam saṃkhye gamanam ca arjunam prati sa tvam ātiṣṭha yānāya yatra yātaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ mama api rakṣaṇam bhīmaḥ kariṣyati mahā balaḥ pārṣataḥ ca sa sodaryaḥ pārthivāḥ ca mahā balāḥ draupadeyāḥ ca mām tāta rakṣiṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ kekayāḥ bhrātaraḥ pañca rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ virāṭaḥ drupadaḥ ca eva śikhaṇḍī ca mahā rathaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca balavān kuntibhojaḥ ca māriṣa nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāḥ tathā ete samāhitāḥ tāta rakṣiṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ samāsādayitum śaktaḥ na ca mām dharṣayiṣyati dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca samare droṇam kruddham paraṃtapaḥ yatra sthāsyati saṃgrāme pārṣataḥ para vīra hā eṣa droṇa vināśāya samutpannaḥ hutāśanāt kavacī sa śarī khaḍgī dhanvī ca vara bhūṣaṇaḥ viśrabdhaḥ gaccha śaineya mā kārṣīḥ mayi saṃbhramam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ raṇe kruddhaḥ droṇam āvārayiṣyati saṃjayaḥ uvāca dharmarājasya tat vākyam niśamya śini puṃgavaḥ pārthāt ca bhayam āśaṅkan parityāgāt mahīpateḥ apavādam hi ātmanaḥ ca lokāt rakṣan viśeṣataḥ na mām bhīta iti brūyuḥ āyāntam phalgunam prati dharmarājam idam vākyam abravīt puruṣa ṛṣabha kṛtām ced manyase rakṣām svasti te astu viśām pate anuyāsyāmi bībhatsum kariṣye vacanam tava na hi me pāṇḍavāt kaḥ cit triṣu lokeṣu vidyate tasya aham padavīm yāsye saṃdeśāt tava mānada yathā hi me guroḥ vākyam viśiṣṭam dvipadām vara tathā tava api vacanam viśiṣṭataram eva me priye hi tava vartete bhrātarau kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau tava ājñām śirasā gṛhya pāṇḍava artham aham prabho droṇa anīkam viśāmi eṣa kruddhaḥ jhaṣaḥ iva arṇavam tatra yāsyāmi yatra asau rājan rājā jayadrathaḥ yatra senām samāśritya bhītaḥ tiṣṭhati pāṇḍavāt guptaḥ ratha vara śreṣṭhaiḥ drauṇi karṇa kṛpa ādibhiḥ itas tri yojanam manye tam adhvānam viśām pate ā saindhava vadhāt rājan su dṛḍhena antarātmanā an ādiṣṭaḥ tu guruṇā kaḥ nu yudhyeta mānavaḥ ādiṣṭaḥ tu tvayā rājan kaḥ na yudhyeta mādṛśaḥ abhijānāmi tam deśam yatra yāsyāmi aham prabho huḍa śakti gadā prāsa khaḍga carma ṛṣṭi tomaram iṣvastra vara saṃbādham kṣobhayiṣye bala arṇavam yat etat kuñjara anīkam sāhasram anupaśyasi kulam añjanakam nāma yatra ete vīrya śālinaḥ āsthitāḥ bahubhiḥ mlecchaiḥ yuddha śauṇḍaiḥ prahāribhiḥ nāgāḥ megha nibhāḥ rājan kṣarantaḥ iva toyadāḥ anyatra hi vadhāt eṣām na asti rājan parājayaḥ ete rukmarathāḥ nāma rāja putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ ratheṣu astreṣu nipuṇāḥ nāgeṣu ca viśām pate dhanurvede gatāḥ pāram muṣṭi yuddhe ca kovidāḥ gadā yuddha viśeṣa jñāḥ niyuddha kuśalāḥ tathā khaḍga praharaṇe yuktāḥ saṃpāte ca asi carmaṇoḥ śūrāḥ ca kṛtavidyāḥ ca spardhante ca parasparam nityam ca samare rājan vijigīṣanti mānavān karṇena vijitāḥ rājan duḥśāsanam anuvratāḥ etān tu vāsudevaḥ api ratha udārān praśaṃsati satatam priya kāmāḥ ca karṇasya ete vaśe sthitāḥ tasya eva vacanāt rājan nivṛttāḥ śvetavāhanāt te na kṣatāḥ na ca śrāntāḥ dṛḍha āvaraṇa kārmukāḥ mad artham viṣṭhitāḥ nūnam dhārtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt prayāsyāmi tatas paścāt padavīm savyasācinaḥ yān tu etān aparān rājan nāgān saptaśatāni ca prekṣase varma saṃchannān kirātaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitān kirāta rājaḥ yān prādāt gṛhītaḥ savyasācinā su alaṃkṛtān tathā preṣyān icchan jīvitam ātmanaḥ āsan ete purā rājan tava karmakarāḥ dṛḍham teṣām ete mahāmātrāḥ kirātāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ hasti śikṣā vidaḥ ca eva sarve ca eva agni yonayaḥ ete vinirjitāḥ sarve saṃgrāme savyasācinā mad artham adya saṃyattāḥ duryodhana vaśa anugāḥ etān bhittvā śaraiḥ rājan kirātān yuddha durmadān ye tu ete su mahā nāgāḥ añjanasya kula udbhavāḥ karkaśāḥ ca vinītāḥ ca prabhinna karaṭāmukhāḥ jāmbūnada mayaiḥ sarvaiḥ varmabhiḥ su vibhūṣitāḥ labdha lakṣyāḥ raṇe rājan airāvaṇa samāḥ yudhi uttarāt parvatāt ete tīkṣṇaiḥ dasyubhiḥ āsthitāḥ karkaśaiḥ pravaraiḥ yodhaiḥ kārṣṇāyasa tanucchadaiḥ aneka yonayaḥ ca anye tathā mānuṣa yonayaḥ mlecchānām pāpa kartṝṇām himavat durga vāsinām kṛpam ca saumadattim ca droṇam ca rathinām varam sindhurājam tathā karṇam avamanyata pāṇḍavān kṛtārtham atha ca ātmānam manyate kāla coditaḥ tena saṃbhāvitā nityam para vīrya upajīvinā vināśam upayāsyanti mad śara ogha nipīḍitāḥ ye tu ete rathinaḥ rājan dṛśyante kāñcana dhvajāḥ ete durvāraṇāḥ nāma kāmbojāḥ yadi te śrutāḥ śūrāḥ ca kṛtavidyāḥ ca dhanurvede ca niṣṭhitāḥ saṃhatāḥ ca bhṛśam hi ete anyonyasya hita eṣiṇaḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ ca saṃrabdhāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrasya bhārata yattāḥ mad artham tiṣṭhanti kuru vīra abhirakṣitāḥ apramattāḥ mahā rāja mām eva pratyupasthitāḥ tān tu aham pramathiṣyāmi tṛṇāni iva hutāśanaḥ tasmāt sarvān upāsaṅgān sarva upakaraṇāni ca yathā upadiṣṭam ācāryaiḥ kāryaḥ pañcaguṇaḥ rathaḥ kāmbojaiḥ hi sameṣyāmi kruddhaiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ nānā śastra samāvāpaiḥ vividha āyudha yodhibhiḥ kirātaiḥ ca sameṣyāmi viṣa kalpaiḥ prahāribhiḥ lālitaiḥ satatam rājñā duryodhana hita eṣibhiḥ śakaiḥ ca api sameṣyāmi śakra tulya parākramaiḥ tasmāt vai vājinaḥ mukhyāḥ viśrāntāḥ śubha lakṣaṇāḥ upāvṛttāḥ ca pītāḥ ca punar yujyantu me rathe tasya sarvān upāsaṅgān sarva upakaraṇāni ca rathe prāsthāpayat rājā śastrāṇi vividhāni ca tatas tān sarvatas muktvā sat aśvān caturaḥ janāḥ rasavat pāyayām āsuḥ pānam mada samīriṇam pīta upavṛttān snātān ca jagdha annān samalaṃkṛtān vinīta śalyān turagān caturaḥ hema mālinaḥ tān yattān rukma varṇa ābhān vinītān śīghra gāminaḥ pāṇḍura abhra prakāśābhiḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛte yojayām āsa vidhivat hema bhāṇḍa vibhūṣitān dārukasya anujaḥ bhrātā sūtaḥ tasya priyaḥ sakhā tatas snātaḥ śuciḥ bhūtvā kṛta kautukamaṅgalaḥ snātakānām sahasrasya svarṇa niṣkān adāpayat āśīrvādaiḥ pariṣvaktaḥ sātyakiḥ śrīmatām varaḥ tatas sa madhuparka arhaḥ pītvā kailāvatam madhu ālabhya vīra kāṃsyam ca harṣeṇa mahatā anvitaḥ dviguṇīkṛta tejāḥ hi prajvalan iva pāvakaḥ utsaṅge dhanuḥ ādāya sa śaram rathinām varaḥ kṛta svastyayanaḥ vipraiḥ kavacī samalaṃkṛtaḥ lājaiḥ gandhaiḥ tathā mālyaiḥ kanyābhiḥ ca abhinanditaḥ yudhiṣṭhirasya caraṇau abhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ tatas te vājinaḥ hṛṣṭāḥ su puṣṭāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ atha harṣa parīta aṅgaḥ sātyakiḥ bhīmam abravīt tvam bhīma rakṣa rājānam etat kāryatamam hi te āyatyām ca tadātve ca śreyaḥ rājñaḥ abhirakṣaṇam jānīṣe mama vīryam tvam tava ca aham ariṃdama aham rājñaḥ kariṣyāmi rakṣām puruṣa sattama evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca bhīmasenam sa mādhavaḥ nihate saindhave pāpe pāṇḍavena mahātmanā pariṣvajiṣye rājānam dharma ātmānam na saṃśayaḥ etāvat uktvā bhīmam tu visṛjya ca mahāmanāḥ saṃpraikṣat tāvakam sainyam vyāghraḥ mṛga gaṇān iva tam dṛṣṭvā pravivikṣantam sainyam tava janādhipa bhūyas evā bhavat mūḍham su bhṛśam ca api akampata tatas prayātaḥ sahasā sainyam tava sa sātyakiḥ didṛkṣuḥ arjunam rājan dharmarājasya śāsanāt saṃjayaḥ uvāca dharmarājaḥ mahā rāja svena anīkena saṃvṛtaḥ prāyāt droṇa ratha prepsuḥ yuyudhānasya pṛṣṭhatas tatas pāñcāla rājasya putraḥ samara durmadaḥ prākrośat pāṇḍava anīke vasudānaḥ ca pārthivaḥ tatas śabdaḥ mahān āsīt yuyudhāna ratham prati sātvatena mahā rāja śatadhā abhivyadīryata tasyām vidīryamāṇāyām śineḥ pautraḥ mahā rathaḥ sapta vīrān mahā iṣvāsān agra anīke vyapothayat te bhītāḥ mṛdyamānāḥ ca pramṛṣṭāḥ dīrgha bāhunā āyodhanam jahuḥ vīrāḥ dṛṣṭvā tam ati mānuṣam rathaiḥ vimathita akṣaiḥ ca bhagna nīḍaiḥ ca māriṣa anukarṣaiḥ patākābhiḥ śirastrāṇaiḥ sa kāñcanaiḥ bāhubhiḥ candana ādigdhaiḥ sa aṅgadaiḥ ca viśām pate ūrubhiḥ pṛthivī channā manujānām nara uttama śaśāṅka saṃnikāśaiḥ ca vadanaiḥ cāru kuṇḍalaiḥ patitaiḥ vṛṣabha akṣāṇām babhau bhārata medinī gajaiḥ ca bahudhā chinnaiḥ śayānaiḥ parvata upamaiḥ rarāja atibhṛśam bhūmiḥ vikīrṇaiḥ iva parvataiḥ gatasattvāḥ mahīm prāpya pramṛṣṭāḥ dīrgha bāhunā nānāvidhāni sainyāni tava hatvā tu sātvataḥ praviṣṭaḥ tāvakam sainyam drāvayitvā camūm bhṛśam iyeṣa sātyakiḥ gantum tatas droṇena vāritaḥ bharadvājam samāsādya yuyudhānaḥ tu māriṣa na abhyavartata saṃkruddhaḥ velām iva jalāśayaḥ nivārya tu raṇe droṇaḥ yuyudhānam mahā ratham vivyādha niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pañcabhiḥ marma bhedibhiḥ sātyakiḥ tu raṇe droṇam rājan vivyādha saptabhiḥ hema puṅkhaiḥ śilā dhautaiḥ kaṅka barhiṇa vājitaiḥ tam ṣaḍbhiḥ sāyakaiḥ droṇaḥ sa aśva yantāram ārdayat sa tam na mamṛṣe droṇam yuyudhānaḥ mahā rathaḥ siṃhanādam tatas kṛtvā droṇam vivyādha sātyakiḥ daśabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ eva ca yuyudhānaḥ punar droṇam vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ tam droṇaḥ sa aśva yantāram sa ratha dhvajam āśugaiḥ tvaran prācchādayat bāṇaiḥ śalabhānām iva vrajaiḥ tathā eva yuyudhānaḥ api droṇam bahubhiḥ āśugaiḥ prācchādayat asaṃbhrāntaḥ tatas droṇaḥ uvāca ha tava ācāryaḥ raṇam hitvā gataḥ kāpuruṣaḥ yathā yudhyamānam hi mām hitvā pradakṣiṇam avartata yadi mām tvam raṇe hitvā na yāsi ācārya vat drutam sātyakiḥ uvāca dhanaṃjayasya padavīm dharmarājasya śāsanāt saṃjayaḥ uvāca etāvat uktvā śaineyaḥ ācāryam parivarjayan prayātaḥ sahasā rājan sārathim ca idam abravīt droṇaḥ kariṣyate yatnam sarvathā mama vāraṇe yattaḥ yāhi raṇe sūta śṛṇu ca idam vacaḥ param etat ālokyate sainyam āvantyānām mahā prabham asya anantaratas tu etat dākṣiṇātyam mahā balam bāhlika abhyāśataḥ yuktam karṇasya api mahat balam etat antaram āsādya codaya aśvān prahṛṣṭa vat bāhlikāḥ yatra dṛśyante nānā praharaṇa udyatāḥ dākṣiṇātyāḥ ca bahavaḥ sūtaputra purogamāḥ hasti aśva ratha saṃbādham yat ca anīkam vilokyate nānā deśa samutthaiḥ ca padātibhiḥ adhiṣṭhitam etāvat uktvā yantāram brahmāṇam parivarjayan prāviśat bhāratīm senām aparyantām sa sātyakiḥ amarṣī kṛtavarmā tu sātyakim paryavārayat tam āpatantam viśikhaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ āhatya sātyakiḥ caturbhiḥ caturaḥ asya aśvān ājaghāna āśu vīryavān tatas punar ṣoḍaśabhiḥ nata parvabhiḥ āśugaiḥ sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇam pratyavidhyat stanāntare sātvatena mahā rāja kṛtavarmā na cakṣame ākṛṣya rājan ākarṇāt vivyādha urasi sātyakim sa tasya deha āvaraṇam bhittvā deham ca sāyakaḥ sa patra puṅkhaḥ pṛthivīm viveśa rudhira ukṣitaḥ sa mārgaṇa guṇam rājan kṛtavarmā śarāsanam tatas praśīrṇe dhanuṣi śaktyā śaktimatām varaḥ abhyahan dakṣiṇam bāhum sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmaṇaḥ tatas anyat su dṛḍham vīraḥ dhanuḥ ādāya sātyakiḥ vyasṛjat viśikhān tūrṇam śataśas atha sahasraśas sa ratham kṛtavarmāṇam samantāt paryavākirat chādayitvā raṇe atyartham hārdikyam tu sa sātyakiḥ atha asya bhallena śiraḥ sāratheḥ samakṛntata sa papāta hataḥ sūtaḥ hārdikyasya mahā rathāt sātyakiḥ ca abhyagāt tasmāt sa tu bhīmam upādravat yuyudhānaḥ api rāja indra droṇa anīkāt viniḥsṛtaḥ prayayau tvaritaḥ tūrṇam kāmbojānām mahā camūm sa tatra bahubhiḥ śūraiḥ saṃniruddhaḥ mahā rathaiḥ na cacāla tadā rājan sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ saṃdhāya ca camūm droṇaḥ bhoje bhāram niveśya ca tathā tam anudhāvantam yuyudhānasya pṛṣṭhatas nyavārayanta saṃkruddhāḥ pāṇḍu sainye bṛhattamāḥ samāsādya tu hārdikyam rathānām pravaram ratham pāñcālāḥ vigata utsāhāḥ bhīmasena purogamāḥ vikramya vāritāḥ rājan vīreṇa kṛtavarmaṇā yatamānān tu tān sarvān īṣat vigata cetasaḥ abhitas tān śara ogheṇa klānta vāhān avārayat nigṛhītāḥ tu bhojena bhoja anīka īpsavaḥ raṇe atiṣṭhan ārya vat vīrāḥ prārthayantaḥ mahat yaśaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca vyūḍham evam yathānyāyam evam bahu ca saṃjaya nityam pūjitam asmābhiḥ abhikāmam ca naḥ sadā prauḍham ati adbhuta ākāram purastāt dṛḍha vikramam na ati vṛddham abālam ca na kṛśam na ati pīvaram laghu vṛtta āyata prāṇam sāra gātram anāmayam śastra grahaṇa vidyāsu bahvīṣu pariniṣṭhitam nāgeṣu aśveṣu bahuśas ratheṣu ca parīkṣitam parīkṣya ca yathānyāyam vetanena upapāditam na goṣṭhyā na upacāreṇa na saṃbandha nimittataḥ kulīna ārya jana upetam tuṣṭa puṣṭam anuddhatam asmān abhisṛtaiḥ kāmāt sa balaiḥ sa padānugaiḥ mahā udadhim iva āpūrṇam āpagābhiḥ samantataḥ apakṣaiḥ pakṣi saṃkāśaiḥ rathaiḥ aśvaiḥ ca saṃvṛtam yodha akṣayya jalam bhīmam vāhana ūrmi taraṅgiṇam kṣepaṇī asi gadā śakti śara prāsa jhaṣa ākulam dhvaja bhūṣaṇa saṃbādham ratna paṭṭena saṃcitam droṇa gambhīra pātālam kṛtavarma mahā hradam gate sainya arṇavam bhittvā tarasā pāṇḍava ṛṣabhe tatra śeṣam na paśyāmi praviṣṭe savyasācini sindhurājam ca saṃprekṣya gāṇḍīvasya iṣu gocare kim tadā kuravaḥ kṛtyam vidadhuḥ kāla coditāḥ dāruṇa ekāyane kāle katham vā pratipedire grastān hi kauravān manye mṛtyunā tāta saṃgatān vikramaḥ hi raṇe teṣām na tathā dṛśyate adya vai akṣatau saṃyuge tatra praviṣṭau kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau bhṛtāḥ ca bahavaḥ yodhāḥ parīkṣya eva mahā rathāḥ pūjitāḥ hi yathāśaktyā dāna māna āsanaiḥ mayā tathā putraiḥ ca me tāta jñātibhiḥ ca sa bāndhavaiḥ te ca prāpya eva saṃgrāme nirjitāḥ savyasācinā śaineyena parāmṛṣṭāḥ kim anyat bhāgadheyataḥ rakṣyate yaḥ ca saṃgrāme ye ca saṃjaya rakṣiṇaḥ ekaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ panthāḥ rakṣyasya saha rakṣibhiḥ arjunam samare dṛṣṭvā saindhavasya agratas sthitam putraḥ mama bhṛśam mūḍhaḥ kim kāryam pratyapadyata sātyakim ca raṇe dṛṣṭvā praviśantam abhīta vat dṛṣṭvā kām vai dhṛtim yuddhe pratyapadyanta māmakāḥ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam tu dāśārham arjuna arthe vyavasthitam śinīnām ṛṣabham ca eva manye śocanti putrakāḥ dṛṣṭvā senām vyatikrāntām sātvatena arjunena ca palāyamānān ca kurūn manye śocanti putrakāḥ vidrutān rathinaḥ dṛṣṭvā nirutsāhān dviṣat jaye palāyane kṛta utsāhān manye śocanti putrakāḥ śūnyān kṛtān rathopasthān sātvatena arjunena ca hatān ca yodhān saṃdṛśya manye śocanti putrakāḥ vyaśva nāga rathān dṛṣṭvā tatra vīrān sahasraśas dhāvamānān raṇe vyagrān manye śocanti putrakāḥ vivīrān ca kṛtān aśvān virathān ca kṛtān narān tatra sātyaki pārthābhyām manye śocanti putrakāḥ patti saṃghān raṇe dṛṣṭvā dhāvamānān ca sarvaśas nirāśāḥ vijaye sarve manye śocanti putrakāḥ kṣaṇena dṛṣṭvā tau vīrau manye śocanti putrakāḥ saṃmūḍhaḥ asmi bhṛśam tāta śrutvā kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau praviṣṭau māmakam sainyam sātvatena saha acyutau tasmin praviṣṭe pṛtanām śinīnām pravare rathe bhoja anīkam vyatikrānte katham āsan hi kauravāḥ tathā droṇena samare nigṛhīteṣu pāṇḍuṣu droṇaḥ hi balavān śūraḥ kṛtāstraḥ dṛḍha vikramaḥ pāñcālāḥ tam mahā iṣvāsam pratyayudhyan katham raṇe baddhavairāḥ tathā droṇe dharmarāja jaya eṣiṇaḥ bhāradvājaḥ tathā teṣu kṛta vairaḥ mahā rathaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca ātma aparādhāt saṃbhūtam vyasanam bharata ṛṣabha prāpya prākṛta vat vīra na tvam śocitum arhasi tava nirguṇa tām jñātvā pakṣapātam suteṣu ca dvaidhībhāvam tathā dharme pāṇḍaveṣu ca matsaram ārta pralāpān ca bahūn manuja adhipa sattama ātma aparādhāt su mahān prāptaḥ te vipulaḥ kṣayaḥ dṛśyate pṛṣṭhatas ca eva tvad mūlaḥ hi parājayaḥ tasmāt adya sthiraḥ bhūtvā jñātvā lokasya nirṇayam śṛṇu yuddham yathā vṛttam ghoram devāsura upamam bhīmasena mukhāḥ pārthāḥ pratīyuḥ vāhinīm tava āgacchataḥ tān sahasā kruddha rūpān saha anugān dadhāra ekaḥ raṇe pāṇḍūn kṛtavarmā mahā rathaḥ yathā udvṛttam dhārayate velā vai salila arṇavam pāṇḍu sainyam tathā saṃkhye hārdikyaḥ samavārayat yat enam sahitāḥ pārthāḥ na aticakramuḥ āhave tatas bhīmaḥ tribhiḥ viddhvā kṛtavarmāṇam āyasaiḥ śaṅkham dadhmau mahā bāhuḥ harṣayan sarva pāṇḍavān sahadevaḥ tu viṃśatyā dharmarājaḥ ca pañcabhiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tribhiḥ ca api kṛtavarmāṇam ārdayat virāṭaḥ drupadaḥ ca eva yājñaseniḥ ca pañcabhiḥ śikhaṇḍī ca api hārdikyam viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ punar vivyādha viṃśatyā sāyakānām hasan iva kṛtavarmā tatas rājan sarvatas tān mahā rathān ekaikam pañcabhiḥ viddhvā bhīmam vivyādha saptabhiḥ athā enam chinna dhanvānam tvaramāṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ saptatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasenam tathā dṛṣṭvā dharmarāja purogamāḥ visṛjantaḥ śarān ghorān kṛtavarmāṇam ārdayan tam tathā koṣṭhakīkṛtya ratha vaṃśena māriṣa vivyadhuḥ sāyakaiḥ hṛṣṭāḥ rakṣā artham māruteḥ mṛdhe pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ śaktim jagrāha samare hema daṇḍām ayasmayīm cikṣepa ca rathāt tūrṇam kṛtavarma ratham prati kṛtavarmāṇam abhitas prajajvāla su dāruṇā tām āpatantīm sahasā yuga anta agni sama prabhām dvābhyām śarābhyām hārdikyaḥ nicakarta dvidhā tadā sā chinnā patitā bhūmau śaktiḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇā śaktim vinihatām dṛṣṭvā bhīmaḥ cukrodha vai bhṛśam athā enam pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare bhojaḥ tu kṣata sarva aṅgaḥ bhīmasenena māriṣa śikhaṇḍinaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ kṣurapreṇa mahā rathaḥ śikhaṇḍī tu tatas kruddhaḥ chinne dhanuṣi sa tvaram bhrāmayitvā mahā carma cāmīkara vibhūṣitam tam asim preṣayām āsa kṛtavarma ratham prati sa tasya sa śaram cāpam chittvā saṃkhye mahān asiḥ abhyagāt dharaṇīm rājan cyutam jyotiḥ iva ambarāt etasmin eva kāle tu tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ vivyadhuḥ sāyakaiḥ gāḍham kṛtavarmāṇam āhave viśīrṇam bharata śreṣṭha hārdikyaḥ para vīra hā śikhaṇḍinam ca vivyādha tribhiḥ pañcabhiḥ eva ca dhanuḥ anyat samādāya śikhaṇḍī tu mahā yaśāḥ avārayat kūrma nakhaiḥ āśugaiḥ hṛdika ātmajam tatas kruddhaḥ raṇe rājan hṛdikasya ātmasaṃbhavaḥ bhīṣmasya samare rājan mṛtyoḥ hetum mahātmanaḥ vidarśayan balam śūraḥ śārdūlaḥ iva kuñjaram tau diśāgaja saṃkāśau jvalitau iva pāvakau vidhunvānau dhanuḥ śreṣṭhe saṃdadhānau ca sāyakān tāpayantau śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ anyonyam tau mahā rathau kṛtavarmā tu rabhasam yājñasenim mahā ratham viddhvā iṣūṇām trisaptatyā punar vivyādha saptabhiḥ visṛjan sa śaram cāpam mūrchayā abhipariplutaḥ tam viṣaṇṇam rathe dṛṣṭvā tāvakāḥ bharata ṛṣabha hārdikyam pūjayām āsuḥ vāsāṃsi ādudhuvuḥ ca ha śikhaṇḍinam tathā jñātvā hārdikya śara pīḍitam apovāha raṇāt yantā tvaramāṇaḥ mahā ratham sāditam tu rathopasthe dṛṣṭvā pārthāḥ śikhaṇḍinam parivavruḥ rathaiḥ tūrṇam kṛtavarmāṇam āhave tatra adbhutam param cakre kṛtavarmā mahā rathaḥ yat ekaḥ samare pārthān vārayām āsa sa anugān pārthān jitvā ajayat cedīn pāñcālān sṛñjayān api kekayān ca mahā vīryān kṛtavarmā mahā rathaḥ te vadhyamānāḥ samare hārdikyena sma pāṇḍavāḥ itas ca itas ca dhāvantaḥ na eva cakruḥ dhṛtim raṇe jitvā pāṇḍu sutān yuddhe bhīmasena purogamān hārdikyaḥ samare atiṣṭhat vidhūmaḥ iva pāvakaḥ te drāvyamāṇāḥ samare hārdikyena mahā rathāḥ vimukhāḥ samapadyanta śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ arditāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ rājan yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi drāvyamāṇe bale tasmin hārdikyena mahātmanā lajjayā avanate ca api prahṛṣṭaiḥ ca eva tāvakaiḥ dvīpaḥ yaḥ āsīt pāṇḍūnām agādhe gādham icchatām śrutvā tu ninadam bhīmam tāvakānām mahā āhave śaineyaḥ tvaritaḥ rājan kṛtavarmāṇam abhyayāt kṛtavarmā tu hārdikyaḥ śaineyam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas su niśitam bhallam śaineyaḥ kṛtavarmaṇe preṣayām āsa samare śarān ca caturaḥ aparān pṛṣṭharakṣam tathā sūtam avidhyat niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas tam viratham kṛtvā sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ senām asya ardayām āsa śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ sā abhajyata atha pṛtanā śaineya śara pīḍitā tatas prāyāt vai tvaritaḥ sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ śṛṇu rājan yat akarot tava sainyeṣu vīryavān atītya sa mahā rāja droṇa anīka mahā arṇavam parājitya ca saṃhṛṣṭaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam āhave yantāram abravīt śūraḥ śanais yāhi iti asaṃbhramam dṛṣṭvā tu tava tat sainyam ratha aśva dvipa saṃkulam padāti jana saṃpūrṇam abravīt sārathim punar yat etat megha saṃkāśam droṇa anīkasya savyatas ete hi bahavaḥ sūta durnivāryāḥ ca saṃyuge duryodhana samādiṣṭāḥ mad arthe tyakta jīvitāḥ rāja putrāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ sarve vikrānta yodhinaḥ trigartānām ratha udārāḥ suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ mām eva abhimukhāḥ vīrāḥ yotsyamānāḥ vyavasthitāḥ atra mām prāpaya kṣipram aśvān codaya sārathe tatas prāyāt śanais sūtaḥ sātvatasya mate sthitaḥ rathena āditya varṇena bhāsvareṇa patākinā tam ūhuḥ sāratheḥ vaśyāḥ valgamānāḥ haya uttamāḥ āpatantam ratham tam tu śaṅkha varṇaiḥ haya uttamaiḥ parivavruḥ tatas śūrāḥ gaja anīkena sarvatas kirantaḥ vividhān tīkṣṇān sāyakān laghu vedhinaḥ sātvataḥ api śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ gaja anīkam ayodhayat vajra aśani sama sparśaiḥ vadhyamānāḥ śaraiḥ gajāḥ prādravan raṇam utsṛjya śini vīrya samīritaiḥ śīrṇa dantāḥ virudhirāḥ bhinna mastaka piṇḍakāḥ viśīrṇa karṇa āsya karāḥ viniyantṛ patākinaḥ saṃbhinna varma ghaṇṭāḥ ca saṃnikṛtta mahā dhvajāḥ hata ārohāḥ diśaḥ rājan bhejire bhraṣṭa kambalāḥ ruvantaḥ vividhān rāvān jalada upama nisvanāḥ nārācaiḥ vatsadantaiḥ ca sātvatena vidāritāḥ yattaḥ saṃprāpayan nāgam rajata aśva ratham prati rukma varṇa karaḥ śūraḥ tapanīya aṅgadaḥ śuciḥ kuṇḍalī mukuṭī śaṅkhī raktacandana rūṣitaḥ śirasā dhārayan dīptām tapanīya mayīm srajam urasā dhārayan niṣkam kaṇṭha sūtram ca bhāsvaram sātyakiḥ vārayām āsa velā iva udvṛttam arṇavam nāgam nivāritam dṛṣṭvā śaineyasya śara uttamaiḥ akrudhyata raṇe rājan jalasaṃdhaḥ mahā balaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ mārgaṇaiḥ bhāra sādhanaiḥ asyataḥ vṛṣṇi vīrasya nicakarta śarāsanam avidhyat māgadhaḥ vīraḥ pañcabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ a cintayan vai sa śarān na atyartham saṃbhramāt balī dhanuḥ anyat samādāya tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti uvāca ha vivyādha ṣaṣṭyā su bhṛśam śarāṇām prahasan iva kṣurapreṇa ca pītena muṣṭideśe mahat dhanuḥ tomaram vyasṛjat tūrṇam sātyakim prati māriṣa abhyagāt dharaṇīm ghoraḥ śvasan iva mahā uragaḥ triṃśadbhiḥ viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ jalasaṃdham atāḍayat pragṛhya tu tatas khaḍgam jalasaṃdhaḥ mahā balaḥ tatas āvidhya tam khaḍgam sātvatāya utsasarja ha atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya sarva kāya avadāraṇam śāla skandha pratīkāśam indra aśani sama svanam tatas sa ābharaṇau bāhū kṣurābhyām mādhava uttamaḥ vasuṃdhara dharāt bhraṣṭau pañca śīrṣau iva uragau tatas su daṃṣṭram su hanu cāru kuṇḍalam unnasam kṣureṇa asya tṛtīyena śiraḥ ciccheda sātyakiḥ tat pātita śiraḥ bāhu kabandham bhīma darśanam jalasaṃdham nihatya ājau tvaramāṇaḥ tu sātvataḥ naiṣādim pātayām āsa gaja skandhāt viśām pate rudhireṇa avasikta aṅgaḥ jalasaṃdhasya kuñjaraḥ vilambamānam avahat saṃśliṣṭam param āsanam śara arditaḥ sātvatena mardamānaḥ sva vāhinīm ghoram ārta svaram kṛtvā vidudrāva mahā gajaḥ hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt tava sainyasya māriṣa jalasaṃdham hatam dṛṣṭvā vṛṣṇīnām ṛṣabheṇa ha vimukhāḥ ca abhyadhāvanta tava yodhāḥ samantataḥ palāyane kṛta utsāhāḥ nirutsāhāḥ dviṣat jaye etasmin antare rājan droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ tam udīrṇam tathā dṛṣṭvā śaineyam kuru puṃgavāḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham kurūṇām sātvatasya ca saṃjayaḥ uvāca te kirantaḥ śara vrātān sarve yattāḥ prahāriṇaḥ tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rāja yuyudhānam ayodhayan tam droṇaḥ saptasaptatyā jaghāna niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ durmarṣaṇaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ duḥsahaḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ vikarṇaḥ ca api niśitaiḥ triṃśadbhiḥ kaṅka patribhiḥ durmukhaḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ tathā duḥśāsanaḥ aṣṭabhiḥ citrasenaḥ ca śaineyam dvābhyām vivyādha māriṣa duryodhanaḥ ca mahatā śara varṣeṇa mādhavam apīḍayat raṇe rājan śūrāḥ ca anye mahā rathāḥ bhāradvājam tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ duḥsaham navabhiḥ tathā vikarṇam pañcaviṃśatyā citrasenam ca saptabhiḥ durmarṣaṇam dvādaśabhiḥ caturbhiḥ ca viviṃśatim tatas rukma aṅgadam cāpam vidhunvānaḥ mahā rathaḥ abhyayāt sātyakiḥ tūrṇam putram tava mahā ratham rājānam sarva lokasya sarva śastrabhṛtām varam śaraiḥ abhyāhanat gāḍham tatas yuddham abhūt tayoḥ vimuñcantau śarān tīkṣṇān saṃdadhānau ca sāyakān śātakumbha maya āpīḍaḥ babhau yūpaḥ iva ucchritaḥ nirbhinnaḥ ca śaraiḥ tena dviṣatā kṣiprakāriṇā na amṛṣyata raṇe rājā śatroḥ vijaya lakṣaṇam atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya hema pṛṣṭham durāsadam vivyādha sātyakim tūrṇam sāyakānām śatena ha pīḍitam nṛpatim dṛṣṭvā tava putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ sātvatam śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsuḥ añjasā duryodhanam ca tvaritaḥ vivyādha aṣṭabhiḥ āśugaiḥ prahasan ca asya ciccheda kārmukam ripu bhīṣaṇam nāgam maṇi mayam ca eva śaraiḥ dhvajam apātayat hatvā tu caturaḥ vāhān caturbhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim pātayām āsa kṣurapreṇa mahā yaśāḥ hāhā bhūtam jagat ca āsīt dṛṣṭvā rājānam āhave grasyamānam sātyakinā khe somam iva rāhuṇā tam tu śabdam mahat śrutvā kṛtavarmā mahā rathaḥ vidhunvānaḥ dhanuḥ śreṣṭham codayan ca eva vājinaḥ bhartsayan sārathim ca ugram yāhi yāhi iti sa tvaraḥ tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya vyādita āsyam iva antakam kṛtavarmā rathena eṣa drutam āpatate śarī āsasāda raṇe bhojam pratimānam dhanuṣmatām kṛtavarmā tu śaineyam ṣaḍviṃśatyā samārpayat niśitaiḥ sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ yantāram ca asya saptabhiḥ caturaḥ ca haya udārān caturbhiḥ parama iṣubhiḥ rukma aṅgadī rukma varmā rukma puṅkhān avākirat tatas aśītim śineḥ pautraḥ sāyakān kṛtavarmaṇe prāhiṇot tvarayā yuktaḥ draṣṭu kāmaḥ dhanaṃjayam saḥ atividdhaḥ balavatā śatruṇā śatru tāpanaḥ triṣaṣṭyā caturaḥ asya aśvān saptabhiḥ sārathim śaraiḥ vivyādha niśitaiḥ tūrṇam sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmaṇaḥ suvarṇa puṅkham viśikham samādhāya sa sātyakiḥ saḥ aviśat kṛtavarmāṇam yama daṇḍa upamaḥ śaraḥ abhyagāt dharaṇīm ugraḥ rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥ saṃjāta rudhiraḥ ca ājau sātvata iṣubhiḥ arditaḥ sa siṃha daṃṣṭraḥ jānubhyām āpannaḥ amita vikramaḥ śara arditaḥ sātyakinā rathopasthe nara ṛṣabhaḥ sahasrabāhoḥ sadṛśam akṣobhyam iva sāgaram nivārya kṛtavarmāṇam sātyakiḥ prayayau tatas khaḍga śakti dhanuḥ kīrṇām gaja aśva ratha saṃkulām pravartitā ugra rudhirām śataśas kṣatriya ṛṣabhaiḥ prekṣatām sarva sainyānām madhyena śini puṃgavaḥ abhyagāt vāhinīm bhittvā vṛtrahā iva āsurīm camūm samāśvāsya ca hārdikyaḥ gṛhya ca anyat mahat dhanuḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca kālyamāneṣu sainyeṣu śaineyena tatas tatas bhāradvājaḥ śara vrātaiḥ mahadbhiḥ samavākirat paśyatām sarva sainyānām bali vāsavayoḥ iva tatas droṇaḥ śineḥ pautram citraiḥ sarva āyasaiḥ śaraiḥ tribhiḥ āśīviṣa ākāraiḥ lalāṭe samavidhyata taiḥ lalāṭa arpitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ yuyudhānaḥ tu a jihma gaiḥ vyarocata mahā rāja triśṛṅgaḥ iva parvataḥ tatas asya bāṇān aparān indra aśani sama svanān bhāradvājaḥ antara prekṣī preṣayām āsa saṃyuge tān droṇa cāpa nirmuktān dāśārhaḥ patataḥ śarān dvābhyām dvābhyām su puṅkhābhyām ciccheda parama astra vid tām asya laghu tām droṇaḥ samavekṣya viśām pate punar pañcāśatā iṣūṇām śatena ca samārpayat laghu tām yuyudhānasya lāghavena viśeṣayan tathā eva yuyudhānena sṛṣṭāḥ śata sahasraśas avākiran droṇa ratham śarāḥ rudhira bhojanāḥ viśeṣam na adhyagacchāma samāvāstām nara ṛṣabhau ājaghāna bhṛśam kruddhaḥ dhvajam ca niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim ca śatena eva bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ lāghavam yuyudhānasya dṛṣṭvā droṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ saptatyā sātyakim viddhvā turagān ca tribhiḥ tribhiḥ gadām jagrāha mahatīm bhāradvājāya ca akṣipat tām āpatantīm sahasā paṭṭa baddhām ayasmayīm atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ vivyādha bahubhiḥ vīram bhāradvājam śilā śitaiḥ sa viddhvā samare droṇam siṃhanādam amuñcata tam vai na mamṛṣe droṇaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ tathaḥ śaktim gṛhītvā tu rukma daṇḍām ayasmayīm tarasā preṣayām āsa mādhavasya ratham prati an āsādya tu śaineyam sā śaktiḥ kāla saṃnibhā bhittvā ratham jagāma ugrā dharaṇīm dāruṇa svanā tatas droṇam śineḥ pautraḥ rājan vivyādha patriṇā dakṣiṇam bhujam āsādya pīḍayan bharata ṛṣabha sa rathopastham āsādya muhūrtam saṃnyaṣīdata cakāra sātyakiḥ rājan tatra karma ati mānuṣam tatas śara śatena eva yuyudhānaḥ mahā rathaḥ avidhyat brāhmaṇam saṃkhye hṛṣṭa rūpaḥ viśām pate tasya droṇaḥ śarān pañca preṣayām āsa bhārata te tasya kavacam bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave sāyakān vyasṛjat ca api vīraḥ rukmaratham prati tatas droṇasya yantāram nipātya eka iṣuṇā bhuvi aśvān vyadrāvayat bāṇaiḥ hata sūtān mahātmanaḥ sa rathaḥ pradrutaḥ saṃkhye maṇḍalāni sahasraśas cakāra rājataḥ rājan bhrājamānaḥ iva aṃśumān abhidravata gṛhṇīta hayān droṇasya dhāvata iti sma cukruśuḥ sarve rāja putrāḥ sa rājakāḥ te sātyakim apāsya āśu rājan yudhi mahā rathāḥ tān dṛṣṭvā pradrutān sarvān sātvatena śara arditān vātāyamānaiḥ taiḥ aśvaiḥ hṛtaḥ vṛṣṇi śara arditaiḥ pāṇḍu pāñcāla saṃbhagnam vyūham ālokya vīryavān śaineye nā akarot yatnam vyūhasya eva abhirakṣaṇe nivārya pāṇḍu pāñcālān droṇa agniḥ pradahan iva tasthau krodha agni saṃdīptaḥ kālasūryaḥ iva uditaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca droṇam sa jitvā puruṣa pravīraḥ tathā eva hārdikya mukhān tvadīyān prahasya sūtam vacanam babhāṣe kiran samantāt sahasā śarān balī samāpatat śyenaḥ iva āmiṣam yathā tam yāntam aśvaiḥ śaśi śaṅkha varṇaiḥ vigāhya sainyam puruṣa pravīram na aśaknuvan vārayitum samantāt āditya raśmi pratimam nara agryam amarṣa pūrṇaḥ tu ati citra yodhī śarāsanī kāñcana varma dhārī tayoḥ abhūt bharata saṃprahāraḥ su dāruṇaḥ tam samabhipraśaṃsan yodhāḥ tvadīyāḥ ca hi somakāḥ ca vṛtra indrayoḥ yuddham iva amara oghāḥ śaraiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ śataśas abhyavidhyat sudarśanaḥ sātvata mukhyam ājau anāgatān eva tu tān pṛṣatkān ciccheda bāṇaiḥ śini puṃgavaḥ api saṃprekṣya bāṇān nihatān tadānīm sudarśanaḥ sātyaki bāṇa vegaiḥ krodhāt didhakṣan iva tigma tejāḥ śarān amuñcat tapanīya citrān punar sa bāṇaiḥ tribhiḥ agni kalpaiḥ ākarṇapūrṇaiḥ niśitaiḥ su puṅkhaiḥ vivyādha deha āvaraṇam vibhidya te sātyakeḥ āviviśuḥ śarīram ājaghnivān tān rajata prakāśān caturbhiḥ aśvān caturaḥ prasahya tathā tu tena abhihataḥ tarasvī naptā śineḥ indra samāna vīryaḥ sudarśanasya iṣu gaṇaiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ hayān nihatya āśu nanāda nādam sudarśanasya api śini pravīraḥ kṣureṇa ciccheda śiraḥ prasahya sa kuṇḍalam pūrṇa śaśi prakāśam bhrājiṣṇu vaktram nicakarta dehāt nihatya tam pārthiva putra pautram raṇe yadūnām ṛṣabhaḥ tarasvī mudā sametaḥ parayā mahātmā rarāja rājan surarāja kalpaḥ sat aśva yuktena rathena niryāt lokān visismāpayiṣuḥ nṛ vīraḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas sa sātyakiḥ dhīmān mahātmā vṛṣṇi puṃgavaḥ ratha aśva nāga kalilam śara śakti ūrmi mālinam khaḍga matsyam gadā grāham śūra āyudha mahā svanam prāṇa apahāriṇam raudram vāditra utkruṣṭa nāditam yodhānām asukha sparśam durdharṣam ajaya eṣiṇām tīrṇāḥ sma dustaram tāta droṇa anīka mahā arṇavam jalasaṃdha balena ājau puruṣādaiḥ iva āvṛtam atas anyam pṛtanā śeṣam manye kunadikām iva tartavyām alpa salilām codaya aśvān asaṃbhramam na hi me jāyate trāsaḥ dṛṣṭvā sainyāni anekaśas vahneḥ iva pradīptasya grīṣme śuṣkam tṛṇa ulapam paśya pāṇḍava mukhyena yātām bhūmim kirīṭinā patti aśva ratha nāga oghaiḥ patitaiḥ viṣamīkṛtām abhyāśa stham aham manye śvetāśvam kṛṣṇasārathim saḥ eṣa śrūyate śabdaḥ gāṇḍīvasya amita ojasaḥ yādṛśāni nimittāni mama prādurbhavanti vai śanais viśrambhayan aśvān yāhi yattaḥ ari vāhinīm yatra ete sa tanutrāṇāḥ suyodhana purogamāḥ daṃśitāḥ krūra karmāṇaḥ kāmbojāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ śara bāṇa āsana dharāḥ yavanāḥ ca prahāriṇaḥ śakāḥ kirātāḥ daradāḥ barbarāḥ tāmraliptakāḥ mām eva abhimukhāḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti samara arthinaḥ etān sa ratha nāga aśvān nihatya ājau sa pattinaḥ idam durgam mahā ghoram tīrṇam eva upadhāraya sūtaḥ uvāca droṇaḥ vā rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ kṛpaḥ madra īśvaraḥ api vā tathā api saṃbhramaḥ na syāt tvām āśritya mahā bhuja na ca me saṃbhramaḥ kaḥ cit bhūta pūrvaḥ kadā cana āyuṣman katareṇa tvā prāpayāmi dhanaṃjayam keṣām kruddhaḥ asi vārṣṇeya keṣām mṛtyuḥ upasthitaḥ keṣām saṃyamanīm adya gantum utsahate manaḥ ke tvām yudhi parākrāntam kāla antaka yama upamam dṛṣṭvā vikrama saṃpannam vidraviṣyanti saṃyuge keṣām vaivasvataḥ rājā smarate adya mahā bhuja sātyakiḥ uvāca muṇḍān etān haniṣyāmi dānavān iva vāsavaḥ pratijñām pārayiṣyāmi kāmbojān eva mā vaha adya eṣām kadanam kṛtvā kṣipram yāsyāmi pāṇḍavam adya drakṣyanti me vīryam kauravāḥ sa suyodhanāḥ muṇḍānīke hate sūta sarva sainyeṣu ca asakṛt śrutvā virāvam bahudhā saṃtapsyati suyodhanaḥ adya pāṇḍava mukhyasya śvetāśvasya mahātmanaḥ ācāryaka kṛtam mārgam darśayiṣyāmi saṃyuge adya mad bāṇa nihatān yodha mukhyān sahasraśas dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaḥ rājā paścāttāpam gamiṣyati mad sāyaka cita aṅgānām rudhiram sravatām bahu sainikānām vadham dṛṣṭvā saṃtapsyati suyodhanaḥ adya rāja sahasrāṇi nihatāni mayā raṇe dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaḥ rājā saṃtapsyati mahā mṛdhe adya sneham ca bhaktim ca pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu hatvā rāja sahasrāṇi darśayiṣyāmi rājasu saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam uktaḥ tadā sūtaḥ śikṣitān sādhu vāhinaḥ śaśāṅka saṃnikāśān vai vājinaḥ acūcudat bhṛśam te pibantaḥ iva ākāśam yuyudhānam haya uttamāḥ prāpayan yavanān śīghram manaḥ pavana raṃhasaḥ sātyakim te samāsādya pṛtanāsu anivartinam teṣām iṣūn atha astrāṇi vegavat nata parvabhiḥ acchinat sātyakiḥ rājan na enam te prāpnuvan śarāḥ uccakarta śirāṃsi ugraḥ yavanānām bhujān api śaikyāyasāni varmāṇi kāṃsyāni ca samantataḥ bhittvā dehān tathā teṣām śarāḥ jagmuḥ mahī talam te hanyamānāḥ vīreṇa mlecchāḥ sātyakinā raṇe su pūrṇa āyata muktaiḥ tān avyavacchinna piṇḍitaiḥ pañca ṣaṭ sapta ca aṣṭau ca bibheda yavanān śaraiḥ kāmbojānām sahasraiḥ tu śakānām ca viśām pate śabarāṇām kirātānām barbarāṇām tathā eva ca agamya rūpām pṛthivīm māṃsa śoṇita kardamām kṛtavān tatra śaineyaḥ kṣapayan tāvakam balam dasyūnām sa śirastrāṇaiḥ śirobhiḥ lūna mūrdhajaiḥ tatra tatra mahī kīrṇā vibarhaiḥ aṇḍajaiḥ iva kabandhaiḥ saṃvṛtam sarvam tāmra abhraiḥ kham iva āvṛtam te sa aśvayānāḥ nihatāḥ samāvavruḥ vasuṃdharām alpa avaśiṣṭāḥ saṃbhagnāḥ kṛcchra prāṇāḥ vicetasaḥ jitāḥ saṃkhye mahā rāja yuyudhānena daṃśitāḥ pārṣṇibhiḥ ca kaśābhiḥ ca tāḍayantaḥ turaṃgamān yavanānām ca tat sainyam śakānām ca mahat balam sa tatas puruṣa vyāghraḥ sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ tāvakān jitvā sūtam yāhi iti acodayat tam yāntam pṛṣṭhagoptāram arjunasya viśām pate cāraṇāḥ prekṣya saṃhṛṣṭāḥ tvadīyāḥ ca api apūjayan saṃjayaḥ uvāca mṛgān vyāghraḥ iva ājighran tava sainyam abhīṣayat rukma pṛṣṭham mahā vegam rukma candraka saṃkulam rukma aṅgada śirastrāṇaḥ rukma varma samāvṛtaḥ rukma dhvaja varaḥ śūraḥ meru śṛṅge iva ābabhau sa dhanuḥ maṇḍalaḥ saṃkhye tejaḥ bhāsvara raśmivān śaradi iva uditaḥ sūryaḥ nṛ sūryaḥ virarāja ha vṛṣabha skandha vikrāntaḥ vṛṣabha akṣaḥ nara ṛṣabhaḥ tāvakānām babhau madhye gavām madhye yathā vṛṣaḥ vyāghrāḥ iva jighāṃsantaḥ tvadīyāḥ abhyadravan raṇe droṇa anīkam atikrāntam bhoja anīkam ca dustaram jalasaṃdha arṇavam tīrtvā kāmbojānām ca vāhinīm hārdikya makarāt muktam tīrṇam vai sainya sāgaram parivavruḥ su saṃkruddhāḥ tvadīyāḥ sātyakim rathāḥ duryodhanaḥ citrasenaḥ duḥśāsana viviṃśatī śakuniḥ duḥsahaḥ ca eva yuvā durmarṣaṇaḥ krathaḥ anye ca bahavaḥ śūrāḥ śastravantaḥ durāsadāḥ pṛṣṭhatas sātyakim yāntam anvadhāvan amarṣitāḥ atha śabdaḥ mahān āsīt tava sainyasya māriṣa tān abhidravataḥ sarvān samīkṣya śini puṃgavaḥ mām eva abhimukham tūrṇam gaja aśva ratha pattimat nādayan vai diśaḥ sarvāḥ ratha ghoṣeṇa sārathe pṛthivīm ca antarikṣam ca kampayan sāgarān api etat bala arṇavam tāta vārayiṣye mahā raṇe paurṇamāsyām iva uddhūtam velā iva salilāśayam eṣa sainyāni śatrūṇām vidhamāmi śitaiḥ śaraiḥ nihatān āhave paśya padāti aśva ratha dvipān mad śaraiḥ agni saṃkāśaiḥ videha asūn sahasraśas samīpam sainikāḥ te tu śīghram īyuḥ yuyutsavaḥ jahi ādravasva tiṣṭha iti paśya paśya iti vādinaḥ tān evam bruvataḥ vīrān sātyakiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ jaghāna tri śatān aśvān kuñjarān ca catur śatān deva asura raṇa prakhyaḥ prāvartata jana kṣayaḥ pratyagṛhṇāt śineḥ pautraḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ pracchādyamānaḥ samare śara jālaiḥ sa vīryavān asaṃbhramam mahā rāja tāvakān avadhīt bahūn āścaryam tatra rāja indra su mahat dṛṣṭavān aham ratha nāga aśva kalilaḥ padāti ūrmi samākulaḥ śaineya velām āsādya sthitaḥ sainya mahā arṇavaḥ saṃbhrānta nara nāga aśvam āvartata muhur muhur babhrāma tatra tatra eva gāvaḥ śīta arditāḥ iva padātinam ratham nāgam sādinam turagam tathā a viddham tatra na adrākṣam yuyudhānasya sāyakaiḥ na tādṛś kadanam rājan kṛtavān tatra phalgunaḥ yādṛś kṣayam anīkānām akarot sātyakiḥ nṛpa vivyādha sūtam niśitaiḥ caturbhiḥ caturaḥ hayān sātyakim ca tribhiḥ viddhvā punar vivyādha saḥ aṣṭabhiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ vivyādha śini puṃgavam śakuniḥ pañcaviṃśatyā citrasenaḥ ca pañcabhiḥ utsmayan vṛṣṇi śārdūlaḥ tathā bāṇaiḥ samāhataḥ gāḍha viddhān arīn kṛtvā mārgaṇaiḥ saḥ ati tejanaiḥ citrasenam śatena eva daśabhiḥ duḥsaham tathā duḥśāsanam ca viṃśatyā vivyādha śini puṃgavaḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya syālaḥ tava viśām pate aṣṭabhiḥ sātyakim viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ ca daśabhiḥ duḥsahaḥ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ durmukhaḥ ca dvādaśabhiḥ rājan vivyādha sātyakim tān sarvān sahitān śūrān yatamānān mahā rathān pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ punar vivyādha sātyakiḥ tatas sa rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ tava putrasya sārathim vātāyamānaiḥ taiḥ aśvaiḥ apānīyata saṃgarāt tatas tava sutāḥ rājan sainikāḥ ca viśām pate rājñaḥ ratham abhiprekṣya vidrutāḥ śataśas abhavan vidrutam tatra tat sainyam dṛṣṭvā bhārata sātyakiḥ avākirat śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ rukma puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ prayayau sātyakiḥ rājan śvetāśvasya ratham prati tam śarān ādadānam ca rakṣamāṇam ca sārathim ātmānam mocayantam ca tāvakāḥ samapūjayan dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca katham ca eṣām tathā yuddhe dhṛtiḥ āsīt mumūrṣatām śaineya caritam dṛṣṭvā sadṛśam savyasācinaḥ kim nu vakṣyanti te kṣātram sainya madhye parājitāḥ katham ca sātyakiḥ yuddhe vyatikrāntaḥ mahā yaśāḥ katham ca mama putrāṇām jīvatām tatra saṃjaya ati adbhutam idam tāta tvad sakāśāt śṛṇomi aham kruddhasya yuyudhānasya sarve tiṣṭhantu pāṇḍavāḥ yathā paśu gaṇān siṃhaḥ tadvat hantā sutān mama yuyudhānaḥ na śakitaḥ hantum yaḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ na etat īdṛśakam yuddham kṛtavān tatra phalgunaḥ yādṛśam kṛtavān yuddham śineḥ naptā mahā yaśāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ bhūtvā yat te vakṣyāmi bhārata te punar saṃnyavartanta kṛtvā saṃśaptakān mithas parām yuddhe matim kṛtvā putrasya tava śāsanāt trīṇi sādi sahasrāṇi duryodhana purogamāḥ śakāḥ kāmboja bāhlīkāḥ yavanāḥ pāradāḥ tathā kuṇindāḥ taṅgaṇa ambaṣṭhāḥ paiśācāḥ ca sa mandarāḥ abhyadravanta śaineyam śalabhāḥ pāvakam yathā yuktāḥ ca pārvatīyānām rathāḥ pāṣāṇa yodhinām śūrāḥ pañcaśatāḥ rājan śaineyam samupādravan dviradānām sahasreṇa dvi sāhasraiḥ ca vājibhiḥ śara varṣāṇi muñcantaḥ vividhāni mahā rathāḥ duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja sātyaktim paryavārayat avadhīt ca ratha anīkam dviradānām ca tat balam sādinaḥ ca eva tān sarvān dasyūn api ca sarvaśas akṣaiḥ ca bahudhā bhagnaiḥ īṣā daṇḍaka bandhuraiḥ kūbaraiḥ mathitaiḥ ca api dhvajaiḥ ca api nipātitaiḥ varmabhiḥ cāmaraiḥ ca eva vyavakīrṇā vasuṃdharā giri rūpa dharāḥ ca api patitāḥ kuñjara uttamāḥ jātāḥ danti varāḥ rājan śerate bahavaḥ hatāḥ vanāyu jān pārvatīyān kāmboja āraṭṭa bāhlikān nānā deśa samutthān ca nānā jātyān ca pattinaḥ nijaghne tatra śaineyaḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas teṣu prakālyamāneṣu dasyūn duḥśāsanaḥ abravīt tān ca api sarvān saṃprekṣya putraḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tava pāṣāṇa yodhinaḥ śūrān pārvatīyān acodayat aśma yuddheṣu kuśalāḥ na etat jānāti sātyakiḥ tathā eva kuravaḥ sarve na aśma yuddha viśāradāḥ abhidravata mā bhaiṣṭa na vaḥ prāpsyati sātyakiḥ tatas gaja śiśu prakhyaiḥ upalaiḥ śaila vāsinaḥ udyataiḥ yuyudhānasya sthitāḥ maraṇa kāṅkṣiṇaḥ kṣepaṇīyaiḥ tathā api anye sātvatasya vadha eṣiṇaḥ teṣām āpatatām eva śilā yuddham cikīrṣatām sātyakiḥ pratisaṃdhāya triṃśatam prāhiṇot śarān tām aśma vṛṣṭim tumulām pārvatīyaiḥ samīritām bibheda uraga saṃkāśaiḥ nārācaiḥ śini puṃgavaḥ taiḥ aśma cūrṇaiḥ dīpyadbhiḥ khadyotānām iva vrajaiḥ prāyas sainyāni avadhyanta hāhā bhūtāni māriṣa tatas pañcaśatāḥ śūrāḥ samudyata mahā śilāḥ pāṣāṇa yodhinaḥ śūrān yatamānān avasthitān tatas punar basta mukhaiḥ aśma vṛṣṭim samantataḥ ayaḥ hastaiḥ śūla hastaiḥ daradaiḥ ambaṣṭhaiḥ ca kuṇindaiḥ ca kṣiptām kṣiptām sa sātyakiḥ nārācaiḥ prativivyādha prekṣamāṇaḥ mahā balaḥ adrīṇām bhidyamānānām antarikṣe śitaiḥ śaraiḥ aśma cūrṇaiḥ samākīrṇāḥ manuṣyāḥ ca vayāṃsi ca na aśaknuvan avasthātum bhramaraiḥ iva daṃśitāḥ hata śiṣṭāḥ virudhirāḥ bhinna mastaka piṇḍikāḥ mādhavena ardyamānasya sāgarasya iva dāruṇaḥ tam śabdam tumulam śrutvā droṇaḥ yantāram abravīt eṣa sūta raṇe kruddhaḥ sātvatānām mahā rathaḥ pāṣāṇa yodhibhiḥ nūnam yuyudhānaḥ samāgataḥ na śaknuvanti yantāraḥ saṃyantum tumule hayān iti evam bruvataḥ rājan bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥ pratyuvāca tatas yantā droṇam śastrabhṛtām varam paśya yodhān raṇe bhinnān dhāvamānān tatas tatas ete ca sahitāḥ śūrāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha atra kāryam samādhatsva prāpta kālam ariṃdama sthāne vā gamane vā api dūram yātaḥ ca sātyakiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ samare yuyudhānena tāvakāḥ yuyudhāna ratham tyaktvā droṇa anīkāya dudruvuḥ yaiḥ tu duḥśāsanaḥ sārdham rathaiḥ pūrvam nyavartata saṃjayaḥ uvāca duḥśāsana ratham dṛṣṭvā samīpe paryavasthitam bhāradvājaḥ tatas vākyam duḥśāsanam atha abravīt duḥśāsana rathāḥ sarve kasmāt ete pravidrutāḥ rāja putraḥ bhavān atra rāja bhrātā mahā rathaḥ svayam vairam mahat kṛtvā pāñcālaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha ekam sātyakim āsādya katham bhītaḥ asi saṃyuge na jānīṣe purā tvam tu gṛhṇan akṣān durodare śarāḥ hi ete bhaviṣyanti dāruṇa āśīviṣa upamāḥ apriyāṇām ca vacanam pāṇḍaveṣu viśeṣataḥ āśīviṣa samān pārthān kopayitvā kva yāsyasi śocyā iyam bhāratī senā rājā ca eva suyodhanaḥ yasya tvam karkaśaḥ bhrātā palāyana parāyaṇaḥ nanu nāma tvayā vīra dīryamāṇā bhaya arditā sva bāhu balam āsthāya rakṣitavyā hi anīkinī kaḥ anyaḥ sthāsyati saṃgrāme bhītaḥ bhīte vyapāśraye yadā gāṇḍīvadhanvānam bhīmasenam ca kaurava yamau ca yudhi draṣṭāsi tadā tvam kim kariṣyasi yudhi phalguna bāṇānām sūrya agni sama tejasām na tulyāḥ sātyaki śarāḥ yeṣām bhītaḥ palāyase yadi tāvat kṛtā buddhiḥ palāyana parāyaṇā pṛthivī dharmarājasya śamena eva pradīyatām yāvat phalguna nārācāḥ nirmukta uraga saṃnibhāḥ na āviśanti śarīram te tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ yāvat te pṛthivīm pārthāḥ hatvā bhrātṛ śatam raṇe na ākṣipanti mahātmānaḥ tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ca samara ślāghī tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ yāvat bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ vigāhya mahatīm camūm sodarān te na mṛdnāti tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ pūrvam uktaḥ ca te bhrātā bhīṣmeṇa sa suyodhanaḥ ajeyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ saṃkhye saumya saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ sa yuddhe dhṛtim āsthāya yattaḥ yudhyasva pāṇḍavaiḥ gaccha tūrṇam rathena eva tatra tiṣṭhati sātyakiḥ tvayā hīnam balam hi etat vidraviṣyati bhārata śrutam ca a śruta vat kṛtvā prāyāt yena sa sātyakiḥ droṇaḥ api rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ pāñcālān pāṇḍavān tathā praviśya ca raṇe droṇaḥ pāñcālānām varūthinīm drāvayām āsa yodhān vai śataśas atha sahasraśas tatas droṇaḥ mahā rāja nāma viśrāvya saṃyuge pāṇḍu pāñcāla matsyānām pracakre kadanam mahat tam jayantam anīkāni bhāradvājam tatas tatas pāñcāla putraḥ dyutimān vīraketuḥ samabhyayāt sa droṇam pañcabhiḥ viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tatra adbhutam mahā rāja dṛṣṭavān asmi saṃyuge yat droṇaḥ rabhasam yuddhe pāñcālyam na abhyavartata saṃniruddham raṇe droṇam pāñcālāḥ vīkṣya māriṣa āvavruḥ sarvatas rājan dharmaputra jaya eṣiṇaḥ te śaraiḥ agni saṃkāśaiḥ tomaraiḥ ca mahādhanaiḥ nihatya tān bāṇa gaṇān droṇaḥ rājan samantataḥ mahā jaladharān vyomni mātariśvā vivān iva tatas śaram mahā ghoram sūrya pāvaka saṃnibham sa bhittvā tu śaraḥ rājan pāñcālyam kula nandanam abhyagāt dharaṇīm tūrṇam lohita ārdraḥ jvalan iva tatas apatat rathāt tūrṇam pāñcālyaḥ kula nandanaḥ parvata agrāt iva mahān campakaḥ vāyu pīḍitaḥ pāñcālāḥ tvaritāḥ droṇam samantāt paryavārayan tathā citrarathaḥ ca eva bhrātṛ vyasana karṣitāḥ muñcantaḥ śara varṣāṇi tapānte jaladāḥ iva vyaśva sūta rathān cakre kumārān kupitaḥ raṇe tathā aparaiḥ su niśitaiḥ bhallaiḥ teṣām mahā yaśāḥ puṣpāṇi iva vicinvan hi sa uttamāṅgāni apātayat devāsure purā yuddhe yathā daiteya dānavāḥ tān nihatya raṇe rājan bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān kārmukam bhrāmayām āsa hema pṛṣṭham durāsadam pāñcālān nihatān dṛṣṭvā deva kalpān mahā rathān dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ netrābhyām pātayan jalam pāñcālyena raṇe dṛṣṭvā droṇam āvāritam śaraiḥ saṃchādyamānaḥ bahudhā pārṣatena mahātmanā tatas droṇam mahā rāja pāñcālyaḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ sa gāḍha viddhaḥ balinā bhāradvājaḥ mahā yaśāḥ tam vai tathāgatam dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ parākramī samutsṛjya dhanuḥ tūrṇam asim jagrāha vīryavān āruroha ratham tūrṇam bhāradvājasya māriṣa yodhayām āsa samare dhṛṣṭadyumnam mahā ratham te hi vaitastikāḥ nāma śarāḥ āsanna yodhinaḥ droṇasya viditāḥ rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnam avākṣipan avaplutya rathāt tūrṇam bhagna vegaḥ parākramī vivyādha samare droṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ kṣatriyāḥ ca mahā rāja ye ca anye tatra sainikāḥ avaśyam samare droṇaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnena saṃgataḥ vaśam eṣyati naḥ rājñaḥ pāñcālāḥ iti cukruśuḥ śiraḥ pracyāvayām āsa phalam pakvam taroḥ iva tatas te pradrutāḥ vāhāḥ rājan tasya mahātmanaḥ teṣu pradravamāṇeṣu pāñcālān sṛñjayān tathā vijitya pāṇḍu pāñcālān bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān svam vyūham punar āsthāya sthiraḥ abhavat ariṃdamaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas duḥśāsanaḥ rājan śaineyam samupādravat kiran śara sahasrāṇi parjanyaḥ iva vṛṣṭimān sa viddhvā sātyakim ṣaṣṭyā tathā ṣoḍaśabhiḥ śaraiḥ sa tu duḥśāsanam vīraḥ sāyakaiḥ āvṛṇot bhṛśam maśakam samanuprāptam ūrṇanābhiḥ iva ūrṇayā dṛṣṭvā duḥśāsanam rājā tathā śara śata ācitam trigartān codayām āsa yuyudhāna ratham prati te agacchan yuyudhānasya samīpam krūra kāriṇaḥ trigartānām tri sāhasrāḥ rathāḥ yuddha viśāradāḥ sthirām kṛtvā matim yuddhe bhūtvā saṃśaptakāḥ mithas teṣām prayatatām yuddhe śara varṣāṇi muñcatām yodhān pañcaśatān mukhyān agra anīke vyapothayat te apatanta hatāḥ tūrṇam śini pravara sāyakaiḥ mahā māruta vegena rugṇāḥ iva mahā drumāḥ hayaiḥ ca kanaka āpīḍaiḥ patitaiḥ tatra medinī śaineya śara saṃkṛttaiḥ śoṇita ogha pariplutaiḥ aśobhata mahā rāja kiṃśukaiḥ iva puṣpitaiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ samare yuyudhānena tāvakāḥ trātāram na adhyagacchanta paṅka magnāḥ iva dvipāḥ bhayāt pataga rājasya gartāni iva mahā uragāḥ hatvā pañcaśatān yodhān śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ tam prayāntam nara śreṣṭham putraḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tava vivyādha navabhiḥ tūrṇam śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ sa tu tam prativivyādha pañcabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tribhiḥ viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ śaineyaḥ tava putram tu viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ tatas duḥśāsanaḥ kruddhaḥ vṛṣṇi vīrāya gacchate sarva pāraśavīm śaktim visasarja jighāṃsayā tām tu śaktim tadā ghorām tava putrasya sātyakiḥ ciccheda śatadhā rājan niśitaiḥ kaṅka patribhiḥ sātyakim daśabhiḥ viddhvā siṃhanādam nanāda ha śaraiḥ agni śikhā ākāraiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare sarva āyasaiḥ tīkṣṇa vaktraiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ vivyadhe punar duḥśāsanaḥ tu viṃśatyā sātyakim pratyavidhyata sātvataḥ api mahā rāja tam vivyādha stanāntare tatas asya vāhān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ jaghne mahā rathaḥ sārathim ca su saṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ dhvajam ca ratha śaktim ca bhallābhyām parama astra vid ciccheda viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī bhīmasenena hi vadhaḥ sutānām tava bhārata pratijñātaḥ sabhā madhye sarveṣām eva saṃyuge tathā duḥśāsanam jitvā sātyakiḥ saṃyuge prabho dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca kim tasyām mama senāyām na āsan ke cit mahā rathāḥ ye tathā sātyakim yāntam na eva aghnan na api avārayan atha vā śūnyam āsīt tat yena yātaḥ sa sātyakiḥ ekaḥ vai bahulāḥ senāḥ pramṛdnan puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ katham ca yudhyamānānām apakrāntaḥ mahātmanām ekaḥ bahūnām śaineyaḥ tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca rājan senā samudyogaḥ ratha nāga aśva pattimān tumulaḥ tava sainyānām yuga anta sadṛśaḥ abhavat āhṇikeṣu samūheṣu tava sainyasya mānada tatra devāḥ sma bhāṣante cāraṇāḥ ca samāgatāḥ etat antāḥ samūhāḥ vai bhaviṣyanti mahī tale na ca eva tādṛśaḥ kaḥ cit vyūhaḥ āsīt viśām pate caṇḍa vāta abhipannānām samudrāṇām iva svanaḥ pārthivānām sametānām bahūni āsan narottama tvad bale pāṇḍavānām ca sahasrāṇi śatāni ca saṃrabdhānām pravīrāṇām samare dṛḍha karmaṇām tatra āsīt su mahān śabdaḥ tumulaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ athā akrandat bhīmasenaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca māriṣa nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca dharmarājaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ praviṣṭau ari senām hi vīrau mādhava pāṇḍavau tayoḥ abhāve kuravaḥ kṛtārthāḥ syuḥ vayam jitāḥ te yūyam sahitāḥ bhūtvā tūrṇam eva bala arṇavam kṣobhayadhvam mahā vegāḥ pavanāḥ sāgaram yathā bhīmasenena te rājan pāñcālyena ca coditāḥ ājaghnuḥ kauravān saṃkhye tyaktvā asūn ātmanaḥ priyān svarga artham mitra kārya artham na abhyarakṣanta jīvitam āryām yuddhe matim kṛtvā yuddhāya eva upatasthire hatvā sarvāṇi sainyāni prāyāt sātyakiḥ arjunam kavacānām prabhāḥ tatra sūrya raśmi vicitritāḥ dṛṣṭīḥ saṃkhye sainikānām pratijaghnuḥ samantataḥ tathā prayatamāneṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu nirbhayaḥ sa saṃnipātaḥ tumulaḥ teṣām tasya ca bhārata dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca kaccit duryodhanaḥ sūta na akārṣīt pṛṣṭhatas raṇam ekasya ca bahūnām ca saṃnipātaḥ mahā āhave viśeṣataḥ nṛpatinā viṣamaḥ pratibhāti me ekaḥ bahūn samāsādya kaccit na āsīt parāṅmukhaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca rājan saṃgrāmam āścaryam tava putrasya bhārata ekasya ca bahūnām ca śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ adbhutam duryodhanena sahasā pāṇḍavī pṛtanā raṇe tathā senām kṛtām dṛṣṭvā tava putreṇa kaurava bhīmasena purogāḥ tam pāñcālāḥ samupādravan virāṭa drupadau ṣaḍbhiḥ śatena ca śikhaṇḍinam dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca viṃśatyā dharmaputram ca saptabhiḥ śataśas ca aparān yodhān sa dvipān ca rathān raṇe na saṃdadhan vimuñcan vā maṇḍalīkṛta kārmukaḥ adṛśyata ripūn nighnan śikṣayā astra balena ca tasya tān nighnataḥ śatrūn hema pṛṣṭham mahat dhanuḥ bhallābhyām pāṇḍavaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ tridhā ciccheda māriṣa vivyādha ca enam bahubhiḥ samyak astaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ varmāṇi āśu samāsādya te bhagnāḥ kṣitim āviśan tatas pramuditāḥ pārthāḥ parivavruḥ yudhiṣṭhiram yathā vṛtra vadhe devāḥ mudā śakram mahā ṛṣibhiḥ atha duryodhanaḥ rājā dṛḍham ādāya kārmukam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti rājānam bruvan pāṇḍavam abhyayāt tam tathā vādinam rājan tava putram mahā ratham pratyudyayuḥ pramuditāḥ pāñcālāḥ jaya gṛddhinaḥ tān droṇaḥ pratijagrāha parīpsan yudhi pāṇḍavam caṇḍa vāta uddhutān meghān sa jalān acalaḥ yathā tatra rājan mahān āsīt saṃgrāmaḥ bhūri vardhanaḥ rudrasya ākrīḍa saṃkāśaḥ saṃhāraḥ sarva dehinām saṃjayaḥ uvāca aparāhṇe mahā rāja saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata śoṇa aśvam ratham āsthāya nara vīraḥ samāhitaḥ samare abhyadravat pāṇḍūn javam āsthāya madhyamam citra puṅkhaiḥ śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ kalaśa uttama saṃbhavaḥ varān varān hi yodhānām vicinvan iva bhārata akrīḍata raṇe rājan bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān tam abhyayāt bṛhatkṣatraḥ kekayānām mahā rathaḥ bhrātṝṇām vīra pañcānām jyeṣṭhaḥ samara karkaśaḥ vimuñcan viśikhān tīkṣṇān ācāryam chādayan bhṛśam mahā meghaḥ yathā varṣam vimuñcan gandhamādane tasya droṇaḥ mahā rāja svarṇa puṅkhān śilā śitān preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ sāyakān daśa sapta ca tān tu droṇa dhanuḥ muktān ghorān āśīviṣa upamān ekaikam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ yudhi ciccheda hṛṣṭa vat tasya tat lāghavam dṛṣṭvā prahasan dvijasattamaḥ preṣayām āsa viśikhān aṣṭau saṃnata parvaṇaḥ tān dṛṣṭvā patataḥ śīghram droṇa cāpa cyutān śarān bṛhatkṣatreṇa tat karma kṛtam dṛṣṭvā su duṣkaram tatas droṇaḥ mahā rāja kekayam vai viśeṣayan prāduścakre raṇe divyam brāhmam astram mahā tapāḥ brāhmeṇa eva mahā bāhuḥ āhave samudīritam vivyādha brāhmaṇam ṣaṣṭyā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ tam droṇaḥ dvipadām śreṣṭhaḥ nārācena samarpayat kṛṣṇasarpaḥ yathā muktaḥ valmīkam nṛpa sattama tathā abhyagāt mahīm bāṇaḥ bhittvā kaikeyam āhave saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā rāja droṇena astra vidā bhṛśam krodhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ vyāvṛtya nayane śubhe droṇam vivyādha saptatyā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ droṇaḥ tu bahudhā viddhaḥ bṛhatkṣatreṇa māriṣa asṛjat viśikhān tīkṣṇān kekayasya ratham prati vyākulīkṛtya tam droṇaḥ bṛhatkṣatram mahā ratham vyasṛjat sāyakam tīkṣṇam kekayam prati bhārata sa gāḍha viddhaḥ tena āśu mahā rāja stanāntare rathāt puruṣa śārdūlaḥ saṃbhinna hṛdayaḥ apatat bṛhatkṣatre hate rājan kekayānām mahā rathe śaiśupāliḥ su saṃkruddhaḥ yantāram idam abravīt sārathe yāhi yatra eṣa droṇaḥ tiṣṭhati daṃśitaḥ vinighnan kekayān sarvān pāñcālānām ca vāhinīm tasya tat vacanam śrutvā sārathiḥ rathinām varam droṇāya prāpayām āsa kāmbojaiḥ javanaiḥ hayaiḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca cedīnām ṛṣabhaḥ ati bala uditaḥ sahasā prāpatat droṇam pataṃgaḥ iva pāvakam saḥ abhyavidhyat tatas droṇam ṣaṣṭyā sa aśva ratha dhvajam punar ca anyaiḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ suptam vyāghram tudan iva atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya śaiśupāliḥ mahā rathaḥ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ droṇam punar su niśitaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ tasya droṇaḥ hayān hatvā sārathim ca mahā balaḥ atha enam pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānām samārpayat gadām cikṣepa saṃkruddhaḥ bhāradvāja ratham prati tām āpatantīm sahasā ghora rūpām bhaya āvahām aśmasāra mayīm gurvīm tapanīya vibhūṣitām sā papāta gadā bhūmau bhāradvājena sāditā gadām vinihatām dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭaketuḥ amarṣaṇaḥ tomaram vyasṛjat tūrṇam śaktim ca kanaka ujjvalām tomaram tu tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ droṇaḥ chittvā mahā mṛdhe śaktim ciccheda sahasā kṛtahastaḥ mahā balaḥ tatas asya viśikham tīkṣṇam vadha artham vadha kāṅkṣiṇaḥ preṣayām āsa samare bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān sa tasya kavacam bhittvā hṛdayam ca amita ojasaḥ abhyagāt dharaṇīm bāṇaḥ haṃsaḥ padma saraḥ yathā pataṃgam hi graset cāṣaḥ yathā rājan bubhukṣitaḥ tathā droṇaḥ agrasat śūraḥ dhṛṣṭaketum mahā mṛdhe nihate cedi rāje tu tat khaṇḍam pitryam āviśat mahā vyāghraḥ mahā araṇye mṛga śāvam yathā balī teṣu prakṣīyamāṇeṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu bhārata jarāsaṃdha sutaḥ vīraḥ svayam droṇam upādravat sa tu droṇam mahā rāja chādayan sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ adṛśyam akarot tūrṇam jaladaḥ bhāskaram yathā tasya tat lāghavam dṛṣṭvā droṇaḥ kṣatriya mardanaḥ vyasṛjat sāyakān tūrṇam śataśas atha sahasraśas chādayitvā raṇe droṇaḥ ratha stham rathinām varam jārāsaṃdhim atho jaghne miṣatām sarva dhanvinām yaḥ yaḥ sma līyate droṇam tam tam droṇaḥ antaka upamaḥ ādatta sarva bhūtāni prāpte kāle yathā antakaḥ tatas droṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ nāma viśrāvya saṃyuge śaraiḥ aneka sāhasraiḥ pāṇḍaveyān vyamohayat tatas droṇa aṅkitāḥ bāṇāḥ svarṇa puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ narān nāgān hayān ca eva nijaghnuḥ sarvatas raṇe te vadhyamānāḥ droṇena śakreṇa iva mahā asurāḥ samakampanta pāñcālāḥ gāvaḥ śīta arditāḥ iva tatas niṣṭānakaḥ ghoraḥ pāṇḍavānām ajāyata mohitāḥ śara varṣeṇa bhāradvājasya saṃyuge ūru grāha gṛhītāḥ hi pāñcālānām mahā rathāḥ cedayaḥ ca mahā rāja sṛñjayāḥ somakāḥ tathā abhyadravanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ bhāradvājam yuyutsayā yatantaḥ puruṣa vyāghrāḥ sarva śaktyā mahā dyutim ninīṣantaḥ raṇe droṇam yamasya sadanam prati yatamānān tu tān vīrān bhāradvājaḥ śilīmukhaiḥ yamāya preṣayām āsa cedi mukhyān viśeṣataḥ teṣu prakṣīyamāṇeṣu cedi mukhyeṣu bhārata pāñcālāḥ samakampanta droṇa sāyaka pīḍitāḥ prākrośan bhīmasenam te dhṛṣṭadyumna ratham prati dṛṣṭvā droṇasya karmāṇi tathārūpāṇi māriṣa brāhmaṇena tapaḥ nūnam caritam duścaram mahat droṇa astram agni saṃsparśam praviṣṭāḥ kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ yathābalam yathotsāham yathāsattvam mahā dyutiḥ teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā kṣatradharmā vyavasthitaḥ sa saṃrabdhataraḥ bhūtvā droṇaḥ kṣatriya mardanaḥ tatra ādhāya śaram tīkṣṇam bhāra ghnam vimalam dṛḍham ākarṇapūrṇam ācāryaḥ balavān abhyavāsṛjat sa hatvā kṣatradharmāṇam jagāma dharaṇī talam atha droṇam samārohat cekitānaḥ mahā rathaḥ sa droṇam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat stanāntare tasya ācāryaḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ avidhyat dakṣiṇam bhujam dhvajam ṣoḍaśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ yantāram ca asya saptabhiḥ tasya sūte hate te aśvāḥ ratham ādāya vidrutāḥ samare śara saṃvītāḥ bhāradvājena māriṣa cekitāna ratham dṛṣṭvā vidrutam hata sārathim pāñcālān pāṇḍavān ca eva mahat bhayam atha āviśat tān sametān raṇe śūrān cedi pāñcāla sṛñjayān samantāt drāvayan droṇaḥ bahu aśobhata māriṣa ākarṇa palitaḥ śyāmaḥ vayasā aśītikāt paraḥ raṇe paryacarat droṇaḥ vṛddhaḥ ṣoḍaśa varṣa vat lubdhaḥ ayam kṣatriyān hanti vyāghraḥ kṣudra mṛgān iva kṛcchrān duryodhanaḥ lokān pāpaḥ prāpsyati durmatiḥ yasya lobhāt vinihatāḥ samare kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ śataśas śerate bhūmau nikṛttāḥ go vṛṣāḥ iva rudhireṇa parīta aṅgāḥ śva sṛgāla adanīkṛtāḥ evam uktvā mahā rāja drupadaḥ akṣauhiṇī patiḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca vyūheṣu āloḍyamāneṣu pāṇḍavānām tatas tatas su dūram anvayuḥ pārthāḥ pāñcālāḥ saha somakaiḥ vartamāne tathā raudre saṃgrāme loma harṣaṇe pāñcāleṣu ca kṣīṇeṣu vadhyamāneṣu pāṇḍuṣu na apaśyat śaraṇam kim cit dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tatra avekṣya diśaḥ sarvāḥ savyasāci didṛkṣayā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dadarśa atha nā eva pārtham na mādhavam saḥ apaśyat nara śārdūlam vānara ṛṣabha lakṣaṇam gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣam aśṛṇvan vyathita indriyaḥ apaśyan sātyakim ca api vṛṣṇīnām pravaram ratham cintayā abhiparīta aṅgaḥ dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ na adhyagacchat tadā śāntim tau apaśyān nara ṛṣabhau loka upakrośa bhīru tvāt dharmarājaḥ mahā yaśāḥ padavīm preṣitaḥ ca eva phalgunasya mayā raṇe śaineyaḥ sātyakiḥ satyaḥ mitrāṇām abhayaṃkaraḥ tat idam hi ekam eva āsīt dvidhā jātam mama adya vai sātyakiḥ ca hi me jñeyaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ ca dhanaṃjayaḥ sātyakim preṣayitvā tu pāṇḍavasya padānugam sātvatasya api kam yuddhe preṣayiṣye padānugam kariṣyāmi prayatnena bhrātuḥ anveṣaṇam yadi bhrātuḥ anveṣaṇam kṛtvā dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ loka apavāda bhīru tvāt saḥ aham pārtham vṛkodaram padavīm preṣayiṣyāmi mādhavasya mahātmanaḥ praviṣṭaḥ bhāratīm senām makaraḥ sāgaram yathā asau hi śrūyate śabdaḥ śūrāṇām anivartinām mithas saṃyudhyamānānām vṛṣṇi vīreṇa dhīmatā śaktaḥ hi eṣa raṇe yattān pṛthivyām sarva dhanvinaḥ sva bāhu balam āsthāya prativyūhitum añjasā yasya bāhu balam sarve samāśritya mahātmanaḥ vana vāsāt nivṛttāḥ sma na ca yuddheṣu nirjitāḥ itas gate bhīmasene sātvatam prati pāṇḍave kāmam tu a śocanīyau tau raṇe sātvata phalgunau rakṣitau vāsudevena svayam ca astra viśāradau avaśyam tu mayā kāryam ātmanaḥ śoka nāśanam tasmāt bhīmam niyokṣyāmi sātvatasya padānugam tatas pratikṛtam manye vidhānam sātyakim prati dharmarāja vacaḥ śrutvā sārathiḥ haya kovidaḥ ratham hema pariṣkāram bhīma antikam upānayat kaśmalam prāviśat rājā bahu tatra samādiśan na eva adrākṣam na ca aśrauṣam tava kaśmalam īdṛśam purā hi duḥkha dīrṇānām bhavān gatiḥ abhūt hi naḥ uttiṣṭha uttiṣṭha rāja indra śādhi kim karavāṇi te ājñāpaya kuru śreṣṭha mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ tam abravīt aśru pūrṇaḥ kṛṣṇa sarpaḥ iva śvasan bhīmasenam idam vākyam pramlāna vadanaḥ nṛpaḥ yathā śaṅkhasya nirghoṣaḥ pāñcajanyasya śrūyate nūnam adya hataḥ śete tava bhrātā dhanaṃjayaḥ yasya sattvavataḥ vīryam upajīvanti pāṇḍavāḥ yam bhayeṣu abhigacchanti sahasrākṣam iva amarāḥ sa śūraḥ saindhava prepsuḥ anvayāt bhāratīm camūm śyāmaḥ yuvā guḍākeśaḥ darśanīyaḥ mahā bhujaḥ arjuna artham mahā bāho sātvatasya ca kāraṇāt vardhate haviṣā iva agniḥ idhyamānaḥ punar punar tam viddhi puruṣa vyāghram sātvatam ca mahā ratham sa tam mahā ratham paścāt anuyātaḥ tava anujam tam apaśyān mahā bāhum aham vindāmi kaśmalam tasmāt kṛṣṇaḥ raṇe nūnam yudhyate yuddha kovidaḥ yasya vīryavataḥ vīryam upajīvanti pāṇḍavāḥ sātyakiḥ ca mahā vīryaḥ kartavyam yadi manyase vacanam mama dharma jña jyeṣṭhaḥ bhrātā bhavāmi te na te arjunaḥ tathā jñeyaḥ jñātavyaḥ sātyakiḥ yathā cikīrṣuḥ mad priyam pārtha prayātaḥ savyasācinaḥ padavīm durgamām ghorām agamyām akṛtātmabhiḥ brahma īśāna indra varuṇān avahat yaḥ purā rathaḥ ājñām tu śirasā bibhrat eṣa gacchāmi mā śucaḥ sametya tān nara vyāghrān tava dāsyāmi saṃvidam saṃjayaḥ uvāca dhṛṣṭadyumnāya balavān suhṛdbhyaḥ ca punar punar dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca idam āha bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ viditam te mahā bāho yathā droṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ na ca me gamane kṛtyam tādṛś pārṣata vidyate yādṛśam rakṣaṇe rājñaḥ kāryam ātyayikam hi naḥ prayāsye tatra yatra asau mumūrṣuḥ saindhavaḥ sthitaḥ etat hi sarva kāryāṇām paramam kṛtyam āhave tam abravīt mahā rāja dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ vṛkodaram īpsitena mahā bāho gaccha pārtha a vicārayan na a hatvā samare droṇaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam katham cana tatas nikṣipya rājānam dhṛṣṭadyumnāya pāṇḍavaḥ āghrātaḥ ca tathā mūrdhni śrāvitaḥ ca āśiṣaḥ śubhāḥ bhīmasenaḥ mahā bāhuḥ kavacī śubha kuṇḍalī sa aṅgadaḥ sa tanutrāṇaḥ sa śarī rathinām varaḥ pīta rakta asita sitaiḥ vāsobhiḥ ca su veṣṭitaḥ kaṇṭha trāṇena ca babhau sa indrāyudhaḥ iva ambudaḥ pāñcajanya ravaḥ ghoraḥ punar āsīt viśām pate tam śrutvā ninadam ghoram trailokya trāsanam mahat eṣa vṛṣṇi pravīreṇa dhmātaḥ salilajaḥ bhṛśam pṛthivīm ca antarikṣam ca vinādayati śaṅkha rāj nūnam āryā mahat kuntī pāpam adya nidarśanam muhyanti iva hi me sarvāḥ dhanaṃjaya didṛkṣayā diśaḥ sa pradiśaḥ pārtha sātvatasya ca kāraṇāt bhṛśam sa prahitaḥ bhrātrā bhrātā bhrātuḥ priyaṃkaraḥ āhatya dundubhim bhīmaḥ śaṅkham pradhmāya ca asakṛt vinadya siṃhanādam ca jyām vikarṣan punar punar tam ūhuḥ javanāḥ dāntāḥ vikurvāṇāḥ haya uttamāḥ viśokena abhisaṃyattāḥ manaḥ māruta raṃhasaḥ ārujan virujan pārthaḥ jyām vikarṣan ca pāṇinā saḥ avakarṣan vikarṣan ca senā agram samaloḍayat tam prayāntam mahā bāhum pāñcālāḥ saha somakāḥ pṛṣṭhatas anuyayuḥ śūrāḥ maghavantam iva amarāḥ tam sa senāḥ mahā rāja sodaryāḥ paryavārayan duḥśalaḥ citrasenaḥ ca kuṇḍabhedī viviṃśatiḥ vṛndārakaḥ suhastaḥ ca suṣeṇaḥ dīrghalocanaḥ vividhaiḥ rathinām śreṣṭhāḥ saha sainyaiḥ saha anugaiḥ saṃyattāḥ samare śūrāḥ bhīmasenam upādravan tān samīkṣya tu kaunteyaḥ bhīmasenaḥ parākramī te mahā astrāṇi divyāni tatra vīrāḥ adarśayan vārayantaḥ śaraiḥ bhīmam meghāḥ sūryam iva uditam sa tān atītya vegena droṇa anīkam upādravat agratas ca gaja anīkam śara varṣaiḥ avākirat saḥ acireṇa eva kālena tat gaja anīkam āśugaiḥ trāsitāḥ śarabhasya iva garjitena vane mṛgāḥ punar ca atītya vegena droṇa anīkam upādravat lalāṭe atāḍayat ca enam nārācena smayan iva ūrdhva raśmiḥ iva ādityaḥ vibabhau tatra pāṇḍavaḥ sa manyamānaḥ tu ācāryaḥ mama ayam phalgunaḥ yathā bhīmaḥ kariṣyate pūjām iti uvāca vṛkodaram bhīmasena na te śakyam praveṣṭum ari vāhinīm yadi te saḥ anujaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ praviṣṭaḥ anumate mama anīkam na tu śakyam bhoḥ praveṣṭum iha vai tvayā kruddhaḥ provāca vai droṇam rakta tāmra īkṣaṇaḥ śvasan praviṣṭaḥ sa hi durdharṣaḥ śakrasya api viśet balam yena vai paramām pūjām kurvatā mānitaḥ hi asi na arjunaḥ aham ghṛṇī droṇa bhīmasenaḥ asmi te ripuḥ iti manyāmahe sarve bhavantam praṇatāḥ sthitāḥ eṣa te sadṛśam śatroḥ karma bhīmaḥ karomi aham athā udbhrāmya gadām bhīmaḥ kāla daṇḍam iva antakaḥ droṇāya avasṛjat rājan sa rathāt avapupluve sa aśva sūta dhvajam yānam droṇasya apothayat tadā prāmṛdnāt ca bahūn yodhān vāyuḥ vṛkṣān iva ojasā anyam ca ratham āsthāya droṇaḥ praharatām varaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ mahā rāja bhīmasenaḥ parākramī agratas syandana anīkam śara varṣaiḥ avākirat te vadhyamānāḥ samare tava putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ bhīmam bhīma balam yuddhe ayodhayan tu jaya eṣiṇaḥ tatas duḥśāsanaḥ kruddhaḥ ratha śaktim samākṣipat sarva pāraśavīm tīkṣṇām jighāṃsuḥ pāṇḍu nandanam āpatantīm mahā śaktim tava putra pracoditām athā anyaiḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ saṃkruddhaḥ kuṇḍabhedinam suṣeṇam dīrghanetram ca tribhiḥ trīn avadhīt balī tatas vṛndārakam vīram kurūṇām kīrti vardhanam putrāṇām tava vīrāṇām yudhyatām avadhīt punar vadhyamānāḥ mahā rāja putrāḥ tava balīyasā bhīmam praharatām śreṣṭham samantāt paryavārayan tatas sudarśanam vīram putram te bharata ṛṣabha vivyādha samare tūrṇam sa papāta mamāra ca saḥ acireṇa eva kālena tat ratha anīkam āśugaiḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ samabhyasya vyadhamat pāṇḍu nandanaḥ vadhyamānāḥ ca samare putrāḥ tava viśām pate prādravan sa rathāḥ sarve bhīmasena bhaya arditāḥ anuyāya tu kaunteyaḥ putrāṇām te mahat balam vadhyamānāḥ mahā rāja bhīmasenena tāvakāḥ siṃhanāda ravam cakre bāhu śabdam ca pāṇḍavaḥ tala śabdam ca su mahat kṛtvā bhīmaḥ mahā balaḥ vyatītya rathinaḥ ca api droṇa anīkam upādravat saṃjayaḥ uvāca tam uttīrṇam ratha anīkāt tamasaḥ bhāskaram yathā didhārayiṣuḥ ācāryaḥ śara varṣaiḥ avākirat piban iva śara oghān tān droṇa cāpa vara atigān tam mṛdhe vegam āsthāya param parama dhanvinaḥ sa tathā saṃvṛtaḥ bhīmaḥ prahasan iva bhārata udayacchat gadām tebhyaḥ ghorām tām siṃha vat nadan sa indra aśaniḥ iva indreṇa praviddhā saṃhata ātmanā ghoṣeṇa mahatā rājan pūrayitvā iva medinīm jvalantī tejasā bhīmā trāsayām āsa te sutān tām patantīm mahā vegām dṛṣṭvā tejobhiḥ saṃvṛtām prādravan tāvakāḥ sarve nadantaḥ bhairavān ravān tam ca śabdam asaṃsahyam tasyāḥ saṃlakṣya māriṣa sa tān vidrāvya kaunteyaḥ saṃkhye amitrān durāsadaḥ suparṇaḥ iva vegena pakṣirāj atyagāt camūm tathā tam viprakurvāṇam ratha yūthapa yūthapam bhāradvājaḥ mahā rāja bhīmasenam samabhyayāt droṇaḥ tu samare bhīmam vārayitvā śara ūrmibhiḥ akarot sahasā nādam pāṇḍūnām bhayam ādadhat droṇasya ca mahā rāja bhīmasya ca mahātmanaḥ yadā tu viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ droṇa cāpa viniḥsṛtaiḥ vadhyante samare vīrāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas tatas rathāt avaplutya vegam āsthāya pāṇḍavaḥ yathā hi go vṛṣaḥ varṣam pratigṛhṇāti līlayā tathā bhīmaḥ nara vyāghraḥ śara varṣam samagrahīt sa vadhyamānaḥ samare ratham droṇasya māriṣa īṣāyām pāṇinā gṛhya pracikṣepa mahā balaḥ ratham anyam samāsthāya vyūha dvāram upāyayau tasmin kṣaṇe tasya yantā tūrṇam aśvān acodayat tatas sva ratham āsthāya bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ sa mṛdnan kṣatriyān ājau vātaḥ vṛkṣān iva uddhataḥ bhoja anīkam samāsādya hārdikyena abhirakṣitam saṃtrāsayan anīkāni tala śabdena māriṣa ajayat sarva sainyāni śārdūlaḥ iva go vṛṣān bhoja anīkam atikramya kāmbojānām ca vāhinīm tathā mleccha gaṇān ca anyān bahūn yuddha viśāradān sātyakim ca api saṃprekṣya yudhyamānam nara ṛṣabham bhīmasenaḥ mahā rāja draṣṭu kāmaḥ dhanaṃjayam atītya samare yodhān tāvakān pāṇḍu nandanaḥ saindhavasya vadha artham hi parākrāntam parākramī arjunam tatra dṛṣṭvā atha cukrośa mahataḥ ravān tam tu tasya mahā nādam pārthaḥ śuśrāva nardataḥ tatas pārthaḥ mahā nādam muñcan vai mādhavaḥ ca ha abhyayātām mahā rāja nardantau go vṛṣau iva vāsudeva arjunau śrutvā ninādam tasya śuṣmiṇaḥ punar punar praṇadatām didṛkṣantau vṛkodaram aprīyata mahā rāja dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ viśokaḥ ca abhavat rājā śrutvā tam ninadam mahat dhanaṃjayasya ca raṇe jayam āśā stavān vibhuḥ smitam kṛtvā mahā bāhuḥ dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ hṛdgatam manasā prāha dhyātvā dharma bhṛtām varaḥ dattā bhīma tvayā saṃvid kṛtam guru vacaḥ tathā na hi teṣām jayaḥ yuddhe yeṣām dveṣṭā asi pāṇḍava diṣṭyā jīvati saṃgrāme savyasācī dhanaṃjayaḥ diṣṭyā ca kuśalī vīraḥ sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ diṣṭyā śṛṇomi garjantau vāsudeva dhanaṃjayau yena śakram raṇe jitvā tarpitaḥ havyavāhanaḥ sa hantā dviṣatām saṃkhye diṣṭyā jīvati phalgunaḥ yasya bāhu balam sarve vayam āśritya jīvitāḥ sa hantā ripu sainyānām diṣṭyā jīvati phalgunaḥ nirjitāḥ rathinā ekena diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati yaḥ ajayat matsya nagare diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati kālakeya sahasrāṇi caturdaśa mahā raṇe yaḥ avadhīt bhuja vīryeṇa diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati jitavān yaḥ astra vīryeṇa diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati kirīṭamālī balavān śveta aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ mama priyaḥ ca satatam diṣṭyā jīvati phalgunaḥ putra śoka abhisaṃtaptaḥ cikīrṣuḥ karma duṣkaram jayadratha vadha anveṣī pratijñām kṛtavān hi yaḥ kaccit tīrṇa pratijñam hi vāsudevena rakṣitam dṛṣṭvā saindhavakam saṃkhye śamam asmāsu dhāsyati dṛṣṭvā vinihatān bhrātṝn bhīmasenena saṃyuge dṛṣṭvā ca anyān bahūn yodhān pātitān dharaṇī tale śeṣasya rakṣaṇa artham ca saṃdhāsyati suyodhanaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca tathā tu nardamānam tam bhīmasenam mahā balam megha stanita nirghoṣam ke vīrāḥ paryavārayan na hi paśyāmi aham tam vai triṣu lokeṣu saṃjaya na hi paśyāmi aham tāta yaḥ tiṣṭheta raṇa ajire ratham rathena yaḥ hanyāt kuñjaram kuñjareṇa ca kaḥ tasya samare sthātā sākṣāt api śatakratuḥ pradhakṣyataḥ raṇa mukhe ke vīrāḥ pramukhe sthitāḥ kālyamānān hi me putrān bhīmena avekṣya saṃyuge kālena iva prajāḥ sarvāḥ ke bhīmam paryavārayan ke śūrāḥ paryavartanta tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca tathā tu nardamānam tam bhīmasenam mahā ratham vyākṣipan balavat cāpam atimātram amarṣaṇaḥ karṇaḥ tu yuddham ākāṅkṣan darśayiṣyan balam balī prāvepan iva gātrāṇi karṇa bhīma samāgame rathinām sādinām ca eva tayoḥ śrutvā tala svanam bhīmasenasya ninadam ghoram śrutvā raṇa ajire kham ca bhūmim ca saṃbaddhām menire kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ punar ghoreṇa nādena pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ samare sarva yodhānām dhanūṃṣi abhyapatan kṣitau vitrastāni ca sarvāṇi śakṛt mūtram prasusruvuḥ vāhanāni mahā rāja babhūvuḥ vimanāṃsi ca prādurāsan nimittāni ghorāṇi ca bahūni ca tatas karṇaḥ tu viṃśatyā śarāṇām bhīmam ārdayat vivyādha ca asya tvaritaḥ sūtam pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ sāyakānām catuḥṣaṣṭyā kṣiprakārī mahā balaḥ tasya karṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ sāyakān caturaḥ akṣipat asaṃprāptān tu tān bhīmaḥ sāyakaiḥ nata parvabhiḥ ciccheda bahudhā rājan darśayan pāṇi lāghavam tam karṇaḥ chādayām āsa śara vrātaiḥ anekaśas saṃchādyamānaḥ karṇena bahudhā pāṇḍu nandanaḥ ciccheda cāpam karṇasya muṣṭideśe mahā rathaḥ atha anyat
