dhanuḥ ādāya sajyam kṛtvā ca sūtajaḥ vivyādha samare bhīmam bhīma karmā mahā rathaḥ tasya bhīmaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ trīn śarān nata parvaṇaḥ dhātu prasyandinaḥ śailāt yathā gairika rājayaḥ kim cit vicalitaḥ karṇaḥ su prahāra abhipīḍitaḥ sa sāyakam dhanuḥ kṛtvā bhīmam vivyādha māriṣa cikṣepa ca punar bāṇān śataśas atha sahasraśas sa chādyamānaḥ sahasā karṇena dṛḍha dhanvinā dhanuḥ jyām acchinat tūrṇam utsmayan pāṇḍu nandanaḥ sārathim ca asya bhallena prāhiṇot yama sādanam vāhān ca caturaḥ saṃkhye vyasūn cakre mahā rathaḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt karṇaḥ samāplutya viśām pate syandanam vṛṣasenasya samārohat mahā rathaḥ nirjitya tu raṇe karṇam bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān tasya tam ninadam śrutvā prahṛṣṭaḥ abhūt yudhiṣṭhiraḥ karṇam ca nirjitam matvā bhīmasenena bhārata samantāt śaṅkha ninadam pāṇḍu senā akarot tadā śatru senā dhvanim śrutvā tāvakāḥ hi api nānadan gāṇḍīvam prākṣipat pārthaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ api abjam avādayat aśrūyata mahā rāja sarva sainyeṣu bhārata mṛdu pūrvam ca rādheyaḥ dṛḍha pūrvam ca pāṇḍavaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tūrṇam abhyapatat droṇam manaḥ māruta vegavān arjunaḥ bhīmasenaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca aparājitaḥ saṃprāptāḥ sindhurājasya samīpam ari karśanāḥ vyāyacchanti ca tatra api sarve eva aparājitāḥ yadi tāvat raṇe pārthaḥ vyatikrāntaḥ mahā rathaḥ katham sātyaki bhīmābhyām vyatikrāntaḥ asi mānada āścarya bhūtam loke asmin samudrasya iva śoṣaṇam nāśaḥ eva tu me nūnam mandabhāgyasya saṃyuge yatra tvām puruṣa vyāghram atikrāntāḥ trayaḥ rathāḥ tat bravītu bhavān kṣipram sādhu tat saṃvidhīyatām droṇaḥ uvāca cintyam bahu mahā rāja kṛtyam yat tatra me śṛṇu trayaḥ hi samatikrāntāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ yāvat eva bhayam paścāt tāvat eṣām puraḥsaram sā purastāt ca paścāt ca gṛhītā bhāratī camūḥ na sabhāyām jayaḥ vṛttaḥ na api tatra parājayaḥ yān sma tān glahate ghorān śakuniḥ kuru saṃsadi akṣān saṃmanyamānaḥ sa pra kśarāḥ te durāsadāḥ senām durodaram viddhi śarān akṣān viśām pate atra sarve mahā rāja tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ tatra naḥ glahamānānām dhruvau tāta jaya ajayau tatra yāhi svayam śīghram tān ca rakṣasva rakṣiṇaḥ iha eva tu aham āsiṣye preṣayiṣyāmi ca aparān nirotsyāmi ca pāñcālān sahitān pāṇḍu sṛñjayaiḥ tatas duryodhanaḥ prāyāt tūrṇam ācārya śāsanāt udyamya ātmānam ugrāya karmaṇe sa padānugaḥ tau hi pūrvam mahā rāja vāritau kṛtavarmaṇā tvaritaḥ tvaramāṇābhyām bhrātṛbhyām bhārataḥ balī yudhāmanyuḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ śarān triṃśatam āyasān jaghāna caturaḥ ca aśvān ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī uttamaujāḥ hata aśvaḥ tu hata sūtaḥ ca saṃyuge sa ratham prāpya tam bhrātuḥ duryodhana hayān śaraiḥ bahubhiḥ tāḍayām āsa te hatāḥ prāpatan bhuvi yudhāmanyuḥ dhanuḥ śīghram śarāvāpam ca saṃyuge hata aśva sūtāt sa rathāt avaplutya mahā rathaḥ gadām ādāya te putraḥ pāñcālyau abhyadhāvata gadayā pothayām āsa sa aśva sūta dhvajam raṇe hatvā ca enam sa putraḥ te hata aśvaḥ hata sārathiḥ madra rāja ratham tūrṇam āruroha paraṃtapaḥ pāñcālānām tu mukhyau tau rāja putrau mahā balau dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca arjunasya ratha upānte kīdṛśaḥ saḥ abhavat raṇaḥ pūrvam hi nirjitaḥ karṇaḥ bhīmasenena saṃyuge katham bhūyas tu rādheyaḥ bhīmam āgāt mahā rathaḥ bhīmaḥ vā sūtatanayam pratyudyātaḥ katham raṇe mahā ratha samākhyātam pṛthivyām pravaram ratham bhīṣma droṇau atikramya dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ katham karṇam yudhām śreṣṭham bhīmaḥ ayudhyata saṃyuge katham nu tau ayudhyetām sūtaputra vṛkodarau bhrātṛ tvam darśitam pūrvam ghṛṇī ca api sa sūtajaḥ bhīmaḥ vā sūtaputreṇa smaran vairam purā kṛtam karṇaḥ jeṣyati saṃgrāme sahitān pāṇḍavān iti sa katham bhīma karmāṇam bhīmasenam ayudhyata yam samāśritya putraiḥ me kṛtam vairam mahā rathaiḥ tam sūta tanayam tāta katham bhīmaḥ hi ayodhayat anekān viprakārān ca sūtaputra samudbhavān smaramāṇaḥ katham bhīmaḥ yuyudhe sūtasūnunā yaḥ ajayat pṛthivīm sarvām rathena ekena vīryavān yaḥ jātaḥ kuṇḍalābhyām ca kavacena saha eva ca yathā tayoḥ yuddham abhūt yaḥ ca āsīt vijayī tayoḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca iyeṣa gantum yatra āstām vīrau kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau abhyavarṣat mahā rāja meghaḥ vṛṣṭyā iva parvatam ājuhāva raṇe yāntam bhīmam ādhirathiḥ tadā bhīmasenaḥ tad āhvānam karṇān nā amarṣayat yudhi dvairathe daṃśitam yattam sarva śastrabhṛtām varam vidhitsuḥ kalahasya antam jighāṃsuḥ karṇam akṣiṇot tam ca hatvā itarān sarvān hantu kāmaḥ mahā balaḥ tasmai prāsṛjat ugrāṇi vividhāni paraṃtapaḥ amarṣī pāṇḍavaḥ kruddhaḥ śara varṣāṇi māriṣa tasya tāni iṣu varṣāṇi matta dvirada gāminaḥ sūtaputraḥ astra māyābhiḥ agrasat su mahā yaśāḥ sa yathāvat mahā rāja vidyayā vai su pūjitaḥ ācārya vat mahā iṣvāsaḥ karṇaḥ paryacarat raṇe tat na amṛṣyata kaunteyaḥ karṇasya smitam āhave yudhyamāneṣu vīreṣu paśyatsu ca samantataḥ tam bhīmasenaḥ saṃprāptam vatsadantaiḥ stanāntare sūtam tu sūtaputrasya su puṅkhaiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ karṇaḥ jāmbūnadaiḥ jālaiḥ saṃchannān vāta raṃhasaḥ vivyādha turagān vīraḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas bāṇa mayam jālam bhīmasena ratham prati karṇena vihitam rājan nimeṣa ardhāt adṛśyata sa rathaḥ sa dhvajaḥ tatra sa sūtaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ tadā prācchādyata mahā rāja karṇa cāpa cyutaiḥ śaraiḥ tasya karṇaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā vyadhamat kavacam dṛḍham kruddhaḥ ca api ahanat pārśve nārācaiḥ marma bhedibhiḥ tatas a cintya mahā vegān karṇa kārmuka niḥsṛtān samāśliṣyat asaṃbhrāntaḥ sūtaputram vṛkodaraḥ sa karṇa cāpa prabhavān iṣūn āśīviṣa upamān bibhrat bhīmaḥ mahā rāja na jagāma vyathām raṇe vivyādha samare karṇam bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān bhīmasenam mahā bāhum saindhavasya vadha eṣiṇam mṛdu pūrvam ca rādheyaḥ bhīmam ājau ayodhayat tam bhīmasenaḥ na amṛṣyat avamānam amarṣaṇaḥ te śarāḥ preṣitāḥ rājan bhīmasenena saṃyuge nipetuḥ sarvatas bhīmāḥ kūjantaḥ iva pakṣiṇaḥ hema puṅkhāḥ mahā rāja bhīmasena dhanuḥ cyutāḥ abhyadravan te rādheyam vṛkāḥ kṣudra mṛgam yathā karṇaḥ tu rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ chādyamānaḥ samantataḥ rājan vyasṛjat ugrāṇi śara varṣāṇi saṃyuge tasya tān aśani prakhyān iṣūn samara śobhinaḥ punar ca śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhārata tatra bhārata bhīmam tu dṛṣṭavantaḥ sma sāyakaiḥ samācita tanum saṃkhye śvāvidham śalalaiḥ iva hema puṅkhān śilā dhautān karṇa cāpa cyutān śarān dadhāra samare vīraḥ sva raśmīn iva bhāskaraḥ tapanīya nibhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ palāśaḥ iva kānane tat tu bhīmaḥ mahā rāja karṇasya caritam raṇe na amṛṣyata mahā iṣvāsaḥ krodhāt udvṛtya cakṣuṣī sa karṇam pañcaviṃśatyā nārācānām samārpayat mahīdharam iva śvetam gūḍha pādaiḥ viṣa ulbaṇaiḥ tam vivyādha punar bhīmaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ eva ca marmasu amara vikrāntaḥ sūtaputram mahā raṇe tatas karṇasya saṃkruddhaḥ bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān ciccheda kārmukam tūrṇam sarva upakaraṇāni ca jaghāna caturaḥ ca aśvān sūtam ca tvaritaḥ śaraiḥ nārācaiḥ arka raśmi ābhaiḥ karṇam vivyādha ca urasi te jagmuḥ dharaṇīm sarve karṇam nirbhidya māriṣa yathā hi jaladam bhittvā rājan sūryasya raśmayaḥ tathā puruṣa mānī sa pratyapāyāt ratha antaram dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca yasmin jaya āśā satatam putrāṇām mama saṃjaya tam dṛṣṭvā vimukham saṃkhye kim nu duryodhanaḥ abravīt karṇaḥ vā samare tāta kim akārṣīt atas param saṃjayaḥ uvāca bhīmasenam raṇe dṛṣṭvā jvalantam iva pāvakam abhyayāt pāṇḍavam karṇaḥ vāta uddhūtaḥ iva arṇavaḥ kruddham ādhirathim dṛṣṭvā putrāḥ tava viśām pate cāpa śabdam mahat kṛtvā tala śabdam ca bhairavam punar eva tatas rājan mahān āsīt su dāruṇaḥ vimardaḥ sūtaputrasya bhīmasya ca viśām pate saṃrabdhau hi mahā bāhū paraspara vadha eṣiṇau anyonyam īkṣām cakrāte dahantau iva locanaiḥ vyāghrau iva su saṃrabdhau śyenau iva ca śīghra gau tatas bhīmaḥ smaran kleśān akṣa dyūte vane api ca virāṭa nagare ca eva prāptam duḥkham ariṃdamaḥ rāṣṭrāṇām sphīta ratnānām haraṇam ca tava ātmajaiḥ satatam ca parikleśān sa putreṇa tvayā kṛtān kṛṣṇāyāḥ ca parikleśam sabhā madhye durātmabhiḥ narakam patitāḥ pārthāḥ sarve ṣaṇḍhatila upamāḥ dāsī bhogena kṛṣṇām ca bhoktu kāmāḥ sutāḥ tava yat ca api tān pravrajataḥ kṛṣṇājina nivāsinaḥ paruṣāṇi uktavān karṇaḥ sabhāyām saṃnidhau tava tṛṇīkṛtya ca yat pārthān tava putraḥ vavalga ha bālyāt prabhṛti ca ari ghnaḥ tāni duḥkhāni cintayan cāpam bharata śārdūlaḥ tyakta ātmā karṇam abhyayāt bhānumadbhiḥ śilā dhautaiḥ bhānoḥ pracchādayat prabhām tatas prahasya ādhirathiḥ tūrṇam asyan śitān śarān mahā rathaḥ mahā bāhuḥ mahā vegaiḥ mahā balaḥ vivyādha ādhirathiḥ bhīmam navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sa tottraiḥ iva mātaṅgaḥ vāryamāṇaḥ patatribhiḥ abhyadhāvat asaṃbhrāntaḥ sūtaputram vṛkodaraḥ tam āpatantam vegena rabhasam pāṇḍava ṛṣabham tatas pradhmāpya jalajam bherī śata nināditam akṣubhyata balam harṣāt uddhūtaḥ iva sāgaraḥ tat uddhūtam balam dṛṣṭva ratha nāga aśva pattimat bhīmaḥ karṇam samāsādya chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ aśvān ṛśya savarṇān tu haṃsa varṇaiḥ haya uttamaiḥ vyāmiśrayat raṇe karṇaḥ pāṇḍavam chādayan śaraiḥ ṛśya varṇān hayān karkaiḥ miśrān māruta raṃhasaḥ nirīkṣya tava putrāṇām hāhākṛtam abhūt balam te hayāḥ bahu aśobhanta miśritāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ sita asitāḥ mahā rāja yathā vyomni balāhakāḥ saṃrabdhau krodha tāmra akṣau prekṣya karṇa vṛkodarau saṃtrastāḥ samakampanta tvadīyānām mahā rathāḥ yama rāṣṭra upamam ghoram āsīt āyodhanam tayoḥ durdarśam bharata śreṣṭha pretarāja puram yathā samājam iva tat citram prekṣamāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ na alakṣayan jayam vyaktam ekaikasya nivāraṇe tayoḥ praikṣanta saṃmardam saṃnikṛṣṭa mahā astrayoḥ chādayantau hi śatrughnau anyonyam sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ śara jāla āvṛtam vyoma cakrāte śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ tau anyonyam jighāṃsantau śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ mahā rathau prekṣaṇīyatarau āstām vṛṣṭimantau iva ambudau suvarṇa vikṛtān bāṇān pramuñcantau ariṃdamau tābhyām muktāḥ vyakāśanta kaṅka barhiṇa vāsasaḥ paṅktyaḥ śaradi mattānām sārasānām iva ambare saṃsaktam sūtaputreṇa dṛṣṭvā bhīmam ariṃdamam atibhāram amanyetām bhīme kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau tatra ādhirathi bhīmābhyām śaraiḥ muktaiḥ dṛḍha āhatāḥ kṛtaḥ mahān mahā rāja putrāṇām te jana kṣayaḥ manuṣya aśva gajānām ca śarīraiḥ gata jīvitaiḥ kṣaṇena bhūmiḥ saṃjajñe saṃvṛtā bharata ṛṣabha dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca vārayet yaḥ raṇe karṇaḥ sa yakṣa asura mānavān sa katham pāṇḍavam yuddhe bhrājamānam iva śriyā na atarat saṃyuge tāta tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya katham ca yuddham bhūyaḥ abhūt tayoḥ prāṇa durodare karṇam prāpya raṇe sūta mama putraḥ suyodhanaḥ śrutvā tu nirjitam karṇam asakṛt bhīma karmaṇā bhīmasenena samare mohaḥ āviśati iva mām na hi karṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsān pārthān saṃjaya kṛtavān yāni yuddhāni karṇaḥ pāṇḍu sutaiḥ saha sarvatra pāṇḍavāḥ karṇam ajayanta raṇa ajire ajayyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ tāta devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ nikṛtyā nikṛti prajñaḥ rājyam hṛtvā mahātmanām jitān iti eva manvānaḥ pāṇḍavān avamanyate putra sneha abhibhūtena mayā ca api akṛtātmanā dharme sthitāḥ mahātmānaḥ nikṛtāḥ pāṇḍu nandanāḥ śama kāmaḥ sadā pārthaḥ dīrghaprekṣī yudhiṣṭhiraḥ aśaktaḥ iti manvānaiḥ putraiḥ mama nirākṛtaḥ tāni duḥkhāni anekāni viprakārān ca sarvaśas hṛdi kṛtvā mahā bāhuḥ bhīmaḥ ayudhyata sūtajam tasmāt me saṃjaya brūhi karṇa bhīmau yathā raṇe ayudhyetām yudhi śreṣṭhau paraspara vadha eṣiṇau saṃjayaḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan yathā vṛttaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ karṇa bhīmayoḥ parākrāntam parākramya vivyādha triṃśatā śaraiḥ mahā vegaiḥ prasanna agraiḥ śātakumbha pariṣkṛtaiḥ āhanat bharata śreṣṭha bhīmam vaikartanaḥ śaraiḥ rathanīḍāt ca yantāram bhallena apātayat kṣitau sa kāṅkṣan bhīmasenasya vadham vaikartanaḥ vṛṣaḥ śaktim kanaka vaiḍūrya citra daṇḍām parāmṛśat pragṛhya ca mahā śaktim kāla śaktim iva aparām samutkṣipya ca rādheyaḥ saṃdhāya ca mahā balaḥ cikṣepa bhīmasenāya jīvitānta karīm iva śaktim visṛjya rādheyaḥ puraṃdaraḥ iva aśanim nanāda su mahā nādam balavān sūtanandanaḥ tam ca nādam tatas śrutvā putrāḥ te hṛṣitāḥ abhavan tām karṇa bhuja nirmuktām arka vaiśvānara prabhām śaktim viyati ciccheda bhīmaḥ saptabhiḥ āśugaiḥ mārgamāṇaḥ iva prāṇān sūtaputrasya māriṣa prāhiṇot nava saṃrabdhaḥ śarān barhiṇa vāsasaḥ svarṇa puṅkhān śilā dhautān yama daṇḍa upamān mṛdhe karṇaḥ api anyat dhanuḥ gṛhya hema pṛṣṭham durāsadam vikṛṣya ca mahā tejāḥ vyasṛjat sāyakān nava vasuṣeṇena nirmuktān nava rājan mahā śarān chittvā bhīmaḥ mahā rāja nādam siṃhaḥ iva anadat tau vṛṣau iva nardantau balinau vāśitā antare śārdūlau iva ca anyonyam atyartham ca hi agarjatām anyonyam prajihīrṣantau anyonyasya antara eṣiṇau mahā gajau iva āsādya viṣāṇa agraiḥ parasparam śaraiḥ pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ nirdahantau mahā rāja śara vṛṣṭyā parasparam śaṅkha śabdam ca kurvāṇau yuyudhāte parasparam tasya bhīmaḥ punar cāpam muṣṭau ciccheda māriṣa śaṅkha varṇāḥ ca tān aśvān bāṇaiḥ ninye yama kṣayam tathā kṛcchra gatam dṛṣṭvā karṇam duryodhanaḥ nṛpaḥ gaccha durjaya rādheyam purā grasati pāṇḍavaḥ jahi tūbarakam kṣipram karṇasya balam ādadhat abhyadravat bhīmasenam vyāsaktam vikiran śarān sa bhīmam navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ aśvān aṣṭabhiḥ ardayat ṣaḍbhiḥ sūtam tribhiḥ ketum punar tam ca api saptabhiḥ bhīmasenaḥ api saṃkruddhaḥ sa aśva yantāram āśugaiḥ su alaṃkṛtam kṣitau kṣuṇṇam ceṣṭamānam yathā uragam samācinot bāṇa gaṇaiḥ śataghnīm iva śaṅkubhiḥ tathā api atirathaḥ karṇaḥ bhidyamānaḥ sma sāyakaiḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca ratham anyam samāsthāya sadyas vivyādha pāṇḍavam mahā gajau iva āsādya viṣāṇa agraiḥ parasparam śaraiḥ pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ tam bhīmaḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat ajihmagaiḥ punar vivyādha viṃśatyā śarāṇām nata parvaṇām sāyakānām tatas pārthaḥ triṣaṣṭyā pratyavidhyata tottraiḥ iva mahā nāgam kaśābhiḥ iva vājinam saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā sṛkviṇī lelihan vīraḥ krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ tatas śaram mahā rāja sarva kāya avadāraṇam prāhiṇot bhīmasenāya balāya indraḥ iva aśanim agacchat dārayan bhūmim citrapuṅkhaḥ śilīmukhaḥ sarva śaikyām catur kiṣkum gurvīm rukma aṅgadām gadām prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya a vicārayan tayā jaghāna ādhiratheḥ sat aśvān sādhu vāhinaḥ gadayā bhārataḥ kruddhaḥ vajreṇa indraḥ iva asurān tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ kṣurābhyām bharata ṛṣabha virathaḥ rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ vārayām āsa yat ripum viratham tam ratha śreṣṭham dṛṣṭvā ādhirathim āhave eṣa durmukha rādheyaḥ bhīmena virathīkṛtaḥ tam rathena nara śreṣṭham saṃpādaya mahā ratham tvaramāṇaḥ abyayāt karṇam bhīmam ca avārayat śaraiḥ vāyuputraḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ abhūt parilelihan tatas karṇam mahā rāja vārayitvā śilīmukhaiḥ durmukhāya ratham śīghram preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ āsthitaḥ prababhau rājan dīpyamānaḥ iva aṃśumān śayānam bhinna marmāṇam durmukham śoṇita ukṣitam dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ aśru pūrṇa akṣaḥ muhūrtam na abhyavartata tam gatāsum atikramya kṛtvā karṇaḥ pradakṣiṇam dīrgham uṣṇam śvasan vīraḥ na kim cit pratyapadyata tasmin tu vivare rājan nārācān gārdhra vāsasaḥ prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya bhīmasenaḥ caturdaśa apiban sūtaputrasya śoṇitam rakta bhojanāḥ kruddhāḥ iva manuṣya indra bhujagāḥ kāla coditāḥ prasarpamāṇāḥ medinyām te vyarocanta mārgaṇāḥ ardha praviṣṭāḥ saṃrabdhāḥ bilāni iva mahā uragāḥ tam pratyavidhyat rādheyaḥ jāmbūnada vibhūṣitaiḥ prāviśan medinīm bhīmāḥ krauñcam patrarathāḥ iva te vyarocanta nārācāḥ praviśantaḥ vasuṃdharām gacchati astam dinakare dīpyamānāḥ iva aṃśavaḥ susrāva rudhiram bhūri parvataḥ salilam yathā sa vihvalaḥ mahā rāja karṇaḥ bhīma bala arditaḥ prādravat javanaiḥ aśvaiḥ raṇam hitvā mahā yaśāḥ bhīmasenaḥ tu visphārya cāpam hema pariṣkṛtam āhave atirathaḥ atiṣṭhat jvalan iva hutāśanaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca yatra ādhirathiḥ āyastaḥ na atarat pāṇḍavam raṇe karṇaḥ pārthān sa govindān jetum utsahate raṇe na ca karṇa samam yodham loke paśyāmi kam cana karṇaḥ hi balavān śūraḥ dṛḍha dhanvā jita klamaḥ vasuṣeṇa sahāyam mām na alam devāḥ api saṃyuge kim u pāṇḍu sutāḥ rājan gata sattvāḥ vicetasaḥ tatra tam nirjitam dṛṣṭvā bhujaṃgam iva nirviṣam aśvatthāmā madra rājaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ ca saṃgatāḥ na śaktāḥ pramukhe sthātum nūnam bhīmasya saṃjaya te api ca asya mahā ghoram balam nāga ayuta upamam jānantaḥ vyavasāyam ca krūram māruta tejasaḥ kimartham krūra karmāṇam yama kāla antaka upamam bala saṃrambha vīrya jñāḥ kopayiṣyanti saṃyuge karṇaḥ tu ekaḥ mahā bāhuḥ sva bāhu balam āśritaḥ bhīmasenam an ādṛtya raṇe ayudhyata sūtajaḥ na sa pāṇḍu sutaḥ jetum śakyaḥ kena cit āhave droṇam yaḥ saṃpramathya ekaḥ praviṣṭaḥ mama vāhinīm bhīmaḥ dhanaṃjaya anveṣī kaḥ tam archet jijīviṣuḥ pretarāja puram prāpya nivarteta api mānavaḥ pataṃgāḥ iva vahnim te prāviśan alpa cetasaḥ śaptam saṃrambhiṇā ugreṇa kurūṇām śṛṇvatām tadā tat nūnam abhisaṃcintya dṛṣṭvā karṇam ca nirjitam duḥśāsanaḥ saha bhrātrā bhayāt bhīmāt upāramat karṇaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ aham ca jeṣyāmaḥ yudhi pāṇḍavān sa nūnam viratham dṛṣṭvā karṇam bhīmena nirjitam pratyākhyānāt ca kṛṣṇasya bhṛśam tapyati saṃjaya dṛṣṭvā bhrātṝn hatān yuddhe bhīmasenena daṃśitān ātma aparādhāt su mahat nūnam tapyati putrakaḥ kaḥ hi jīvitam anvicchan pratīpam pāṇḍavam vrajet bhīmam bhīma āyudham kruddham sākṣāt kālam iva sthitam na pāṇḍavāḥ na pāñcālāḥ na ca keśava sātyakī jānanti yudhi saṃrabdhāḥ jīvitam parirakṣitum saṃjayaḥ uvāca tvam asya jagataḥ mūlam vināśasya na saṃśayaḥ svayam vairam mahat kṛtvā putrāṇām vacane sthitaḥ ucyamānaḥ na gṛhṇīṣe martyaḥ pathyam iva auṣadham svayam pītvā mahā rāja kālakūṭam su durjaram tasya idānīm phalam kṛtsnam avāpnuhi narottama dṛṣṭvā karṇam tu putrāḥ te bhīmasena parājitam na amṛṣyanta mahā iṣvāsāḥ sodaryāḥ pañca māriṣa pāṇḍavam citra saṃnāhāḥ tam pratīpam upādravan te samantāt mahā bāhum parivārya vṛkodaram diśaḥ śaraiḥ samāvṛṇvan śalabhānām iva vrajaiḥ āgacchataḥ tān sahasā kumārān deva rūpiṇaḥ tava dṛṣṭvā tu tanayān bhīmasena samīpa gān visṛjan viśikhān rājan svarṇa puṅkhān śilā śitān tam tu bhīmaḥ abhyayāt tūrṇam vāryamāṇaḥ sutaiḥ tava avākiran bhīmasenam śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tān bāṇaiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā sa aśvān rājan nara ṛṣabhān sa sūtān bhīma dhanuṣaḥ bhīmaḥ ninye yama kṣayam citra puṣpa dharāḥ bhagnāḥ vātena iva mahā drumāḥ saṃvārya ādhirathim bāṇaiḥ yat jaghāna tava ātmajān sa vāryamāṇaḥ bhīmena śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ samantataḥ tam bhīmasenaḥ saṃrambhāt krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tava ātmajān tu patitān dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ pratāpavān krodhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ nirviṇṇaḥ abhūt sa jīvitāt āgaskṛtam iva ātmānam mene ca ādhirathiḥ tadā bhīmasenam tatas kruddhaḥ samādravata saṃbhramāt punar vivyādha saptatyā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ avahāsam tu tam pārthaḥ na amṛṣyata vṛkodaraḥ tatas vivyādha rādheyam śatena nata parvaṇām punar ca viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya karṇaḥ bhārata durmanāḥ iṣubhiḥ chādayām āsa bhīmasenam samantataḥ prajahāsa mahā hāsam kṛte pratikṛtam punar iṣubhiḥ kārmukam ca asya cakarta puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ tat papāta mahā rāja svarṇa pṛṣṭham mahā svanam avārohat rathāt tasmāt atha karṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ gadām gṛhītvā samare bhīmasenāya ca akṣipat tām āpatantīm sahasā gadām dṛṣṭvā vṛkodaraḥ tatas bāṇa sahasrāṇi preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ sūtaputra vadha ākāṅkṣī tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī tān iṣūn iṣubhiḥ karṇaḥ vārayitvā mahā mṛdhe kavacam bhīmasenasya pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥ atha enam pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām samārpayat paśyatām sarva bhūtānām tat adbhutam iva abhavat raṇe apreṣayata kruddhaḥ sūtaputrasya māriṣa te tasya kavacam bhittvā tathā bāhum ca dakṣiṇam abhyaguḥ dharaṇīm tīkṣṇāḥ valmīkam iva pannagāḥ rādheyam tu raṇe dṛṣṭvā padātinam avasthitam abhyayus pāṇḍavam yuddhe visṛjantaḥ śitān śarān citropacitraḥ citrākṣaḥ cārucitraḥ śarāsanaḥ āgacchataḥ tān sahasā bhīmaḥ rājan mahā rathaḥ sa aśva sūta dhvajān yattān pātayām āsa saṃyuge te hatāḥ nyapatan bhūmau vāta nunnāḥ iva drumāḥ dṛṣṭvā vinihatān putrān tava rājan mahā rathān aśru pūrṇa mukhaḥ karṇaḥ kaśmalam samapadyata abhyayāt pāṇḍavam yuddhe tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī tau anyonyam śaraiḥ viddhvā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ vyabhrājetām mahā rāja puṣpitau iva kiṃśukau vyadhamat kavacam kruddhaḥ sūtaputrasya pāṇḍavaḥ raktacandana digdha aṅgau śaraiḥ kṛta mahā vraṇau śoṇita aktau vyarājetām kāla sūryau iva uditau tau śoṇita ukṣitaiḥ gātraiḥ śaraiḥ chinna tanucchadau vivarmāṇau vyarājetām nirmuktau iva pannagau vyāghrau iva nara vyāghrau daṃṣṭrābhiḥ itaretaram śara daṃṣṭrāḥ vidhunvānau tatakṣatuḥ ariṃdamau vāraṇau iva saṃsaktau raṅga madhye virejatuḥ rathābhyām nādayantau ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ viceratuḥ tau rathābhyām mahā rāja maṇḍala āvartana ādiṣu vyarocetām mahātmānau vṛtra vajradharau iva sa hasta ābharaṇābhyām tu bhujābhyām vikṣipan dhanuḥ sa cāpa ghoṣa stanitaḥ śara dhārā ambudaḥ mahān pāṇḍavaḥ vyakirat karṇam ghanaḥ adrim iva vṛṣṭibhiḥ su puṅkhaiḥ kaṅka vāsobhiḥ yat karṇam chādayat śaraiḥ sa nandayan raṇe pārtham keśavam ca yaśasvinam putrāḥ tava mahā rāja dadṛśuḥ pāṇḍavasya ha saṃjayaḥ uvāca tava ca ādhirathiḥ dṛṣṭvā syandanebhyaḥ cyutān sutān niḥśvasan dīrgham uṣṇam ca punar pāṇḍavam abhyayāt babhau karṇaḥ śarān asyan raśmivān iva bhāskaraḥ karṇa cāpa cyutaiḥ bāṇaiḥ prācchādyata vṛkodaraḥ karṇa cāpa cyutāḥ citrāḥ śarāḥ barhiṇa vāsasaḥ viviśuḥ sarvatas pārtham vāsāya iva aṇḍajāḥ drumam karṇa cāpa cyutāḥ bāṇāḥ saṃpatantaḥ tatas tatas rukma puṅkhāḥ vyarājanta haṃsāḥ śreṇīkṛtāḥ iva cāpa dhvaja upaskarebhyaḥ chatrāt īṣā mukhāt yugāt prabhavantaḥ vyadṛśyanta rājan ādhiratheḥ śarāḥ kham pūrayan mahā vegān khagamān khaga vāsasaḥ suvarṇa vikṛtān citrān mumoca ādhirathiḥ śarān tyaktvā prāṇān abhikrudhya vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥ tasya vegam asaṃsahyam dṛṣṭvā karṇasya pāṇḍavaḥ mahataḥ ca śara oghān tān na eva avyathata vīryavān tatas vidhamya ādhiratheḥ śara jālāni pāṇḍavaḥ vivyādha karṇam viṃśatyā punar anyaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ yathā eva hi śaraiḥ pārthaḥ sūtaputreṇa chāditaḥ tathā eva karṇam samare chādayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ dṛṣṭvā tu bhīmasenasya vikramam yudhi bhārata abhyanandan tvadīyāḥ ca saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ ca cāraṇāḥ bhūriśravāḥ kṛpaḥ drauṇiḥ madra rājaḥ jayadrathaḥ uttamaujāḥ yudhāmanyuḥ sātyakiḥ keśava arjunau kuru pāṇḍavānām pravarāḥ daśa rājan mahā rathāḥ rājñaḥ ca rāja putrān ca sodaryān ca viśeṣataḥ karṇam gacchata bhadram vaḥ parīpsantaḥ vṛkodarāt purā nighnanti rādheyam bhīma cāpa cyutāḥ śarāḥ te yatadhvam mahā iṣvāsāḥ sūtaputrasya rakṣaṇe duryodhana samādiṣṭāḥ sodaryāḥ sapta māriṣa te samāsādya kaunteyam āvṛṇvan śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ parvatam vāri dhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣi iva balāhakāḥ te apīḍayan bhīmasenam kruddhāḥ sapta mahā rathāḥ prajā saṃharaṇe rājan somam sapta grahāḥ iva tatas vāmena kaunteyaḥ pīḍayitvā śarāsanam muṣṭinā pāṇḍavaḥ rājan dṛḍhena su pariṣkṛtam manuṣya sama tām jñātvā sapta saṃdhāya sāyakān tebhyaḥ vyasṛjat āyastaḥ sūrya raśmi nibhān prabhuḥ te kṣiptāḥ bhīmasenena śarāḥ bhārata bhāratān vidārya kham samutpetuḥ svarṇa puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ teṣām vidārya cetāṃsi śarāḥ hema vibhūṣitāḥ vyarājanta mahā rāja suparṇāḥ iva khecarāḥ śoṇita ādigdha vāja agrāḥ sapta hema pariṣkṛtāḥ putrāṇām tava rāja indra pītvā śoṇitam udgatāḥ giri sānu ruhāḥ bhagnāḥ dvipena iva mahā drumāḥ śatruṃjayaḥ śatru sahaḥ citraḥ citra āyudhaḥ dṛḍhaḥ tān nihatya mahā bāhuḥ rādheyasya eva paśyataḥ siṃhanāda ravam ghoram asṛjat pāṇḍu nandanaḥ tam śrutvā su mahā nādam bhīmasenasya dhanvinaḥ tatas hṛṣṭaḥ mahā rāja vāditrāṇām mahā svanaiḥ bhīmasena ravam pārthaḥ pratijagrāha sarvaśas harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaḥ kṛta saṃjñe vṛkodare ekatriṃśat mahā rāja putrān tava mahā rathān hatān duryodhanaḥ dṛṣṭvā kṣattuḥ sasmāra tat vacaḥ yat ca karṇaḥ abravīt kṛṣṇām sabhāyām paruṣam vacaḥ pramukhe pāṇḍu putrāṇām tava ca eva viśām pate kauravāṇām ca sarveṣām ācāryasya ca saṃnidhau vinaṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇe śāśvatam narakam gatāḥ patim anyam vṛṇīṣva iti tasya idam phalam āgatam yat sma tām paruṣāṇi āhuḥ sabhām ānāyya draupadīm pāṇḍavān ugra dhanuṣaḥ krodhayantaḥ tava ātmajāḥ tam bhīmasenaḥ krodha agnim trayodaśa samāḥ sthitam visṛjan tava putrāṇām antam gacchati kaurava vilapan ca bahu kṣattā śamam na alabhata tvayi pravarān ātmajānām te sutān ca anyān mahā rathān yān yān ca dadṛśe bhīmaḥ cakṣuḥ viṣayam āgatān putrān tava mahā bāho tvarayā tān jaghāna ha tvad kṛte hi aham adrākṣam dahyamānām varūthinīm sahasraśas śaraiḥ muktaiḥ pāṇḍavena vṛṣeṇa ca dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca mahān apanayaḥ sūta mama eva atra viśeṣataḥ saḥ idānīm anuprāptaḥ manye saṃjaya śocataḥ idānīm atra kim kāryam prakariṣyāmi saṃjaya yathā tu eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ mama apanaya saṃbhavaḥ vīrāṇām tat mama ācakṣva sthirībhūtaḥ asmi saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca karṇa bhīmau mahā rāja parākrāntau mahā āhave bāṇa varṣāṇi avarṣetām vṛṣṭimantau iva ambudau bhīma nāma aṅkitāḥ bāṇāḥ svarṇa puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ viviśuḥ karṇam āsādya bhindantaḥ iva jīvitam ākīryata raṇe bhīmaḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas tayoḥ śaraiḥ mahā rāja saṃpatadbhiḥ samantataḥ babhūva tava sainyānām saṃkṣobhaḥ sāgara upamaḥ avadhyata camū madhye ghoraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ vāraṇaiḥ patitaiḥ rājan vājibhiḥ ca naraiḥ saha adṛśyata mahī kīrṇā vāta nunnaiḥ drumaiḥ iva te vadhyamānāḥ samare bhīma cāpa cyutaiḥ śaraiḥ prādravan tāvakāḥ yodhāḥ kim etat iti ca abruvan protsāritam mahā vegaiḥ karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ śaraiḥ te śara ātura bhūyiṣṭhāḥ hata aśva nara vāhanāḥ utsṛjya karṇam bhīmam ca prādravan sarvatodiśam nūnam pārtha artham eva asmān mohayanti divaukasaḥ evam bruvantaḥ yodhāḥ te tāvakāḥ bhaya pīḍitāḥ śarapātam samutsṛjya sthitāḥ yuddha didṛkṣavaḥ tatas prāvartata nadī ghora rūpā mahā āhave babhūva ca viśeṣeṇa bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhinī vāraṇa aśva manuṣyāṇām rudhira ogha samudbhavā saṃvṛtāḥ gata sattvaiḥ ca manuṣya gaja vājibhiḥ sa anukarṣa patākaiḥ ca dvipa aśva ratha bhūṣaṇaiḥ jātarūpa pariṣkāraiḥ dhanurbhiḥ su mahādhanaiḥ suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ iṣubhiḥ nārācaiḥ ca sahasraśas prāsa tomara saṃghātaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ ca sa paraśvadhaiḥ suvarṇa vikṛtaiḥ ca api gadā musala paṭṭiśaiḥ kanaka aṅgada keyūraiḥ kuṇḍalaiḥ maṇibhiḥ śubhaiḥ gaja aśva manujaiḥ bhinnaiḥ śastraiḥ syandana bhūṣaṇaiḥ dṛṣṭvā cāraṇa siddhānām vismayaḥ samapadyata gajābhyām saṃprayuktābhyām āsīt naḍa vanam yathā tathābhūtam mahat sainyam āsīt bhārata saṃyuge vimardaḥ karṇa bhīmābhyām āsīt ca paramaḥ raṇe saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja bhīmam viddhvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥ mumoca śara varṣāṇi citrāṇi ca bahūni ca vadhyamānaḥ mahā rāja sūtaputreṇa pāṇḍavaḥ sa karṇam karṇinā karṇe pītena niśitena ca vivyādha yudhi rāja indra bhīmasenaḥ patatriṇā sa kuṇḍalam mahat karṇāt karṇasya apātayat bhuvi tapanīyam mahā rāja dīptam jyotiḥ iva ambarāt ājaghāna bhṛśam bhīmaḥ smayan iva mahā balaḥ punar asya tvaran bhīmaḥ nārācān daśa bhārata raṇe praiṣīt mahā vegān yama daṇḍa upamān tathā te lalāṭam samāsādya sūtaputrasya māriṣa viviśuḥ ca uditāḥ tena valmīkam iva pannagāḥ nīlotpala mayīm mālām dhārayan sa purā yathā tatas kruddhaḥ raṇe karṇaḥ pīḍitaḥ dṛḍhadhanvanā tasmai karṇaḥ śatam rājan iṣūṇām gārdhra vāsasām amarṣī balavān kruddhaḥ preṣayām āsa bhārata tatas prāsṛjat ugrāṇi śara varṣāṇi pāṇḍavaḥ tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ kruddha rūpam paraṃtapaḥ jīmūtau iva ca anyonyam tau vavarṣatuḥ āhave śara jālaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ chādayām āsatuḥ mṛdhe tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ rādheyasya mahātmanaḥ kṣurapreṇa dhanuḥ chittvā karṇam vivyādha patriṇā tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam sūtaputraḥ mahā manāḥ dṛṣṭvā ca kuru sauvīra saindhavānām bala kṣayam sa varma dhvaja śastraiḥ ca patitaiḥ saṃvṛtām mahīm hasti aśva nara dehān ca gatāsūn prekṣya sarvatas sūtaputrasya saṃrambhāt dīptam vapuḥ ajāyata bhīmam praikṣata rādheyaḥ rājan ghoreṇa cakṣuṣā madhyaṃdina gataḥ arciṣmān śaradi iva divākaraḥ āsīt ādhiratheḥ ghoram vapuḥ śara śata arciṣaḥ karābhyām ādadānasya saṃdadhānasya ca āśugān vikarṣataḥ muñcataḥ vā nā antaram dadṛśuḥ raṇe agni cakra upamam ghoram maṇḍalīkṛtam āyudham karṇasya āsīt mahā rāja savya dakṣiṇam asyataḥ svarṇa puṅkhāḥ su niśitāḥ karṇa cāpa cyutāḥ śarāḥ prācchādayan mahā rāja diśaḥ sūryasya ca prabhām tatas kanaka puṅkhānām śarāṇām nata parvaṇām dhanuḥ cyutānām viyati dadṛśe bahudhā vrajaḥ śarāsanāt ādhiratheḥ prabhavantaḥ sma sāyakāḥ śreṇīkṛtāḥ vyarājanta rājan krauñcāḥ iva ambare gārdhra patrān śilā dhautān kārtasvara vibhūṣitān mahā vegān pradīpta agrān mumoca ādhirathiḥ śarān te tu cāpa bala uddhūtāḥ śātakumbha vibhūṣitāḥ te vyomni ratna vikṛtāḥ vyakāśanta sahasraśas śalabhānām iva vrātāḥ śarāḥ karṇa samīritāḥ cāpāt ādhiratheḥ muktāḥ prapatantaḥ sma sāyakāḥ ekaḥ dīrghaḥ iva prāṃśuḥ prabhavan dṛśyate śaraḥ parvatam vāri dhārābhiḥ chādayan iva toyadaḥ karṇaḥ prācchādayat kruddhaḥ bhīmam sāyaka vṛṣṭibhiḥ tām samudram iva uddhūtām śara vṛṣṭim samutthitām rukma pṛṣṭham mahat cāpam bhīmasya āsīt viśām pate ākarṣāt maṇḍalībhūtam śakra cāpam iva aparam tasmāt śarāḥ prādurāsan pūrayantaḥ iva ambaram gagane racitā mālā kāñcanī iva vyarājata tatas vyomni viṣaktāni śara jālāni bhāgaśas āhatāni vyaśīryanta bhīmasenasya patribhiḥ taiḥ taiḥ kanaka puṅkhānām dyauḥ āsīt saṃvṛtā vrajaiḥ sa bhīmam chādayan bāṇaiḥ sūtaputraḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ upārohat an ādṛtya tasya vīryam mahātmanaḥ tayoḥ visṛjatoḥ tatra śara jālāni māriṣa vāyu bhūtāni adṛśyanta saṃsaktāni itaretaram tasmai karṇaḥ śitān bāṇān karmāra parimārjitān suvarṇa vikṛtān kruddhaḥ prāhiṇot vadha kāṅkṣayā viśeṣayan sūtaputram bhīmaḥ tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt punar ca asṛjat ugrāṇi śara varṣāṇi pāṇḍavaḥ amarṣī balavān kruddhaḥ didhakṣan iva pāvakaḥ tasya tāni ādade karṇaḥ sarvāṇi astrāṇi abhīta vat yudhyataḥ pāṇḍu putrasya sūtaputraḥ astra māyayā tasya iṣudhī dhanuḥ jyām ca bāṇaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ raśmīn yoktrāṇi ca aśvānām karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ acchinat atha asya aśvān punar hatvā tribhiḥ vivyādha sārathim dhvajam ciccheda rādheyaḥ patākāḥ ca nyapātayat sa vidhanvā mahā rāja ratha śaktim parāmṛśat tām avāsṛjat āvidhya kruddhaḥ karṇa ratham prati tām ādhirathiḥ āyastaḥ śaktim hema pariṣkṛtām āpatantīm mahā ulkā ābhām ciccheda daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ sā apatat daśadhā rājan nikṛttā karṇa sāyakaiḥ sa vicarmā mahā rāja virathaḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ sa dhanuḥ sūtaputrasya chittvā jyām ca su saṃśitaḥ tasya tat caritam dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāme vijaya eṣiṇaḥ tat asya kuravaḥ sarve cāraṇāḥ ca abhyapūjayan yat iyeṣa rathāt karṇam hantum tārkṣyaḥ iva uragam sva ratham pṛṣṭhatas kṛtvā yuddhāya eva vyavasthitaḥ saṃrabdhaḥ pāṇḍavam saṃkhye yuddhāya samupasthitam tayoḥ āsīt saṃprahāraḥ kruddhayoḥ nara siṃhayoḥ a mṛṣyamāṇayoḥ saṃkhye deva dānavayoḥ iva kṣīṇa śastraḥ tu kaunteyaḥ karṇena samabhidrutaḥ dṛṣṭvā arjuna hatān nāgān patitān parvata upamān ratha mārga vighāta artham vyāyudhaḥ praviveśa ha pāṇḍavaḥ jīvita ākāṅkṣī rādheyam na abhyahārayat vyavasthānam atha ākāṅkṣan dhanaṃjaya śaraiḥ hatam hasti aṅgāni atha karṇāya prāhiṇot pāṇḍavaḥ nadan cakrāṇi aśvān tathā vāhān yat yat paśyati bhū tale tat tat ādāya cikṣepa kruddhaḥ karṇāya pāṇḍavaḥ tat asya sarvam ciccheda kṣiptam kṣiptam śitaiḥ śaraiḥ vyāyudham na avadhīt ca enam karṇaḥ kuntyāḥ vacaḥ smaran dhanuṣaḥ agreṇa tam karṇaḥ tu abhidrutya parāmṛśat a kṛtāstraka mā yotsīḥ bāla saṃgrāma kātara yatra bhojyam bahuvidham bhakṣyam peyam ca pāṇḍava puṣpa mūla phala āhāraḥ vrateṣu niyameṣu ca ucitaḥ tvam vane bhīma na tvam yuddha viśāradaḥ sūdān bhṛtyajanān dāsān tvam gṛhe tvarayan bhṛśam yogyaḥ tāḍayitum krodhāt bhojana artham vṛkodara kaumāre yāni ca api āsan apriyāṇi viśām pate pūrva vṛttāni ca api enam rūkṣāṇi aśrāvayat bhṛśam atha enam tatra saṃlīnam aspṛśat dhanuṣā punar prahasan ca punar vākyam bhīmam āha vṛṣaḥ tadā yoddhavyam āviśān yatra na yoddhavyam tu mādṛśaiḥ mādṛśaiḥ yudhyamānānām etat ca anyat ca vidyate gaccha vā yatra tau kṛṣṇau tau tvā rakṣiṣyataḥ raṇe evam tam viratham kṛtvā karṇaḥ rājan vyakatthata pramukhe vṛṣṇi siṃhasya pārthasya ca mahātmanaḥ tatas rājan śilā dhautān śarān śākhāmṛga dhvajaḥ prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya keśavena pracoditaḥ tatas pārtha bhuja utsṛṣṭāḥ śarāḥ kāñcana bhūṣaṇāḥ gāṇḍīva prabhavāḥ karṇam haṃsāḥ krauñcam iva āviśan sa bhujaṃgaiḥ iva āyastaiḥ gāṇḍīva preṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasenāt apāsedhat sūtaputram dhanaṃjayaḥ sa chinna dhanvā bhīmena dhanaṃjaya śara āhataḥ karṇaḥ bhīmāt apāyāsīt rathena mahatā drutam bhīmaḥ api sātyakeḥ vāham samāruhya nara ṛṣabhaḥ anvayāt bhrātaram saṃkhye pāṇḍavam savyasācinam tatas karṇam samuddiśya tvaramāṇaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ nārācam krodha tāmra akṣaḥ praiṣīt mṛtyum iva antakaḥ nārācaḥ abhyapatat karṇam tūrṇam gāṇḍīva coditaḥ tam antarikṣe nārācam drauṇiḥ ciccheda patriṇā dhanaṃjaya bhayāt karṇam ujjihīrṣuḥ mahā rathaḥ tatas drauṇim catuḥṣaṣṭyā vivyādha kupitaḥ arjunaḥ śilīmukhaiḥ mahā rāja mā gāḥ tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt sa tu matta gaja ākīrṇam anīkam ratha saṃkulam tūrṇam abhyāviśat drauṇiḥ dhanaṃjaya śara arditaḥ tatas suvarṇa pṛṣṭhānām dhanuṣām kūjatām raṇe śabdam gāṇḍīva ghoṣeṇa kaunteyaḥ abhyabhavat balī dhanaṃjayaḥ tathā yāntam pṛṣṭhatas drauṇim abhyayāt na ati dīrgham iva adhvānam śaraiḥ saṃtrāsayan balam vidārya dehān nārācaiḥ nara vāraṇa vājinām tat balam bharata śreṣṭha sa vāji dvipa mānavam pākaśāsanaḥ āyastaḥ pārthaḥ saṃnijaghāna ha dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca dhanaṃjayaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ praviṣṭaḥ māmakam balam rakṣitam droṇa karṇābhyām apraveśyam suraiḥ api tābhyām ūrjita vīryābhyām āpyāyita parākramaḥ sahitaḥ kṛṣṇa bhīmābhyām śinīnām ṛṣabheṇa ca tadā prabhṛti mā śokaḥ dahati agniḥ iva āśayam grastān hi pratipaśyāmi bhūmipālān sa saindhavān apriyam su mahat kṛtvā sindhurājaḥ kirīṭinaḥ cakṣuḥ viṣayam āpannaḥ katham mucyeta jīvitaḥ anumānāt ca paśyāmi na asti saṃjaya saindhavaḥ yuddham tu tat yathā vṛttam tat mama ācakṣva pṛcchataḥ yat ca vikṣobhya mahatīm senām saṃloḍya ca asakṛt ekaḥ praviṣṭaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ nalinīm iva kuñjaraḥ tasya vṛṣṇi pravīrasya brūhi yuddham yathātatham saṃjayaḥ uvāca tathā tu vaikartana pīḍitam tam bhīmam prayāntam puruṣa pravīram na aśaknuvan vārayitum tvadīyāḥ sarve rathāḥ bhārata mādhava agryam amarṣa pūrṇaḥ tu anivṛtta yodhī śarāsanī kāñcana varma dhārī anāgatān eva tu tān pṛṣatkān ciccheda bāṇaiḥ śini puṃgavaḥ api punar sa bāṇaiḥ tribhiḥ agni kalpaiḥ ākarṇapūrṇaiḥ niśitaiḥ su puṅkhaiḥ vivyādha deha āvaraṇam vidārya te sātyakeḥ āviviśuḥ śarīram ājaghnivān tān rajata prakāśān aśvān caturbhiḥ caturaḥ prasahya sa kuṇḍalam pūrṇa śaśi prakāśam bhrājiṣṇu vaktram nicakarta dehāt nihatya tam pārthiva putra pautram saṃkhye madhūnām ṛṣabhaḥ pramāthī tatas anvayāt arjunam eva vīraḥ sainyāni rājan tava saṃnivārya anvāgatam vṛṣṇi varam samīkṣya tathā ari madhye parivartamānam ghnantam kurūṇām iṣubhiḥ balāni punar punar vāyuḥ iva abhra pūgān tatas avahan saindhavāḥ sādhu dāntāḥ go kṣīra kunda indu hima prakāśāḥ suvarṇa jāla avatatāḥ sat aśvāḥ yatas yatas kāmayate nṛ siṃhaḥ kṛtvā mukham bhārata yodha mukhyam duḥśāsanam tvad sutam ājamīḍha te sarvatas saṃparivārya saṃkhye śaineyam ājaghnuḥ anīka sāhāḥ sa ca api tān pravaraḥ sātvatānām nyavārayat bāṇa jālena vīraḥ nivārya tān tūrṇam amitra ghātī naptā śineḥ patribhiḥ agni kalpaiḥ duḥśāsanasya api jaghāna vāhān udyamya bāṇāsanam ājamīḍha saṃjayaḥ uvāca tam udyatam mahā bāhum duḥśāsana ratham prati tvaritam tvaraṇīyeṣu dhanaṃjaya hita eṣiṇam trigartānām mahā iṣvāsāḥ suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ senā samudram āviṣṭam ānartam paryavārayan atha enam ratha vaṃśena sarvatas saṃnivārya te avākiran śara vrātaiḥ kruddhāḥ parama dhanvinaḥ ajayat rāja putrān tān yatamānān mahā raṇe ekaḥ pañcāśatam śatrūn sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ saṃprāpya bhāratī madhyam tala ghoṣa samākulam asi śakti gadā pūrṇam aplavam salilam yathā tatra adbhutam apaśyāma śaineya caritam raṇe pratīcyām diśi tam dṛṣṭvā prācyām paśyāma lāghavāt udīcīm dakṣiṇām prācīm pratīcīm prasṛtaḥ tathā nṛtyan iva acarat śūraḥ yathā ratha śatam tathā tat dṛṣṭvā caritam tasya siṃha vikrānta gāminaḥ trigartāḥ saṃnyavartanta saṃtaptāḥ sva janam prati tam anye śūrasenānām śūrāḥ saṃkhye nyavārayan niyacchantaḥ śara vrātaiḥ mattam dvipam iva aṅkuśaiḥ tān nyavārayat āyastān muhūrtam iva sātyakiḥ tām ca senām atikramya kaliṅgānām duratyayām atha pārtham mahā bāhuḥ dhanaṃjayam upāsadat tam dṛṣṭvā puruṣa vyāghram yuyudhānaḥ samāśvasat asau āyāti śaineyaḥ tava pārtha padānugaḥ eṣa śiṣyaḥ sakhā ca eva tava satya parākramaḥ sarvān yodhān tṛṇīkṛtya vijigye puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ eṣa kaurava yodhānām kṛtvā ghoram upadravam tava prāṇaiḥ priyataraḥ kirīṭin eti sātyakiḥ eṣa droṇam tathā bhojam kṛtavarmāṇam eva ca kadarthīkṛtya viśikhaiḥ phalguna abhyeti sātyakiḥ dharmarāja priya anveṣī hatvā yodhān varān varān śūraḥ ca eva kṛtāstraḥ ca phalguna abhyeti sātyakiḥ tava darśanam anvicchan pāṇḍava abhyeti sātyakiḥ ācārya pramukhān pārtha āyāti eṣa hi sātyakiḥ sva bāhu balam āśritya vidārya ca varūthinīm nihatya bahulāḥ senāḥ pārtha eṣaḥ abhyeti sātyakiḥ eṣa rāja sahasrāṇām vaktraiḥ paṅkaja saṃnibhaiḥ āstīrya vasudhām pārtha kṣipram āyāti sātyakiḥ eṣa duryodhanam jitvā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitam raṇe nihatya jalasaṃdham ca kṣipram āyāti sātyakiḥ rudhira oghavatīm kṛtvā nadīm śoṇita kardamām tṛṇa vat nyasya kauravyān eṣaḥ āyāti sātyakiḥ tatas aprahṛṣṭaḥ kaunteyaḥ keśavam vākyam abravīt na me priyam mahā bāho yat mām abhyeti sātyakiḥ na hi jānāmi vṛttāntam dharmarājasya keśava sātvatena vihīnaḥ sa yadi jīvati vā na vā etena hi mahā bāho rakṣitavyaḥ sa pārthivaḥ tam eṣa katham utsṛjya mama kṛṣṇa padānugaḥ rājā droṇāya ca utsṛṣṭaḥ saindhavaḥ ca a nipātitaḥ pratyudyātaḥ ca śaineyam eṣa bhūriśravāḥ raṇe saḥ ayam gurutaraḥ bhāraḥ saindhavāt me samāhitaḥ jñātavyaḥ ca hi me rājā rakṣitavyaḥ ca sātyakiḥ śrāntaḥ ca eṣa mahā bāhuḥ alpa prāṇaḥ ca sāṃpratam pariśrāntāḥ hayāḥ ca asya haya yantā ca mādhava na ca bhūriśravāḥ śrāntaḥ sa sahāyaḥ ca keśava api idānīm bhavet asya kṣemam asmin samāgame kaccit na sāgaram tīrtvā sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ goṣpadam prāpya sīdeta mahā ojāḥ śini puṃgavaḥ ācāryāt bhayam utsṛjya yaḥ preṣayati sātyakim grahaṇam dharmarājasya khagaḥ śyenaḥ iva āmiṣam nityam āśaṃsate droṇaḥ kaccit syāt kuśalī nṛpaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca krodhāt bhūriśravāḥ rājan sahasā samupādravat tam abravīt mahā bāhuḥ kauravyaḥ śini puṃgavam adya prāptaḥ asi diṣṭyā me cakṣuḥ viṣayam iti uta cira abhilaṣitam kāmam adya prāpsyāmi saṃyuge adya tvām samare hatvā nityam śūra abhimāninam nandayiṣyāmi dāśārha kuru rājam suyodhanam adya mad bāṇa nirdagdham patitam dharaṇī tale drakṣyataḥ tvām raṇe vīrau sahitau keśava arjunau adya dharmasutaḥ rājā śrutvā tvām nihatam mayā sa vrīḍaḥ bhavitā sadyas yena asi iha praveśitaḥ adya yuddham mahā ghoram tava dāsyāmi sātvata adya saṃyamanīm yātā mayā tvam nihataḥ raṇe yathā rāma anujena ājau rāvaṇiḥ lakṣmaṇena vai adya kṛṣṇaḥ ca pārthaḥ ca dharmarājaḥ ca mādhava hate tvayi nirutsāhāḥ raṇam tyakṣyanti asaṃśayam adya te apacitim kṛtvā śitaiḥ mādhava sāyakaiḥ cakṣuḥ viṣaya saṃprāptaḥ na tvam mādhava mokṣyase siṃhasya viṣayam prāptaḥ yathā kṣudra mṛgaḥ tathā sa mām nihanyāt saṃgrāme yaḥ mām kuryāt nirāyudham samāḥ tu śāśvatīḥ hanyāt yaḥ mām hanyāt hi saṃyuge kim mṛṣā uktena bahunā karmaṇā tu samācara śrutvā etat garjitam vīra hāsyam hi mama jāyate tvarate me matiḥ tāta tvayi yuddha abhikāṅkṣiṇi na a hatvā saṃnivartiṣye tvām adya puruṣa adhama bhūriśravāḥ sātyakiḥ ca vavarṣatuḥ ariṃdamau śara varṣāṇi bhīmāni meghau iva parasparam saumadattiḥ tu śaineyam pracchādya iṣubhiḥ āśugaiḥ jighāṃsuḥ bharata śreṣṭha vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ daśabhiḥ sātyakim viddhvā saumadattiḥ atha aparān mumoca niśitān bāṇān jighāṃsuḥ śini puṃgavam tān asya viśikhān tīkṣṇān antarikṣe viśām pate tau pṛthak śara varṣābhyām avarṣetām parasparam uttama abhijanau vīrau kuru vṛṣṇi yaśaskarau ratha śaktibhiḥ anyonyam viśikhaiḥ ca api akṛntatām vyaṣṭambhayetām anyonyam prāṇa dyūta abhidevinau evam uttama karmāṇau kuru vṛṣṇi yaśaskarau parasparam ayudhyetām vāraṇau iva yūthapau sātyakiḥ saumadattiḥ ca śara vṛṣṭyā parasparam hṛṣṭa vat dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām paśyatām abhyavarṣatām saṃpraikṣanta janāḥ tatra yudhyamānau yudhām patī yūthapau vāśitā hetoḥ prayuddhau iva kuñjarau virathau asi yuddhāya sameyātām mahā raṇe ārṣabhe carmaṇī citre pragṛhya vipule śubhe vikośau ca api asī kṛtvā samare tau viceratuḥ carantau vividhān mārgān maṇḍalāni ca bhāgaśas sa khaḍgau citra varmāṇau sa niṣka aṅgada bhūṣaṇau raṇe raṇa utkaṭau rājan anyonyam paryakarṣatām paśyatām sarva sainyānām vīrau āśvasatām punar asibhyām carmaṇī śubhre vipule ca śarāvare śikṣā bala samudbhūtāḥ sarva yodha praharṣaṇāḥ dvipau iva viṣāṇa agraiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ iva mahā ṛṣabhau kṣīṇa āyudhe sātvate yudhyamāne tatas abravīt arjunam vāsudevaḥ paśyasva enam viratham yudhyamānam raṇe ketum sarva dhanurdharāṇām praviṣṭaḥ bhāratīm senām tava pāṇḍava pṛṣṭhatas yodhitaḥ ca mahā vīryaiḥ sarvaiḥ bhārata bhārataiḥ pariśrāntaḥ yudhām śreṣṭhaḥ saṃprāptaḥ bhūri dakṣiṇam yuddha kāṅkṣiṇam āyāntam na etat samam iva arjuna tatas bhūriśravāḥ kruddhaḥ sātyakim yuddha durmadam keśava arjunayoḥ rājan samare prekṣamāṇayoḥ atha kṛṣṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ arjunam pratyabhāṣata paśya vṛṣṇi andhaka vyāghram saumadatti vaśam gatam pariśrāntam gatam bhūmau kṛtvā karma su duṣkaram tava antevāsinam śūram pālaya arjuna sātyakim na vaśam yajñaśīlasya gacchet eṣa vara ari han tvad kṛte puruṣa vyāghra tat āśu kriyatām vibho athā bravīt dhṛṣṭa manāḥ vāsudevam dhanaṃjayaḥ paśya vṛṣṇi pravīreṇa krīḍantam kuru puṃgavam hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt sainyānām bharata ṛṣabha sa siṃhaḥ iva mātaṅgam vikarṣan bhūri dakṣiṇaḥ atha kośāt viniṣkṛṣya khaḍgam bhūriśravāḥ raṇe mūrdhajeṣu nijagrāha padā ca urasi atāḍayat tathā tu parikṛṣyantam dṛṣṭvā sātvatam āhave paśya vṛṣṇi andhaka vyāghram saumadatti vaśam gatam tava śiṣyam mahā bāho dhanuṣi an avaram tvayā asatyaḥ vikramaḥ pārtha yatra bhūriśravāḥ raṇe viśeṣayati vārṣṇeyam sātyakim satya vikramam evam uktaḥ mahā bāhuḥ vāsudevena pāṇḍavaḥ manasā pūjayām āsa bhūriśravasam āhave vikarṣan sātvata śreṣṭham krīḍamānaḥ iva āhave saṃharṣayati mām bhūyas kurūṇām kīrti vardhanaḥ pravaram vṛṣṇi vīrāṇām yat na hanyāt hi sātyakim evam tu manasā rājan pārthaḥ saṃpūjya kauravam vāsudevam mahā bāhuḥ arjunaḥ pratyabhāṣata saindhava āsakta dṛṣṭi tvāt na enam paśyāmi mādhava iti uktvā vacanam kurvan vāsudevasya pāṇḍavaḥ sa khaḍgam yajñaśīlasya patriṇā bāhum acchinat saṃjayaḥ uvāca sa bāhuḥ apatat bhūmau sa khaḍgaḥ sa śubha aṅgadaḥ prahariṣyan hṛtaḥ bāhuḥ adṛśyena kirīṭinā sa mogham kṛtam ātmānam dṛṣṭvā pārthena kauravaḥ utsṛjya sātyakim krodhāt garhayām āsa pāṇḍavam nṛśaṃsam bata kaunteya karma idam kṛtavān asi kim nu vakṣyasi rājānam dharmaputram yudhiṣṭhiram kim kurvāṇaḥ mayā saṃkhye hataḥ bhūriśravāḥ iti idam indreṇa te sākṣāt upadiṣṭam mahātmanā astram rudreṇa vā pārtha droṇena atha kṛpeṇa vā āryeṇa sukaram hi āhuḥ ārya karma dhanaṃjaya āśu tad śīla tām eti tat idam tvayi dṛśyate katham hi rāja vaṃśyaḥ tvam kauraveyaḥ viśeṣataḥ kṣatra dharmāt apakrāntaḥ su vṛttaḥ carita vrataḥ idam tu yat ati kṣudram vārṣṇeya arthe kṛtam tvayā īdṛśam vyasanam dadyāt yaḥ na kṛṣṇasakhaḥ bhavet vrātyāḥ saṃśliṣṭa karmāṇaḥ prakṛtyā eva vigarhitāḥ vṛṣṇi andhakāḥ katham pārtha pramāṇam bhavatā kṛtāḥ evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ yūpaketuḥ mahā yaśāḥ yuyudhānam parityajya raṇe prāyam upāviśat śarān āstīrya savyena pāṇinā puṇya lakṣaṇaḥ yiyāsuḥ brahma lokāya prāṇān prāṇeṣu atha ajuhot sūrye cakṣuḥ samādhāya prasannam salile manaḥ tatas sa sarva senāyām janaḥ kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau garhayām āsa tam ca api śaśaṃsa puruṣa ṛṣabham nindyamānau tathā kṛṣṇau na ūcatuḥ kim cit apriyam praśasyamānaḥ ca tathā na ahṛṣyat yūpaketanaḥ tān tathā vādinaḥ rājan putrān tava dhanaṃjayaḥ amṛṣyamāṇaḥ manasā teṣām tasya ca bhāṣitam asaṃkruddha manāḥ vācā smārayan iva bhārata uvāca pāṇḍu tanayaḥ sa ākṣepam iva phalgunaḥ na śakyaḥ māmakaḥ hantum yaḥ me syāt bāṇa gocare yūpaketo samīkṣya tvam na mām garhitum arhasi ātta śastrasya hi raṇe vṛṣṇi vīram jighāṃsataḥ evam uktaḥ tu pārthena śirasā bhūmim aspṛśat pāṇinā ca eva savyena prāhiṇot asya dakṣiṇam yūpaketuḥ mahā rāja tūṣṇīm āsīt avāṅmukhaḥ yā prītiḥ dharmarāje me bhīme ca vadatām vare mayā tu samanujñātaḥ kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanā gaccha puṇya kṛtām lokān śibiḥ auśīnaraḥ yathā saṃjayaḥ uvāca khaḍgam ādāya cicchitsuḥ śiraḥ tasya mahātmanaḥ nihatam pāṇḍu putreṇa pramattam bhūri dakṣiṇam iyeṣa sātyakiḥ hantum śala agrajam akalmaṣam krośatām sarva sainyānām nindyamānaḥ su durmanāḥ vāryamāṇaḥ sa kṛṣṇena pārthena ca mahātmanā bhīmena cakrarakṣābhyām aśvatthāmnā kṛpeṇa ca vikrośatām ca sainyānām avadhīt tam yata vratam prāya upaviṣṭāya raṇe pārthena chinna bāhave sātyakiḥ kaurava indrāya khaḍgena apāharat śiraḥ na abhyanandanta tat sainyāḥ sātyakim tena karmaṇā sahasrākṣa samam tatra siddha cāraṇa mānavāḥ pakṣa vādān ca bahuśas prāvadan tasya sainikāḥ na vārṣṇeyasya aparādhaḥ bhavitavyam hi tat tathā tasmāt manyuḥ na vaḥ kāryaḥ krodhaḥ duḥkha karaḥ nṛṇām hantavyaḥ ca eṣa vīreṇa na atra kāryā vicāraṇā sātyakiḥ uvāca dharma vādaiḥ adharmiṣṭhāḥ dharma kañcukam āsthitāḥ yadā bālaḥ subhadrāyāḥ sutaḥ śastra vinākṛtaḥ mayā tu etat pratijñātam kṣepe kasmin cit eva hi yaḥ mām niṣpiṣya saṃgrāme jīvan hanyāt padā ruṣā ceṣṭamānam pratīghāte sa bhujam mām sa cakṣuṣaḥ yuktaḥ hi asya pratīghātaḥ kṛtaḥ me kuru puṃgavāḥ yat tu pārthena mad snehāt svām pratijñām ca rakṣatā sa khaḍgaḥ asya hṛtaḥ bāhuḥ etena eva asmi vañcitaḥ bhavitavyam ca yat bhāvi daivam ceṣṭayati iva ca api ca ayam purā gītaḥ ślokaḥ vālmīkinā bhuvi pīḍā karam amitrāṇām yat syāt kartavyam eva tat saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam ukte mahā rāja sarve kaurava pāṇḍavāḥ su nīla keśam vara dasya tasya śūrasya pārāvata lohita akṣam ākrāmat ūrdhvam vara daḥ vara arhaḥ vyāvṛtya dharmeṇa pareṇa rodasī dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca tīrṇaḥ sainya arṇavam vīraḥ pratiśrutya yudhiṣṭhire nigṛhya bhūriśravasā balāt bhuvi nipātitaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan iha utpattim śaineyasya yathā purā yathā ca bhūriśravasaḥ yatra te saṃśayaḥ nṛpa budhasya āsīt mahā indra ābhaḥ putraḥ ekaḥ purūravāḥ purūravasaḥ āyuḥ tu āyuṣaḥ nahuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ nahuṣasya yayātiḥ tu rājarṣiḥ deva saṃmitaḥ yayāteḥ devayānyām tu yaduḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ abhavat sutaḥ yadoḥ abhūt anvavāye devamīḍhaḥ iti śrutaḥ śūrasya śauriḥ nṛvaraḥ vasudevaḥ mahā yaśāḥ dhanuṣi an avaraḥ śūraḥ kārtavīrya samaḥ yudhi tad vīryaḥ ca api tatra eva kule śiniḥ abhūt nṛpaḥ tatra vai devakīm devīm vasudeva artham āptavān tām dṛṣṭvā devakīm śaure ratha sthām puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ na amṛṣyata mahā tejāḥ somadattaḥ śineḥ nṛpa madhye rāja sahasrāṇām prekṣakāṇām samantataḥ prasādayan mahādevam amarṣa vaśam āsthitaḥ tasya tuṣṭaḥ mahādevaḥ varāṇām vara daḥ prabhuḥ vareṇa chandayām āsa sa tu vavre varam nṛpaḥ madhye rāja sahasrāṇām padā hanyāt ca saṃyuge na hi śakyāḥ raṇe jetum sātvatāḥ manuja ṛṣabha labdha lakṣyāḥ ca saṃgrāme bahavaḥ citra yodhinaḥ na tulyam vṛṣṇibhiḥ iha dṛśyate kim cana prabho na jñātim avamanyante vṛddhānām śāsane ratāḥ na deva asura gandharvāḥ na yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ jetāraḥ vṛṣṇi vīrāṇām na punar mānuṣāḥ raṇe eteṣām rakṣitāraḥ ca ye syuḥ kasyām cit āpadi nityam deva parāḥ dāntāḥ dātāraḥ ca a vikatthanāḥ tena vṛṣṇi pravīrāṇām cakram na pratihanyate na tu vṛṣṇi pravīrāṇām sametya antam vrajet nṛpa dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca saṃjayaḥ uvāca bhūriśravasi saṃkrānte para lokāya bhārata vāsudevam mahā bāhuḥ arjunaḥ samacūcudat codaya aśvān bhṛśam kṛṣṇa yatas rājā jayadrathaḥ astam eti mahā bāho tvaramāṇaḥ divākaraḥ kāryam saṃrakṣyate ca eṣa kuru senā mahā rathaiḥ codaya aśvān tathā kṛṣṇa yathā hanyām jayadratham tatas kṛṣṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ rajata pratimān hayān tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rāja senā mukhyāḥ samāvrajan duryodhanaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ atha madra rāj netrābhyām krodha dīptābhyām saṃpraikṣat nirdahan iva arjunam vīkṣya saṃyāntam jayadratha ratham prati alpa avaśiṣṭam divasam nṛ vīra vighātayasva adya ripum śara oghaiḥ mithyāpratijñaḥ kaunteyaḥ pravekṣyati hutāśanam jīvitum na utsaheran vai bhrātaraḥ asya saha anugāḥ vinaṣṭaiḥ pāṇḍaveyaiḥ ca sa śaila vana kānanām vasuṃdharām imām karṇa bhokṣyāmaḥ hata kaṇṭakām kārya akāryam a jānan vai pratijñām kṛtavān raṇe nūnam ātma vināśāya pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā rakṣitam madra rājena kṛpeṇa ca mahātmanā drauṇinā rakṣyamāṇam ca mayā duḥśāsanena ca katham prāpsyati bībhatsuḥ saindhavam kāla coditaḥ yudhyante bahavaḥ śūrāḥ lambate ca divākaraḥ sa tvam karṇa mayā sārdham śūraiḥ ca anyaiḥ mahā rathaiḥ dṛḍha lakṣyeṇa śūreṇa bhīmasenena dhanvinā bhṛśam udvejitaḥ saṃkhye śara jālaiḥ anekaśas sthātavyam iti tiṣṭhāmi raṇe saṃprati mānada na eva aṅgam iṅgati kim cit me saṃtaptasya raṇa iṣubhiḥ yotsyāmi tu tathā rājan śaktyā aham parayā raṇe na hi me yudhyamānasya sāyakān ca asyataḥ śitān saindhavam prāpsyate vīraḥ savyasācī dhanaṃjayaḥ yat tu śaktimatā kāryam satatam hita kāriṇā adya yotsye arjunam aham pauruṣam svam vyapāśritaḥ paśyantu sarva bhūtāni dāruṇam loma harṣaṇam karṇa kauravayoḥ evam raṇe saṃbhāṣamāṇayoḥ arjunaḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ jaghāna tava vāhinīm ciccheda tīkṣṇa agra mukhaiḥ śūrāṇām anivartinām bhujān parigha saṃkāśān hasti hasta upamān raṇe śirāṃsi ca mahā bāhuḥ ciccheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ hasti hastān haya grīvāḥ ratha akṣān ca samantataḥ śoṇita aktān haya ārohān gṛhīta prāsa tomarān haya vāraṇa mukhyāḥ ca prāpatanta sahasraśas dhvajāḥ chatrāṇi cāpāni cāmarāṇi śirāṃsi ca acireṇa mahīm pārthaḥ cakāra rudhira uttarām hata bhūyiṣṭha yodham tat kṛtvā tava balam balī āsasāda durādharṣaḥ saindhavam satya vikramaḥ tam tathā avasthitam dṛṣṭvā tvadīyāḥ vīrya saṃmatāḥ na amṛṣyanta mahā iṣvāsāḥ phalgunam puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ duryodhanaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ atha madra rāj saṃrabdhāḥ saindhavasya arthe samāvṛṇvan kirīṭinam saṃgrāma kovidam pārtham sarve yuddha viśāradāḥ abhītāḥ paryavartanta vyādita āsyam iva antakam saindhavam pṛṣṭhatas kṛtvā jighāṃsantaḥ arjuna acyutau te bhujaiḥ bhogi bhoga ābhaiḥ dhanūṃṣi āyamya sāyakān mumucuḥ sūrya raśmi ābhān śataśas phalgunam prati tān astān asyamānān ca kirīṭī yuddha durmadaḥ dvidhā tridhā aṣṭadhā ekaikam chittvā vivyādha tān raṇe siṃha lāṅgūla ketuḥ tu darśayan śaktim ātmanaḥ śāradvatī sutaḥ rājan arjunam pratyavārayat sa viddhvā daśabhiḥ pārtham vāsudevam ca saptabhiḥ athā enam kaurava śreṣṭhāḥ sarve eva mahā rathāḥ visphārayantaḥ cāpāni visṛjantaḥ ca sāyakān tatra pārthasya śūrasya bāhvoḥ balam adṛśyata iṣūṇām akṣaya tvam ca dhanuṣaḥ gāṇḍivasya ca astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya drauṇeḥ śāradvatasya ca tam drauṇiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā vṛṣasenaḥ ca saptabhiḥ duryodhanaḥ ca viṃśatyā karṇa śalyau tribhiḥ tribhiḥ śliṣṭam tu sarvatas cakruḥ ratha maṇḍalam āśu te sūrya astamayam icchantaḥ tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ siṣicuḥ mārgaṇaiḥ ghoraiḥ girim meghāḥ iva ambuṣu te mahā astrāṇi divyāni tatra rājan vyadarśayan dhanaṃjayasya gātreṣu śūrāḥ parigha bāhavaḥ hata bhūyiṣṭha yodham tat kṛtvā tava balam balī āsasāda durādharṣaḥ saindhavam satya vikramaḥ tam karṇaḥ saṃyuge rājan pratyavārayat āśugaiḥ tam pārthaḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat raṇa ajire sūtaputram mahā bāhuḥ sarva sainyasya paśyataḥ sātvataḥ ca tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ karṇam vivyādha māriṣa tān karṇaḥ prativivyādha ṣaṣṭyā ṣaṣṭyā mahā rathaḥ tatra adbhutam apaśyāma sūtaputrasya māriṣa phalgunaḥ tu mahā bāhuḥ karṇam vaikartanam raṇe sāyakānām śatena eva sarva marmasu atāḍayat rudhira ukṣita sarva aṅgaḥ sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān śaraiḥ pañcāśatā vīraḥ phalgunam pratyavidhyata tasya tat lāghavam dṛṣṭvā na amṛṣyata raṇe arjunaḥ tatas pārthaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā vivyādha enam stanāntare cikṣepa tvarayā yuktaḥ tvarā kāle dhanaṃjayaḥ athā anyat dhanuḥ ādāya sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān karṇaḥ api dviṣatām hantā chādayām āsa phalgunam sāyakaiḥ bahu sāhasraiḥ kṛta pratikṛta īpsayā pārthaḥ aham asmi tiṣṭha tvam karṇaḥ aham tiṣṭha phalguna prekṣaṇīyau ca abhavatām sarva yodha samāgame praśasyamānau samare siddha cāraṇa vātikaiḥ ayudhyetām mahā rāja paraspara vadha eṣiṇau tatas duryodhanaḥ rājan tāvakān abhyabhāṣata yattāḥ rakṣata rādheyam na a hatvā samare arjunam nivartiṣyati rādheyaḥ iti mām uktavān vṛṣaḥ ākarṇa muktaiḥ iṣubhiḥ karṇasya caturaḥ hayān sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apāharat chādayām āsa ca śaraiḥ tava putrasya paśyataḥ sa chādyamānaḥ samare hata aśvaḥ hata sārathiḥ tam tathā viratham dṛṣṭvā ratham āropya svam tadā aśvatthāmā mahā rāja bhūyas arjunam ayodhayat śāradvataḥ tu viṃśatyā vāsudevam samārpayat dhanaṃjayam dvādaśabhiḥ ājaghāna śilīmukhaiḥ caturbhiḥ sindhurājaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ ca saptabhiḥ pṛthak pṛthak mahā rāja kṛṣṇa pārthau avidhyatām droṇaputram catuḥṣaṣṭyā madra rājam śatena ca saindhavam daśabhiḥ bhallaiḥ vṛṣasenam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ śāradvatam ca viṃśatyā viddhvā pārthaḥ samunnadat te pratijñā apratīghātam icchantaḥ savyasācinaḥ sahitāḥ tāvakāḥ tūrṇam abhipetuḥ dhanaṃjayam atha arjunaḥ sarvatodhāram astram prāduścakre trāsayan dhārtarāṣṭrān tam pratyudīyuḥ kuravaḥ pāṇḍu sūnum rathaiḥ mahārhaiḥ śara varṣāṇi avarṣan na amuhyata prāpya sa rāja putraḥ kirīṭamālī visṛjan pṛṣatkān rājya prepsuḥ savyasācī kurūṇām smaran kleśān dvādaśa varṣa vṛttān gāṇḍīva muktaiḥ iṣubhiḥ mahātmā sarvāḥ diśaḥ vyāvṛṇot aprameyaiḥ pradīpta ulkam abhavat ca antarikṣam deheṣu bhūrīṇi apatan vayāṃsi kirīṭamālī mahatā mahā yaśāḥ śarāsanena asya śarān anīka jit gadāḥ ca gurvīḥ parighān ayasmayān asīn ca śaktīḥ ca raṇe narādhipāḥ mahānti śastrāṇi ca bhīma darśanāḥ pragṛhya pārtham sahasā abhidudruvuḥ sa tān udīrṇān sa ratha aśva vāraṇān padāti saṃghān ca mahā dhanuḥ dharaḥ vipanna sarva āyudha jīvitān raṇe cakāra vīraḥ yama rāṣṭra vardhanān saṃjayaḥ uvāca sa raṇe vyacarat pārthaḥ prekṣaṇīyaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ yugapad dikṣu sarvāsu citrāṇi astrāṇi darśayan na śekuḥ sarva bhūtāni pāṇḍavam prativīkṣitum prasṛtān tasya gāṇḍīvāt śara vrātān mahātmanaḥ saṃgrāme samapaśyāma haṃsa paṅktīḥ iva ambare vinivārya sa vīrāṇām astraiḥ astrāṇi sarvaśas darśayan raudram ātmānam ugre karmaṇi dhiṣṭhitaḥ visṛjan dikṣu sarvāsu śarān asita sārathiḥ sa raṇe vyacarat tūrṇam prekṣaṇīyaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ bhramantaḥ iva śūrasya śara vrātāḥ mahātmanaḥ adṛśyanta antarikṣa sthāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas ādadānam mahā iṣvāsam saṃdadhānam ca pāṇḍavam visṛjantam ca kaunteyam na anupaśyāmahe tadā tathā sarvāḥ diśaḥ rājan sarvān ca rathinaḥ raṇe vivyādha ca catuḥṣaṣṭyā śarāṇām nata parvaṇām saindhavaḥ tu tathā viddhaḥ śaraiḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā sa varāha dhvajaḥ tūrṇam gārdhra patrān a jihma gān āśīviṣa sama prakhyān karmāra parimārjitān mumoca niśitān saṃkhye sāyakān savyasācini tribhiḥ tu viddhvā gāṇḍīvam nārācaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ arjunam aṣṭābhiḥ vājinaḥ avidhyat dhvajam ca ekena patriṇā sa vikṣipya arjunaḥ tīkṣṇān saindhava preṣitān śarān sāratheḥ ca śiraḥ kāyāt dhvajam ca samalaṃkṛtam sa chinna yaṣṭiḥ su mahān śīryamāṇaḥ śara āhataḥ varāhaḥ sindhurājasya papāta agni śikhā upamaḥ abravīt pāṇḍavam tatra tvaramāṇaḥ janārdanaḥ astam mahīdhara śreṣṭham yiyāsati divākaraḥ śṛṇuṣva eva ca me vākyam jayadratha vadham prati antarhitā tadā vāṇī megha dundubhi nisvanā tava ātmajaḥ ayam martyeṣu kula śīla dama ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ bhaviṣyati vibho sadṛśaḥ vaṃśayoḥ dvayoḥ kṣatriya pravaraḥ loke nityam śūra abhisatkṛtaḥ śiraḥ chetsyati saṃkruddhaḥ śatruḥ na ālakṣitaḥ bhuvi jñātīn sarvān uvāca idam putra sneha abhipīḍitaḥ dharaṇyām mama putrasya pātayiṣyati yaḥ śiraḥ tasya api śatadhā mūrdhā phaliṣyati na saṃśayaḥ vṛddhakṣatraḥ vanam yātaḥ tapaḥ ca iṣṭam samāsthitaḥ tasmāt jayadrathasya tvam śiraḥ chittvā mahā mṛdhe divyena astreṇa ripu han ghoreṇa adbhuta karmaṇā sa kuṇḍalam sindhupateḥ prabhañjana suta anuja utsaṅge pātayasva āśu vṛddhakṣatrasya bhārata atha tvam asya mūrdhānam pātayiṣyasi bhū tale tava api śatadhā mūrdhā phaliṣyati na saṃśayaḥ yathā ca etat na jānīyāt sa rājā pṛthivīpatiḥ tathā kuru kuru śreṣṭha divyam astram upāśritaḥ etat śrutvā tu vacanam parisaṃlihan sarva bhāra saham śaśvat gandha mālya arcitam śaram sa tu gāṇḍīva nirmuktaḥ śaraḥ śyenaḥ iva āśu gaḥ durhṛdām a praharṣāya suhṛdām harṣaṇāya ca śaraiḥ kadambakīkṛtya kāle tasmin ca pāṇḍavaḥ saṃdhyām upāste tejasvī saṃbandhī tava māriṣa upāsīnasya tasya atha kṛṣṇa keśam sa kuṇḍalam tasya utsaṅge nipatitam śiraḥ tat cāru kuṇḍalam gate tasya api śatadhā mūrdhā agacchat ariṃdama tatas sarvāṇi bhūtāni vismayam jagmuḥ uttamam vāsudevaḥ ca bībhatsum praśaśaṃsa mahā ratham tatas dṛṣṭvā vinihatam sindhurājam jayadratham bhīmasenaḥ api saṃgrāme bodhayan iva pāṇḍavam siṃhanādena mahatā pūrayām āsa rodasī tam śrutvā tu mahā nādam dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tatas vāditra ghoṣeṇa svān yodhān abhiharṣayan abhyavartata saṃgrāme bhāradvājam yuyutsayā droṇasya somakaiḥ sārdham saṃgrāmaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ tu jayam labdhvā saindhavam vinihatya ca arjunaḥ api raṇe yodhān tāvakān ratha sattamān sa deva śatrūn iva devarājaḥ kirīṭamālī vyadhamat samantāt yathā tamāṃsi abhyuditaḥ tamoghnaḥ pūrvām pratijñām samavāpya vīraḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca saṃjayaḥ uvāca saindhavam nihatam dṛṣṭvā raṇe pārthena māriṣa amarṣa vaśam āpannaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ tadā mahatā śara varṣeṇa pāṇḍavam samavākirat tau enam rathinām śreṣṭhau rathābhyām ratha sattamam ubhau ubhayatas tīkṣṇaiḥ viśikhaiḥ abhyavarṣatām sa tathā śara varṣābhyām su mahadbhyām mahā bhujaḥ pīḍyamānaḥ parām ārtim agamat rathinām varaḥ cakāra ācāryakam tatra kuntī putraḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya drauṇeḥ śāradvatasya ca manda vegān iṣūn tābhyām ajighāṃsuḥ avāsṛjat te na ati bhṛśam abhyaghnan viśikhāḥ jaya coditāḥ bahu tvāt tu parām ārtim śarāṇām tau agacchatām atha śāradvataḥ rājan kaunteya śara pīḍitaḥ vihvalam tam abhijñāya bhartāram śara pīḍitam aśvatthāmā api apāyāsīt pāṇḍaveyāt ratha antaram dṛṣṭvā śāradvatam pārthaḥ mūrchitam śara pīḍitam rathaḥ eva mahā iṣvāsaḥ kṛpaṇam paryadevayat paśyan idam mahā prājñaḥ kṣattā rājānam uktavān nīyatām para lokāya sādhu ayam kula pāṃsanaḥ tat idam samanuprāptam vacanam satya vādinaḥ tad kṛte hi adya paśyāmi śara talpa gatam kṛpam kaḥ hi brāhmaṇam ācāryam abhidruhyeta mādṛśaḥ ṛṣi putraḥ mama ācāryaḥ droṇasya dayitaḥ sakhā eṣa śete rathopasthe mad bāṇaiḥ abhipīḍitaḥ a kāmayānena mayā viśikhaiḥ arditaḥ bhṛśam avāsīdat rathopasthe prāṇān pīḍayati iva me śara arditena hi mayā prekṣaṇīyaḥ mahā dyutiḥ kṛpaṇam sva rathe sannam paśya kṛṣṇa yathā gatam upākṛtya tu vai vidyām ācāryebhyaḥ nara ṛṣabhāḥ ye tu vidyām upādāya gurubhyaḥ puruṣa adhamāḥ tat idam narakāya adya kṛtam karma mayā dhruvam ācāryam śara varṣeṇa rathe sādayatā kṛpam yat tat pūrvam upākurvan astram mām abravīt kṛpaḥ tat idam vacanam sādhoḥ ācāryasya mahātmanaḥ na anuṣṭhitam tam eva ājau viśikhaiḥ abhivarṣatā saindhavam nihatam dṛṣṭvā rādheyaḥ samupādravat upāyāntam tu rādheyam dṛṣṭvā pārthaḥ mahā rathaḥ eṣa prayāti ādhirathiḥ sātyakeḥ syandanam prati na mṛṣyati hatam nūnam bhūriśravasam āhave yatra yāti eṣa tatra tvam codaya aśvān janārdana mā somadatteḥ padavīm gamayet sātyakim vṛṣaḥ evam uktaḥ mahā bāhuḥ keśavaḥ savyasācinā pratyuvāca mahā tejāḥ kāla yuktam idam vacaḥ alam eṣa mahā bāhuḥ karṇāya ekaḥ hi pāṇḍava kim punar draupadeyābhyām sahitaḥ sātvata ṛṣabhaḥ na ca tāvat kṣamaḥ pārtha karṇena tava saṃgaraḥ tvad artham pūjyamānā eṣā rakṣyate para vīra han atas karṇaḥ prayātu atra sātvatasya yathā tathā aham jñāsyāmi kauravya kālam asya durātmanaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca yaḥ asau karṇena vīreṇa vārṣṇeyasya samāgamaḥ sātyakiḥ ca api virathaḥ kam samārūḍhavān ratham cakrarakṣau ca pāñcālyau tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca hanta te varṇayiṣyāmi yathāvṛttam mahā raṇe śuśrūṣasva sthiraḥ bhūtvā durācaritam ātmanaḥ vijetavyaḥ yathā vīraḥ sātyakiḥ yūpaketunā atīta anāgatam rājan sa hi vetti janārdanaḥ atas sūtam samāhūya dārukam saṃdideśa ha rathaḥ me yujyatām kālyam iti rājan mahā balaḥ na hi devāḥ na gandharvāḥ na yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ mānavāḥ vā vijetāraḥ kṛṣṇayoḥ santi ke cana pitāmaha purogāḥ ca devāḥ siddhāḥ ca tam viduḥ tayoḥ prabhāvam atulam śṛṇu yuddham ca tat yathā sātyakim viratham dṛṣṭvā karṇam ca abhyudyata āyudham dadhmau śaṅkham mahā vegam ārṣabheṇa atha mādhavaḥ dārukaḥ avetya saṃdeśam śrutvā śaṅkhasya ca svanam haya udagraiḥ mahā vegaiḥ hema bhāṇḍa vibhūṣitaiḥ dhanaṃjaya ratham hitvā rādheyam pratyudīyayuḥ rādheyaḥ api mahā rāja śara varṣam samutsṛjan tādṛśam bhuvi vā yuddham divi vā śrutam iti uta tayoḥ dṛṣṭvā mahā rāja karma saṃmūḍha cetanam gata pratyāgata āvṛttaiḥ maṇḍalaiḥ saṃnivartanaiḥ atīva avahitāḥ draṣṭum karṇa śaineyayoḥ raṇam mitra arthe tau parākrāntau spardhinau śuṣmiṇau raṇe karṇaḥ ca amara saṃkāśaḥ yuyudhānaḥ ca sātyakiḥ anyonyam tau mahā rāja śara varṣaiḥ avarṣatām pramamātha śineḥ pautram karṇaḥ sāyaka vṛṣṭibhiḥ amṛṣyamāṇaḥ nidhanam kauravya jalasaṃdhayoḥ karṇaḥ śoka samāviṣṭaḥ mahā uragaḥ iva śvasan sa śaineyam raṇe kruddhaḥ pradahan iva cakṣuṣā mahatā śara varṣeṇa gajaḥ pratigajam yathā tatas karṇam śineḥ pautraḥ sarva pāraśavaiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apāharat aśvān ca caturaḥ śvetān nijaghne niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ chittvā dhvajam śatena eva śatadhā puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ cakāra viratham karṇam tava putrasya paśyataḥ tatas vimanasaḥ rājan tāvakāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ vṛṣasenaḥ karṇa sutaḥ śalyaḥ madra adhipaḥ tathā tatas paryākulam sarvam na prājñāyata kim cana tathā sātyakinā vīre virathe sūtaje kṛte hāhākāraḥ tatas rājan sarva sainyeṣu ca abhavat karṇaḥ api vihvalaḥ rājan sātvatena arditaḥ śaraiḥ kṛtām rājya pradānena pratijñām paripālayan duḥśāsana mukhān śūrān na avadhīt sātyakiḥ vaśī rakṣan pratijñām ca punar bhīmasena kṛtām purā bhīmasenena tu vadhaḥ putrāṇām te pratiśrutaḥ punar dyūte ca pārthena vadhaḥ karṇasya śaṃśrutaḥ na aśaknuvan ca tam hantum sātyakim pravarāḥ rathāḥ drauṇiḥ ca kṛtavarmā ca tathā eva anye mahā rathāḥ nirjitāḥ dhanuṣā ekena śataśas kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ kāṅkṣatā para lokam ca dharmarājasya ca priyam kṛṣṇayoḥ sadṛśaḥ vīrye sātyakiḥ śatru karśanaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ vā api bhavet loke pārthaḥ vā api dhanurdharaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca ajayyam ratham āsthāya vāsudevasya sātyakiḥ viratham kṛtavān karṇam vāsudeva samaḥ yuvā dārukeṇa samāyuktam sva bāhu bala darpitaḥ kaccit anyam samārūḍhaḥ sa ratham sātyakiḥ punar etat icchāmi aham śrotum kuśalaḥ hi asi bhāṣitum saṃjayaḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan yathā tasya ratham anyam mahāmatiḥ dārukasya anujaḥ tūrṇam kalpanā vidhi kalpitam āyasaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ ca api paṭṭaiḥ naddham sa kūbaram aśvaiḥ vāta javaiḥ yuktam hema bhāṇḍa paricchadaiḥ pāṇḍuraiḥ indu saṃkāśaiḥ sarva śabda atigaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ citra kāñcana saṃnāhaiḥ vāji mukhyaiḥ viśām pate ghaṇṭā jāla ākula ravam śakti tomara vidyutam ratham saṃpādayām āsa megha gambhīra nisvanam dārukaḥ api yathākāmam prayayau keśava antikam karṇasya api mahā rāja śaṅkha go kṣīra pāṇḍuraiḥ citra kāñcana saṃnāhaiḥ sat aśvaiḥ vegavattaraiḥ etat te sarvam ākhyātam yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi bhūyas ca api nibodha tvam tava apanaya jam kṣayam ekatriṃśat tava sutāḥ bhīmasenena pātitāḥ śataśas nihatāḥ śūrāḥ sātvatena arjunena ca bhīṣmam pramukhatas kṛtvā bhagadattam ca māriṣa dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca tathā gateṣu śūreṣu teṣām mama ca saṃjaya kim vai bhīmaḥ tadā akārṣīt tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca virathaḥ bhīmasenaḥ vai karṇa vāc śalya pīḍitaḥ amarṣa vaśam āpannaḥ phalgunam vākyam abravīt a kṛtāstraka mā yodhīḥ bāla saṃgrāma kātara iti mām abravīt karṇaḥ paśyataḥ te dhanaṃjaya etat vratam mahā bāho tvayā saha kṛtam mayā karṇa karṇa vṛthādṛṣṭe sūtaputra ātma saṃstuta adharmabuddhe śṛṇu me yat tvā vakṣyāmi sāṃpratam dvividham karma śūrāṇām yuddhe jaya parājayau yadṛcchayā bhīmasenam viratham kṛtavān asi pūrayantam yathāśakti śūra karma āhave tathā paśyatām sarva sainyānām keśavasya mama eva ca na ca tvām paruṣam kim cit uktavān paṇḍu nandanaḥ yasmāt tu bahu rūkṣam ca śrāvitaḥ te vṛkodaraḥ tvayā tasya dhanuḥ chinnam ātma nāśāya durmate tasmāt vadhyaḥ asi me mūḍha sa bhṛtya bala vāhanaḥ hantāsmi vṛṣasenam te prekṣamāṇasya saṃyuge ye ca anye api upayāsyanti buddhi mohena mām nṛpāḥ tān ca sarvān haniṣyāmi satyena āyudham ālabhe tvām ca mūḍha a kṛta prajñam atimāninam āhave dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaḥ mandaḥ bhṛśam tapsyati pātitam mahān su tumulaḥ śabdaḥ babhūva rathinām tadā manda raśmiḥ sahasrāṃśuḥ astam girim upāgamat tatas rājan hṛṣīkeśaḥ saṃgrāma śirasi sthitam tīrṇa pratijñam bībhatsum pariṣvajya idam abravīt diṣṭyā saṃpāditā jiṣṇo pratijñā mahatī tvayā diṣṭyā ca nihataḥ pāpaḥ vṛddhakṣatraḥ saha ātmajaḥ dhārtarāṣṭra balam prāpya deva senā api bhārata sīdeta samare jiṣṇo na atra kāryā vicāraṇā na tam paśyāmi lokeṣu cintayan puruṣam kva cit mahā prabhāvāḥ bahavaḥ tvayā tulya adhikā api vā sametāḥ pṛthivīpālāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrasya kāraṇāt te tvām prāpya raṇe kruddham na abhyavartanta daṃśitāḥ na īdṛśam śaknuyāt kaḥ cit raṇe kartum parākramam yādṛśam kṛtavān adya tvam ekaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ vardhayiṣyāmi bhūyas tvām vijita arim hata dviṣam pratijñā iyam mayā uttīrṇā vibudhaiḥ api dustarā anāścaryaḥ jayaḥ teṣām yeṣām nāthaḥ asi mādhava tvad prasādāt mahīm kṛtsnām saṃprāpsyati yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vardhanīyāḥ tava vayam preṣyāḥ ca madhusūdana evam uktaḥ smayan kṛṣṇaḥ śanakais vāhayan hayān darśayām āsa pārthāya krūram āyodhanam mahat śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca pṛthivyām śerate śūrāḥ pārthivāḥ tvad śaraiḥ hatāḥ vikīrṇa śastra ābharaṇāḥ vipanna aśva ratha dvipāḥ saṃchinna bhinna varmāṇaḥ vaiklavyam paramam gatāḥ sa sattvāḥ gatasattvāḥ ca prabhayā parayā yutāḥ sa jīvāḥ iva lakṣyante gatasattvāḥ narādhipāḥ teṣām śaraiḥ svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śastraiḥ ca vividhaiḥ śitaiḥ vāhanaiḥ āyudhaiḥ ca eva saṃpūrṇām paśya medinīm varmabhiḥ carmabhiḥ hāraiḥ śirobhiḥ ca sa kuṇḍalaiḥ uṣṇīṣaiḥ mukuṭaiḥ sragbhiḥ cūḍāmaṇibhiḥ ambaraiḥ kaṇṭha sūtraiḥ aṅgadaiḥ ca niṣkaiḥ api ca su prabhaiḥ anyaiḥ ca ābharaṇaiḥ citraiḥ bhāti bhārata medinī vividhaiḥ ca paristomaiḥ aśvānām ca prakīrṇakaiḥ kuthābhiḥ ca vicitrābhiḥ varūthaiḥ ca mahādhanaiḥ saṃstīrṇām vasudhām paśya citra paṭṭaiḥ iva āvṛtām saṃsyūtān vājibhiḥ sārdham dharaṇyām paśya ca aparān padāti sādi saṃghān ca kṣataja ogha pariplutān saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam saṃdarśayan kṛṣṇaḥ raṇa bhūmim kirīṭinaḥ svaiḥ sametaḥ sa muditaḥ pāñcajanyam vyanādayat saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā rathāt āplutya bhārata paryaṣvajat tadā kṛṣṇau ānanda aśru pariplutaḥ pramṛjya vadanam śubhram puṇḍarīka sama prabham abravīt vāsudevam ca pāṇḍavam ca dhanaṃjayam diṣṭyā paśyāmi saṃgrāme tīrṇa bhārau mahā rathau diṣṭyā ca nihataḥ pāpaḥ saindhavaḥ puruṣa adhamaḥ kṛṣṇa diṣṭyā mama prītiḥ mahatī pratipāditā diṣṭyā śatru gaṇāḥ ca eva nimagnāḥ śoka sāgare na teṣām duṣkaram kim cit triṣu lokeṣu vidyate sarva loka guruḥ yeṣām tvam nāthaḥ madhusūdana tava prasādāt govinda vayam jeṣyāmahe ripūn yathā pūrvam prasādāt te dānavān pākaśāsanaḥ dhruvaḥ hi teṣām vārṣṇeya yeṣām tuṣṭaḥ asi mādhava na teṣām vidyate pāpam saṃgrāme vā parājayaḥ tridaśa īśvara nāthaḥ tvam yeṣām tuṣṭaḥ asi mādhava tvad prasādāt dhṛṣīkeśa śakraḥ sura gaṇa īśvaraḥ trailokya vijayam śrīmān prāptavān raṇa mūrdhani amara tvam gatāḥ kṛṣṇa lokān ca aśnuvate akṣayān sura īśa tvam gataḥ śakraḥ hatvā daityān sahasraśas tvad prasādāt dhṛṣīkeśa jagat sthāvara jaṅgamam ekārṇavam idam pūrvam sarvam āsīt tamaḥ mayam tvad prasādāt prakāśa tvam jagat prāptam narottama sraṣṭāram sarva lokānām paramātmānam acyutam ye prapannāḥ hṛṣīkeśam na te muhyanti karhi cit tvām bhaktāḥ ye hṛṣīkeśa durgāṇi atitaranti te param purāṇam puruṣam purāṇānām param ca yat tam prapadya mahātmānam bhūtim āpnoti anuttamām dhanaṃjaya sakhā yaḥ ca dhanaṃjaya hitaḥ ca yaḥ iti uktau tau mahātmānau ubhau keśava pāṇḍavau tau abrūtām tadā hṛṣṭau rājānam pṛthivīpatim tava kopa agninā dagdhaḥ pāpaḥ rājā jayadrathaḥ udīrṇam ca api su mahat dhārtarāṣṭra balam raṇe tvām hi cakṣuḥ haṇam vīram kopayitvā suyodhanaḥ sa mitra bandhuḥ samare prāṇān tyakṣyati durmatiḥ śara talpa gataḥ śete bhīṣmaḥ kuru pitāmahaḥ durlabhaḥ hi jayaḥ teṣām saṃgrāme ripu sūdana yātāḥ mṛtyu vaśam te vai yeṣām kruddhaḥ asi pāṇḍava rājyam prāṇāḥ priyāḥ putrāḥ saukhyāni vividhāni ca acirāt tasya naśyanti yeṣām kruddhaḥ asi mānada vinaṣṭān kauravān manye sa putra paśu bāndhavān tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ abhivādya gurum jyeṣṭham mārgaṇaiḥ kṣata vikṣatau sthitau āstām mahā iṣvāsau pāñcālyaiḥ parivāritau tau dṛṣṭva muditau vīrau prāñjalī ca agratas sthitau diṣṭyā paśyāmi vām vīrau vimuktau sainya sāgarāt droṇa grāhāt durādharṣāt dhārdikya makara ālayāt diṣṭyā ca nirjitāḥ saṃkhye pṛthivyām sarva pārthivāḥ yuvām vijayinau ca api diṣṭyā paśyāmi saṃyuge diṣṭyā droṇaḥ jitaḥ saṃkhye hārdikyaḥ ca mahā balaḥ sainya arṇavam samuttīrṇau diṣṭyā paśyāmi ca anaghau mama prāṇa samau ca eva diṣṭyā paśyāmi vām aham iti uktvā pāṇḍavaḥ rājā yuyudhāna vṛkodarau sasvaje puruṣa vyāghrau harṣāt bāṣpam mumoca ha tatas pramuditam sarvam balam āsīt viśām pate pāṇḍavānām jayam dṛṣṭvā yuddhāya ca manaḥ dadhe saṃjayaḥ uvāca na droṇaḥ na ca rādheyaḥ na aśvatthāmā kṛpaḥ na ca na hi asya vidyate trātā sākṣāt api puraṃdaraḥ yam upāśritya saṃgrāme kṛtaḥ śastra samudyamaḥ paruṣāṇi sabhā madhye proktavān yaḥ sma pāṇḍavān yasya vīryam samāśritya śamam yācantam acyutam evam klānta manāḥ rājan upāyāt droṇam īkṣitum tatas tat sarvam ācakhyau kurūṇām vaiśasam mahat parān vijayataḥ ca api dhārtarāṣṭrān nimajjataḥ paśya mūrdhāvasiktānām ācārya kadanam kṛtam kṛtvā pramukhatas śūram bhīṣmam mama pitāmaham tam nihatya pralubdhaḥ ayam śikhaṇḍī pūrṇamānasaḥ pāñcālaiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ senā agram abhikarṣati aparaḥ ca api durdharṣaḥ śiṣyaḥ te savyasācinā akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta hatvā hataḥ rājā jayadrathaḥ asmad vijaya kāmānām suhṛdām upakāriṇām gantāsmi katham ānṛṇyam gatānām yama sādanam ye mad artham parīpsanti vasudhām vasudhādhipāḥ saḥ aham kāpuruṣaḥ kṛtvā mitrāṇām kṣayam īdṛśam na aśvamedha sahasreṇa pātum ātmānam utsahe vyāyacchantaḥ jigīṣantaḥ prāptāḥ vaivasvata kṣayam katham patita vṛttasya pṛthivī suhṛdām druhaḥ vivaram nā aśakat dātum mama pārthiva saṃsadi saḥ aham rudhira sikta aṅgam rājñām madhye pitāmaham śayānam nā aśakam trātum bhīṣmam āyodhane hatam tam mām an ārya puruṣam mitra druham a dhārmikam jalasaṃdham mahā iṣvāsam paśya sātyakinā hatam mad artham udyatam śūram prāṇān tyaktvā mahā ratham kāmbojam nihatam dṛṣṭvā tathā alambuṣam eva ca anyān bahūn ca suhṛdaḥ jīvita arthaḥ adya kaḥ mama vyāyacchantaḥ hatāḥ śūrāḥ mad arthe ye a parāṅmukhāḥ yatamānāḥ param śaktyāḥ vijetum ahitān mama teṣām gatvā aham ānṛṇyam adya śaktyā paraṃtapa satyam te pratijānāmi sarva śastrabhṛtām vara iṣṭāpūrtena ca śape vīryeṇa ca sutaiḥ api nihatya tān raṇe sarvān pāñcālān pāṇḍavaiḥ saha śāntim labdhāsmi teṣām vā raṇe gantā salokatām na hi idānīm sahāyāḥ me parīpsanti anupaskṛtāḥ śreyaḥ hi pāṇḍūn manyante na tathā asmān mahā bhuja bhavān upekṣām kurute su śiṣya tvāt dhanaṃjaye yaḥ hi mitram a vijñāya yāthātathyena manda dhīḥ tādṛś rūpam idam kāryam kṛtam mama suhṛd bruvaiḥ abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayaḥ atha vasātayaḥ saḥ aham adya gamiṣyāmi yatra te puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ hatāḥ mad artham saṃgrāme yudhyamānāḥ kirīṭinā na hi me jīvitena arthaḥ tān ṛte puruṣa ṛṣabhān ācāryaḥ pāṇḍu putrāṇām anujānātu naḥ bhavān dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca saṃjayaḥ uvāca niṣṭānakaḥ mahān āsīt sainyānām tava bhārata saindhavam nihatam dṛṣṭvā bhūriśravasam eva ca yena mantreṇa nihatāḥ śataśas kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ muhūrtam iva tu dhyātvā bhṛśam ārtaḥ abhyabhāṣata duryodhana kim evam mām vāc śaraiḥ abhikṛntasi ajayyam samare nityam bruvāṇam savyasācinam etena eva arjunam jñātum alam kaurava saṃyuge yat śikhaṇḍī avadhīt bhīṣmam pālyamānaḥ kirīṭinā avadhyam nihatam dṛṣṭvā saṃyuge deva mānuṣaiḥ tadā eva ajñāsiṣam aham na iyam asti iti bhāratī yam puṃsām triṣu lokeṣu sarva śūram amaṃsmahi tasmin vinihate śūre kim śeṣam paryupāsmahe yān sma tān glahate tātaḥ śakuniḥ kuru saṃsadi akṣān na te akṣāḥ niśitāḥ bāṇāḥ te śatru tāpanāḥ yān tadā khyāpyamānān tvam vidureṇa na budhyase tāḥ tāḥ vilapataḥ ca api vidurasya mahātmanaḥ dhīrasya vācaḥ nā aśrauṣīḥ kṣemāya vadataḥ śivāḥ yat ca naḥ prekṣamāṇānām kṛṣṇām ānāyayaḥ sabhām an arhatīm kule jātām sarva dharma anucāriṇīm tasya adharmasya gāndhāre phalam prāptam idam tvayā yat ca tān pāṇḍavān dyūte viṣameṇa vijitya ha prāvrājayaḥ tadā araṇye raurava ajina vāsasaḥ putrāṇām iva ca eteṣām dharmam ācaratām sadā pāṇḍavānām ayam kopaḥ tvayā śakuninā saha āhṛtaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya saṃmate kuru saṃsadi duḥśāsanena saṃyuktaḥ karṇena parivardhitaḥ kṣattuḥ vākyam an ādṛtya tvayā abhyastaḥ punar punar āśaṃsata paritrāṇam arjunāt sa mahīpatiḥ na kim cit anupaśyāmi jīvita trāṇam ātmanaḥ majjantam iva ca ātmānam dhṛṣṭadyumnasya kilbiṣe paśyāmi a hatvā pāñcālān saha tena śikhaṇḍinā aśaktaḥ sindhurājasya bhūtvā trāṇāya bhārata sauvarṇam satya saṃdhasya dhvajam akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ apaśyan yudhi bhīṣmasya katham āśaṃsase jayam hataḥ bhūriśravāḥ ca eva kim śeṣam tatra manyase yat ca apaśyam hatam bhīṣmam paśyataḥ te anujasya vai duḥśāsanasya kauravya kurvāṇam karma duṣkaram imāni pāṇḍavānām ca sṛñjayānām ca bhārata anīkāni ādravante mām sahitāni adya māriṣa na a hatvā sarva pāñcālān kavacasya vimokṣaṇam kartāsmi samare karma dhārtarāṣṭra hitam tava rājan brūyāḥ sutam me tvam aśvatthāmānam āhave na somakāḥ pramoktavyāḥ jīvitam parirakṣatā yat ca pitrā anuśiṣṭaḥ asi tat vacaḥ paripālaya dharma artha kāma kuśalaḥ dharma arthau api a pīḍayan dharma pradhānaḥ kāryāṇi kuryāḥ ca iti punar punar cakṣuḥ manobhyām saṃtoṣyāḥ viprāḥ sevyāḥ ca śaktitaḥ na ca eṣām vipriyam kāryam te hi vahni śikhā upamāḥ eṣa tu aham anīkāni praviśāmi ari sūdana raṇāya mahate rājan tvayā vāc śalya pīḍitaḥ rātrau api hi yotsyante saṃrabdhāḥ kuru sṛñjayāḥ evam uktvā tatas prāyāt droṇaḥ pāṇḍava sṛñjayān muṣṇan kṣatriya tejāṃsi nakṣatrāṇām iva aṃśumān saṃjayaḥ uvāca paśya kṛṣṇa sahāyena pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā ācārya vihitam vyūham bhinnam devaiḥ su durbhidam miṣatām yodha mukhyānām saindhavaḥ vinipātitaḥ paśya rādheya rājānaḥ pṛthivyām pravarāḥ yudhi pārthena ekena nihatāḥ siṃhena iva itarāḥ mṛgāḥ alpa avaśeṣam sainyam me kṛtam śakrātmajena ha abhayam saindhavasya ājau dattvā droṇaḥ paraṃtapaḥ prādāt kirīṭine dvāram paśya nirguṇa tām mama yadi adāsyam anujñām vai pūrvam eva gṛhān prati jayadrathaḥ jīvita arthī gacchamānaḥ gṛhān prati mayā anāryeṇa saṃruddhaḥ droṇāt prāpya abhayam raṇe adya me bhrātaraḥ kṣīṇāḥ citrasena ādayaḥ yudhi bhīmasenam samāsādya paśyatām naḥ durātmanām karṇaḥ uvāca ācāryam mā vigarhasva śaktyā yudhyati asau dvijaḥ ajayyān pāṇḍavān manye droṇena astra vidā mṛdhe tathā hi enam atikramya praviṣṭaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ tatas naḥ yudhyamānānām param śaktyā suyodhana param yatnam kurvatām ca tvayā sārdham raṇa ajire hatvā asmākam pauruṣam hi daivam paścāt karoti naḥ satatam ceṣṭamānānām nikṛtyā vikrameṇa ca yat kartavyam manuṣyeṇa vyavasāyavatā satā nikṛtyā nikṛtāḥ pārthāḥ viṣa yogaiḥ ca bhārata dagdhāḥ jatu gṛhe ca api dyūtena ca parājitāḥ rāja nītim vyapāśritya prahitāḥ ca eva kānanam yatataḥ tava teṣām ca daivam mārgeṇa yāsyati na teṣām mati pūrvam hi su kṛtam dṛśyate kva cit duṣkṛtam tava vā vīra buddhyā hīnam kuru udvaha daivam pramāṇam sarvasya sukṛtasya itarasya vā na tathā pāṇḍu putrāṇām evam yuddham avartata taiḥ alpaiḥ bahavaḥ yūyam kṣayam nītāḥ prahāriṇaḥ śaṅke daivasya tat karma pauruṣam yena nāśitam saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam saṃbhāṣamāṇānām bahu tat tat janādhipa pāṇḍavānām anīkāni samadṛśyanta saṃyuge tāvakānām paraiḥ sārdham rājan durmantrite tava saṃjayaḥ uvāca tat udīrṇa gaja aśva ogham balam tava janādhipa pāṇḍu senām abhidrutya yodhayām āsa sarvatas pāñcālāḥ kuravaḥ ca eva yodhayantaḥ parasparam yama rāṣṭrāya mahate para lokāya dīkṣitāḥ śūrāḥ śūraiḥ samāgamya śara tomara śaktibhiḥ rathinām rathibhiḥ sārdham rudhira srāvi dāruṇam vāraṇāḥ ca mahā rāja samāsādya parasparam viṣāṇaiḥ dārayām āsuḥ saṃkruddhāḥ ca mada utkaṭāḥ haya ārohān haya ārohāḥ prāsa śakti paraśvadhaiḥ pattayaḥ ca mahā bāho śataśas śastra pāṇayaḥ gotrāṇām nāmadheyānām kulānām ca eva māriṣa śravaṇāt hi vijānīmaḥ pāñcālān kurubhiḥ saha anyonyam samare yodhāḥ śara śakti paraśvadhaiḥ śaraiḥ daśa diśaḥ rājan teṣām muktaiḥ sahasraśas tathā prayudhyamāneṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu nirbhayaḥ abhyavartata putraḥ te pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm sa saṃnipātaḥ tumulaḥ tasya teṣām ca bhārata na śekuḥ bhāratam yuddhe pāṇḍavāḥ samavekṣitum palāyane kṛta utsāhāḥ nirutsāhāḥ dviṣat jaye paryadhāvanta pāñcālāḥ vadhyamānāḥ mahātmanā ardyamānāḥ śaraiḥ tūrṇam nyapatan pāṇḍu sainikāḥ na tādṛśam raṇe karma kṛtavantaḥ tu tāvakāḥ yādṛśam kṛtavān rājā putraḥ tava viśām pate putreṇa tava sā senā pāṇḍavī mathitā raṇe kṣīṇa toya anila arkābhyām hata tviṣ iva padminī babhūva pāṇḍavī senā tava putrasya tejasā pāṇḍu senām hatām dṛṣṭvā tava putreṇa bhārata bhīmasena purogāḥ tu pāñcālāḥ samupādravan virāṭa drupadau ṣaḍbhiḥ śatena ca śikhaṇḍinam dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca saptatyā dharmaputram ca saptabhiḥ kekayān ca eva cedīn ca bahubhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ śataśas ca aparān yodhān sa dvipa aśva rathān raṇe tasya tān nighnataḥ śatrūn rukma pṛṣṭham mahat dhanuḥ bhallābhyām pāṇḍavaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ tridhā ciccheda māriṣa vivyādha ca enam daśabhiḥ samyak astaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ marmāṇi bhittvā te sarve saṃbhagnāḥ kṣitim āviśan tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā tava putrasya māriṣa śaram parama durvāram preṣayām āsa saṃyuge tatas pāñcāla sainyānām bhṛśam āsīt ravaḥ mahān hataḥ rājā iti rāja indra muditānām samantataḥ bāṇa śabda ravaḥ ca ugraḥ śuśruve tatra māriṣa hṛṣṭaḥ duryodhanaḥ ca api dṛḍham ādāya kārmukam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti rājānam bruvan pāṇḍavam abhyayāt pratyudyayuḥ tam tvaritāḥ pāñcālāḥ rāja gṛddhinaḥ caṇḍa vāta uddhatān meghān nighnan raśmi mucaḥ yathā tatas rājan mahān āsīt saṃgrāmaḥ bhūri vardhanaḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca sametānām yuyutsayā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca yat tadā prāviśat pāṇḍūn ācāryaḥ kupitaḥ vaśī uktvā duryodhanam samyak mama śāstra atigam sutam katham droṇam mahā iṣvāsam pāṇḍavāḥ paryavārayan ke arakṣan dakṣiṇam cakram ācāryasya mahātmanaḥ ke ca uttaram arakṣanta nighnataḥ śātravān raṇe nṛtyan sa ratha mārgeṣu sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca sāyāhne saindhavam hatvā rājñā pārthaḥ sametya ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā iṣvāsaḥ droṇam eva abhyadhāvatām tathā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tūrṇam bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ pṛthak camūbhyām saṃsaktau droṇam eva abhyadhāvatām dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śatānīkaḥ virāṭaḥ ca sa kekayaḥ matsyāḥ śālveya senāḥ ca droṇam eva yayuḥ yudhi drupadaḥ ca tathā rājā pāñcālaiḥ abhirakṣitaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna pitā rājan droṇam eva abhyavartata draupadeyāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ prabhadrakāḥ ca pāñcālāḥ ṣaṣ sahasrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ tathā itare nara vyāghrāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ teṣu śūreṣu yuddhāya gateṣu bharata ṛṣabha babhūva rajanī ghorā bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhinī yodhānām aśivā raudrā rājan antaka gāminī kuñjara aśva manuṣyāṇām prāṇānta karaṇī tadā tasyām rajanyām ghorāyām nadantyaḥ sarvatas śivāḥ ulūkāḥ ca api adṛśyanta śaṃsantaḥ vipulam bhayam viśeṣataḥ kauravāṇām dhvajinyām ati dāruṇam bherī śabdena mahatā mṛdaṅgānām svanena ca gajānām garjitaiḥ ca api turaṅgāṇām ca heṣitaiḥ tatas samabhavat yuddham saṃdhyāyām ati dāruṇam droṇasya ca mahā rāja sṛñjayānām ca sarvaśas tamasā ca āvṛte loke na prājñāyata kim cana na apaśyāma rajaḥ bhaumam kaśmalena abhisaṃvṛtāḥ ghoraḥ caṭacaṭā śabdaḥ śastrāṇām patatām abhūt bhaumam rajaḥ atha rāja indra śoṇitena praśāmitam śātakaumbhaiḥ ca kavacaiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ ca tamaḥ abhyagāt tatas sā bhāratī senā maṇi hema vibhūṣitā dyauḥ iva āsīt sa nakṣatrā rajanyām bharata ṛṣabha gomāyu baḍa saṃghuṣṭā śakti dhvaja samākulā dāruṇa abhirutā ghorā kṣveḍita utkruṣṭa nāditā samāvṛṇvan diśaḥ sarvāḥ mahā indra aśani nisvanaḥ sā niśīthe mahā rāja senā adṛśyata bhāratī aṅgadaiḥ kuṇḍalaiḥ niṣkaiḥ śastraiḥ ca eva avabhāsitā tatra nāgāḥ rathāḥ ca eva jāmbūnada vibhūṣitāḥ niśāyām pratyadṛśyanta meghāḥ iva sa vidyutaḥ ṛṣṭi śakti gadā bāṇa musala prāsa paṭṭiśāḥ saṃpatantaḥ vyadṛśyanta bhrājamānāḥ iva agnayaḥ duryodhana purovātām ratha nāga balāhakām vāditra ghoṣa stanitām cāpa vidyut dhvajaiḥ vṛtām droṇa pāṇḍava parjanyām khaḍga śakti gadā aśanim śara dhārā astra pavanām bhṛśam śīta uṣṇa saṃkulām ghorām vismāpanīm ugrām jīvita chidam aplavām tām prāviśan ati bhayām senām yuddha cikīrṣavaḥ bhīrūṇām trāsa janane śūrāṇām harṣa vardhane droṇam abhyadravan kruddhāḥ sahitāḥ pāṇḍu sṛñjayāḥ tān sarvān vimukhān cakre kān cit ninye yama kṣayam dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca a mṛṣyamāṇe saṃrabdhe kā vaḥ abhūt vai matiḥ tadā duryodhanam tathā putram uktvā śāstra atigam mama yat prāviśat ameya ātmā kim pārthaḥ pratyapadyata yat abhyagāt mahā tejāḥ pāñcālān aparājitaḥ kim amanyata durdharṣaḥ praviṣṭe śatru tāpane ke ca asya pṛṣṭhatas agacchan vīrāḥ śūrasya yudhyataḥ manye aham pāṇḍavān sarvān bhāradvāja śara arditān śiśire kampamānāḥ vai kṛśāḥ gāvaḥ iva abhibho praviśya sa mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāñcālān ari mardanaḥ sarveṣu sainyeṣu ca saṃgateṣu rātrau sameteṣu mahā ratheṣu saṃloḍyamāneṣu pṛthagvidheṣu ke vaḥ tadānīm matimantaḥ āsan hatān ca eva viṣaktān ca parābhūtān ca śaṃsasi rathinaḥ virathān ca eva kṛtān yuddheṣu māmakān katham eṣām tadā tatra pārthānām apalāyinām prakāśam abhavat rātrau katham kuruṣu saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca rātri yuddhe tadā rājan vartamāne su dāruṇe droṇam abhyadravan rātrau pāṇḍavāḥ saha sainikāḥ tatas droṇaḥ kekayān ca dhṛṣṭadyumnasya ca ātmajān preṣayat mṛtyu lokāya sarvān iṣubhiḥ āśugaiḥ tān sarvān preṣayām āsa para lokāya bhārata pramathnantam tadā vīram bhāradvājam mahā ratham abhyavartata saṃkruddhaḥ śibiḥ rājan pratāpavān tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya pāṇḍavānām mahā ratham vivyādha daśabhiḥ droṇaḥ sarva pāraśavaiḥ śaraiḥ tam śibiḥ prativivyādha triṃśatā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tasya droṇaḥ hayān hatvā sārathim ca mahātmanaḥ atha asya sa śirastrāṇam śiraḥ kāyāt apāharat kaliṅgānām ca sainyena kaliṅgasya sutaḥ raṇe kaliṅgānām tu tam śūram kruddham kruddhaḥ vṛkodaraḥ tasya muṣṭi hatasya ājau pāṇḍavena balīyasā sarvāṇi asthīni sahasā prāpatan vai pṛthak pṛthak tam karṇaḥ bhrātaraḥ ca asya na amṛṣyanta mahā rathāḥ te bhīmasenam nārācaiḥ jaghnuḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ tatas śatru ratham tyaktvā bhīmaḥ dhruva ratham gataḥ dhruvam ca asyantam aniśam muṣṭinā samapothayat sa tathā pāṇḍu putreṇa balinā nihataḥ apatat tam nihatya mahā rāja bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ jayarāta ratham prāpya muhur siṃhaḥ iva anadat jayarātam atha ākṣipya nadan savyena pāṇinā talena nāśayām āsa karṇasya eva agratas sthitam karṇaḥ tu pāṇḍave śaktim kāñcanīm samavāsṛjat tatas tām eva jagrāha prahasan pāṇḍu nandanaḥ karṇāya eva ca durdharṣaḥ cikṣepa ājau vṛkodaraḥ mahatā śara varṣeṇa chādayantaḥ vṛkodaram sārathim ca hayān ca eva śaraiḥ ninye yama kṣayam tau eka ratham ārūḍhau bhrātarau para tāpanau saṃgrāma śirasaḥ madhye bhīmam dvau abhyadhāvatām ratham ekam samāruhya bhīmam bāṇaiḥ avidhyatām kṛpasya somadattasya bāhlīkasya ca pāṇḍavaḥ pāda prahāreṇa dharām prāveśayat ariṃdamaḥ tatas hāhākṛte sainye dṛṣṭvā bhīmam nṛpa abruvan rudraḥ ayam bhīma rūpeṇa dhārtarāṣṭreṣu gṛdhyati evam uktvā apalāyanta sarve bhārata pārthivāḥ visaṃjñāḥ avāhayan vāhān na ca dvau saha dhāvataḥ tatas bale bhṛśa lulite niśā mukhe su pūjitaḥ nṛpa vṛṣabhaiḥ vṛkodaraḥ
