tatas yamau drupada virāṭa kekayāḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ca api parām mudam yayuḥ vṛkodaram bhṛśam abhipūjayan ca te yathā andhake pratinihate haram surāḥ tatas sutāḥ tava varuṇa ātmaja upamāḥ ruṣā anvitāḥ saha guruṇā mahātmanā niśā mukhe mahātmanām nṛpa vara yuddham adbhutam saṃjayaḥ uvāca prāya upaviṣṭe tu hate putre sātyakinā tatas somadattaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ sātyakim vākyam abravīt kṣatra dharmaḥ purā dṛṣṭaḥ yaḥ tu devaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ parāṅmukhāya dīnāya nyasta śastrāya yācate kṣatra dharma rataḥ prājñaḥ katham nu praharet raṇe dvau eva kila vṛṣṇīnām tatra khyātau mahā rathau katham prāya upaviṣṭāya pārthena chinna bāhave nṛśaṃsam patanīyam ca tādṛśam kṛtavān asi śape sātvata putrābhyām iṣṭena sukṛtena ca an atītām imām rātrim yadi tvām vīra māninam arakṣyamāṇam pārthena jiṣṇunā sa suta anujam na hanyām niraye ghore pateyam vṛṣṇi pāṃsana dadhmau śaṅkham ca tāreṇa siṃhanādam nanāda ca tatas kamala patra akṣaḥ siṃha daṃṣṭraḥ mahā balaḥ sātvataḥ bhṛśa saṃkruddhaḥ somadattam atha abravīt hataḥ bhūriśravāḥ vīraḥ tava putraḥ mahā rathaḥ śalaḥ ca eva tathā rājan bhrātṛ vyasana karśitaḥ tvām ca api adya vadhiṣyāmi sa putra paśu bāndhavam tiṣṭha idānīm raṇe yattaḥ kauravaḥ asi viśeṣataḥ yasmin dānam damaḥ śaucam ahiṃsā hrīḥ dhṛtiḥ kṣamā anapāyīni sarvāṇi nityam rājñi yudhiṣṭhire mṛdaṅga ketoḥ tasya tvam tejasā nihataḥ purā sa karṇa saubalaḥ saṃkhye vināśam samupeṣyasi śape aham kṛṣṇa caraṇaiḥ iṣṭāpūrtena ca eva ha yadi tvām sa sutam pāpam na hanyām yudhi roṣitaḥ pravṛttau śara saṃpātam kartum puruṣa sattamau śakuniḥ ca su saṃkruddhaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ sāgram śata sahasram tu hayānām tasya dhīmataḥ somadattam mahā iṣvāsam samantāt paryarakṣata rakṣyamāṇaḥ ca balibhiḥ chādayām āsa sātyakim tam chādyamānam viśikhaiḥ dṛṣṭvā saṃnata parvabhiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ abhyayāt kruddhaḥ pragṛhya mahatīm camūm caṇḍa vāta abhisṛṣṭānām udadhīnām iva svanaḥ tam vimūḍham samālakṣya sārathiḥ tvarayā anvitaḥ apovāha raṇāt vīram somadattam mahā ratham tam visaṃjñam samālokya yuyudhāna śara arditam kārṣṇāyasa mayam ghoram ṛkṣa carma āvṛtam mahat vikṣiptam aṣṭa cakreṇa vivṛta akṣeṇa kūjatā dhvajena ucchrita tuṇḍena gṛdhra rājena rājatā lohita ārdra patākam tam antra mālā vibhūṣitam aṣṭa cakra samāyuktam āsthāya vipulam ratham śūla mudgara dhāriṇyā śaila pādapa hastayā rakṣasām ghora rūpāṇām akṣauhiṇyā samāvṛtaḥ tam udyata mahā cāpam niśāmya vyathitāḥ nṛpāḥ vāyunā kṣobhita āvartā gaṅgā iva ūrdhva taraṅgiṇī ghaṭotkaca prayuktena siṃhanādena bhīṣitāḥ prasusruvuḥ gajāḥ mūtram vivyathuḥ ca narāḥ bhṛśam tatas aśma vṛṣṭiḥ atyartham āsīt tatra samantataḥ saṃdhyā kāla adhika balaiḥ pramuktāḥ rākṣasaiḥ kṣitau āyasāni ca cakrāṇi bhuśuṇḍyaḥ prāsa tomarāḥ patanti aviralāḥ śūlāḥ śataghnyaḥ paṭṭiśāḥ tathā tat ugram ati raudram ca dṛṣṭvā yuddham narādhipāḥ tanayāḥ tava karṇaḥ ca vyathitāḥ prādravan diśaḥ nihatāyām tu māyāyām amarṣī sa ghaṭotkacaḥ visasarja śarān ghorān te aśvatthāmānam āviśan bhujagāḥ iva vegena valmīkam krodha mūrchitāḥ te śarāḥ rudhira abhyaktāḥ bhittvā śāradvatī sutam viviśuḥ dharaṇīm śīghrāḥ rukma puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ aśvatthāmā tu saṃkruddhaḥ laghu hastaḥ pratāpavān cakram śata sahasra aram agṛhṇāt vyathitaḥ bhṛśam kṣura antam bāla sūrya ābham maṇi vajra vibhūṣitam vegena mahatā gacchat vikṣiptam drauṇinā śaraiḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ tatas tūrṇam dṛṣṭvā cakram nipātitam drauṇim prācchādayat bāṇaiḥ svarbhānuḥ iva bhāskaram ghaṭotkaca sutaḥ śrīmān bhinnāñjana caya upamaḥ rurodha drauṇim āyāntam prabhañjanam iva adrirāj pautreṇa bhīmasenasya śaraiḥ saḥ añjanaparvaṇā dhvajam ekena bāṇena ciccheda añjanaparvaṇaḥ dvābhyām tu ratha yantāram tribhiḥ ca asya triveṇukam gadā hema aṅgadā rājan tūrṇam haiḍimba sūnunā bhrāmya utkṣiptā śaraiḥ sā api drauṇinā abhyāhatā apatat vavarṣa añjanaparvā sa druma varṣam nabhastalāt tatas māyā dharam drauṇiḥ ghaṭotkaca sutam divi mārgaṇaiḥ abhivivyādha ghanam sūryaḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ mahīdharaḥ iva ati uccaḥ śrīmān añjanaparvataḥ tam ayasmaya varmāṇam drauṇiḥ bhīma ātmaja ātmajam jaghāna añjanaparvāṇam maheśvaraḥ iva andhakam atha dṛṣṭvā hatam putram aśvatthāmnā mahā balam drauṇeḥ sakāśam abhyetya roṣāt pracalita aṅgadaḥ prāha vākyam asaṃbhrāntaḥ vīram śāradvatī sutam dahantam pāṇḍava anīkam vanam agnim iva uddhatam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha na me jīvan droṇaputra gamiṣyasi aśvatthāmā uvāca kim tu roṣa anvitaḥ jantuḥ hanyāt ātmānam api uta saṃjayaḥ uvāca śrutvā etat krodha tāmra akṣaḥ putra śoka samanvitaḥ aśvatthāmānam āyastaḥ bhaimaseniḥ abhāṣata bhīmāt khalu aham utpannaḥ kurūṇām vipule kule pāṇḍavānām aham putraḥ samareṣu anivartinām rakṣasām adhirājaḥ aham daśagrīva samaḥ bale tiṣṭha tiṣṭha na me jīvan droṇaputra gamiṣyasi yuddha śraddhām aham te adya vineṣyāmi raṇa ajire iti uktvā roṣa tāmra akṣaḥ rākṣasaḥ su mahā balaḥ ratha akṣa mātraiḥ iṣubhiḥ abhyavarṣat ghaṭotkacaḥ rathinām ṛṣabham drauṇim dhārābhiḥ iva toyadaḥ śara vṛṣṭim śaraiḥ drauṇiḥ aprāptām tām vyaśātayat tatas antarikṣe bāṇānām saṃgrāmaḥ anyaḥ iva abhavat athā astra saṃgharṣa kṛtaiḥ visphuliṅgaiḥ samābabhau niśāmya nihatām māyām drauṇinā raṇa māninā ghaṭotkacaḥ tatas māyām sasarja antarhitaḥ punar śūla prāsa asi musala jala prasravaṇaḥ mahān tam añjana caya prakhyam drauṇiḥ dṛṣṭvā mahīdharam sa tena astreṇa śaila indraḥ kṣiptaḥ kṣipram anaśyata tatas sa toyadaḥ bhūtvā nīlaḥ sa indrāyudhaḥ divi aśma vṛṣṭibhiḥ ati ugraḥ drauṇim ācchādayat raṇe sa mārgaṇa gaṇaiḥ drauṇiḥ diśaḥ pracchādya sarvatas śatam ratha sahasrāṇām jaghāna dvipadām varaḥ sa dṛṣṭvā punar āyāntam rathena āyata kārmukam ghaṭotkacam asaṃbhrāntam rākṣasaiḥ bahubhiḥ vṛtam siṃha śārdūla sadṛśaiḥ matta dvirada vikramaiḥ vivṛta āsya śiraḥ grīvaiḥ haiḍimba anucaraiḥ saha nānā śastra dharaiḥ vīraiḥ nānā kavaca bhūṣaṇaiḥ viṣaṇṇam abhisaṃprekṣya putram te drauṇiḥ abravīt tiṣṭha duryodhana adya tvam na kāryaḥ saṃbhramaḥ tvayā nihaniṣyāmi amitrān te na tava asti parājayaḥ satyam te pratijānāmi paryāśvāsaya vāhinīm saṃjayaḥ uvāca vṛtaḥ śata sahasreṇa rathānām raṇa śobhinām ṣaṣṭyā gaja sahasraiḥ ca prayāhi tvam dhanaṃjayam karṇaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ ca kṛpaḥ nīlaḥ tathā eva ca udīcyāḥ kṛtavarmā ca purumitraḥ śrutārpaṇaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ nikumbhaḥ ca kuṇḍabhedī urukramaḥ puraṃjayaḥ dṛḍharathaḥ patākī hemapaṅkajaḥ śalya aruṇi indrasenāḥ ca saṃjayaḥ vijayaḥ jayaḥ kamalākṣaḥ puruḥ krāthī jayavarmā sudarśanaḥ ete tvām anuyāsyanti pattīnām ayutāni ṣaḍ dāritān drauṇinā bāṇaiḥ bhṛśam vikṣata vigrahān piprīṣuḥ te sutān rājan didhakṣuḥ ca eva pāṇḍavān vibhāvaryām su tumulam śakra prahrādayoḥ iva jaghāna urasi saṃkruddhaḥ viṣa agni pratimaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ sa taiḥ abhyāhataḥ gāḍham śaraiḥ bhīma suta īritaiḥ bhūyas ca añjalikena asya mārgaṇena mahā prabham drauṇi hasta sthitam cāpam ciccheda āśu ghaṭotkacaḥ vavarṣa viśikhān tīkṣṇān vāri dhārāḥ iva ambudaḥ tatas śāradvatī putraḥ preṣayām āsa bhārata suvarṇa puṅkhān śatru ghnān kha carān kha carān prati tad bāṇaiḥ arditam yūtham rakṣasām pīna vakṣasām siṃhaiḥ iva babhau mattam gajānām ākulam kulam vidhamya rākṣasān bāṇaiḥ sa aśva sūta rathān vibhuḥ dadāha bhagavān vahniḥ bhūtāni iva yuga kṣaye sa dagdhvā akṣauhiṇīm bāṇaiḥ nairṛtān ruruce bhṛśam rarāja jayatām śreṣṭhaḥ droṇaputraḥ tava ahitān teṣu rāja sahasreṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu bhārata na enam nirīkṣitum kaḥ cit śaknoti drauṇim āhave ṛte ghaṭotkacāt vīrāt rākṣasa indrāt mahā balāt sa cikṣepa tatas kruddhaḥ droṇaputrāya rākṣasaḥ aṣṭa cakrām mahā raudrām aśanīm rudra nirmitām sa aśva sūta dhvajam vāham bhasma kṛtvā mahā prabhā viveśa vasudhām bhittvā sa aśaniḥ bhṛśa dāruṇā drauṇeḥ tat karma dṛṣṭvā tu sarva bhūtāni apūjayan yat avaplutya jagrāha ghorām śaṃkara nirmitām mumoca niśitān bāṇān punar drauṇeḥ mahā urasi dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api asaṃbhrāntaḥ mumoca āśīviṣa upamān suvarṇa puṅkhān viśikhān droṇaputrasya vakṣasi tatas mumoca nārācān drauṇiḥ tābhyām sahasraśas ati tīvram abhūt yuddham tayoḥ puruṣa siṃhayoḥ yodhānām prīti jananam drauṇeḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha ṣaḍbhiḥ vāji sahasraiḥ ca bhīmaḥ tam deśam āvrajat tatas bhīma ātmajam rakṣaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca sa anugam nimeṣa antara mātreṇa sa aśva sūta ratha dvipām akṣauhiṇīm rākṣasānām śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ aśātayat miṣataḥ bhīmasenasya haiḍimbeḥ pārṣatasya ca pragāḍham añjaḥ gatibhiḥ nārācaiḥ abhitāḍitāḥ nipetuḥ dviradāḥ bhūmau dvi śṛṅgāḥ iva parvatāḥ rarāja vasudhā kīrṇā visarpadbhiḥ iva uragaiḥ kṣiptaiḥ kāñcana daṇḍaiḥ ca nṛpa chatraiḥ kṣitiḥ babhau dyauḥ iva udita candra arkā graha ākīrṇā yuga kṣaye pravṛddha dhvaja maṇḍūkām bherī vistīrṇa kacchapām chatra haṃsa āvalī juṣṭām phena cāmara mālinīm kaṅka gṛdhra mahā grāhām na eka āyudha jhaṣa ākulām ratha kṣipta mahā vaprām patākā rucira drumām śara mīnām mahā raudrām prāsa śakti ugra ḍuṇḍubhām majjā māṃsa mahā paṅkām kabandha āvarjita uḍupām keśa śaivala kalmāṣām bhīrūṇām kaśmala āvahām nāga indra haya yodhānām śarīra vyaya saṃbhavām śoṇita ogha mahā vegām drauṇiḥ prāvartayat nadīm yodha ārta rava nirghoṣām kṣataja ūrmi samākulām nihatya rākṣasān bāṇaiḥ drauṇiḥ haiḍimbam ārdayat punar api ati saṃkruddhaḥ sa vṛkodara pārṣatān sa nārāca gaṇaiḥ pārthān drauṇiḥ viddhvā mahā balaḥ punar śrutaṃjayam nāma surathasya anujam raṇe balānīkam jayānīkam jayāśvam ca abhijaghnivān tribhiḥ ca anyaiḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ su puṅkhaiḥ rukmamālinam śatruṃjayam ca balinam śakra lokam nināya ha jaghāna sa pṛṣadhram ca candradevam ca māninam kuntibhoja sutān ca ājau daśabhiḥ daśa jaghnivān aśvatthāmā su saṃkruddhaḥ saṃdhāya ugram ajihmagam mumoca ākarṇa pūrṇena dhanuṣā śaram uttamam yama daṇḍa upamam ghoram uddiśya āśu ghaṭotkacam sa bhittvā hṛdayam tasya rākṣasasya mahā śaraḥ viveśa vasudhām śīghram sa puṅkhaḥ pṛthivīpate tam hatam patitam jñātvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ drauṇeḥ sakāśāt rāja indra apaninye ratha antaram tathā parāṅmukha ratham sainyam yaudhiṣṭhiram nṛpa tam siddha gandharva piśāca saṃghāḥ nāgāḥ suparṇāḥ pitaraḥ vayāṃsi rakṣaḥ gaṇāḥ bhūta gaṇāḥ ca drauṇim apūjayan apsarasaḥ surāḥ ca saṃjayaḥ uvāca drupadasya ātmajān dṛṣṭvā kuntibhoja sutān tathā droṇaputreṇa nihatān rākṣasān ca sahasraśas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīmasenaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ somadattaḥ punar dṛṣṭvā sātyakim āhave mahatā śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsa sarvatas tvadīyānām pareṣām ca ghoram vijaya kāṅkṣiṇām vṛddham ṛddham guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ yayātim iva nāhuṣam vivyādha daśabhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ śaraiḥ vajra nipātibhiḥ sātyakiḥ ca agni saṃkāśam mumoca śaram uttamam visṛjan śara varṣāṇi kāla varṣī iva toyadaḥ bhīmaḥ atha sātvatasya arthe vāhlīkam navabhiḥ śaraiḥ pīḍayan vai mahātmānam vivyādha raṇa mūrdhani prātipīyaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ śaktim bhīmasya vakṣasi nicakhāna mahā bāhuḥ puraṃdaraḥ iva aśanim sā pāṇḍavena prahitā bāhlīkasya śiraḥ aharat sa papāta hataḥ pṛthvyām vajra āhataḥ iva adrirāj putrāḥ te abhyardayan bhīmam daśa dāśaratheḥ samāḥ nārācaiḥ daśabhiḥ bhīmaḥ tān nihatya tava ātmajān karṇasya dayitam putram vṛṣasenam avākirat tatas vṛṣarathaḥ nāma bhrātā karṇasya viśrutaḥ jaghāna bhīmam nārācaiḥ tam api abhi avadhīt balī tatas sapta rathān vīraḥ syālānām tava bhārata śakuneḥ bhrātaraḥ vīrāḥ gaja akṣaḥ śarabhaḥ vibhuḥ abhidrutya śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bhīmasenam atāḍayan sa tudyamānaḥ nārācaiḥ vṛṣṭi vegaiḥ iva ṛṣabhaḥ jaghāna pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pañca eva ati balaḥ rathān tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān vīrān viceluḥ nṛpa sattamāḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kruddhaḥ tava anīkam aśātayat miṣataḥ kumbhayoneḥ ca putrāṇām ca tava anagha ambaṣṭhān mālavān śūrān trigartān sa śibīn api prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya gaṇān yuddhe yudhiṣṭhiraḥ abhīṣāhān śūrasenān vāhlīkān sa vasātikān nikṛtya pṛthivīm rājā cakre śoṇita kardamām yaudheya āraṭṭa rājanya madrakāṇām gaṇān yudhi prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya śūrān bāṇaiḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ iti āsīt tumulaḥ śabdaḥ yudhiṣṭhira ratham prati sainyāni drāvayantam tam droṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiram vāruṇam yāmyam āgneyam tvāṣṭram sāvitram eva ca cikṣepa parama kruddhaḥ jighāṃsuḥ pāṇḍu nandanam kṣiptāni kṣipyamāṇāni tāni ca astrāṇi dharmajaḥ satyām cikīrṣamāṇaḥ tu pratijñām kumbhasaṃbhavaḥ prāduścakre astram aindram vai prājāpatyam ca bhārata patiḥ kurūṇām gaja siṃha gāmī viśāla vakṣāḥ pṛthu lohita akṣaḥ tatas kim cit ghoreṇa tamasā āvṛte sarva bhūtāni ca param trāsam jagmuḥ mahīpate brahmāstram udyatam dṛṣṭvā kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vyadhamat roṣa tāmra akṣaḥ vāyavya astreṇa bhārata te hanyamānāḥ droṇena pāñcālāḥ prādravan bhayāt tatas kirīṭī bhīmaḥ ca sahasā saṃnyavartatām mahadbhyām ratha vaṃśābhyām parigṛhya balam tava bībhatsuḥ dakṣiṇam pārśvam uttaram tu vṛkodaraḥ bhāradvājam śara oghābhyām mahadbhyām abhyavarṣatām tau tadā sṛñjayāḥ ca eva pāñcālāḥ ca mahā ojasaḥ tatas sā bhāratī senā vadhyamānā kirīṭinā droṇena vāryamāṇāḥ te svayam tava sutena ca na aśakyanta mahā rāja yodhāḥ vārayitum tadā saṃjayaḥ uvāca udīryamāṇam tat dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānām mahat balam aviṣahyam ca manvānaḥ karṇam duryodhanaḥ abravīt ayam sa kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ mitrāṇām mitra vatsala pāñcālaiḥ matsya kaikeyaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ ca mahā rathaiḥ ete nadanti saṃhṛṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ jita kāśinaḥ śakra upamāḥ ca bahavaḥ pāñcālānām ratha vrajāḥ karṇaḥ uvāca paritrātum iha prāptaḥ yadi pārtham puraṃdaraḥ tam api āśu parājitya tatas hantāsmi pāṇḍavam satyam te pratijānāmi samāśvasihi bhārata hantāsmi pāṇḍu tanayān pāñcālān ca samāgatān jayam te pratijānāmi vāsavasya iva pāvakiḥ priyam tava mayā kāryam iti jīvāmi pārthiva sarveṣām eva pārthānām phalgunaḥ balavattaraḥ tasya amoghām vimokṣyāmi śaktim śakra vinirmitām tava vaśyāḥ bhaviṣyanti vanam yāsyanti vā punar mayi jīvati kauravya viṣādam mā kṛthāḥ kva cit aham jeṣyāmi samare sahitān sarva pāṇḍavān pāñcālān kekayān ca eva vṛṣṇīn ca api samāgatān bāṇa oghaiḥ śakalīkṛtya tava dāsyāmi medinīm saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam bruvāṇam karṇam tu kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ abravīt smayan iva mahā bāhuḥ sūtaputram idam vacaḥ śobhanam śobhanam karṇa sa nāthaḥ kuru puṃgavaḥ samāgamaḥ pāṇḍu sutaiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ te bahuśas yudhi sarvatra nirjitaḥ ca asi pāṇḍavaiḥ sūtanandana hriyamāṇe tadā karṇa gandharvaiḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra je virāṭa nagare ca api sametāḥ sarva kauravāḥ katham utsahase jetum sa kṛṣṇān sarva pāṇḍavān garjitvā sūtaputra tvam śārada abhram iva ajalam niṣphalaḥ dṛśyase karṇa tat ca rājā na budhyate tāvat garjasi rādheya yāvat pārtham na paśyasi purā pārtham hi te dṛṣṭvā durlabham garjitam bhavet tvam an āsādya tān bāṇān phalgunasya vigarjasi bāhubhiḥ kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ vāgbhiḥ śūrāḥ dvijātayaḥ dhanuṣā phalgunaḥ śūraḥ karṇaḥ śūraḥ manorathaiḥ evam paruṣitaḥ tena tadā śāradvatena saḥ karṇaḥ praharatām śreṣṭhaḥ kṛpam vākyam atha abravīt śūrāḥ garjanti satatam prāvṛṣi iva balāhakāḥ phalam ca āśu prayacchanti bījam uptam ṛtau iva doṣam atra na paśyāmi śūrāṇām raṇa mūrdhani tat tat vikatthamānānām bhāram ca udvahatām mṛdhe yam bhāram puruṣaḥ voḍhum manasā hi vyavasyati vṛthā śūrāḥ na garjanti sa jalāḥ iva toyadāḥ sāmarthyam ātmanaḥ jñātvā tatas garjanti paṇḍitāḥ saḥ aham adya raṇe yattaḥ sahitau kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau hatvā pāṇḍu sutān ājau saha kṛṣṇān sa sātvatān duryodhanāya dāsyāmi pṛthivīm hata kaṇṭakām kṛpaḥ uvāca yadā kṣipasi vai kṛṣṇau dharmarājam ca pāṇḍavam deva gandharva yakṣāṇām manuṣya uraga rakṣasām daṃśitānām api raṇe ajeyau kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau nityam dharma rataḥ ca eva kṛtāstraḥ ca viśeṣataḥ dhṛtimān ca kṛtajñaḥ ca dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhrātaraḥ ca asya balinaḥ sarva astreṣu kṛta śramāḥ guru vṛtti ratāḥ prājñāḥ dharma nityāḥ yaśasvinaḥ saṃbandhinaḥ ca indra vīryāḥ su anuraktāḥ prahāriṇaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca daurmukhiḥ janamejayaḥ yeṣām arthāya saṃyattaḥ matsya rājaḥ saha anugaḥ śatānīkaḥ sudaśanaḥ śrutānīkaḥ śrutadhvajaḥ balānīkaḥ jayānīkaḥ jayāśvaḥ rathavāhanaḥ candrodayaḥ kāmarathaḥ virāṭa bhrātaraḥ śubhāḥ yamau ca draupadeyāḥ ca rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ yeṣām arthāya yudhyante na teṣām vidyate kṣayaḥ sa yakṣa rākṣasa gaṇam sa bhūta bhujaga dvipam niḥśeṣam astra vīryeṇa kuryātām bhīma phalgunau yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ca pṛthivīm nirdahet ghora cakṣuṣā aprameya balaḥ śauriḥ yeṣām arthe ca daṃśitaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca abravīt ca tadā karṇaḥ gurum śāradvatam kṛpam satyam uktam tvayā brahman pāṇḍavān prati yat vacaḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ guṇāḥ pāṇḍu suteṣu vai ajayyāḥ ca raṇe pārthāḥ devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ tathā api pārthān jeṣyāmi śaktyā vāsava dattayā mama api amoghā dattā iyam śaktiḥ śakreṇa vai dvija etayā nihaniṣyāmi savyasācinam āhave hate tu pāṇḍave kṛṣṇaḥ bhrātaraḥ ca asya sodarāḥ anarjunāḥ na śakṣyanti mahīm bhoktum katham cana teṣu naṣṭeṣu sarveṣu pṛthivī iyam sa sāgarā su nītaiḥ iha sarva arthāḥ sidhyante na atra saṃśayaḥ tvam tu vṛddhaḥ ca vipraḥ ca aśaktaḥ ca api saṃyuge kṛta snehaḥ ca pārtheṣu mohāt mām avamanyase yat ca api pāṇḍavān vipra stotum icchasi saṃyuge atrā api śṛṇu me vākyam yathāvat gadataḥ dvija duḥśāsanaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ madra rājaḥ tvam eva ca somadattaḥ ca bhūriḥ ca tathā drauṇiḥ viviṃśatiḥ tiṣṭheyuḥ daṃśitāḥ yatra sarve yuddha viśāradāḥ śūrāḥ ca hi kṛtāstrāḥ ca balinaḥ svarga lipsavaḥ ete sthāsyanti saṃgrāme pāṇḍavānām vadha arthinaḥ jayam ākāṅkṣamāṇāḥ hi kauraveyasya daṃśitāḥ yatra bhīṣmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ śete śara śata ācitaḥ bhūriśravāḥ jayaḥ ca eva jalasaṃdhaḥ sudakṣiṇaḥ śalaḥ ca rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ bhagadattaḥ ca vīryavān nihatāḥ samare śūrāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ balavattarāḥ yān ca tān stauṣi satatam duryodhana ripūn dvija teṣām api hatāḥ śūrāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas kṣīyante sarva sainyāni kurūṇām pāṇḍavaiḥ saha prabhāvam nā atra paśyāmi pāṇḍavānām katham cana yatiṣye aham yathāśakti yoddhum taiḥ saha saṃyuge saṃjayaḥ uvāca tathā paruṣitam dṛṣṭvā sūtaputreṇa mātulam aśvatthāmā uvāca karṇa paśya su durbuddhe tiṣṭha idānīm nara adhama eṣa te adya śiraḥ kāyāt uddharāmi su durmate saṃjayaḥ uvāca nyavārayat mahā rāja kṛpaḥ ca dvipadām varaḥ karṇaḥ uvāca śūraḥ ayam samara ślāghī durmatiḥ ca dvija adhamaḥ āsādayatu mad vīryam muñca imam kurusattama aśvatthāmā uvāca āyānti pāṇḍavāḥ brahman āhvayantaḥ samantataḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca karṇaḥ api rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ cāpam udyamya vīryavān kaurava agryaiḥ parivṛtaḥ śakraḥ deva gaṇaiḥ iva paryatiṣṭhata tejasvī sva bāhu balam āśritaḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham karṇasya saha pāṇḍavaiḥ saṃrabdhasya mahā rāja siṃhanāda vināditam tatas te pāṇḍavāḥ rājan pāñcālāḥ ca yaśasvinaḥ dṛṣṭvā karṇam mahā bāhum uccais śabdam atha anadan ayam karṇaḥ kutas karṇaḥ tiṣṭha karṇa mahā raṇe anye tu dṛṣṭvā rādheyam krodha rakta īkṣaṇāḥ abruvan sarvaiḥ pārthiva śārdūlaiḥ na anena arthaḥ asti jīvatā atyanta vairī pārthānām satatam pāpa pūruṣaḥ eṣa mūlam hi anarthānām duryodhana mate sthitaḥ mahatā śara varṣeṇa chādayantaḥ mahā rathāḥ vadha artham sūtaputrasya pāṇḍaveyena coditāḥ tān tu sarvān tathā dṛṣṭvā dhāvamānān mahā rathān dṛṣṭvā nagara kalpam tam uddhūtam sainya sāgaram piprīṣuḥ tava putrāṇām saṃgrāmeṣu aparājitaḥ sāyaka oghena balavān kṣiprakārī mahā balaḥ tatas tu śara varṣeṇa pārthivāḥ tam avārayan dhanūṃṣi te vidhunvānāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas ayodhayanta rādheyam śakram daitya gaṇāḥ iva śara varṣam tu tat karṇaḥ pārthivaiḥ samudīritam tat yuddham abhavat teṣām kṛta pratikṛta eṣiṇām nivārya ca śara oghān tān pārthivānām mahā rathaḥ yugeṣu īṣāsu chatreṣu dhvajeṣu ca hayeṣu ca ātma nāma aṅkitān bāṇān rādheyaḥ prāhiṇot śitān tatas te vyākulībhūtāḥ rājānaḥ karṇa pīḍitāḥ babhramuḥ tatra tatra eva gāvaḥ śīta arditāḥ iva hayānām vadhyamānānām gajānām rathinām tathā tatra tatra abhyavekṣāmaḥ saṃghān karṇena pātitān śirobhiḥ patitaiḥ rājan bāhubhiḥ ca samantataḥ āstīrṇā vasudhā sarvā śūrāṇām anivartinām hataiḥ ca hanyamānaiḥ ca niṣṭanadbhiḥ ca sarvaśas tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramam aśvatthāmānam āsādya tadā vākyam uvāca ha yudhyate asau raṇe karṇaḥ daṃśitaḥ sarva pārthivaiḥ paśya etām dravatīm senām karṇa sāyaka pīḍitām kārttikeyena vidhvastām āsurīm pṛtanām iva dṛṣṭvā etām nirjitām senām raṇe karṇena dhīmatā abhiyāti eṣa bībhatsuḥ sūtaputra jighāṃsayā tat yathā paśyamānānām sūtaputram mahā ratham na hanyāt pāṇḍavaḥ saṃkhye tathā nītiḥ vidhīyatām tatas drauṇiḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ hārdikyaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ āyāntam dṛśya kaunteyam vṛtram deva camūm iva pratyudyayau tadā karṇaḥ yathā śakraḥ pratāpavān dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca saṃrabdham phalgunam dṛṣṭvā kāla antaka yama upamam āśaṃsate ca bībhatsum yuddhe jetum su dāruṇe saṃjayaḥ uvāca āyāntam pāṇḍavam dṛṣṭvā gajaḥ pratigajam yathā asaṃbhrāntataraḥ karṇaḥ partyudīyāt dhanaṃjayam vārayām āsa tejasvī pāṇḍavaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ tam karṇaḥ śara jālena chādayām āsa māriṣa tasya tat lāghavam pārthaḥ na amṛṣyata mahā balaḥ tasmai bāṇān śilā dhautān prasanna agrān a jihma gān prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya triṃśatam śatru tāpanaḥ vivyādha ca enam saṃrabdhaḥ bāṇena ekena vīryavān punar ādāya tat cāpam nimeṣa ardhāt mahā balaḥ chādayām āsa bāṇa oghaiḥ phalgunam kṛtahasta vat śara vṛṣṭim tu tām muktām sūtaputreṇa bhārata tau parasparam āsādya śara varṣeṇa pārthiva chādayetām mahā iṣvāsau kṛta pratikṛta eṣiṇau tat adbhutam abhūt yuddham karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ mṛdhe tatas pārthaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramam sāratheḥ ca śiraḥ kāyāt aharat śatru tāpanaḥ atha enam chinna dhanvānam hata aśvam hata sārathim vivyādha sāyakaiḥ pārthaḥ caturbhiḥ pāṇḍu nandanaḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya nara ṛṣabhaḥ āruroha ratham tūrṇam kṛpasya śara pīḍitaḥ rādheyam nirjitam dṛṣṭvā tāvakāḥ bharata ṛṣabha dhanaṃjaya śaraiḥ nunnāḥ prādravanta diśaḥ daśa nivartayām āsa tadā vākyam ca idam uvāca ha alam drutena vaḥ śūrāḥ tiṣṭhadhvam kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ eṣa pārtha vadhāya aham svayam gacchāmi saṃyuge aham pārthān haniṣyāmi sa pāñcālān sa somakān adya me yudhyamānasya saha gāṇḍīvadhanvanā drakṣyanti vikramam pārthāḥ kālasya iva yuga kṣaye adya mad bāṇa jālāni vimuktāni sahasraśas drakṣyanti samare yodhāḥ śalabhānām iva āyatīḥ adya bāṇa mayam varṣam sṛjataḥ mama dhanvinaḥ jeṣyāmi adya raṇe pārtham sāyakaiḥ nata parvabhiḥ tiṣṭhadhvam samare śūrāḥ bhayam tyajata phalgunāt yathā velām samāsādya sāgaraḥ makara ālayaḥ iti uktvā prayayau rājā sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ tam prayāntam mahā bāhum dṛṣṭvā śāradvataḥ tadā aśvatthāmānam āsādya vākyam etat uvāca ha eṣa rājā mahā bāhuḥ amarṣī krodha mūrchitaḥ yāvat naḥ paśyamānānām prāṇān pārthena saṃgataḥ yāvat phalguna bāṇānām gocaram na adhigacchati na bhasmīkriyate rājā tāvat yuddhāt nivāryatām ayuktam iva paśyāmi tiṣṭhatsu asmāsu mānada svayam yuddhāya yat rājā pārtham yāti asahāyavān durlabham jīvitam manye kauravyasya kirīṭinā yudhyamānasya pārthena śārdūlena iva hastinaḥ mātulena evam uktaḥ tu drauṇiḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ duryodhanam idam vākyam tvaritam samabhāṣata mām an ādṛtya kauravya tava nityam hita eṣiṇam aham āvārayiṣyāmi pārtham tiṣṭha suyodhana ācāryaḥ pāṇḍu putrān vai putra vat parirakṣati tvam api upekṣām kuruṣe teṣu nityam dvijottama sukha arhāḥ paramam duḥkham prāpnuvanti aparājitāḥ aśvatthāman prasīdasva nāśaya etān mama ahitān tava astra gocare śaktāḥ sthātum devāḥ api nā anagha pāñcālān somakān ca eva jahi drauṇe saha anugān vayam śeṣān haniṣyāmaḥ tvayā eva parirakṣitāḥ ete hi somakāḥ vipra pāñcālāḥ ca yaśasvinaḥ tān vāraya mahā bāho kekayān ca narottama purā kurvanti niḥśeṣam rakṣyamāṇāḥ kirīṭinā ādau vā yadi vā paścāt tava idam karma māriṣa tvam utpannaḥ mahā bāho pāñcālānām vadham prati kariṣyasi jagat sarvam apāñcālam kila acyuta na te astra gocare śaktāḥ sthātum devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ kim u pārthāḥ sa pāñcālāḥ satyam etat vacaḥ mama saṃjayaḥ uvāca priyāḥ hi pāṇḍavāḥ nityam mama ca api pituḥ ca me tathā eva āvām priyau teṣām na tu yuddhe kuru udvaha śaktitaḥ tāta yudhyāmaḥ tyaktvā prāṇān abhīta vat aham karṇaḥ ca śalyaḥ ca kṛpaḥ hārdikyaḥ eva ca nimeṣāt pāṇḍavīm senām kṣapayema nṛpa uttama te ca api kauravīm senām nimeṣa ardhāt kuru udvaha yudhyatām pāṇḍavān śaktyā teṣām ca asmān yuyutsatām tejaḥ tu tejaḥ āsādya praśamam yāti bhārata aśakyā tarasā jetum pāṇḍavānām anīkinī jīvatsu pāṇḍu putreṣu tat hi satyam bravīmi te ātma artham yudhyamānāḥ te samarthāḥ pāṇḍu nandanāḥ sarva atiśaṅkī mānī ca tatas asmān atiśaṅkase eṣa gacchāmi saṃgrāmam tvad kṛte kuru nandana yotsye aham śatrubhiḥ sārdham jeṣyāmi ca varān varān pāñcālaiḥ saha yotsyāmi somakaiḥ kekayaiḥ tathā pāṇḍaveyaiḥ ca saṃgrāme tvad priya artham ariṃdama adya mad bāṇa nirdagdhāḥ pāñcālāḥ somakāḥ tathā siṃhena iva arditāḥ gāvaḥ vidraviṣyanti sarvatas adya dharmasutaḥ rājā dṛṣṭvā mama parākramam aśvatthāma mayam lokam maṃsyate saha somakaiḥ dṛṣṭvā vinihatān saṃkhye pāñcālān somakaiḥ saha evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ putram duryodhanam tava cikīrṣuḥ tava putrāṇām priyam prāṇabhṛtām varaḥ tatas abravīt sa kaikeyān pāñcālān gautamīsutaḥ evam uktāḥ tu te sarve śastra vṛṣṭim apātayan drauṇim prati mahā rāja jalam jaladharāḥ iva tān nihatya śarān drauṇiḥ daśa vīrān apothayat pramukhe pāṇḍu putrāṇām dhṛṣṭadyumnasya ca abhibho te hanyamānāḥ samare pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāḥ tathā tān dṛṣṭvā dravataḥ śūrān pāñcālān saha somakān tatas kāñcana citrāṇām sa jala ambuda nādinām vṛtaḥ śatena śūrāṇām rathānām anivartinām putraḥ pāñcāla rājasya dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ drauṇim iti abravīt vākyam dṛṣṭvā yodhān nipātitān samāgaccha mayā sārdham yadi śūraḥ asi saṃyuge aham tvām nihaniṣyāmi tiṣṭha idānīm mama agratas tatas tam ācārya sutam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān te tu paṅktīkṛtāḥ drauṇim śarāḥ viviśuḥ āśugāḥ rukma puṅkhāḥ prasanna agrāḥ sarva kāya avadāraṇāḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ pada ākrāntaḥ iva uragaḥ mānī drauṇiḥ asaṃbhrāntaḥ bāṇa pāṇiḥ abhāṣata dhṛṣṭadyumna sthiraḥ bhūtvā muhūrtam pratipālaya yāvat tvām niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ preṣayāmi yama kṣayam drauṇiḥ evam atha ābhāṣya pārṣatam para vīra hā chādayām āsa bāṇa oghaiḥ samantāt laghu hasta vat drauṇim pāñcāla tanayaḥ vāgbhiḥ ātarjayat tadā na jānīṣe pratijñām me vipra utpattim tathā eva ca imām tu rajanīm prāptām aprabhātām su durmate yaḥ te pārtheṣu vidveṣaḥ yā bhaktiḥ kauraveṣu ca tām darśaya sthiraḥ bhūtvā na me jīvan vimokṣyase iti uktaḥ paruṣam vākyam pārṣatena dvijottamaḥ krodham āhārayat tīvram tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt nirdahan iva cakṣurbhyām pārṣatam saḥ abhyavaikṣata chādayām āsa ca śaraiḥ niḥśvasan pannagaḥ yathā sa chādyamānaḥ samare drauṇinā rāja sattama sarva pāñcāla senābhiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ ratha sattamaḥ na akampata mahā bāhuḥ sva dhairyam samupāśritaḥ sāyakān ca eva vividhān aśvatthāmni mumoca ha tau punar saṃnyavartetām prāṇa dyūta pare raṇe utsṛjantau mahā iṣvāsau śara vṛṣṭīḥ samantataḥ drauṇi pārṣatayoḥ yuddham ghora rūpam bhayānakam dṛṣṭvā saṃpūjayām āsuḥ siddha cāraṇa vātikāḥ śara oghaiḥ pūrayantau tau ākāśam pradiśaḥ tathā alakṣyau samayudhyetām mahat kṛtvā śaraiḥ tamaḥ nṛtyamānau iva raṇe maṇḍalīkṛta kārmukau ayudhyetām mahā bāhū citram laghu ca suṣṭhu ca siṃhanāda ravāḥ ca āsan dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān ca māriṣa vāditrāṇi abhyavādyanta śataśas atha sahasraśas tatas drauṇiḥ mahā rāja pārṣatasya mahātmanaḥ dhvajam dhanuḥ tathā chatram ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī sūtam aśvān ca caturaḥ nihatya abhyadravat raṇe pāñcālān ca eva tān sarvān bāṇaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ vyadrāvayat ameya ātmā śataśas atha sahasraśas tatas pravivyathe senā pāṇḍavī bharata ṛṣabha dṛṣṭvā drauṇeḥ mahat karma vāsavasya iva saṃyuge śatena ca śatam hatvā pāñcālānām mahā rathaḥ tribhiḥ ca niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ hatvā trīn vai mahā rathān nāśayām āsa pāñcālān bhūyiṣṭham ye vyavasthitāḥ te vadhyamānāḥ pāñcālāḥ samare saha sṛñjayaiḥ sa jitvā samare śatrūn droṇaputraḥ mahā rathaḥ nanāda su mahā nādam tapānte jaladaḥ yathā sa nihatya bahūn śūrān aśvatthāmā vyarocata yuga ante sarva bhūtāni bhasma kṛtvā iva pāvakaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ca eva bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ droṇaputram mahā rāja samantāt paryavārayan tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā bhāradvājena saṃvṛtaḥ ghora rūpam mahā rāja bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhanam ambaṣṭhān mālavān vaṅgān śibīn traigartakān api prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya gaṇān kruddhaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ abhīṣāhān śūrasenān kṣatriyān yuddha durmadān nikṛtya pṛthivīm cakre bhīmaḥ śoṇita kardamām yaudheya āraṭṭa rājanyān madrakān ca gaṇān yudhi prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya kirīṭī niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ pragāḍham añjaḥ gatibhiḥ nārācaiḥ abhipīḍitāḥ nipetuḥ dviradāḥ bhūmau dvi śṛṅgāḥ iva parvatāḥ rarāja vasudhā kīrṇā visarpadbhiḥ iva uragaiḥ dyauḥ iva āditya candra ādyaiḥ grahaiḥ kīrṇā yuga kṣaye iti āsīt tumulaḥ śabdaḥ śoṇāśvasya ratham prati te hanyamānāḥ droṇena pāñcālāḥ prādravan bhayāt tatas kirīṭī bhīmaḥ ca sahasā saṃnyavartatām bībhatsuḥ dakṣiṇam pārśvam uttaram tu vṛkodaraḥ bhāradvājam śara oghābhyām mahadbhyām abhyavarṣatām tau tadā sṛñjayāḥ ca eva pāñcālāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ tathā eva tava putrasya ratha udārāḥ prahāriṇaḥ tatas sā senā vadhyamānā kirīṭinā droṇena vāryamāṇāḥ te svayam tava sutena ca na śakyante mahā rāja yodhāḥ vārayitum tadā sā pāṇḍu putrasya śaraiḥ dāryamāṇā mahā camūḥ utsṛjya śataśas vāhān tatra ke cit narādhipāḥ prādravanta mahā rāja bhaya āviṣṭāḥ samantataḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca sātyakiḥ prāha yantāram somadattāya mām vaha na hi a hatvā raṇe śatrum bāhlīkam kaurava adhamam tatas saṃpreṣayat yantā saindhavān tān mahā javān turaṅgamān śaṅkha varṇān sarva śabda atigān raṇe tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya sātvatam rabhasam raṇe vimuñcan śara varṣāṇi parjanyaḥ iva vṛṣṭimān chādayām āsa śaineyam jaladaḥ bhāskaram yathā asaṃbhrāntaḥ ca samare sātyakiḥ kuru puṃgavam chādayām āsa bāṇa oghaiḥ samantāt bharata ṛṣabha somadattaḥ tu tam ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha urasi mādhavam sātyakiḥ ca api tam rājan avidhyat sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ tau anyonyam śaraiḥ kṛttau vyarājetām nara ṛṣabhau su puṣpau puṣpa samaye puṣpitau iva kiṃśukau rudhira ukṣita sarva aṅgau kuru vṛṣṇi yaśaskarau ghora rūpau hi tau āstām vṛṣṭimantau iva ambudau śara saṃbhinna gātrau tau sarvatas śakalīkṛtau śvāvidhau iva rāja indra vyadṛṣyetām śara kṣatau khadyotaiḥ āvṛtau rājan prāvṛṣi iva vanaspatī adṛśyetām raṇe kruddhau ulkābhiḥ iva kuñjarau atha enam pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānām samārpayat tvaramāṇaḥ tvarā kāle punar ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ vāhlīkasya raṇe rājan sātyakiḥ prahasan iva somadattaḥ tu asaṃbhrāntaḥ dṛṣṭvā ketum nipātitam śaineyam pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānām samācinot atha enam rukma puṅkhānām śatena nata parvaṇām sātyakim chādayām āsa śara vṛṣṭyā mahā balaḥ sātyakim ca iṣu jālena somadattaḥ apīḍayat daśabhiḥ sātvatasya arthe bhīmaḥ ahan bāhlika ātmajam samīpam preṣayām āsa pretarājasya bhārata sāratheḥ ca śiraḥ kāyāt bhallena nata parvaṇā jahāra ratha śārdūlaḥ prahasan śini puṃgavaḥ tatas śaram mahā ghoram jvalantam iva pāvakam mumoca sātvataḥ rājan svarṇa puṅkham śilā śitam tam dṛṣṭvā nihatam tatra somadattam mahā rathāḥ mahatā śara varṣeṇa yuyudhānam upādravan chādyamānam śaraiḥ dṛṣṭvā yuyudhānam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ mahatyā senayā sārdham droṇa anīkam upādravat tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kruddhaḥ tāvakānām mahā balam śaraiḥ vidrāvayām āsa bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ sainyāni drāvayantam tu droṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiram tatas su niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pārtham vivyādha saptabhiḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā bāhuḥ parisaṃlihan tatas śara sahasreṇa droṇam vivyādha pārthivaḥ tatas muhūrtam vyathitaḥ śara ghāta prapīḍitaḥ pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām muhūrtāt dvijasattamaḥ krodhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ vāyavya astram avāsṛjat asaṃbhrāntaḥ tatas pārthaḥ dhanuḥ ākṛṣya vīryavān tatas abravīt vāsudevaḥ kuntī putram yudhiṣṭhiram yudhiṣṭhira mahā bāho yat tvā vakṣyāmi tat śṛṇu yaḥ asya sṛṣṭaḥ vināśāya saḥ enam śvas haniṣyati vāsudeva vacaḥ śrutvā dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ muhūrtam cintayitvā tu tatas dāruṇam āhavam vinighnan tāvakān yodhān vyādita āsyaḥ iva antakaḥ bhīmasya nighnataḥ śatrūn pārṣṇim jagrāha pāṇḍavaḥ droṇaḥ api pāṇḍu pāñcālān vyadhamat rajanī mukhe saṃjayaḥ uvāca tamasā saṃvṛte loke rajasā ca mahīpate na apaśyanta raṇe yodhāḥ parasparam avasthitāḥ anumānena saṃjñābhiḥ yuddham tat vavṛte mahat nara nāga aśva mathanam paramam loma harṣaṇam droṇa karṇa kṛpāḥ vīrāḥ bhīma pārṣata sātyakāḥ anyonyam kṣobhayām āsuḥ sainyāni nṛpa sattama ahanyanta mahā rāja dhāvamānāḥ ca saṃyuge tatas sarvāṇi sainyāni senā gopāḥ ca bhārata dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca teṣām saṃloḍyamānānām pāṇḍavaiḥ nihata ojasām andhe tamasi magnānām āsīt kā vaḥ matiḥ tadā katham prakāśaḥ teṣām vā mama sainyeṣu vā punar babhūva loke tamasā tathā saṃjaya saṃvṛte saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas sarvāṇi sainyāni hata śiṣṭāni yāni vai droṇaḥ purastāt jaghane tu śalyaḥ tathā drauṇiḥ pārśvatas saubalaḥ ca svayam tu sarvāṇi balāni rājan rājā abhyayāt gopayan vai niśāyām uvāca sarvān ca padāti saṃghān duryodhanaḥ pārthiva sāntva pūrvam utsṛjya sarve parama āyudhāni gṛhṇīta hastaiḥ jvalitān pradīpān te coditāḥ pārthiva sattamena tatas prahṛṣṭāḥ jagṛhuḥ pradīpān sā bhūyas eva dhvajinī vibhaktā vyarocata agni prabhayā niśāyām mahādhanaiḥ ābharaṇaiḥ ca divyaiḥ śastraiḥ pradīptaiḥ abhisaṃpatadbhiḥ kṣaṇena sarve vihitāḥ pradīpāḥ vyadīpayan ca dhvajinīm tadā āśu sarvāḥ tu senāḥ vyatisevyamānāḥ padātibhiḥ pāvaka taila hastaiḥ prakāśyamānāḥ dadṛśuḥ niśāyām prakāśitāyām tu tathā dhvajinyām droṇaḥ agni kalpaḥ pratapan samantāt rarāja rāja indra suvarṇa varmā madhyam gataḥ sūryaḥ iva aṃśumālī jāmbūnadeṣu ābharaṇeṣu ca eva niṣkeṣu śuddheṣu śarāvareṣu gadāḥ ca śaikyāḥ parighāḥ ca śubhrāḥ ratheṣu śaktyaḥ ca vivartamānāḥ pratiprabhāḥ raśmibhiḥ ājamīḍha punar punar saṃjanayanti dīptāḥ chatrāṇi bāla vyajana anuṣaṅgāḥ dīptāḥ mahā ulkāḥ ca tathā eva rājan vyāghūrṇamānāḥ ca suvarṇa mālāḥ vyāyacchatām tatra tadā virejuḥ śastra prabhābhiḥ ca virājamānam dīpa prabhābhiḥ ca tadā balam tat prakāśitam ca ābharaṇa prabhābhiḥ bhṛśam prakāśam nṛpate babhūva pītāni śastrāṇi asṛj ukṣitāni vīra avadhūtāni tanu druhāṇi dīptām prabhām prājanayanta tatra tapātyaye vidyut iva antarikṣe vaktrāṇi aśobhanta tadā narāṇām vāyu īritāni iva mahā ambujāni mahā vane dāve iva pradīpte tathā tava āsīt dhvajinī pradīptā mahā bhaye bhārata bhīma rūpā tat saṃpradīptam balam asmadīyam niśāmya pārthāḥ tvaritāḥ tathā eva sarveṣu sainyeṣu padāti saṃghān acodayan te atha cakruḥ pradīpān gaje gaje sapta kṛtāḥ pradīpāḥ rathe rathe ca eva daśa pradīpāḥ dvau aśva pṛṣṭhe paripārśvatas anye dhvajeṣu ca anye jaghaneṣu ca anye sarveṣu sainyeṣu padāti saṃghāḥ vyāmiśritāḥ hasti ratha aśva vṛndaiḥ bhās kurvatā bhānumatā graheṇa divākareṇa agniḥ iva abhitaptaḥ tayoḥ prabhāḥ pṛthivīm antarikṣam sarvāḥ vyatikramya diśaḥ ca vṛddhāḥ tena prakāśena bhṛśam prakāśam babhūva teṣām tava ca eva sainyam tena prakāśena divaṃgamena saṃbodhitāḥ deva gaṇāḥ ca rājan gandharva yakṣa asura siddha saṃghāḥ samāgaman apsarasaḥ ca sarvāḥ tat deva gandharva samākulam ca yakṣa asura indra apsarasām gaṇaiḥ ca ratha aśva nāga ākula dīpa dīptam saṃrabdha yodha āhata vidruta aśvam mahat balam vyūḍha ratha aśva nāgam sura asura vyūha samam babhūva tat śakti saṃgha ākula caṇḍa vātam mahā ratha abhram ratha vāji ghoṣam śastra ogha varṣam rudhira ambu dhāram niśi pravṛttam naradeva yuddham tasmin mahā agni pratimaḥ mahātmā saṃtāpayan pāṇḍavān vipra mukhyaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca samājagmuḥ atho vīrāḥ paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ te sametya raṇe rājan śastra prāsa asi dhāriṇaḥ pradīpānām sahasraiḥ ca dīpyamānaiḥ samantataḥ ulkā śataiḥ prajvalitaiḥ raṇa bhūmiḥ vyarājata dahyamānā iva lokānām abhāve vai vasuṃdharā prādīpyanta diśaḥ sarvāḥ pradīpaiḥ taiḥ samantataḥ varṣā pradoṣe khadyotaiḥ vṛtāḥ vṛkṣāḥ iva ābabhuḥ asajjanta tatas vīrāḥ vīreṣu eva pṛthak pṛthak nāgāḥ nāgaiḥ samājagmuḥ turagāḥ saha vājibhiḥ tatas arjunaḥ mahā rāja kauravāṇām anīkinīm dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca a mṛṣyamāṇe durdharṣe kim vaḥ āsīt manaḥ tadā ke arakṣan dakṣiṇam cakram ke ca droṇasya savyatas ke pṛṣṭhatas asya hi abhavan vīrāḥ vīrasya yudhyataḥ yat prāviśat mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāñcālān aparājitaḥ dadāha ca śaraiḥ droṇaḥ pāñcālānām ratha vrajān hatān ca eva viṣaṇṇān ca viprakīrṇān ca śaṃsasi rathinaḥ virathān ca eva kṛtān yuddheṣu māmakān saṃjayaḥ uvāca droṇasya matam ājñāya yoddhu kāmasya tām niśām duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja vaśyān bhrātṝn abhāṣata vikarṇam citrasenam ca mahābāhum ca kauravam durdharṣam dīrghabāhum ca ye ca teṣām padānugāḥ droṇam yattāḥ parākrāntāḥ sarve rakṣata pṛṣṭhatas hārdikyaḥ dakṣiṇam cakram śalyaḥ ca eva uttaram tathā trigartānām ca ye śūrāḥ hata śiṣṭāḥ mahā rathāḥ ācāryaḥ hi su saṃyattaḥ bhṛśam yattāḥ ca pāṇḍavāḥ tam rakṣata su saṃyattāḥ nighnantam śātravān raṇe te yūyam sahitāḥ sarve bhṛśam yattāḥ mahā rathāḥ droṇam rakṣata pāñcālyāt dhṛṣṭadyumnāt mahā rathāt pāṇḍaveyeṣu sainyeṣu yodham paśyāmi aham na tam yaḥ jayeta raṇe droṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnāt ṛte nṛpāḥ sa guptaḥ somakān hanyāt sṛñjayān ca sa rājakān sṛñjayeṣu atha sarveṣu nihateṣu camū mukhe dhṛṣṭadyumnam raṇe drauṇiḥ nāśayiṣyati asaṃśayam tathā arjunam raṇe karṇaḥ vijeṣyati mahā rathaḥ bhīmasenam aham ca api yuddhe jeṣyāmi daṃśitaḥ tasmāt rakṣata saṃgrāme droṇam eva mahā rathāḥ vyādideśa tatas sainyam tasmin tamasi dāruṇe ubhayoḥ senayoḥ ghoram vijayam prati kāṅkṣiṇoḥ nānā śastra samāvāpaiḥ anyonyam paryapīḍayan drauṇiḥ pāñcāla rājānam bhāradvājaḥ ca sṛñjayān chādayām āsatuḥ saṃkhye śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ pāṇḍu pāñcāla senānām kauravāṇām ca māriṣa āsīt niṣṭānakaḥ ghoraḥ nighnatām itaretaram na eva asmābhiḥ na pūrvaiḥ naḥ dṛṣṭam pūrvam tathāvidham yuddham yādṛśam eva āsīt tām rātrim su mahā bhayam saṃjayaḥ uvāca vartamāne tathā raudre rātri yuddhe viśām pate abravīt pāṇḍavān ca eva pāñcālān ca sa somakān rājñaḥ te vacanāt rājan pāñcālāḥ somakāḥ tathā tān vayam pratigarjantaḥ pratyudyātāḥ tu amarṣitāḥ yathāśakti yathotsāham yathāsattvam ca saṃyuge kṛtavarmā ca hārdikyaḥ yudhiṣṭhiram upādravat śaineyam śara varṣāṇi vikirantam samantataḥ abhyayāt kauravaḥ rājan bhūriḥ saṃgrāma mūrdhani karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ rājan vārayām āsa pāṇḍavam bhīmasenam atha āyāntam vyādita āsyam iva antakam nakulam ca yudhām śreṣṭham sarva yuddha viśāradam śakuniḥ saubalaḥ rājan vārayām āsa sa tvaraḥ śikhaṇḍinam atha āyāntam rathena rathinām varam kṛpo śāradvataḥ rājan vārayām āsa saṃyuge prativindhyam atha āyāntam mayūra sadṛśaiḥ hayaiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja yattaḥ yattam avārayat bhaimasenim atha āyāntam māyā śata viśāradam aśvatthāmā pituḥ mānam kurvāṇaḥ pratyaṣedhayat vārayām āsa samare droṇa prepsum mahā ratham virāṭam drutam āyāntam droṇasya nidhanam prati madra rājaḥ su saṃkruddhaḥ vārayām āsa bhārata śatānīkam atha āyāntam nākulim rabhasam raṇe arjunam ca yudhām śreṣṭham prādravantam mahā ratham tathā droṇam mahā iṣvāsam nighnantam śātravān raṇe dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ atha pāñcālyaḥ hṛṣṭa rūpam avārayat tathā anyān pāṇḍu putrāṇām samāyātān mahā rathān tāvakāḥ rathinaḥ rājan vārayām āsuḥ ojasā gaja ārohāḥ gajaiḥ tūrṇam saṃnipatya mahā mṛdhe yodhayantaḥ sma dṛśyante śataśas atha sahasraśas niśīthe turagāḥ rājan ādravantaḥ parasparam sādinaḥ sādibhiḥ sārdham prāsa śakti ṛṣṭi pāṇayaḥ gadābhiḥ musalaiḥ ca eva nānā śastraiḥ ca saṃghaśas vārayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ velā iva udvṛttam arṇavam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tu hārdikyam viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ punar vivyādha viṃśatyā tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt hārdikyam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ bāhvoḥ urasi ca arpayat tasya pārthaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā hasta āvāpam nikṛtya ca prāhiṇot niśitān bāṇān pañca rājan śilā śitān prāviśan dharaṇīm ugrāḥ valmīkam iva pannagāḥ akṣṇoḥ nimeṣa mātreṇa saḥ anyat ādāya kārmukam vivyādha pāṇḍavam ṣaṣṭyā sūtam ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ tasya śaktim ameya ātmā pāṇḍavaḥ bhujaga upamām sā hema citrā mahatī pāṇḍavena praveritā nirbhidya dakṣiṇam bāhum prāviśat dharaṇī talam hārdikyam chādayām āsa śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tatas tu samare śūraḥ vṛṣṇīnām pravaraḥ rathī vyaśva sūta ratham cakre nimeṣa ardhāt yudhiṣṭhiram tatas tu pāṇḍavaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ khaḍga carma samādade tomaram tu tatas gṛhya svarṇa daṇḍam durāsadam preṣayat samare tūrṇam hārdikyasya yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kavacam ca asya saṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ adārayat hārdikya śara saṃchinnam kavacam tat mahātmanaḥ vyaśīryata raṇe rājan tārā jālam iva ambarāt sa chinna dhanvā virathaḥ śīrṇa varmā śara arditaḥ apāyāsīt raṇāt tūrṇam dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca bhūriḥ tu samare rājan śaineyam rathinām varam athā enam sātyakiḥ kruddhaḥ pañcabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha hṛdaye tūrṇam prāsravat tasya śoṇitam tau anyonyam mahā rāja tatakṣāte śaraiḥ bhṛśam tayoḥ āsīt mahā rāja śastra vṛṣṭiḥ su dāruṇā kruddhayoḥ sāyaka mucoḥ yama antaka nikāśayoḥ athā enam chinna dhanvānam navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha hṛdaye tūrṇam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt saḥ atividdhaḥ balavatā śatruṇā śatru tāpanaḥ sa viddhvā sātvatam bāṇaiḥ tribhiḥ eva viśām pate chinna dhanvā mahā rāja sātyakiḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ prajahāra mahā vegām śaktim tasya mahā urasi sa tu śaktyāḥ vibhinna aṅgaḥ nipapāta ratha uttamāt lohitāṅgaḥ iva ākāśāt dīpta raśmiḥ yadṛcchayā tam tu dṛṣṭvā hatam śūram aśvatthāmā mahā rathaḥ abhyavarṣat śara ogheṇa merum vṛṣṭyā yathā ambudaḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ abravīt rājan nādam muktvā mahā rathaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha na me jīvan droṇaputra gamiṣyasi eṣa tvā adya haniṣyāmi mahiṣam skanda rāj iva yuddha śraddhām aham te adya vineṣyāmi raṇa ajire iti uktvā roṣa tāmra akṣaḥ rākṣasaḥ para vīra hā ratha akṣa mātraiḥ iṣubhiḥ abhyavarṣat ghaṭotkacaḥ rathinām ṛṣabham drauṇim dhārābhiḥ iva toyadaḥ śara vṛṣṭim tu tām prāptām śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ śātayām āsa samare tarasā drauṇiḥ utsmayan tatas śara śataiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ marma bhedibhiḥ āśugaiḥ samācinot rākṣasa indram ghaṭotkacam ariṃdama sa śaraiḥ ācitaḥ tena rākṣasaḥ raṇa mūrdhani vyakāśata mahā rāja śvāvidh śalalitaḥ yathā tatas krodha samāviṣṭaḥ bhaimaseniḥ pratāpavān kṣurapraiḥ ardhacandraiḥ ca nārācaiḥ sa śilīmukhaiḥ varāhakarṇaiḥ nālīkaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ ca api vikarṇibhiḥ tām śastra vṛṣṭim atulām vajra aśani sama svanām vyadhamat sa mahā tejāḥ mahā abhrāṇi iva mārutaḥ tatas antarikṣe bāṇānām saṃgrāmaḥ anyaḥ iva abhavat ghora rūpaḥ mahā rāja yodhānām harṣa vardhanaḥ sa mārgaṇa gaṇaiḥ drauṇiḥ diśaḥ pracchādya sarvatas priya artham tava putrāṇām rākṣasam samavākirat tatas pravavṛte yuddham drauṇi rākṣasayoḥ mṛdhe tatas ghaṭotkacaḥ bāṇaiḥ daśabhiḥ drauṇim āhave sa moham anusaṃprāptaḥ dhvaja yaṣṭim samāśritaḥ tatas hāhākṛtam sainyam tava sarvam janādhipa hatam sma menire sarve tāvakāḥ tam viśām pate tam tu dṛṣṭvā tathā avastham aśvatthāmānam āhave pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāḥ ca eva siṃhanādam pracakrire pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām aśvatthāmā mahā balaḥ dhanuḥ prapīḍya vāmena kareṇa amitra karśanaḥ mumoca ākarṇa pūrṇena dhanuṣā śaram uttamam yama daṇḍa upamam ghoram uddiśya āśu ghaṭotkacam sa bhittvā hṛdayam tasya rākṣasasya śara uttamaḥ viveśa vasudhām ugraḥ su puṅkhaḥ pṛthivīpate rākṣasa indraḥ su balavān drauṇinā raṇa māninā dṛṣṭvā vimūḍham haiḍimbam sārathiḥ tam raṇa ajirāt drauṇeḥ sakāśāt saṃbhrāntaḥ tu apaninye tvarā anvitaḥ nanāda su mahā nādam droṇaputraḥ mahā balaḥ vapuṣā pratijajvāla madhyāhne iva bhāskaraḥ tam bhīmasenaḥ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha māriṣa duryodhanaḥ api viṃśatyā śarāṇām pratyavidhyata tau sāyakaiḥ avacchannau adṛśyetām raṇa ajire pañcabhiḥ bharata śreṣṭha tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tasya bhīmaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā dhvajam ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha kaurava śreṣṭham navatyā nata parvaṇām cikṣepa sa śarān rājan paśyatām sarva dhanvinām kauravam pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām samārpayat atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ vivyādha nṛpatim tūrṇam saptabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ dvitīyam ca tṛtīyam ca caturtham pañcamam tathā āttam āttam mahā rāja bhīmasya dhanuḥ ācchinat tava putraḥ mahā rāja jita kāśī mada utkaṭaḥ sa tadā chidyamāneṣu kārmukeṣu punar punar śaktim cikṣepa samare sarva pāraśavīm śubhām aprāptām eva tām śaktim tridhā ciccheda kauravaḥ tatas bhīmaḥ mahā rāja gadām gurvīm mahā prabhām tatas sā sahasā vāhān tava putrasya saṃyuge āplutaḥ sahasā yānam nandakasya mahātmanaḥ tāvakāḥ sainikāḥ ca api menire nihatam nṛpam teṣām tu ninadam śrutvā trastānām sarva yodhinām bhīmasenasya nādam ca śrutvā rājan mahātmanaḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā hatam matvā suyodhanam pāñcālāḥ kekayāḥ matsyāḥ sṛñjayāḥ ca viśām pate saṃjayaḥ uvāca sahadevam atha āyāntam droṇa prepsum viśām pate tam karṇaḥ prativivyādha śatena nata parvaṇām tatas anyat dhanuḥ ādāya mādrī putraḥ pratāpavān karṇam vivyādha viṃśatyā tat adbhutam iva abhavat tasya karṇaḥ hayān hatvā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tatas gurvīm mahā ghorām hema citrām mahā gadām tām āpatantīm sahasā sahadeva praveritām vyaṣṭambhayat śaraiḥ karṇaḥ bhūmau ca enām apātayat gadām vinihatām dṛṣṭvā sahadevaḥ tvarā anvitaḥ śaktim cikṣepa karṇāya tām api asya ācchinat śaraiḥ sahadevaḥ mahā rāja dṛṣṭvā karṇam vyavasthitam vāryamāṇaḥ ca viśikhaiḥ sahadevaḥ raṇam jahau abravīt prahasan vākyam sahadevam viśām pate mā yudhyasva raṇe vīra viśiṣṭai rathibhiḥ saha sadṛśaiḥ yudhya mādreya vacaḥ me mā viśaṅkithāḥ evam uktvā tu tam karṇaḥ rathena rathinām varaḥ prāyāt pāñcāla pāṇḍūnām sainyāni prahasan iva vadha prāptam tu mādreyam na avadhīt samare ari hā kuntyāḥ smṛtvā vacaḥ rājan satya saṃdhaḥ mahā rathaḥ sahadevaḥ tatas rājan vimanāḥ śara pīḍitaḥ karṇa vāc śalya taptaḥ ca jīvitāt niravidyata āruroha ratham ca api pāñcālyasya mahātmanaḥ virāṭam saha senam tu droṇa arthe drutam āgatam madra rājaḥ śara ogheṇa chādayām āsa dhanvinam yādṛśam hi abhavat rājan jambha vāsavayoḥ purā madra rājaḥ mahā rāja virāṭam vāhinīpatim ājaghne tvaritam tīkṣṇaiḥ śatena nata parvaṇām prativivyādha tam rājā navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahā rathaḥ tasthau visphārayan cāpam vimuñcan ca śitān śarān śatānīkaḥ tatas dṛṣṭvā bhrātaram hata vāhanam śatānīkam atha āyāntam madra rājaḥ mahā mṛdhe āruroha ratham tūrṇam tam eva dhvaja mālinam madra rāja ratham tūrṇam chādayām āsa patribhiḥ ājaghāna urasi dṛḍham virāṭam vāhinīpatim kaśmalam ca aviśat tīvram virāṭaḥ bharata ṛṣabha tatas sā mahatī senā prādravat niśi bhārata vadhyamānā śara śataiḥ śalyena āhava śobhinā tām dṛṣṭvā vidrutām senām vāsudeva dhanaṃjayau prāyātām tatra rāja indra yatra śalyaḥ vyavasthitaḥ aṣṭa cakra samāyuktam āsthāya pravaram ratham lohita ārdra patākam tam rakta mālya vibhūṣitam kārṣṇāyasa mayam ghoram ṛkṣa carma āvṛtam mahat raudreṇa citra pakṣeṇa vivṛta akṣeṇa kūjatā dhvajena ucchrita tuṇḍena gṛdhra rājena rājatā sa babhau rākṣasaḥ rājan bhinnāñjana caya upamaḥ rurodha arjunam āyāntam prabhañjanam iva adrirāj kiran bāṇa gaṇān rājan śataśas arjuna mūrdhani ati tīvram abhūt yuddham nara rākṣasayoḥ mṛdhe draṣṭṝṇām prīti jananam sarveṣām bharata ṛṣabha tam arjunaḥ śatena eva patriṇām abhyatāḍayat virathasya udyatam khaḍgam śareṇa asya dvidhā ācchinat tam vijitya arjunaḥ tūrṇam droṇa antikam upāyayau kiran śara gaṇān rājan nara vāraṇa vājiṣu vadhyamānāḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā sainikāḥ nyapatan urvyām vāta nunnāḥ iva drumāḥ teṣu tu utsādyamāneṣu phalgunena mahātmanā saṃprādravat balam sarvam putrāṇām te viśām pate saṃjayaḥ uvāca śatānīkam śaraiḥ tūrṇam nirdahantam camūm tava nākuliḥ citrasenam tu nārācena ārdayat bhṛśam sa ca tam prativivyādha daśabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ citrasenaḥ mahā rāja śatānīkam punar yudhi navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare gātrāt saṃcyāvayām āsa tat adbhutam iva abhavat saḥ apeta varmā putraḥ te virarāja bhṛśam nṛpa dhanuḥ anyat mahā rāja jagrāha ari vidāraṇam tatas tūrṇam citrasenaḥ nākulim navabhiḥ śaraiḥ śatānīkaḥ atha saṃkruddhaḥ citrasenasya māriṣa jaghāna caturaḥ vāhān sārathim ca nara uttamaḥ nākulim pañcaviṃśatyā śarāṇām ārdayat balī āruroha ratham tūrṇam hārdikyasya mahātmanaḥ drupadam tu saha anīkam droṇa prepsum mahā ratham vṛṣasenaḥ abhyayāt tūrṇam kiran śara śataiḥ tadā ṣaṣṭyā śarāṇām vivyādha bāhvoḥ urasi ca anagha bahubhiḥ sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare tau ubhau śara nunna aṅgau śara kaṇṭakinau raṇe vyabhrājetām mahā rāja śvāvidhau śalalaiḥ iva kiṃśukau iva ca utphullau vyakāśetām raṇa ajire vṛṣasenaḥ tatas rājan navabhiḥ drupadam śaraiḥ viddhvā vivyādha saptatyā punar ca anyaiḥ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas śara sahasrāṇi vimuñcan vibabhau tadā karṇa putraḥ mahā rāja varṣamāṇaḥ iva ambudaḥ saṃprādravat raṇe rājan niśīthe bhairave sati vyarājata mahī rājan vīta abhrā dyauḥ iva grahaiḥ prāvṛṣ kāle mahā rāja vidyudbhiḥ iva toyadaḥ tatas karṇa suta trastāḥ somakāḥ vipradudruvuḥ tena ardyamānāḥ samare dravamāṇāḥ ca somakāḥ vyarājanta mahā rāja pradīpaiḥ avabhāsitāḥ teṣu rāja sahasreṣu tāvakeṣu pareṣu ca ekaḥ eva jvalan tasthau vṛṣasenaḥ pratāpavān sa vijitya raṇe śūrān somakānām mahā rathān jagāma tvaritaḥ tatra yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tayoḥ samāgamaḥ rājan citra rūpaḥ babhūva ha duḥśāsanaḥ tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ lalāṭe samavidhyata virarāja mahā bāhuḥ sa śṛṅgaḥ iva parvataḥ duḥśāsanam tu samare prativindhyaḥ mahā rathaḥ patākāḥ ca sa tūṇīrān raśmīn yoktrāṇi ca abhibho ciccheda tilaśas kruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ virathaḥ sa tu dharma ātmā dhanuṣpāṇiḥ avasthitaḥ ayodhayat tava sutam kiran śara śatān bahūn tam dṛṣṭvā viratham tatra bhrātaraḥ asya mahā rathāḥ abhyavartanta saṃgrāme mahatyā senayā vṛtāḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham tava teṣām ca bhārata niśīthe dāruṇe kāle yama rāṣṭra vivardhanam saṃjayaḥ uvāca abhyayāt saubalaḥ kruddhaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt kṛta vairau tu tau vīrau anyonya vadha kāṅkṣiṇau śaraiḥ pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ yathā eva saubalaḥ kṣipram śara varṣāṇi muñcati tathā eva nakulaḥ rājan śikṣām saṃdarśayan yudhi tau ubhau samare śūrau śara kaṇṭakinau tadā vyarājetām mahā rāja kaṇṭakaiḥ iva śālmalī su jihmam prekṣamāṇau ca rājan vivṛta locanau niṣasāda rathopasthe kaśmalam ca enam āviśat atyanta vairiṇam dṛptam dṛṣṭvā śatrum tathāgatam nanāda śakuniḥ rājan tapānte jaladaḥ yathā pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām nakulaḥ pāṇḍu nandanaḥ abhyayāt saubalam bhūyas vyātta ānanaḥ iva antakaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ śakunim ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha bharata ṛṣabha punar ca eva śatena eva nārācānām stanāntare tatas asya sa śaram cāpam muṣṭideśe sa cicchide dhvajam ca tvaritam chittvā rathāt bhūmau apātayat tam visaṃjñam nipatitam dṛṣṭvā syālam tava anagha apovāha rathena āśu sārathiḥ dhvajinī mukhāt tatas saṃcukruśuḥ pārthāḥ ye ca teṣām padānugāḥ nirjitya ca raṇe śatrūn nakulaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ abravīt sārathim kruddhaḥ droṇa anīkāya mām vaha tasya tat vacanam śrutvā mādrī putrasya dhīmataḥ śikhaṇḍinam tu samare droṇa prepsum viśām pate gautamam drutam āyāntam droṇa antikam ariṃdamam tam ācāryaḥ mahā rāja viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ punar vivyādha viṃśatyā putrāṇām priya kṛt tava mahat yuddham tayoḥ āsīt ghora rūpam viśām pate yathā devāsure yuddhe śambara amararājayoḥ śara jāla āvṛtam vyoma cakratuḥ tau mahā rathau prakṛtyāḥ ghora rūpam tat āsīt ghorataram punar rātriḥ ca bharata śreṣṭha yodhānām yuddha śālinām kālarātri nibhā hi āsīt ghora rūpā bhaya āvahā śikhaṇḍī tu mahā rāja gautamasya mahat dhanuḥ tasya kruddhaḥ kṛpaḥ rājan śaktim cikṣepa dāruṇām svarṇa daṇḍām akuṇṭha agrām karmāra parimārjitām tām āpatantīm ciccheda śikhaṇḍī bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ sā apatat medinīm dīptā bhāsayantī mahā prabhā atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya gautamaḥ rathinām varaḥ prācchādayat śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ mahā rāja śikhaṇḍinam vyaṣīdata rathopasthe śikhaṇḍī rathinām varaḥ sīdantam ca enam ālokya kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ yudhi vimukham tam raṇe dṛṣṭvā yājñasenim mahā ratham pāñcālāḥ somakāḥ ca eva parivavruḥ samantataḥ rathānām ca raṇe rājan anyonyam abhidhāvatām babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ meghānām nadatām iva dravatām sādinām ca eva gajānām ca viśām pate pattīnām dravatām ca eva pada śabdena medinī nyagṛhṇan bahavaḥ rājan śalabhān vāyasāḥ iva tathā gajān prabhinnān ca su prabhinnāḥ mahā gajāḥ sādī sādinam āsādya padātī ca padātinam samāsādya raṇe anyonyam saṃrabdhāḥ na aticakramuḥ dhāvatām dravatām ca eva punar āvartatām api babhūva tatra sainyānām śabdaḥ su tumulaḥ niśi dīpyamānāḥ pradīpāḥ ca ratha vāraṇa vājiṣu adṛśyanta mahā rāja mahā ulkāḥ iva khāt cyutāḥ sā niśā bharata śreṣṭha pradīpaiḥ avabhāsitā ādityena yathā vyāptam tamaḥ loke praṇaśyati tathā naṣṭam tamaḥ ghoram dīpaiḥ dīptaiḥ alaṃkṛtam śastrāṇām kavacānām ca maṇīnām ca mahātmanām antardadhuḥ prabhāḥ sarvāḥ dīpaiḥ taiḥ avabhāsitāḥ putraḥ ca pitaram mohāt sakhāyam ca sakhā tathā saṃbandhinam ca saṃbandhī svasrīyam ca api mātulaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rāja droṇam eva abhyavartata saṃmṛjānaḥ dhanuḥ śreṣṭham jyām vikarṣan punar punar dhṛṣṭadyumnam tadā āyāntam droṇasya anta cikīrṣayā parivavruḥ mahā rāja pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha tathā parivṛtam dṛṣṭvā droṇam ācārya sattamam bala arṇavau tatas tau tu sameyātām niśā mukhe tatas droṇam mahā rāja pāñcālyaḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha hṛdaye tūrṇam siṃhanādam nanāda ca tam droṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā viddhvā bhārata saṃyuge tatas kruddhaḥ mahā rāja dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān ādade anyat dhanuḥ śreṣṭham droṇasya anta cikīrṣayā vikṛṣya ca dhanuḥ citram ākarṇāt para vīra hā droṇasya anta karam ghoram vyasṛjat sāyakam tatas sa visṛṣṭaḥ balavatā śaraḥ ghoraḥ mahā mṛdhe bhāsayām āsa tat sainyam divākaraḥ iva uditaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā tu śaram ghoram deva gandharva mānavāḥ tam tu sāyakam a prāptam ācāryasya ratham prati karṇaḥ dvādaśadhā rājan ciccheda kṛtahasta vat sa chinnaḥ bahudhā rājan sūtaputreṇa māriṣa nipapāta śaraḥ tūrṇam nikṛttaḥ karṇa sāyakaiḥ chittvā tu samare bāṇam śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam raṇe karṇaḥ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ śalyaḥ ca navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ tribhiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tathā duryodhanaḥ ca viṃśatyā śakuniḥ ca api pañcabhiḥ pāñcālyam tvaritāḥ avidhyan sarve eva mahā rathāḥ sa viddhaḥ saptabhiḥ vīraiḥ droṇa trāṇa artham āhave droṇam drauṇim ca karṇam ca vivyādha tava ca ātmajam te viddhvā dhanvinā tena dhṛṣṭadyumnam punar mṛdhe vivyadhuḥ pañcabhiḥ tūrṇam ekaikaḥ rathinām varaḥ tribhiḥ ca anyaiḥ śaraiḥ tūrṇam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā dhautaiḥ prāṇānta karaṇaiḥ yudhi unmamātha śiraḥ kāyāt drumasenasya vīryavān tad śiraḥ nyapatat bhūmau saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭha puṭam raṇe mahā vāta samuddhūtam pakvam tāla phalam yathā tān ca viddhvā punar vīrān vīraḥ su niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ na tu tat mamṛṣe karṇaḥ dhanuṣaḥ chedanam tathā nikartanam iva ati ugraḥ lāṅgūlasya yathā hariḥ saḥ anyat dhanuḥ samādāya krodha rakta īkṣaṇaḥ śvasan dṛṣṭvā tu karṇam saṃrabdham te vīrāḥ ṣaṭ ratha ṛṣabhāḥ pāñcālya putram tvaritāḥ parivavruḥ jighāṃsayā ṣaṇṇām yodha pravīrāṇām tāvakānām puraskṛtam mṛtyoḥ āsyam anuprāptam dhṛṣṭadyumnam amaṃsmahi etasmin eva kāle tu dāśārhaḥ vikiran śarān dhṛṣṭadyumnam parākrāntam sātyakiḥ pratyapadyata tam āyāntam mahā iṣvāsam sātyakim yuddha durmadam tam sātyakiḥ mahā rāja vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ paśyatām sarva vīrāṇām mā gāḥ tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt trāsayan tala ghoṣeṇa kṣatriyān kṣatriya ṛṣabhaḥ rājīva locanam karṇam sātyakiḥ pratyavidhyata kampayan iva ghoṣeṇa dhanuṣaḥ vasudhām balī vipāṭha karṇi nārācaiḥ vatsadantaiḥ kṣuraiḥ api karṇaḥ śara śataiḥ ca api śaineyam pratyavidhyata tathā eva yuyudhānaḥ api vṛṣṇīnām pravaraḥ rathaḥ tāvakāḥ ca mahā rāja karṇa putraḥ ca daṃśitaḥ sātyakim vivyadhuḥ tūrṇam samantāt niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya teṣām karṇasya ca abhibho tena bāṇena nirviddhaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ viśām pate tatas karṇaḥ hatam matvā vṛṣasenam mahā rathaḥ putra śoka abhisaṃtaptaḥ sātyakim pratyapīḍayat pīḍyamānaḥ tu karṇena yuyudhānaḥ mahā rathaḥ vivyādha bahubhiḥ karṇam tvaramāṇaḥ punar punar sa karṇam daśabhiḥ viddhvā vṛṣasenam ca saptabhiḥ sa hasta āvāpa dhanuṣī tayoḥ ciccheda sātvataḥ tau anye dhanuṣī sajye kṛtvā śatru bhayaṃkare yuyudhānam avidhyetām samantāt niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ atīva śuśruve rājan gāṇḍīvasya mahā svanaḥ śrutvā tu ratha nirghoṣam gāṇḍīvasya ca nisvanam eṣa sarvān śibīn hatvā mukhyaśas ca nara ṛṣabhān pauravān ca mahā iṣvāsān gāṇḍīva ninadaḥ mahān śrūyate ratha ghoṣaḥ ca vāsavasya iva nardataḥ karoti pāṇḍavaḥ vyaktam karma aupayikam ātmanaḥ eṣā vidīryate rājan bahudhā bhāratī camūḥ viprakīrṇāni anīkāni na avatiṣṭhanti karhi cit dravatām yodha mukhyānām gāṇḍīva preṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ viddhānām śataśas rājan śrūyate ninadaḥ mahān niśīthe rāja śārdūla stanayitnoḥ iva ambare hāhākāra ravān ca eva siṃhanādān ca puṣkalān śṛṇu śabdān bahuvidhān arjunasya ratham prati ayam madhye sthitaḥ asmākam sātyakiḥ sātvata adhamaḥ iha ced labhyate lakṣyam kṛtsnān jeṣyāmahe parān eṣa pāñcāla rājasya putraḥ droṇena saṃgataḥ sātyakim yadi hanyāmaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca pārṣatam prayatāmaḥ mahā rāja nihantum vṛṣṇi pārṣatau savyasācī puras abhyeti droṇa anīkāya bhārata saṃsaktam sātyakim jñātvā bahubhiḥ kuru puṃgavaiḥ yāvat pārthaḥ na jānāti sātyakim bahubhiḥ vṛtam te tvaradhvam yathā śūrāḥ śarāṇām mokṣaṇe bhṛśam yathā tūrṇam vrajati eṣa para lokāya mādhavaḥ yathā indraḥ samare rājan prāha viṣṇum yaśasvinam vṛtaḥ sahasraiḥ daśabhiḥ gajānām anivartinām duḥśāsanaḥ durviṣahaḥ subāhuḥ duṣpradharṣaṇaḥ jahi kṛṣṇau mahā bāho dharmarājam ca mātula devānām iva devendre jaya āśā me tvayi sthitā priya artham tava putrāṇām didhakṣuḥ pāṇḍu nandanān tatas pravavṛte yuddham tāvakānām paraiḥ saha prayāte saubale rājan pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm abhyayāt tvaritam yuddhe kiran śara śatān bahūn tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve sātyakim paryavārayan mahat yuddham tadā āsīt tu droṇasya niśi bhārata dhṛṣṭadyumnena śūreṇa pāñcālaiḥ ca mahātmanaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca a mṛṣyamāṇāḥ saṃrabdhāḥ yuyudhāna ratham prati athā enam koṣṭhakīkṛtya sarvatas te mahā rathāḥ siṃhanādān tadā cakruḥ tarjayantaḥ sma sātyakim te abhyavarṣan śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ sātyakim satya vikramam tvaramāṇāḥ mahā vīryāḥ mādhavasya vadha eṣiṇaḥ tān dṛṣṭvā patataḥ tūrṇam śaineyaḥ para vīra hā pratyagṛhṇāt mahā bāhuḥ pramuñcan viśikhān bahūn nicakarta śirāṃsi ugraiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ hasti hastān haya grīvān bāhūn api ca sa āyudhān kṣurapraiḥ pātayām āsa tāvakānām sa mādhavaḥ babhūva dharaṇī pūrṇā nakṣatraiḥ dyauḥ iva prabho teṣām tu yuyudhānena yudhyatām yudhi bhārata babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ pretānām iva krandatām tena śabdena mahatā pūritā āsīt vasuṃdharā rātriḥ samabhavat ca eva tīvra rūpā bhaya āvahā dīryamāṇam balam dṛṣṭvā yuyudhāna śara āhatam śrutvā ca vipulam nādam niśīthe loma harṣaṇam sutaḥ tava abravīt rājan sārathim rathinām varaḥ yatra eṣa śabdaḥ tatra aśvān codaya iti punar punar sūtaḥ saṃcodayām āsa yuyudhāna ratham prati tatas pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ māṃsa śoṇita bhojanaiḥ śaineyam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat amarṣitaḥ pāñcālānām ca sarveṣām bhāratānām ca dāruṇam sāyakānām aśītyā tu vivyādha urasi bhārata sārathim ca rathāt tūrṇam pātayām āsa patriṇā hata aśve tu rathe tiṣṭhan putraḥ tava viśām pate mumoca niśitān bāṇān śaineyasya ratham prati śarān pañcāśataḥ tān tu śaineyaḥ kṛtahasta vat atha apareṇa bhallena muṣṭideśe mahat dhanuḥ āruroha ratham tūrṇam bhāsvaram kṛtavarmaṇaḥ drāvayām āsa viśikhaiḥ niśā madhye viśām pate śakuniḥ ca arjunam rājan parivārya samantataḥ arjunam yodhayanti sma kṣatriyāḥ kāla coditāḥ tāni arjunaḥ sahasrāṇi ratha vāraṇa vājinām tatas tu samare śūraḥ śakuniḥ saubalaḥ tadā saṃvārya tān bāṇa gaṇaiḥ yudhi rājan dhanaṃjayaḥ avadhīt tāvakān yodhān vajrapāṇiḥ iva asurān bhujaiḥ chinnaiḥ mahā rāja śarīraiḥ ca sahasraśas samāstīrṇā dharā tatra babhau puṣpaiḥ iva ācitā sa viddhvā śakunim bhūyas pañcabhiḥ nata parvabhiḥ tam ulūkaḥ tathā viddhvā vāsudevam atāḍayat nanāda ca mahā nādam pūrayan vasudhā talam ulūkasya ratham tūrṇam āruroha viśām pate tau eka ratham ārūḍhau pitāputrau mahā rathau pārtham siṣicatuḥ bāṇaiḥ girim meghau iva utthitau tau tu viddhvā mahā rāja pāṇḍavaḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vidrāvayan tava camūm śataśas vyadhamat śaraiḥ vicchinnāni tathā rājan balāni āsan viśām pate tat balam bharata śreṣṭha vadhyamānam tathā niśi pradudrāva diśaḥ sarvāḥ vīkṣamāṇam bhaya arditam saṃbhrāntāḥ paryadhāvanta tasmin tamasi dāruṇe dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rāja droṇam viddhvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥ ciccheda dhanuṣaḥ tūrṇam jyām śareṇa śitena ha tat nidhāya dhanuḥ nīḍe droṇaḥ kṣatriya mardanaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam tatas droṇaḥ viddhvā saptabhiḥ āśugaiḥ sārathim pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ rājan vivyādha saṃyuge tam nivārya śaraiḥ tūrṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ vyadhamat kauravīm senām śataśas atha sahasraśas prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇita ogha taraṅgiṇī yathā vaitaraṇī rājan yama rāṣṭra puram prati drāvayitvā tu tat sainyam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān atha dadhmuḥ mahā śaṅkhān dhṛṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍinau yamau ca yuyudhānaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ ca vṛkodaraḥ jitvā ratha sahasrāṇi tāvakānām mahā rathāḥ siṃhanāda ravān cakruḥ pāṇḍavāḥ jita kāśinaḥ tathā droṇasya śūrasya drauṇeḥ ca eva viśām pate saṃjayaḥ uvāca vidrutam sva balam dṛṣṭvā vadhyamānam mahātmabhiḥ krodhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ putraḥ tava viśām pate abhyetya sahasā karṇam droṇam ca jayatām varam amarṣa vaśam āpannaḥ vākya jñaḥ vākyam abravīt bhavadbhyām iha saṃgrāmaḥ kruddhābhyām saṃpravartitaḥ āhave nihatam dṛṣṭvā saindhavam savyasācinā nihanyamānām pāṇḍūnām balena mama vāhinīm bhūtvā tad vijaye śaktau aśaktau iva paśyataḥ āvām pāṇḍu sutān saṃkhye jeṣyāvaḥ iti mānadau tadā eva aham vacaḥ śrutvā bhavadbhyām anusaṃmatam kṛtavān pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham vairam yodha vināśanam yadi na aham parityājyaḥ bhavadbhyām puruṣa ṛṣabhau prāvartayetām tau yuddham ghaṭṭitau iva pannagau śaineya pramukhān pārthān abhidudruvatuḥ raṇe tathā eva sahitāḥ pārthāḥ svena sainyena saṃvṛtāḥ atha droṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ daśabhiḥ śini puṃgavam avidhyat tvaritam kruddhaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ karṇaḥ ca daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ putraḥ ca tava saptabhiḥ daśabhiḥ vṛṣasenaḥ ca saubalaḥ ca api saptabhiḥ dṛṣṭvā ca samare droṇam nighnantam pāṇḍavīm camūm vivyadhuḥ somakāḥ tūrṇam samantāt śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ tatas droṇaḥ aharat prāṇān kṣatriyāṇām viśām pate raśmibhiḥ bhāskaraḥ rājan tamasām iva bhārata droṇena vadhyamānānām pāñcālānām viśām pate śuśruve tumulaḥ śabdaḥ krośatām itaretaram putrān anye pitṝn anye bhrātṝn anye ca mātulān bhāgineyān vayasyān ca tathā saṃbandhi bāndhavān pāṇḍavānām raṇe yodhāḥ para lokam tathā apare sā tathā pāṇḍavī senā vadhyamānā mahātmabhiḥ niśi saṃprādravat rājan utsṛjya ulkāḥ sahasraśas tamasā saṃvṛte loke na prājñāyata kim cana kauravāṇām prakāśena dṛśyante tu drutāḥ pare dravamāṇam tu tat sainyam droṇa karṇau mahā rathau jaghnatuḥ pṛṣṭhatas rājan kirantau sāyakān bahūn pāñcāleṣu prabhagneṣu dīryamāṇeṣu sarvaśas janārdanaḥ dīna manāḥ pratyabhāṣata phalgunam droṇa karṇau mahā iṣvāsau etau pārṣata sātyakī pāñcālān ca eva sahitau jaghnatuḥ sāyakaiḥ bhṛśam etayoḥ śara varṣeṇa prabhagnāḥ naḥ mahā rathāḥ vāryamāṇā api kaunteya pṛtanā na avatiṣṭhate etau āvām sarva sainyaiḥ vyūḍhaiḥ samyak udāyudhaiḥ droṇam ca sūtaputram ca prayatāvaḥ prabādhitum etau hi balinau śūrau kṛtāstrau jita kāśinau upekṣitau balam kruddhau nāśayetām niśām imām eṣa bhīmaḥ abhiyāti ugraḥ punar āvartya vāhinīm vṛkodaram tathā āyāntam dṛṣṭvā tatra janārdanaḥ punar eva abravīt rājan harṣayan iva pāṇḍavam eṣa bhīmaḥ raṇa ślāghī vṛtaḥ somaka pāṇḍavaiḥ etena sahitaḥ yudhya pāñcālaiḥ ca mahā rathaiḥ āśvāsana artham sarveṣām sainyānām pāṇḍu nandana tatas tau puruṣa vyāghrau ubhau mādhava pāṇḍavau droṇa karṇau samāsādya dhiṣṭhitau raṇa mūrdhani tatas droṇaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca parān mamṛdatuḥ yudhi yathā sāgarayoḥ rājan candra udaya vivṛddhayoḥ tatas utsṛjya pāṇibhyaḥ pradīpān tava vāhinī yuyudhe pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham unmatta vat ahar kṣaye rajasā tamasā ca eva saṃvṛte bhṛśa dāruṇe kevalam nāma gotreṇa prāyudhyanta jaya eṣiṇaḥ aśrūyanta hi nāmāni śrāvyamāṇāni pārthivaiḥ niḥśabdam āsīt sahasā punar śabdaḥ mahān abhūt kruddhānām yudhyamānānām jayatām jīyatām api tathā saṃyudhyamānānām vigāḍhā abhūt mahā niśā pāṇḍavānām ca rāja indra kauravāṇām ca sarvaśas saṃjayaḥ uvāca tatas karṇaḥ raṇe dṛṣṭvā pārṣatam para vīra hā prativivyādha tam tūrṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api māriṣa pañcabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ hṛṣṭaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tau anyonyam śaraiḥ saṃkhye saṃchādya su mahā rathau punar pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ vivyadhāte parasparam tatas pāñcāla mukhyasya dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyuge sārathim caturaḥ ca aśvān karṇaḥ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ kārmuka pravaram ca asya praciccheda śitaiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apātayat dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu virathaḥ hata aśvaḥ hata sārathiḥ gṛhītvā parigham ghoram karṇasya aśvān apīpiṣat viddhaḥ ca bahubhiḥ tena śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhira anīkam padbhyām eva anvavartata karṇasya api rathe vāhān anyān sūtaḥ nyayojayat śaṅkha varṇān mahā vegān saindhavān sādhu vāhinaḥ labdha lakṣyaḥ tu rādheyaḥ pāñcālānām mahā rathān abhyapīḍayat āyastaḥ śaraiḥ meghaḥ iva acalān sā pīḍyamānā karṇena pāñcālānām mahā camūḥ saṃprādravat su saṃtrastā siṃhena iva arditā mṛgī rathebhyaḥ ca narāḥ tūrṇam adṛśyanta tatas tatas bāhū ciccheda vai karṇaḥ śiraḥ ca eva sa kuṇḍalam ūrū ciccheda ca anyasya gaja sthasya viśām pate vāji pṛṣṭha gatasya api bhūmiṣṭhasya ca māriṣa dhāvamānāḥ bahavaḥ ca mahā rathāḥ saṃchinnāni ātma gātrāṇi vāhanāni ca saṃyuge te vadhyamānāḥ samare pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ saha tṛṇa praspandanāt ca api sūtaputram sma menire api svam samare yodham dhāvamānam vicetasaḥ tāni anīkāni bhagnāni dravamāṇāni bhārata abhyadravat drutam karṇaḥ pṛṣṭhatas vikiran śarān avekṣamāṇāḥ te anyonyam su saṃmūḍhāḥ vicetasaḥ na aśaknuvan avasthātum kālyamānāḥ mahātmanā karṇena abhyāhatāḥ rājan pāñcālāḥ parama iṣubhiḥ droṇena ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ vīkṣamāṇāḥ pradudruvuḥ apayāne matim kṛtvā phalgunam vākyam abravīt paśya karṇam mahā iṣvāsam dhanuṣpāṇim avasthitam niśīthe dāruṇe kāle tapantam iva bhāskaram karṇa sāyaka nunnānām krośatām eṣa nisvanaḥ aniśam śrūyate pārtha tvad bandhūnām anātha vat yathā visṛjataḥ ca asya saṃdadhānasya ca āśugān yat atra anantaram kāryam prāpta kālam prapaśyasi evam uktaḥ mahā bāhuḥ pārthaḥ kṛṣṇam atha abravīt bhītaḥ kuntī sutaḥ rājā rādheyasya ati vikramāt evam gate prāpta kālam karṇa anīke punar punar bhavān vyavasyatām kṣipram dravate hi varūthinī droṇa sāyaka nunnānām bhagnānām madhusūdana karṇena trāsyamānānām avasthānam na vidyate paśyāmi ca tathā karṇam vicarantam abhīta vat dravamāṇān ratha udārān kirantam viśikhaiḥ śitaiḥ pratyakṣam vṛṣṇi śārdūla pāda sparśam iva uragaḥ sa bhavān atra yātu āśu yatra karṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ aham enam vadhiṣyāmi mām vā eṣa madhusūdana vāsudevaḥ uvāca paśyāmi karṇam kaunteya devarājam iva āhave ṛte tvām puruṣa vyāghra rākṣasāt vā ghaṭotkacāt na tu tāvat aham manye prāpta kālam tava anagha samāgamam mahā bāho sūtaputreṇa saṃyuge dīpyamānā mahā ulkā iva tiṣṭhati asya hi vāsavī sa hi bhīmena balinā jātaḥ sura parākramaḥ tasmin astrāṇi divyāni rākṣasāni āsurāṇi ca satatam ca anuraktaḥ vaḥ hita eṣī ca ghaṭotkacaḥ vijeṣyati raṇe karṇam iti me na atra saṃśayaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ pārtham puṣkara locanaḥ ājuhāva atha tat rakṣaḥ tat ca āsīt prādur agratas kavacī sa śarī khaḍgī sa dhanvā ca viśām pate abhivādya tatas kṛṣṇam pāṇḍavam ca dhanaṃjayam abravīt tam tadā hṛṣṭaḥ tu ayam asmi anuśādhi mām tatas tam megha saṃkāśam dīpta āsyam dīpta kuṇḍalam abhyabhāṣata haiḍimbam dāśārhaḥ prahasan iva ghaṭotkaca vijānīhi yat tvām vakṣyāmi putraka sa bhavān majjamānānām bandhūnām tvam plavaḥ yathā vividhāni tava astrāṇi santi māyā ca rākṣasī paśya karṇena haiḍimba pāṇḍavānām anīkinī kālyamānāḥ yathā gāvaḥ pālena raṇa mūrdhani eṣa karṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ matimān dṛḍha vikramaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkeṣu nihanti kṣatriya ṛṣabhān kirantaḥ śara varṣāṇi mahānti dṛḍha dhanvinaḥ na śaknuvanti avasthātum pīḍyamānāḥ śara arciṣā niśīthe sūtaputreṇa śara varṣeṇa pīḍitāḥ ete dravanti pāñcālāḥ siṃhasya iva bhayāt mṛgāḥ mātulānām pitṝṇām ca tejasaḥ astra balasya ca katham naḥ tārayet duḥkhāt sa tvam tāraya bāndhavān tava hi astra balam bhīmam māyāḥ ca tava dustarāḥ pāṇḍavānām prabhagnānām karṇena śita sāyakaiḥ majjatām dhārtarāṣṭreṣu bhava pāram paraṃtapa rātrau hi rākṣasāḥ bhūyas bhavanti amita vikramāḥ balavantaḥ su durdharṣāḥ śūrāḥ vikrānta cāriṇaḥ jahi karṇam mahā iṣvāsam niśīthe māyayā raṇe pārthāḥ droṇam vadhiṣyanti dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamāḥ keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā bībhatsuḥ api rākṣasam ghaṭotkaca bhavān ca eva dīrgha bāhuḥ ca sātyakiḥ matau me sarva sainyeṣu bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ sa bhavān yātu karṇena dvairatham yudhyatām niśi sātyakiḥ pṛṣṭhagopaḥ te bhaviṣyati mahā rathaḥ jahi karṇam raṇe śūram sātvatena sahāyavān alam eva asmi karṇāya droṇāya alam ca sattama anyeṣām kṣatriyāṇām ca kṛtāstrāṇām mahātmanām adya dāsyāmi saṃgrāmam sūtaputrāya tam niśi yam janāḥ saṃpravakṣyanti yāvat bhūmiḥ dhariṣyati na ca atra śūrān mokṣyāmi na bhītān na kṛtāñjalīn sarvān eva vadhiṣyāmi rākṣasam dharmam āsthitaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ haiḍimbaḥ para vīra hā abhyasyan parama iṣvāsaḥ pratijagrāha sūtajaḥ garjatoḥ rāja śārdūla śakra prahrādayoḥ iva saṃjayaḥ uvāca dṛṣṭvā ghaṭotkacam rājan sūtaputra ratham prati prayāntam tvararyā yuktam jighāṃsum karṇam āhave abravīt tava putraḥ tu duḥśāsanam idam vacaḥ etat rakṣaḥ raṇe tūrṇam dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramam abhiyāti drutam karṇam tat vāraya mahā ratham vṛtaḥ sainyena mahatā yāhi yatra mahā balaḥ rakṣa karṇam raṇe yattaḥ vṛtaḥ sainyena mānada pāṇḍavān hantum icchāmi tvayā ājñaptaḥ saha anugān jaṭāsuraḥ mama pitā rakṣasām agraṇīḥ purā tasya apacitim icchāmi tvad diṣṭaḥ gantum īśvara tam abravīt tatas rājā prīyamāṇaḥ punar punar droṇa karṇa ādibhiḥ sārdham paryāptaḥ aham dviṣat vadhe tathā iti uktvā mahā kāyaḥ samāhūya ghaṭotkacam jaṭāsuriḥ bhaimasenim nānā śastraiḥ avākirat haiḍimbaḥ pramamātha ekaḥ mahā vātaḥ ambudān iva tatas māyā mayam dṛṣṭvā ratham tūrṇam alaṃbalaḥ ghaṭotkacam śara vrātaiḥ nānā liṅgaiḥ samārdayat vyadrāvayat śara vrātaiḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm tena vidrāvyamāṇāni pāṇḍu sainyāni māriṣa niśīthe viprakīryanta vāta nunnāḥ ghanāḥ iva niśīthe prādravat rājan utsṛjya ulkāḥ sahasraśas tilaśas tasya tat yānam sūtam sarva āyudhāni ca ghaṭotkacaḥ praciccheda prāṇadat ca ati dāruṇam tatas karṇam śara vrātaiḥ kurūn anyān sahasraśas tatas saṃcukṣubhe sainyam kurūṇām rākṣasa arditam jaṭāsuriḥ mahā rāja virathaḥ hata sārathiḥ ghaṭotkacam raṇe kruddhaḥ muṣṭinā abhyahanat dṛḍham muṣṭinā abhihataḥ tena pracacāla ghaṭotkacaḥ kṣiti kampe yathā śailaḥ sa vṛkṣa gaṇa gulmavān jaṭāsurim bhaimaseniḥ avadhīt muṣṭinā bhṛśam tam pramathya tatas kruddhaḥ tūrṇam haiḍimbiḥ ākṣipat dorbhyām indra dhvaja ābhābhyām niṣpipeṣa mahī tale ghaṭotkacam raṇe roṣāt niṣpipeṣa mahī tale ghaṭotkaca alaṃbalayoḥ tumulam loma harṣaṇam viśeṣayantau anyonyam māyābhiḥ ati māyinau pāvaka ambunidhī bhūtvā punar garuḍa takṣakau punar kuñjara śārdūlau punar svarbhānu bhāskarau evam māyā śata sṛjau anyonya vadha kāṅkṣiṇau parighaiḥ ca gadābhiḥ ca prāsa mudgara paṭṭiśaiḥ hayābhyām ca gajābhyām ca padāti rathinau punar utpapāta bhṛśam kruddhaḥ śyena vat nipapāta ha gṛhītvā ca mahā kāyam rākṣasa indram alaṃbalam udyamya nyavadhīt bhūmau mayam viṣṇuḥ iva āhave cakarta kāyāt hi śiraḥ bhīmam vikṛta darśanam tad śiraḥ rudhira abhyaktam gṛhya keśeṣu rākṣasaḥ abhyetya ca mahā bāhuḥ smayamānaḥ sa rākṣasaḥ prāṇadat bhairavam nādam prāvṛṣi iva balāhakaḥ eṣa te nihataḥ bandhuḥ tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ asya vikramaḥ punar draṣṭāsi karṇasya niṣṭhām etām tathā ātmanaḥ evam uktvā tatas prāyāt karṇam prati janeśvara kiran śara śatān tīkṣṇān vimuñcan karṇa mūrdhani vismāpanam mahā rāja nara rākṣasayoḥ mṛdhe dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca yatra vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ kīdṛśam ca abhavat yuddham tasya ghorasya rakṣasaḥ rathaḥ ca kīdṛśaḥ tasya māyāḥ sarva āyudhāni ca kīdṛśam varma ca eva asya kaṇṭha trāṇam ca kīdṛśam pṛṣṭaḥ tvam etat ācakṣva kuśalaḥ hi asi saṃjaya saṃjayaḥ uvāca lohita akṣaḥ mahā kāyaḥ tāmra āsyaḥ nimnita udaraḥ ūrdhva romā hari śmaśruḥ śaṅku karṇaḥ mahā hanuḥ ākarṇāt dārita āsyaḥ ca tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭraḥ karālavān su dīrgha tāmra jihvā uṣṭhaḥ lamba bhrūḥ sthūla nāsikaḥ mahā kāyaḥ mahā bāhuḥ mahā śīrṣaḥ mahā balaḥ sthūla sphic gūḍha nābhiḥ ca śithila upacayaḥ mahān tathā eva hasta ābharaṇī mahā māyaḥ aṅgadī tathā urasā dhārayan niṣkam agni mālām yathā acalaḥ tasya hema mayam citram bahu rūpa aṅga śobhitam toraṇa pratimam śubhram kirīṭam mūrdhni aśobhata kuṇḍale bāla sūrya ābhe mālām hema mayīm śubhām dhārayan vipulam kāṃsyam kavacam ca mahā prabham kiṅkiṇī śata nirghoṣam rakta dhvaja patākinam ṛkṣa carma avanaddha aṅgam nalva mātram mahā ratham tatra mātaṅga saṃkāśāḥ lohita akṣāḥ vibhīṣaṇāḥ kāma varṇa javāḥ yuktāḥ balavantaḥ avahan hayāḥ rākṣasaḥ asya virūpa akṣaḥ sūtaḥ dīpta āsya kuṇḍalaḥ raśmibhiḥ sūrya raśmi ābhaiḥ saṃjagrāha hayān raṇe saṃsaktaḥ iva ca abhreṇa yathā adriḥ mahatā mahān rakta uttamāṅgaḥ kravya ādaḥ gṛdhraḥ parama bhīṣaṇaḥ vāsava aśani nirghoṣam dṛḍha jyam abhivikṣipan vyaktam kiṣku parīṇāham dvādaśa aratni kārmukam ratha akṣa mātraiḥ iṣubhiḥ sarvāḥ pracchādayan diśaḥ tasyām vīra apahāriṇyām niśāyām karṇam abhyayāt tasya vikṣipataḥ cāpam rathe viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhataḥ aśrūyata dhanuḥ ghoṣaḥ visphūrjitam iva aśaneḥ tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya virūpākṣam vibhīṣaṇam mātaṅgaḥ iva mātaṅgam yūtha ṛṣabhaḥ iva ṛṣabham sa saṃnipātaḥ tumulaḥ tayoḥ āsīt viśām pate prācchādayetām anyonyam takṣamāṇau mahā iṣubhiḥ tatas pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ nyavārayetām anyonyam kāṃsye nirbhidya varmaṇī saṃchindantau hi gātrāṇi saṃdadhānau ca sāyakān dhakṣyamāṇau śara vrātaiḥ na udīkṣitum aśaknutām na akampayetām anyonyam yatamānau mahā dyutī tat pravṛttam niśā yuddham ciram samam iva abhavat prāṇayoḥ dīvyataḥ rājan karṇa rākṣasayoḥ mṛdhe tasya saṃdadhataḥ tīkṣṇān śarān ca asaktam asyataḥ ghaṭotkacam yadā karṇaḥ viśeṣayati naḥ nṛpa karṇena vihitam dṛṣṭvā divyam astram ghaṭotkacaḥ prāduścakre mahā māyām rākṣasaḥ pāṇḍu nandanaḥ śūla mudgara dhāriṇyā śaila pādapa hastayā rakṣasām ghora rūpāṇām mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ tam udyata mahā cāpam dṛṣṭvā te vyathitāḥ nṛpāḥ bhūtāntakam iva āyāntam kāla daṇḍa ugra dhāriṇam ghaṭotkaca pramuktena siṃhanādena bhīṣitāḥ prasusruvuḥ gajāḥ mūtram vivyathuḥ ca narāḥ bhṛśam tatas aśma vṛṣṭiḥ ati ugrā mahatī āsīt samantataḥ āyasāni ca cakrāṇi bhuśuṇḍyaḥ śakti tomarāḥ patanti aviralāḥ śūlāḥ śataghnyaḥ paṭṭiśāḥ tathā tat ugram ati raudram ca dṛṣṭvā yuddham narādhipāḥ māyāyām tu prahīṇāyām amarṣāt sa ghaṭotkacaḥ visasarja śarān ghorān sūtaputram te āviśan viviśuḥ dharaṇīm bāṇāḥ saṃkruddhāḥ iva pannagāḥ cakram divyam sahasra aram agṛhṇāt vyathitaḥ bhṛśam kṣura antam bāla sūrya ābham maṇi ratna vibhūṣitam ghaṭotkacaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ dṛṣṭvā cakram nipātitam karṇam prācchādayat bāṇaiḥ svarbhānuḥ iva bhāskaram ghaṭotkaca ratham tūrṇam chādayām āsa patribhiḥ ghaṭotkacena kruddhena gadā hema aṅgadā tadā kṣiptā bhrāmya śaraiḥ sā api pravavarṣa mahā kāyaḥ druma varṣam nabhastalāt tatas māyāvinam karṇaḥ bhīmasena sutam divi mārgaṇaiḥ abhivivyādha ghanam sūryaḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ abhyavarṣat śaraiḥ karṇaḥ parjanyaḥ iva vṛṣṭimān saḥ adṛśyata muhūrtena śvāvidh śalalitaḥ yathā dṛṣṭavantaḥ sma samare śara oghaiḥ abhisaṃvṛtam māyā yuddhena māyāvī sūtaputram ayodhayat saḥ ayodhayat tadā karṇam māyayā lāghavena ca alakṣyamāṇaḥ atha divi śara jāleṣu saṃpatan pracakāra mahā māyām mohayan iva bhārata sa sma kṛtvā virūpāṇi vadanāni aśubha ānanaḥ agrasat sūtaputrasya divyāni astrāṇi māyayā punar ca api mahā kāyaḥ saṃchinnaḥ śatadhā raṇe hatam tam manyamānāḥ sma prāṇadan kuru puṃgavāḥ punar ca api mahā kāyaḥ śata śīrṣaḥ śata udaraḥ vyadṛśyata mahā bāhuḥ mainākaḥ iva parvataḥ aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ bhūtvā ca punar eva sa rākṣasaḥ kṣitim dyām ca diśaḥ ca eva māyayā āvṛtya daṃśitaḥ gatvā karṇa ratha abhyāśam vicalat kuṇḍala ānanaḥ prāha vākyam asaṃbhrāntaḥ sūtaputram viśām pate tiṣṭha idānīm na me jīvan sūtaputra gamiṣyasi yuddha śraddhām aham te adya vineṣyāmi raṇa ajire iti uktvā roṣa tāmra akṣam rakṣaḥ krūra parākramam ratha akṣa mātraiḥ iṣubhiḥ abhyavarṣat ghaṭotkacaḥ rathinām ṛṣabham karṇam dhārābhiḥ iva toyadaḥ śara vṛṣṭim ca tām karṇaḥ dūra prāptām aśātayat dṛṣṭvā ca vihatām māyām karṇena bharata ṛṣabha ghaṭotkacaḥ tatas māyām sasarja antarhitaḥ punar śūla prāsa asi musala jala prasravaṇaḥ mahān tam añjana caya prakhyam karṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā mahīdharam prapātaiḥ āyudhāni ugrāṇi udvahantam na cukṣubhe tatas sa toyadaḥ bhūtvā nīlaḥ sa indrāyudhaḥ divi aśma vṛṣṭibhiḥ ati ugraḥ sūtaputram avākirat vyadhamat kāla megham tam karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ vṛṣā sa mārgaṇa gaṇaiḥ karṇaḥ diśaḥ pracchādya sarvaśas jaghāna astram mahā rāja ghaṭotkaca samīritam prāduścakre mahā māyām karṇam prati mahā ratham sa dṛṣṭvā punar āyāntam rathena rathinām varam ghaṭotkacam asaṃbhrāntam rākṣasaiḥ bahubhiḥ vṛtam siṃha śārdūla sadṛśaiḥ matta dvirada vikramaiḥ gaja sthaiḥ ca ratha sthaiḥ ca vāji pṛṣṭha gataiḥ tathā nānā śastra dharaiḥ ghoraiḥ nānā kavaca bhūṣaṇaiḥ dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ yodhayām āsa rākṣasam ghaṭotkacaḥ tatas karṇam viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ nanāda bhairavam nādam bhīṣayan sarva pārthivān bhūyas ca añjalikena atha sa mārgaṇa gaṇam mahat karṇa hasta sthitam cāpam ciccheda āśu ghaṭotkacaḥ athā anyat dhanuḥ ādāya dṛḍham bhāra saham mahat tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja preṣayām āsa sāyakān suvarṇa puṅkhān śatru ghnān kha carān rākṣasān prati tat bāṇaiḥ arditam yūtham rakṣasām pīna vakṣasām siṃhena iva arditam vanyam gajānām ākulam kulam vidhamya rākṣasān bāṇaiḥ sa aśva sūta gajān vibhuḥ dadāha bhagavān vahniḥ bhūtāni iva yuga kṣaye sa hatvā rākṣasīm senām śuśubhe sūtanandanaḥ teṣu rāja sahasreṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu māriṣa ṛte ghaṭotkacāt rājan rākṣasa indrāt mahā balāt mahā ulkābhyām yathā rājan sa arciṣaḥ sneha bindavaḥ ratham āsthāya ca punar māyayā nirmitam punar yuktam gaja nibhaiḥ vāhaiḥ piśāca vadanaiḥ kharaiḥ sa sūtam abravīt kruddhaḥ sūtaputrāya mā vaha dvairatham sūtaputreṇa punar eva viśām pate sa cikṣepa punar kruddhaḥ sūtaputrāya rākṣasaḥ aṣṭa cakrām mahā ghorām aśanim rudra nirmitām sa aśva sūta dhvajam yānam bhasma kṛtvā mahā prabhā karṇam tu sarva bhūtāni pūjayām āsuḥ añjasā yat avaplutya jagrāha deva sṛṣṭām mahā aśanim evam kṛtvā raṇe karṇaḥ āruroha ratham punar tatas mumoca nārācān sūtaputraḥ paraṃtapaḥ yat akārṣīt tadā karṇaḥ saṃgrāme bhīma darśane sa hanyamānaḥ nārācaiḥ dhārābhiḥ iva parvataḥ evam sa vai mahā māyaḥ māyayā lāghavena ca astrāṇi tāni divyāni jaghāna ripu sūdanaḥ nihanyamāneṣu astreṣu māyayā tena rakṣasā cakāra bahudhā ātmānam bhīṣayāṇaḥ narādhipān tatas digbhyaḥ samāpetuḥ siṃha vyāghra tarakṣavaḥ agni jihvāḥ ca bhujagāḥ vihagāḥ ca api ayaḥ mukhāḥ sa kīryamāṇaḥ niśitaiḥ karṇa cāpa cyutaiḥ śaraiḥ rākṣasāḥ ca piśācāḥ ca yātudhānāḥ śalāvṛkāḥ te karṇam bhakṣayiṣyantaḥ sarvatas samupādravan athā enam vāgbhiḥ ugrābhiḥ trāsayām cakrire tadā teṣām anekaiḥ ekaikam karṇaḥ vivyādha ca āśugaiḥ pratihatya tu tām māyām divyena astreṇa rākṣasīm ājaghāna hayān asya śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ te bhagnāḥ vikṛta aṅgāḥ ca chinna pṛṣṭhāḥ ca sāyakaiḥ sa bhagna māyaḥ haiḍimbaḥ karṇam vaikartanam tatas saṃjayaḥ uvāca tasmin tathā vartamāne karṇa rākṣasayoḥ mṛdhe rākṣasānām virūpāṇām sahasraiḥ parivāritaḥ tasya jñātiḥ hi vikrāntaḥ brāhmaṇa ādaḥ bakaḥ hataḥ kirmīraḥ ca mahā tejāḥ hiḍimbaḥ ca sakhā tathā vijñāya etat niśā yuddham jighāṃsuḥ bhīmam āhave viditam te mahā rāja yathā bhīmena rākṣasāḥ hiḍimba baka kirmīrāḥ nihatāḥ mama bāndhavāḥ parāmarśaḥ ca kanyāyāḥ hiḍimbāyāḥ kṛtaḥ purā kim anyat rākṣasān anyān asmān ca paribhūya ha tam aham sa gaṇam rājan sa vāji ratha kuñjaram haiḍimbam ca saha amātyam hantum abhyāgataḥ svayam nivāraya balam sarvam vayam yotsyāma pāṇḍavān tasya tat vacanam śrutvā hṛṣṭaḥ duryodhanaḥ tadā pratipūjya abravīt vākyam bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ tvām puraskṛtya sa gaṇam vayam yotsyāmahe parān evam astu iti rājānam uktvā rākṣasa puṃgavaḥ abhyayāt tvaritaḥ bhīmam sahitaḥ puruṣa aśanaiḥ dīpyamānena vapuṣā rathena āditya varcasā tādṛśena eva rāja indra yādṛśena ghaṭotkacaḥ ṛkṣa carma avanaddha aṅgaḥ nalva mātraḥ mahā rathaḥ tasya api turagāḥ śīghrāḥ hasti kāyāḥ khara svanāḥ śatam yuktāḥ mahā kāyāḥ māṃsa śoṇita bhojanāḥ tasya api su mahat cāpam dṛḍha jyam balavattaram tasya api akṣa samāḥ bāṇāḥ rukma puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ sa ca api rūpeṇa ghaṭotkacasya śrīmattamaḥ vyākula dīpita āsyaḥ dīpta aṅgadaḥ dīpta kirīṭa mālī baddha sraj uṣṇīṣa nibaddha khaḍgaḥ gadī bhuśuṇḍī musalī halī ca rathena tena anala varcasā ca vidrāvayan pāṇḍava vāhinīm tām te ca api sarve pravarāḥ narendrāḥ mahā balāḥ varmiṇaḥ carmiṇaḥ ca harṣa anvitāḥ yuyudhuḥ tatra rājan samantataḥ pāṇḍava yodha vīrāḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca tam āgatam abhiprekṣya bhīma karmāṇam āhave harṣam āhārayām cakruḥ kuravaḥ sarve eva te aplavāḥ plavam āsādya tartu kāmāḥ iva arṇavam punar jātam iva ātmānam manvānāḥ pārthivāḥ tadā alāyudham rākṣasa indram svāgatena abhyapūjayan karṇa rākṣasayoḥ naktam dāruṇa pratidarśane upapraikṣanta pāñcālāḥ smayamānāḥ sa rājakāḥ tathā eva tāvakāḥ rājan ghūrṇamānāḥ tatas tatas cukruśuḥ na idam asti iti droṇa drauṇi kṛpa ādayaḥ tat karma dṛṣṭvā saṃbhrāntāḥ haiḍimbasya raṇa ajire tava sainyam mahā rāja nirāśam karṇa jīvite duryodhanaḥ tu saṃprekṣya karṇam ārtim parām gatam alāyudham rākṣasa indram āhūya idam atha abravīt eṣa vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ haiḍimbena samāgataḥ paśya etān pārthivān śūrān nihatān bhaimaseninā nānā śastraiḥ abhihatān pādapān iva dantinā tava eṣa bhāgaḥ samare rāja madhye mayā kṛtaḥ purā vaikartanam karṇam eṣa pāpaḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ māyā balam upāśritya karśayati ari karśanaḥ evam uktaḥ sa rājñā tu rākṣasaḥ tīvra vikramaḥ pratyamitram upāyāntam mardayām āsa mārgaṇaiḥ rakṣasā vipramuktaḥ tu karṇaḥ api rathinām varaḥ tam āyāntam an ādṛtya dṛṣṭvā grastam ghaṭotkacam rathena āditya vapuṣā bhīmaḥ praharatām varaḥ tam bhīmaḥ sahasā abhyetya rākṣasa anta karaḥ prabho sa gaṇam rākṣasa indram tam śara varṣaiḥ avākirat tathā eva alāyudhaḥ rājan śilā dhautaiḥ ajihmagaiḥ tathā te rākṣasāḥ sarve bhīmasenam upādravan nānā praharaṇāḥ bhīmāḥ tvad sutānām jaya eṣiṇaḥ sa tāḍyamānaḥ balibhiḥ bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ sarvān tān avidhyat śitaiḥ śaraiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ bhīmena rākṣasāḥ khara yonayaḥ vineduḥ tumulān nādān dudruvuḥ ca diśaḥ daśa tān trāsyamānān bhīmena dṛṣṭvā rakṣaḥ mahā balam tam bhīmasenaḥ samare tīkṣṇa agraiḥ akṣiṇot śaraiḥ alāyudhaḥ tu tān astān bhīmena viśikhān raṇe ciccheda kān cit samare tvarayā kān cit agrahīt sa tam dṛṣṭvā rākṣasa indram bhīmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ gadām cikṣepa vegena vajra pāta upamām tadā tām āpatantīm vegena gadām jvālā ākulām tatas gadayā tāḍayām āsa sā gadā bhīmam āvrajat sa rākṣasa indram kaunteyaḥ śara varṣaiḥ avākirat tān api asya akarot moghān rākṣasaḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ te ca api rākṣasāḥ sarve sainikāḥ bhīma rūpiṇaḥ śāsanāt rākṣasa indrasya nijaghnuḥ ratha kuñjarān pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāḥ ca eva vājinaḥ parama dvipāḥ na śāntim lebhire tatra rakṣasaiḥ bhṛśa pīḍitāḥ tam tu dṛṣṭvā mahā ghoram vartamānam mahā āhave abravīt puruṣa
