kṛṣṇayoḥ tatas cakṛṣatuḥ bhīmam tasya sarva āyudhāni ca nārāyaṇa astra śānti artham nara nārāyaṇau balāt apakṛṣyamāṇaḥ kaunteyaḥ nadati eva mahā rathaḥ tam abravīt vāsudevaḥ kim idam pāṇḍu nandana evam uktvā tatas kṛṣṇaḥ rathāt bhūmim apātayat niḥśvasantam yathā nāgam krodha saṃrakta locanam yadā apakṛṣṭaḥ sa rathāt nyāsitaḥ ca āyudham bhuvi tatas nārāyaṇa astram tat praśāntam śatru tāpanam babhūvuḥ vimalāḥ sarvāḥ diśaḥ pradiśaḥ eva ca pravavuḥ ca śivāḥ vātāḥ praśāntāḥ mṛga pakṣiṇaḥ vāhanāni ca hṛṣṭāni yodhāḥ ca manuja īśvara babhau bhīmaḥ niśā apāye dhīmān sūryaḥ iva uditaḥ hata śeṣam balam tatra pāṇḍavānām atiṣṭhata astra vyuparamāt dhṛṣṭam tava putra jighāṃsayā vyavasthitāḥ hi pāñcālāḥ punar eva jaya eṣiṇaḥ aśvatthāmā tathā uktaḥ tu tava putreṇa māriṣa su dīnam abhiniḥśvasya rājānam idam abravīt eṣa ca astra pratīghātam vāsudevaḥ prayuktavān parājayaḥ vā mṛtyuḥ vā śreyaḥ mṛtyuḥ na nirjayaḥ nirjitāḥ ca arayaḥ hi ete śastra utsargāt mṛta upamāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca dṛṣṭvā pārthān ca saṃgrāme yuddhāya samavasthitān nārāyaṇa astra nirmuktān carataḥ pṛtanā mukhe saṃjayaḥ uvāca jānan pituḥ sa nidhanam siṃha lāṅgūla ketanaḥ abhidrutya ca viṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām nara ṛṣabhaḥ pañcabhiḥ ca ati vegena vivyādha puruṣa ṛṣabham droṇaputram triṣaṣṭyā tu rājan vivyādha patriṇām sārathim ca asya viṃśatyā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ hayān ca caturaḥ avidhyat caturbhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ādadat sarva lokasya prāṇān iva mahā raṇe pārṣataḥ tu balī rājan kṛtāstraḥ kṛta niśramaḥ drauṇim eva abhidudrāva kṛtvā mṛtyum nivartanam tatas bāṇa mayam varṣam droṇaputrasya mūrdhani avāsṛjat ameya ātmā pāñcālyaḥ rathinām varaḥ tam drauṇiḥ samare kruddhaḥ chādayām āsa patribhiḥ dvābhyām ca su vikṛṣṭābhyām kṣurābhyām dhvaja kārmuke chittvā pāñcāla rājasya drauṇiḥ anyaiḥ samārdayat vyaśva sūta ratham ca enam drauṇiḥ cakre mahā āhave pradrudrāva tatas sainyam pāñcālānām viśām pate saṃbhrānta rūpam ārtam ca śara varṣa parikṣatam dṛṣṭvā ca vimukhān yodhān dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca pīḍitam śaineyaḥ acodayat tūrṇam raṇam drauṇi ratham prati aṣṭabhiḥ niśitaiḥ ca eva saḥ aśvatthāmānam ārdayat viṃśatyā punar āhatya nānā rūpaiḥ amarṣaṇam vivyādha ca tathā sūtam caturbhiḥ caturaḥ hayān saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ nānā liṅgaiḥ amarṣaṇaḥ śaineya abhyavapattim te jānāmi ācārya ghātinaḥ evam uktvā arka raśmi ābham su parvāṇam śara uttamam vyasṛjat sātvate drauṇiḥ vajram vṛtre yathā hariḥ sa tam nirbhidya tena astaḥ sāyakaḥ sa śarāvaram viveśa vasudhām bhittvā śvasan bilam iva uragaḥ vimucya sa śaram cāpam bhūri vraṇa parisravaḥ sūtena apahṛtaḥ tūrṇam droṇaputrāt ratha antaram athā anyena su puṅkhena śareṇa nata parvaṇā ājaghāna bhruvoḥ madhye dhṛṣṭadyumnam paraṃtapaḥ sa pūrvam atividdhaḥ ca bhṛśam paścāt ca pīḍitaḥ sasāda yudhi pāñcālyaḥ vyapāśrayata ca dhvajam javena abhyadravan śūrāḥ pañca pāṇḍavataḥ rathāḥ kirīṭī bhīmasenaḥ ca vṛddhakṣatraḥ ca pauravaḥ yuvarājaḥ ca cedīnām mālavaḥ ca sudarśanaḥ āśīviṣa ābhaiḥ viṃśadbhiḥ pañcabhiḥ ca api tān śaraiḥ ciccheda yugapad drauṇiḥ pañcaviṃśati sāyakān saptabhiḥ ca śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pauravam drauṇiḥ ārdayat mālavam tribhiḥ ekena pārtham ṣaḍbhiḥ vṛkodaram tatas te vivyadhuḥ sarve drauṇim rājan mahā rathāḥ yugapad ca pṛthak ca eva rukma puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ yuvarājaḥ tu viṃśatyā drauṇim vivyādha patriṇām pārthaḥ ca punar aṣṭābhiḥ tathā sarve tribhiḥ tribhiḥ tatas arjunam ṣaḍbhiḥ atha ājaghāna drauṇāyaniḥ daśabhiḥ vāsudevam bhīmam daśārdhaiḥ yuvarājam caturbhiḥ dvābhyām chittvā kārmukam ca dhvajam ca punar pārtham śara varṣeṇa viddhvā drauṇiḥ ghoram siṃhanādam nanāda tasya asyataḥ su niśitān pīta dhārān drauṇeḥ śarān pṛṣṭhatas ca agratas ca dharā viyat dyauḥ pradiśaḥ diśaḥ ca channāḥ bāṇaiḥ abhavan ghora rūpaiḥ āsīnasya sva ratham tu ugra tejāḥ sudarśanasya indra ketu prakāśau sa pauravam ratha śaktyā nihatya chittvā ratham tilaśas ca api bāṇaiḥ yuvānam indīvara dāma varṇam cedi priyam yuvarājam prahasya bāṇaiḥ tvarāvān jvalita agni kalpaiḥ viddhvā prādāt mṛtyave sa aśva sūtam tān nihatya raṇe vīraḥ droṇaputraḥ yudhām patiḥ dadhmau pramuditaḥ śaṅkham bṛhantam aparājitaḥ tatas sarve ca pāñcālāḥ bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna ratham bhītāḥ tyaktvā saṃprādravan diśaḥ tān prabhagnān tathā drauṇiḥ pṛṣṭhatas vikiran śaraiḥ abhyavartata vegena kāla vat pāṇḍu vāhinīm te vadhyamānāḥ samare droṇaputreṇa kṣatriyāḥ droṇaputram bhayāt rājan dikṣu sarvāsu menire saṃjayaḥ uvāca tat prabhagnam balam dṛṣṭvā kuntī putraḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ savyasācī mahā iṣvāsam aśvatthāmānam abravīt yā śaktiḥ yat ca te vīryam yat jñānam yat ca pauruṣam dhārtarāṣṭreṣu yā prītiḥ pradveṣaḥ asmāsu yaḥ ca te saḥ eva droṇa hantā te darpam bhetsyati pārṣataḥ samāsādaya pāñcālyam mām ca api saha keśavam dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca ācārya putraḥ māna arhaḥ balavān ca api saṃjaya prītiḥ dhanaṃjaye ca asya priyaḥ ca api sa vāsaveḥ na bhūta pūrvam bībhatsoḥ vākyam paruṣam īdṛśam atha kasmāt sa kaunteyaḥ sakhāyam rūkṣam abravīt saṃjayaḥ uvāca dhṛṣṭadyumne sātyakau ca bhīme ca api parājite abhūta pūrvaḥ bībhatsoḥ duḥkhāt manyuḥ ajāyata mānyam ācārya tanayam rūkṣam kāpuruṣaḥ yathā evam uktaḥ śvasan krodhāt mahā iṣvāsatamaḥ nṛpa pārthena paruṣam vākyam sarva marma ghnayā girā drauṇiḥ cukopa pārthāya kṛṣṇāya ca viśeṣataḥ dṛśya adṛśyān ari gaṇān uddiśya ācārya nandanaḥ sarvatas krodham āviśya cikṣepa para vīra hā tatas tumulam ākāśe śara varṣam ajāyata vavuḥ ca śiśirāḥ vātāḥ sūryaḥ nā eva tatāpa ca cukruśuḥ dānavāḥ ca api dikṣu sarvāsu bhairavam pakṣiṇaḥ paśavaḥ gāvaḥ munayaḥ ca api suvratāḥ śara tejaḥ abhisaṃtaptāḥ nāgāḥ bhūmiśayāḥ tathā na śāntim upajagmuḥ hi tapyamānaiḥ jalāśayaiḥ diśaḥ kham pradiśaḥ ca eva bhuvam ca śara vṛṣṭayaḥ uccāvacāḥ nipetuḥ vai garuḍa anila raṃhasaḥ pradagdhāḥ śatravaḥ petuḥ agni dagdhāḥ iva drumāḥ dahyamānāḥ mahā nāgāḥ petuḥ urvyām samantataḥ apare pradrutāḥ tatra dahyamānāḥ mahā gajāḥ tresuḥ tathā apare ghore vane dāva agni saṃvṛtāḥ drumāṇām śikharāṇi iva dāva dagdhāni māriṣa aśva vṛndāni adṛśyanta ratha vṛndāni ca abhibho yuga ante sarva bhūtāni saṃvartakaḥ iva analaḥ dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavīm senām dahyamānām mahā āhave prahṛṣṭāḥ tāvakāḥ rājan siṃhanādān vinedire tatas tūrya sahasrāṇi nānā liṅgāni bhārata tūrṇam ājaghnire hṛṣṭāḥ tāvakāḥ jita kāśinaḥ kṛtsnā hi akṣauhiṇī rājan savyasācī ca pāṇḍavaḥ tamasā saṃvṛte loke na adṛśyata mahā āhave na eva naḥ tādṛśam rājan dṛṣṭa pūrvam na ca śrutam yādṛśam droṇaputreṇa sṛṣṭam astram amarṣiṇā pravavau ca anilaḥ śītaḥ diśaḥ ca vimalāḥ abhavan tatra adbhutam apaśyāma kṛtsnām akṣauhiṇīm hatām an abhijñeya rūpām ca pradagdhām astra māyayā sahitau saṃpradṛśyetām nabhasi iva tamonudau tatas kilakilā śabdaḥ śaṅkha bherī ravaiḥ saha pāṇḍavānām prahṛṣṭānām kṣaṇena samajāyata tarasā abhyāgatau dṛṣṭvā vimuktau keśava arjunau dṛṣṭvā pramuditān pārthān tvadīyāḥ vyathitāḥ abhavan vimuktau ca mahātmānau dṛṣṭvā drauṇiḥ su duḥkhitaḥ muhūrtam cintayām āsa kim tu etat iti māriṣa cintayitvā tu rāja indra dhyāna śoka parāyaṇaḥ niḥśvasan dīrgham uṣṇam ca vimanāḥ ca abhavat tadā tatas snigdha ambuda ābhāsam vedavyāsam akalmaṣam āvāsam ca sarasvatyāḥ sa vai vyāsam dadarśa ha tam drauṇiḥ agratas dṛṣṭvā sthitam kuru kula udvaha bho bho māyā yadṛcchā vā na vidmaḥ kim idam bhavet adhara uttaram etat vā lokānām vā parābhavaḥ yat imau jīvataḥ kṛṣṇau kālaḥ hi duratikramaḥ na asura amara gandharvāḥ na piśācāḥ na rākṣasāḥ na sarpa yakṣa patagāḥ na manuṣyāḥ katham cana tat idam kevalam hatvā yuktām akṣauhiṇīm jvalat etat prabrūhi bhagavat mayā pṛṣṭaḥ yathātatham vyāsaḥ uvāca mahāntam etam artham mām yam tvam pṛcchasi vismayāt tat pravakṣyāmi te sarvam samādhāya manaḥ śṛṇu yaḥ asau nārāyaṇaḥ nāma pūrveṣām api pūrvajaḥ ūrdhvabāhuḥ mahā tejāḥ jvalana āditya saṃnibhaḥ ṣaṣṭim varṣa sahasrāṇi tāvanti eva śatāni ca aśoṣayat tadā ātmānam vāyubhakṣaḥ ambuja īkṣaṇaḥ dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ vivaram tejasā samapūrayat tatas viśveśvaram yonim viśvasya jagataḥ patim dadarśa bhṛśa durdarśam sarva devaiḥ api īśvaram aṇīyasām aṇīyāṃsam bṛhadbhyaḥ ca bṛhattaram rudram īśānam ṛṣabham cekitānam ajam param durvāraṇam durdṛśam tigma manyum mahātmānam sarva haram pracetasam divyam cāpam iṣudhī ca ādadānam hiraṇya varmāṇam ananta vīryam pinākinam vajriṇam dīpta śūlam paraśvadhim gadinam su āyata asim subhrum jaṭā maṇḍala candra maulim vyāghra ajinam parigham daṇḍapāṇim śubha aṅgadam nāga yajña upavītim viśvaiḥ gaṇaiḥ śobhitam bhūta saṃghaiḥ ekībhūtam tapasām saṃnidhānam vayotigaiḥ suṣṭutam iṣṭa vāgbhiḥ jalam divam kham kṣitim candra sūryau tathā vāyu agnī pratimānam jagat ca na alam draṣṭum yama jam bhinna vṛttā yam paśyanti brāhmaṇāḥ sādhu vṛttāḥ kṣīṇe pāpe manasā ye viśokāḥ sa tad niṣṭhaḥ tapasā dharmam īḍyam tad bhaktyā vai viśvarūpam dadarśa dṛṣṭvā ca enam vāc manaḥ buddhi dehaiḥ saṃhṛṣṭa ātmā mumude devadevam akṣa mālā parikṣiptam jyotiṣām paramam nidhim tatas nārāyaṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā vavande viśva saṃbhavam vara dam pṛthu cāru aṅgyā pārvatyā sahitam prabhum ajam īśānam avyagram kāraṇa ātmānam acyutam padmākṣaḥ tam virūpākṣam abhituṣṭāva bhaktimān tvat saṃbhūtāḥ bhūta kṛtaḥ vareṇya goptāraḥ adya bhuvanam pūrvadevāḥ āviśya imām dharaṇīm ye abhyarakṣan purā purāṇām tava deva sṛṣṭim sura asurān nāga rakṣaḥ piśācān narān suparṇān atha gandharva yakṣān pṛthagvidhān bhūta saṃghān ca viśvān tvad saṃbhūtān vidma sarvān tathā eva aindram yāmyam vāruṇam vaittapālyam maitram tvāṣṭram karma saumyam ca tubhyam rūpam jyotiḥ śabdaḥ ākāśa vāyuḥ sparśaḥ svādyam salilam gandhaḥ urvī kāmaḥ brahmā brahma ca brāhmaṇāḥ ca tvad saṃbhūtam sthāsnu cariṣṇu ca idam adbhyaḥ stokāḥ yānti yathā pṛthaktvam tābhiḥ ca aikyam saṃkṣaye yānti bhūyas evam vidvān prabhavam ca api ayam ca hitvā bhūtānām tatra sāyujyam eti divya āvṛtau mānasau dvau suparṇau avāc śākhaḥ pippalaḥ sapta gopāḥ daśa api anye ye puram dhārayanti tvayā sṛṣṭāḥ te hi tebhyaḥ paraḥ tvam bhūtam bhavyam bhavitā ca api adhṛṣyam tvad saṃbhūtā bhuvanāni iha viśvā bhaktam ca mām bhajamānam bhajasva mā rīriṣaḥ mām ahita ahitena ātmānam tvām ātmanaḥ an anya bhāvaḥ astauṣam tvām tava saṃmānam icchan vicinvan vai sa vṛṣam deva varya su durlabhān dehi varān mama iṣṭān abhiṣṭutaḥ pratikārṣīḥ ca mā mām tasmai varān acintya ātmā nīlakaṇṭhaḥ pinākadhṛk arhate deva mukhyāya prāyacchat ṛṣi saṃstutaḥ nīlakaṇṭhaḥ uvāca aprameya bala ātmā tvam nārāyaṇa bhaviṣyasi na piśācāḥ na gandharvāḥ na narāḥ na ca rākṣasāḥ na suparṇāḥ tathā nāgāḥ na ca viśve viyoni jāḥ na śastreṇa na vajreṇa na agninā na ca vāyunā na ārdreṇa na ca śuṣkeṇa trasena sthāvareṇa vā vyāsaḥ uvāca evam ete varāḥ labdhāḥ purastāt viddhi śauriṇā tasya eva tapasā jātam naram nāma mahā munim tau etau pūrvadevānām parama upacitau ṛṣī lokayātrā vidhāna artham saṃjāyete yuge yuge sa bhavān deva vat prājñaḥ jñātvā bhava mayam jagat śubham aurvam navam kṛtvā mahā puruṣa vigraham ījivān tvam japaiḥ homaiḥ upahāraiḥ ca mānada sa tathā pūjyamānaḥ te pūrvadevaḥ api atūtuṣat puṣkalān ca varān prādāt tava vidvan hṛdi sthitān tābhyām liṅge arcitaḥ devaḥ tvayā arcāyām yuge yuge sarva rūpam bhavam jñātvā liṅge yaḥ arcayati prabhum ātma yogāḥ ca tasmin vai śāstra yogāḥ ca śāśvatāḥ evam devāḥ yajantaḥ hi siddhāḥ ca parama ṛṣayaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ eva hi yaṣṭavyaḥ yajñaiḥ ca eṣa sanātanaḥ sarva bhūta bhavam jñātvā liṅge arcayati yaḥ prabhum tasmin abhyadhikām prītim karoti vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ saṃjayaḥ uvāca hṛṣṭa lomā ca vaśya ātmā namaskṛtya mahā ṛṣaye tatas pratyavahāraḥ abhūt pāṇḍavānām viśām pate kauravāṇām ca dīnānām droṇe yudhi nipātite yuddham kṛtvā dinān pañca droṇaḥ hatvā varūthinīm brahma lokam gataḥ rājan brāhmaṇaḥ vedapāragaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ uvāca māmakāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca eva kim akurvan atas param saṃjayaḥ uvāca dṛṣṭvā su mahat āścaryam ātmanaḥ vijaya āvaham saṃgrāme nighnataḥ śatrūn śara oghaiḥ vimalaiḥ aham agratas lakṣaye yāntam puruṣam pāvaka prabham jvalantam śūlam udyamya yām diśam pratipadyate tasyām diśi viśīryante śatravaḥ me mahā mune na padbhyām spṛśate bhūmim na ca śūlam vimuñcati śūlāt śūla sahasrāṇi niṣpetuḥ tasya tejasā tena dagdhāni sainyāni pṛṣṭhatas anudahāmi aham śūla pāṇiḥ mahān kṛṣṇa tejasā sūrya saṃnibhaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca prajāpatīnām prathamam taijasam puruṣam vibhum īśānam vara dam pārtha dṛṣṭavān asi śaṃkaram tam gaccha śaraṇam devam sarva ādim bhuvaneśvaram mahādevam mahātmānam īśānam jaṭilam śivam tryakṣam mahā bhujam rudram śikhinam cīra vāsasam dātāram ca eva bhaktānām prasāda vihitān varān tasya te pārṣadāḥ divyāḥ rūpaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ vibhoḥ vāmanāḥ jaṭilāḥ muṇḍāḥ hrasva grīvāḥ mahā udarāḥ mahā kāyāḥ mahā utsāhāḥ mahā karṇāḥ tathā apare ānanaiḥ vikṛtaiḥ pādaiḥ pārtha veṣaiḥ ca vaikṛtaiḥ īdṛśaiḥ sa mahādevaḥ pūjyamānaḥ maheśvaraḥ sa śivaḥ tāta tejasvī prasādāt yāti te agratas tasmin ghore tadā pārtha saṃgrāme loma harṣaṇe droṇa karṇa kṛpaiḥ guptām mahā iṣvāsaiḥ prahāribhiḥ kaḥ tām senām tadā pārtha manasā api pradharṣayet ṛte devāt mahā iṣvāsāt bahu rūpāt maheśvarāt visaṃjñāḥ hata bhūyiṣṭhāḥ vepanti ca patanti ca ye bhaktāḥ vara dam devam śivam rudram umāpatim rudrāya śitikaṇṭhāya kaniṣṭhāya su varcase yāmyāya avyakta keśāya sat vṛtte śaṃkarāya ca kāmyāya hari netrāya sthāṇave puruṣāya ca hari keśāya muṇḍāya kṛśāya uttaraṇāya ca bhāskarāya su tīrthāya devadevāya raṃhase bahurūpāya śarvāya priyāya priya vāsase uṣṇīṣiṇe su vaktrāya sahasra akṣāya mīḍhuṣe giriśāya praśāntāya pataye cīra vāsase vṛkṣāṇām pataye ca eva apām ca pataye tathā vṛkṣaiḥ āvṛta kāyāya senānye madhyamāya ca umāpatim virūpākṣam dakṣa yajña nibarhaṇam prajānām patim avyagram bhūtānām patim avyayam kapardinam vṛṣāvartam vṛṣanābham vṛṣadhvajam vṛṣa darpam vṛṣa patim vṛṣa śṛṅgam vṛṣa ṛṣabham vṛṣāṅkam vṛṣabha udāram vṛṣabham vṛṣabha īkṣaṇam vṛṣa āyudham vṛṣa śaram vṛṣa bhūtam maheśvaram mahodaram mahā kāyam dvīpi carma nivāsinam lokeśam vara dam muṇḍam brahmaṇyam brāhmaṇapriyam triśūla pāṇim vara dam khaḍga carma dharam prabhum pinākinam khaṇḍaparaśum lokānām patim īśvaram prapadye śaraṇam devam śaraṇyam cīra vāsasam namaḥ tasmai sura īśāya yasya vaiśravaṇaḥ sakhā vanaspatīnām pataye narāṇām pataye namaḥ apām ca pataye nityam yajñānām pataye namaḥ pūṣṇaḥ danta vināśāya tryakṣāya vara dāya ca nīlakaṇṭhāya piṅgāya svarṇa keśāya vai namaḥ karmāṇi ca eva divyāni mahādevasya dhīmataḥ tāni te kīrtayiṣyāmi yathāprajñam yathāśrutam na surāḥ na asurāḥ loke na gandharvāḥ na rākṣasāḥ dhanuṣā bāṇam utsṛjya sa ghoṣam vinanāda ca te na śarma kutas śāntim lebhire sma surāḥ tadā tena jyā tala ghoṣeṇa sarve lokāḥ samākulāḥ babhūvuḥ vaśa gāḥ pārtha nipetuḥ ca sura asurāḥ āpaḥ cukṣubhire sarvāḥ cakampe ca vasuṃdharā parvatāḥ ca vyaśīryanta diśaḥ nāgāḥ ca mohitāḥ andhāḥ ca tamasā lokāḥ na prakāśanta saṃvṛtāḥ jaghnivān saha sūryeṇa sarveṣām jyotiṣām prabhāḥ cukruśuḥ bhaya bhītāḥ ca śāntim cakruḥ tathā eva ca ṛṣayaḥ sarva bhūtānām ātmanaḥ ca sukha eṣiṇaḥ pūṣāṇam abhyadravata śaṃkaraḥ prahasan iva puroḍāśam bhakṣayataḥ daśanān vai vyaśātayat tatas niścakramuḥ devāḥ vepamānāḥ natāḥ sma tam punar ca saṃdadhe dīptam devānām niśitam śaram rudrasya yajña bhāgam ca viśiṣṭam te nu akalpayan bhayena tridaśāḥ rājan śaraṇam ca prapedire yattāḥ ca api surāḥ āsan yattāḥ ca adya api tam prati asurāṇām purāṇi āsan trīṇi vīryavatām divi āyasam rājatam ca eva sauvarṇam aparam mahat āyasam tārakākṣasya kamalākṣasya rājatam sauvarṇam paramam hi āsīt vidyunmālinaḥ eva ca atha sarve amarāḥ rudram jagmuḥ śaraṇam arditāḥ te tam ūcuḥ mahātmānam sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ atiṣṭhat sthāṇu bhūtaḥ sa sahasram parivatsarān yadā trīṇi sametāni antarikṣe purāṇi vai purāṇi na ca tam śekuḥ dānavāḥ prativīkṣitum śaram kālāgni saṃyuktam viṣṇu soma samāyutam bālam aṅka gatam kṛtvā svayam pañcaśikham punar umā jijñāsamānā vai kaḥ ayam iti abravīt surān saḥ eṣa bhagavān devaḥ sarva loka īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ sa prajāpatayaḥ sarve bāla arka sadṛśa prabham athā abhyetya tatas brahmā dṛṣṭvā ca sa maheśvaram ayam śreṣṭhaḥ iti jñātvā vavande tam pitāmahaḥ tatas prasādayām āsuḥ umām rudram ca te surāḥ teṣām prasannaḥ bhagavān sa patnīkaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ devānām tridaśa śreṣṭhaḥ dakṣa yajña vināśanaḥ sa candramāḥ sa ca īśānaḥ sa sūryaḥ varuṇaḥ ca saḥ sa kālaḥ saḥ antakaḥ mṛtyuḥ sa yamaḥ rātri ahāni ca māsa ardha māsāḥ ṛtavaḥ saṃdhye saṃvatsaraḥ ca saḥ sa ca dhātā vidhātā ca viśvātmā viśva karma kṛt sarvāsām devatānām ca dhārayati avapuḥ vapuḥ īdṛśaḥ sa mahādevaḥ bhūyas ca bhagavān ajaḥ na hi sarve mayā śakyāḥ vaktum bhagavataḥ guṇāḥ sa mocayati su prītaḥ śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇa āgatān āyuḥ ārogyam aiśvaryam vittam kāmān ca puṣkalān sa dadāti manuṣyebhyaḥ sa ca eva ākṣipate punar sa ca eva vyāhṛte loke manuṣyāṇām śubha aśubhe aiśvaryāt ca eva kāmānām īśvaraḥ punar ucyate maheśvaraḥ ca bhūtānām mahatām īśvaraḥ ca saḥ eṣa ca eva śmaśāneṣu devaḥ vasati nityaśas yajanti enam janāḥ tatra vīrasthāne iti īśvaram asya dīptāni rūpāṇi ghorāṇi ca bahūni ca vede ca asya samāmnātam śatarudrīyam uttamam nāmnā ca ananta rudra iti upasthānam mahātmanaḥ sa kāmānām prabhuḥ devaḥ ye divyāḥ ye ca mānuṣāḥ jyeṣṭham bhūtam vadanti enam brāhmaṇāḥ munayaḥ tathā prathamaḥ hi eṣa devānām mukhāt asya analaḥ abhavat sarvathā yat paśūn pāti taiḥ ca yat ramate punar teṣām adhipatiḥ yat ca tasmāt paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca eva devāḥ ca gandharva apsarasaḥ tathā sukhī prītaḥ ca bhavati prahṛṣṭaḥ ca eva śaṃkaraḥ sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca eva bahurūpaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ eka akṣaḥ jājvalan āste sarvata ukṣi mayaḥ api vā krodhāt yaḥ ca aviśat lokān tasmāt śarvaḥ iti smṛtaḥ viśve devāḥ ca yat tasmin viśvarūpaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ dyām apaḥ pṛthivīm ca eva tryambakaḥ ca tatas smṛtaḥ śivam icchan manuṣyāṇām tasmāt eśa śivaḥ smṛtaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ ayuta akṣaḥ vā sarvata ukṣi mayaḥ api vā yat ca viśvam mahat pāti mahādevaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ sthita liṅgaḥ ca yat nityam tasmāt sthāṇuḥ iti smṛtaḥ viṣama sthaḥ śarīreṣu samaḥ ca prāṇinām iha sa vāyuḥ viṣama stheṣu prāṇa apāna śarīriṣu liṅgam pūjayitā nityam mahatīm śriyam aśnute ūrubhyām ardham āgneyam soma ardham ca śivā tanuḥ taijasī mahatī dīptā devebhyaḥ ca śivā tanuḥ bhāsvatī mānuṣeṣu asya tanuḥ ghorā agniḥ ucyate brahmacaryam carati eṣa śivā yā asya tanuḥ tayā yā asya ghoratarā mūrtiḥ sarvān atti tayā īśvaraḥ saṃgrāme śātravān nighnan tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ pinākadhṛk eṣa vai bhagavān devaḥ saṃgrāme yāti te agratas yena dattāni te astrāṇi yaiḥ tvayā dānavāḥ hatāḥ dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam puṇyam vedaiḥ ca saṃjñitam sarva artha sādhakam puṇyam sarva kilbiṣa nāśanam caturvidham idam stotram yaḥ śṛṇoti naraḥ sadā caritam mahātmanaḥ divyam sāṃgrāmikam idam śubham paṭhan vai śatarudrīyam śṛṇvan ca satata utthitaḥ bhaktaḥ viśveśvaram devam mānuṣeṣu tu yaḥ sadā saṃjayaḥ uvāca evam uktvā arjunam saṃkhye parāśara sutaḥ tadā jagāma bharata śreṣṭha yathāgatam ariṃdama
